# Piancilna (Pia)

## Chapter 1

**1:1**
Zolai: A kipat cil-in Pasian in vantung le leitung a piangsak hi.
English: In the beginning God created the heaven and the earth.

**1:2**
Zolai: Leitung in limlemel nei loin a awngthawlpi ahi hi. Tuipi tung tengah khua mial bikbek a, tua tui tungah Pasian’ Kha in na a sem hi.
English: And the earth was without form, and void; and darkness was upon the face of the deep. And the Spirit of God moved upon the face of the waters.

**1:3**
Zolai: Pasian in, “Khuavak om hen,” ci hi; tua ciangin khuavak om pah hi.
English: And God said, Let there be light: and there was light.

**1:4**
Zolai: Pasian in tua khuavak hoih hi, ci-in a mu hi. Pasian in khuamial panin khuavak khenkhia hi.
English: And God saw the light, that it was good: and God divided the light from the darkness.

**1:5**
Zolai: Pasian in khuavak pen “Sun” ci a, khuamial pen “Zan” ci hi. Nitak hong bei-in, zingsang hong tung a, ni khat ni ahi hi.
English: And God called the light Day, and the darkness he called Night. And the evening and the morning were the first day.

**1:6**
Zolai: Pasian in, “Tuite’ laizangah van kuumpi om hen la, tua van kuumpi in tui le tui kikhensak hen,” ci hi.
English: And God said, Let there be a firmament in the midst of the waters, and let it divide the waters from the waters.

**1:7**
Zolai: Pasian in van kuumpi bawl a, van kuumpi tunga om tuite le van kuumpi nuai-a om tuite a khen hi. Tua mah bangin a piang pah hi.
English: And God made the firmament, and divided the waters which were under the firmament from the waters which were above the firmament: and it was so.

**1:8**
Zolai: Pasian in van kuumpi pen “Vantung” ci hi. Nitak hong bei-in zingsang hong tung a, ni nih ni ahi hi.
English: And God called the firmament Heaven. And the evening and the morning were the second day.

**1:9**
Zolai: Pasian in, “Vantungte nuai-a om tuite mun khatah kikhawm hen la, lei keu kidawk hen,” ci hi. Tua mah bangin a piang pah hi.
English: And God said, Let the waters under the heaven be gathered together unto one place, and let the dry land appear: and it was so.

**1:10**
Zolai: Pasian in lei keu pen “Leitung” ci a, a kikaikhawm tuite pen “Tuipi” ci hi. Pasian in tua pen hoih hi, ci-in a mu hi.
English: And God called the dry land Earth; and the gathering together of the waters called he Seas: and God saw that it was good.

**1:11**
Zolai: Pasian in, “Leitung in kung tuamtuamte piangsak hen la, tang a nei kungnote, a gah sungah tang a om singgah kungte, amau’ nam ciatin leitungah piangsak hen,” ci hi. Tua mah bangin a piang pah hi.
English: And God said, Let the earth bring forth grass, the herb yielding seed, and the fruit tree yielding fruit after his kind, whose seed is in itself, upon the earth: and it was so.

**1:12**
Zolai: Leitung in kung tuamtuamte piangkhiasak a, kungnote in amau’ nam ciatin tang piangsakin, singkung in a sungah tang a om gahte piangsakin, amau’ nam ciatciatin piangsak hi. Pasian in tua pen hoih hi, ci-in a mu hi.
English: And the earth brought forth grass, and herb yielding seed after his kind, and the tree yielding fruit, whose seed was in itself, after his kind: and God saw that it was good.

**1:13**
Zolai: Nitak hong bei-in zingsang hong tung a, ni thum ni ahi hi.
English: And the evening and the morning were the third day.

**1:14**
Zolai: Pasian in, “Sun le zan a khen dingin vantungah khuavakte om hen; tuate pen pawi hun le khuahun, ni le kumte khen nading hi hen la,
English: And God said, Let there be lights in the firmament of the heaven to divide the day from the night; and let them be for signs, and for seasons, and for days, and years:

**1:15**
Zolai: leitung khua a vaksak dingin vantungah khuavak hi uh hen,” ci hi. Tua mah bangin a piang pah hi.
English: and let them be for lights in the firmament of the heaven to give light upon the earth: and it was so.

**1:16**
Zolai: Pasian in khuavak lian nih bawl a, khuavak lianzaw pen sun a uk ding, khuavak neuzaw pen zan a uk dingin bawl a, amah in aksite zong a bawl hi.
English: And God made two great lights; the greater light to rule the day, and the lesser light to rule the night: he made the stars also.

**1:17**
Zolai: Leitungah khua a vaksak ding, sun le zan a uk ding, khuamial panin khuavak a khenkhia dingin Pasian in vantungah tuate a koih hi. Pasian in tua pen hoih hi, ci-in a mu hi.
English: And God set them in the firmament of the heaven to give light upon the earth,

**1:19**
Zolai: Nitak hong bei-in zingsang hong tung a, ni li ni ahi hi.
English: And the evening and the morning were the fourth day.

**1:20**
Zolai: Pasian in, “Tuite in a nungta ganhing honpite piangsak hen la, vantung kantanin leitungah vasate leeng ta hen,” ci hi.
English: And God said, Let the waters bring forth abundantly the moving creature that hath life, and fowl that may fly above the earth in the open firmament of heaven.

**1:21**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in tuipi ganhing golpite le amau nam ciatin tuipi sungah tampi a pha, nuntakna a nei a gamtang thei ganhing namkim le kha a nei vasa khempeuh amau nam ciatin a piangsak hi. Pasian in tua pen hoih hi, ci-in a mu hi.
English: And God created great whales, and every living creature that moveth, which the waters brought forth abundantly, after their kind, and every winged fowl after his kind: and God saw that it was good.

**1:22**
Zolai: Pasian in amaute thupha pia a, “Ci pha-in tampi pha-in, tuipi sung dim unla, leitungah vasate tampi pha un,” ci hi.
English: And God blessed them, saying, Be fruitful, and multiply, and fill the waters in the seas, and let fowl multiply in the earth.

**1:23**
Zolai: Nitak hong bei-in zingsang hong tung a, a ni nga ni ahi hi.
English: And the evening and the morning were the fifth day.

**1:24**
Zolai: Pasian in, “Nuntakna a nei ganhingte amau nam ciatin leitung in piangsak hen: Innsa, gamsa, le a bokvak ganhingte amau nam ciatin piang ta hen,” a ci hi. Tua mah bangin a piang pah hi.
English: And God said, Let the earth bring forth the living creature after his kind, cattle, and creeping thing, and beast of the earth after his kind: and it was so.

**1:25**
Zolai: Innsa, gamsa, le a bokvak ganhing khempeuh amau nam ciatin Pasian in a piangsak hi. Pasian in tua pen hoih hi, ci-in a mu hi.
English: And God made the beast of the earth after his kind, and cattle after their kind, and every thing that creepeth upon the earth after his kind: and God saw that it was good.

**1:26**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Pasian in, “Eima lim, eimah hong sunin mihing bawl ni. Tuipi ngasate tung, huihlak vasate tung, ganhingte tung, le leitung a a bokvakte khempeuh tungah ukna neisak ni,” a ci hi.
English: And God said, Let us make man in our image, after our likeness: and let them have dominion over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over the cattle, and over all the earth, and over every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth.

**1:27**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in ama lim bangin mihing piangsakin, Pasian’ lim bangin amah a piangsak hi. Amah in pasal le numei a piangsak hi.
English: So God created man in his own image, in the image of God created he him; male and female created he them.

**1:28**
Zolai: Pasian in amaute thupha pia a, Pasian in amaute tungah, “Ci pha-in tampi pha unla, leitung dimin zo un. Tuipi ngasate tung, leitungah a gamtang, a nungtate khempeuh tungah ukna nei ta un,” a ci hi.
English: And God blessed them, and God said unto them, Be fruitful, and multiply, and replenish the earth, and subdue it: and have dominion over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over every living thing that moveth upon the earth.

**1:29**
Zolai: Pasian in, “En un, leitung maitang khempeuhah a om, tang a piangsak kungnote khempeuh le a gah sungah tang a om singkung khempeuh note tungah kong pia khinta hi. Tuate an-in na nei ding uh hi.
English: And God said, Behold, I have given you every herb bearing seed, which is upon the face of all the earth, and every tree, in the which is the fruit of a tree yielding seed; to you it shall be for meat.

**1:30**
Zolai: Leitung ganhing khempeuhte tung, huih lak vasate khempeuh tung, leitungah a bokvakte khempeuh tung, nuntakna hu a neite khempeuh tungah an dingin kung hing khempeuh ka hong pia khinta hi,” a ci hi. Tua mah bangin a piang pah hi.
English: And to every beast of the earth, and to every fowl of the air, and to every thing that creepeth upon the earth, wherein there is life, I have given every green herb for meat: and it was so.

**1:31**
Zolai: Pasian in a bawlsate khempeuh en a, hoih sa mahmah hi. Nitak hong bei-in zingsang hong tung a, a ni guk ni ahi hi.
English: And God saw every thing that he had made, and, behold, it was very good. And the evening and the morning were the sixth day.

## Chapter 2

**2:1**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin vantung, leitung, le a sunga omte khempeuh kiman khin hi.
English: Thus the heavens and the earth were finished, and all the host of them.

**2:2**
Zolai: Ni sagih ma-in Pasian in a nasepte zo khinta a, ama hihsa nasep khempeuh panin ni sagih ni-in a tawlnga hi.
English: And on the seventh day God ended his work which he had made; and he rested on the seventh day from all his work which he had made.

**2:3**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in ni sagih ni thupha pia-in siangthosak hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh piansak nasepna ama nasep khempeuh panin tua ni-in Pasian a tawlnga hi.
English: And God blessed the seventh day, and sanctified it: because that in it he had rested from all his work which God created and made.

**2:4**
Zolai: Hihte pen, a kipiansak lai-a vantung le leitung tangthu ahi hi. Topa Pasian in leitung le vantungte a bawl hi.
English: These are the generations of the heavens and of the earth when they were created, in the day that the LORD God made the earth and the heavens,

**2:5**
Zolai: Topa Pasian in leitungah guah zusak nai lo a, leitang a kho ding mi om lo ahih manin gam sung kungnote lei sungah om nai lo a, lo sung ankungte pokhia lo hi.
English: and every plant of the field before it was in the earth, and every herb of the field before it grew: for the LORD God had not caused it to rain upon the earth, and there was not a man to till the ground.

**2:6**
Zolai: Tua ciangin leitung panin meiilum kaaito-in, lei maitang khempeuh a buah hunin
English: But there went up a mist from the earth, and watered the whole face of the ground.

**2:7**
Zolai: Topa Pasian in leilak pana leivui tawh mihing bawl a, a nak sungah nuntakna hu sang suk hi. Tua mi pen leitung nuntakna a nei mihing hong suak pah hi.
English: And the LORD God formed man of the dust of the ground, and breathed into his nostrils the breath of life; and man became a living soul.

**2:8**
Zolai: Topa Pasian in nisuahna lamah Eden huan khat bawl hi. Tua lai munah ama bawlsa mipa koih hi.
English: And the LORD God planted a garden eastward in Eden; and there he put the man whom he had formed.

**2:9**
Zolai: A deihhuai, nek dinga a hoih singkung nam khempeuh, huan laizangah nuntakna singkung, le a pha le a sia theihna singkung, lei sung panin Topa Pasian in posak hi.
English: And out of the ground made the LORD God to grow every tree that is pleasant to the sight, and good for food; the tree of life also in the midst of the garden, and the tree of knowledge of good and evil.

**2:10**
Zolai: Huan sung a kawtsak dingin Eden nawkin gun khat hong luang a, tua mun panin gun hong kikhenin li hong pha hi.
English: And a river went out of Eden to water the garden; and from thence it was parted, and became into four heads.

**2:11**
Zolai: A masa pen gun a min Pishon hi a, kham a omna, Havilah gambup kimkotah a luang pen ahi hi.
English: The name of the first is Pison: that is it which compasseth the whole land of Havilah, where there is gold;

**2:12**
Zolai: Tua gam a khamte hoih hi. Tua munah bedolak singnai le onik suang om hi.
English: and the gold of that land is good: there is bdellium and the onyx stone.

**2:13**
Zolai: A nihna gun min Gihon hi a, Kush gam kimkotah a luang pen ahi hi.
English: And the name of the second river is Gihon: the same is it that compasseth the whole land of Ethiopia.

**2:14**
Zolai: Assiria gam nisuahna lamah a luang a thumna gun min Hiddekel ahi hi. A lina gun pen Eufratis gun ahi hi.
English: And the name of the third river is Hiddekel: that is it which goeth toward the east of Assyria. And the fourth river is Euphrates.

**2:15**
Zolai: Topa Pasian in mipa la-in, Eden huan kho-in a kem dingin a koih hi.
English: And the LORD God took the man, and put him into the garden of Eden to dress it and to keep it.

**2:16**
Zolai: Topa Pasian in mipa thu pia a, “Na ut utin huan sung singkung gah khempeuh na ne thei ding hi.
English: And the LORD God commanded the man, saying, Of every tree of the garden thou mayest freely eat:

**2:17**
Zolai: Ahih hangin a pha le a sia theihna singkung gah pen na ne kei ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh tua na nek ni-in na si ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: but of the tree of the knowledge of good and evil, thou shalt not eat of it: for in the day that thou eatest thereof thou shalt surely die.

**2:18**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa Pasian in, “Mipa amah guak a om ding hoih lo hi. Ama a’ ding a kituak a huh ding ka bawlsak ding hi,” ci hi.
English: And the LORD God said, It is not good that the man should be alone; I will make him an help meet for him.

**2:19**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Topa Pasian in gam sung ganhing khempeuh le huih lak vasa khempeuh lei tawh bawl a, mipa in tuate bang a ci hiam ci-in a theihna dingin mipa kiangah tuate a paipih hi. Nuntakna a nei khempeuhte pen mipa’ cih bangbang a min hi pahpah hi.
English: And out of the ground the LORD God formed every beast of the field, and every fowl of the air; and brought them unto Adam to see what he would call them: and whatsoever Adam called every living creature, that was the name thereof.

**2:20**
Zolai: Mipa in ganhing namte khempeuh, huihlak vasate khempeuh le gam sung ganhing khempeuh min a vawh hi. Ahih hangin mipa a’ dinga a kilawm, amah a huh ding khat zong om lo hi.
English: And Adam gave names to all cattle, and to the fowl of the air, and to every beast of the field; but for Adam there was not found an help meet for him.

**2:21**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Topa Pasian in mipa ihmut suak mahmah sak a, ama ihmut kalin a nakguhte khat la-in tua mun pen satak tawh a dimsak hi.
English: And the LORD God caused a deep sleep to fall upon Adam, and he slept: and he took one of his ribs, and closed up the flesh instead thereof;

**2:22**
Zolai: Topa Pasian in mipa’ tung panin a lakkhiat nakguh pen numei khatin bawl a, mipa kiangah tua nu a paipih hi.
English: and the rib, which the LORD God had taken from man, made he a woman, and brought her unto the man.

**2:23**
Zolai: Tua ciangin mipa in, “Tu petpetin hih pen keima guhte le keima sate ahi hi. Amah pen mipa sung panin a kilakhia ahih manin ‘Numei’ kici ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Adam said, This is now bone of my bones, and flesh of my flesh: she shall be called Woman, because she was taken out of Man.

**2:24**
Zolai: Tua thu hangin pasal in a nu le a pa nusia-in a zi tawh kigawm a, amau tegel pum khat a bang uh hi.
English: Therefore shall a man leave his father and his mother, and shall cleave unto his wife: and they shall be one flesh.

**2:25**
Zolai: Mipa le a zi a guaktangin om uh a, maizum lo uh hi.
English: And they were both naked, the man and his wife, and were not ashamed.

## Chapter 3

**3:1**
Zolai: Tu-in gulpi pen, Topa Pasian’ bawlsa gamlak ganhing dangte khempeuh sangin ngiansiam zaw hi. Amah in numei kiangah, “Pasian in, ‘Huan sung singgah khat peuhpeuh ne lo ding,’ hong ci ahi hiam?” ci hi.
English: Now the serpent was more subtil than any beast of the field which the LORD God had made. And he said unto the woman, Yea, hath God said, Ye shall not eat of every tree of the garden?

**3:2**
Zolai: Numei in gulpi kiangah, “Huan sung singgahte ka ne thei ding uh hi.
English: And the woman said unto the serpent, We may eat of the fruit of the trees of the garden:

**3:3**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Pasian in, ‘Huan laizang a om singgah na ne kei ding uh hi, zong na lawng kei ding uh hi. Tua bang hih le-uhcin na si ding uh hi,’ hong ci hi,” a ci hi.
English: but of the fruit of the tree which is in the midst of the garden, God hath said, Ye shall not eat of it, neither shall ye touch it, lest ye die.

**3:4**
Zolai: Ahih hangin gulpi in numei kiangah, “Na si kei ding uh hi.
English: And the serpent said unto the woman, Ye shall not surely die:

**3:5**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh tua singgah na nek ciangun na mitte uh hong vak ding a, a pha le a sia thei-in, Pasian tawh na kibat ding lamtak uh Pasian in thei hi,” a ci hi.
English: for God doth know that in the day ye eat thereof, then your eyes shall be opened, and ye shall be as gods, knowing good and evil.

**3:6**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin singkung a hoihna, mi a pilsak dingin tua a gah a deihhuaina a muh ciangin, a singgah loin a ne hi. Amah in singgah kimkhat a pasal pia a, a pasal in zong a ne hi.
English: And when the woman saw that the tree was good for food, and that it was pleasant to the eyes, and a tree to be desired to make one wise, she took of the fruit thereof, and did eat, and gave also unto her husband with her; and he did eat.

**3:7**
Zolai: A nek khit phetun amau tegel in khua phawk uh a, a guaktangin a omlam uh kithei uh hi. Amaute in theitehte khui tuahin puansilh dingin a bawl uh hi.
English: And the eyes of them both were opened, and they knew that they were naked; and they sewed fig leaves together, and made themselves aprons.

**3:8**
Zolai: A nitak ciangin huan sungah Topa Pasian a hong paina ging amaute in za uh a, Topa Pasian’ muh loh dingin mipa le a zi, huan sung singte lakah a bu uh hi.
English: And they heard the voice of the LORD God walking in the garden in the cool of the day: and Adam and his wife hid themselves from the presence of the LORD God amongst the trees of the garden.

**3:9**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa Pasian in mipa samin ama kiangah, “Koi lai-ah om na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And the LORD God called unto Adam, and said unto him, Where art thou?

**3:10**
Zolai: Amah in, “Nangma gin na huan sungah ka za a, ka lau hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh ka guaktangin om ka hih manin ka bucip hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, I heard thy voice in the garden, and I was afraid, because I was naked; and I hid myself.

**3:11**
Zolai: Amah in, “Na guaktanga na omna kua in hong gen ahi hiam? Na nek loh dinga kong thupiak singgah ne kha na hi hiam?” ci hi.
English: And he said, Who told thee that thou wast naked? Hast thou eaten of the tree, whereof I commanded thee that thou shouldest not eat?

**3:12**
Zolai: Mipa in, “Kei tawh a om dinga nong piak numei in singgah hong pia a, ke’n ka ne hi,” ci hi.
English: And the man said, The woman whom thou gavest to be with me, she gave me of the tree, and I did eat.

**3:13**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa Pasian in numei kiangah, “Bangci a hici gamtat na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Numei in, “Gulpi in kei hong khem a, ka ne hi,” ci hi.
English: And the LORD God said unto the woman, What is this that thou hast done? And the woman said, The serpent beguiled me, and I did eat.

**3:14**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa Pasian in gulpi kiangah, “Nang, hih bangin gamta khin na hih manin, ganhing khempeuhte le gamlak ganhing khempeuhte sangin samsiatna na ngahzaw hi. Na gilpi-in lam na pai ding a, na nuntak sung tawntungin leivui na ne ding hi.
English: And the LORD God said unto the serpent, Because thou hast done this, thou art cursed above all cattle, and above every beast of the field; upon thy belly shalt thou go, and dust shalt thou eat all the days of thy life:

**3:15**
Zolai: Nang le numei kikal na suanlekhakte le ama suanlekhakte kikalah kilangneihna ka omsak ding hi. Amah in na lutang hong sunim ding a, nang in ama khetul na sunim ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: and I will put enmity between thee and the woman, and between thy seed and her seed; it shall bruise thy head, and thou shalt bruise his heel.

**3:16**
Zolai: Tua ciangin numei kiangah, “Naupaiina-ah na gimna nakpitakin ka khangsak ding a, na a sapipi-in nau na nei ding hi. Ahi zongin na pasal mah na deih ding a, amah in nang tungah hong uk ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: Unto the woman he said, I will greatly multiply thy sorrow and thy conception; in sorrow thou shalt bring forth children; and thy desire shall be to thy husband, and he shall rule over thee.

**3:17**
Zolai: Tua ciangin mipa kiangah, “Nang in na zi’ thu mangin, ‘Nang in na ne kei ding hi,’ ci-in nang kong thupiak singgah ne na hih ciangin, nangma hangin leitang in samsiatna ngah hi. Na nuntak tawntung gimpi-in na semin na annek ding na zong ding hi.
English: And unto Adam he said, Because thou hast hearkened unto the voice of thy wife, and hast eaten of the tree, of which I commanded thee, saying, Thou shalt not eat of it: cursed is the ground for thy sake; in sorrow shalt thou eat of it all the days of thy life;

**3:18**
Zolai: Ling le kiakte, nang a dingin hong pokhiasak ding a, nang in gamlak kungte na ne ding hi.
English: thorns also and thistles shall it bring forth to thee; and thou shalt eat the herb of the field;

**3:19**
Zolai: Lei-ah na ciahkik matengin khua-ul kai-in na na sep ciang bekin an na ne ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh lei sung panin nang hong kipiangsak a, nang, leivui na hih manin, leivui mah na suakkik ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: in the sweat of thy face shalt thou eat bread, till thou return unto the ground; for out of it wast thou taken: for dust thou art , and unto dust shalt thou return.

**3:20**
Zolai: Mipa in a zi’ min pen Eve, ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah pen mihing khempeuh’ nu ahi hi.
English: And Adam called his wife's name Eve; because she was the mother of all living.

**3:21**
Zolai: Topa Pasian in mipa le a zi a dingin savun puan bawl a, amaute silhsak hi.
English: Unto Adam also and to his wife did the LORD God make coats of skins, and clothed them.

**3:22**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa Pasian in, “En un, mipa pen eite khat tawh kibang a, a pha le a sia thei hi. Amah in nuntakna singgah ne-in a hin tawntung khak loh nadingin i vaihawm ding hi,” ci hi.
English: And the LORD God said, Behold, the man is become as one of us, to know good and evil: and now, lest he put forth his hand, and take also of the tree of life, and eat, and live for ever:

**3:23**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Topa Pasian in, amah a kipiansakna leitang a kho dingin Eden Huan panin mipa a sawlkhia hi.
English: therefore the LORD God sent him forth from the garden of Eden, to till the ground from whence he was taken.

**3:24**
Zolai: Amah in mipa hawlkhia hi. Kherub-te le mun khempeuh a nga thei meikuang namsau pen nuntakna singkung lampi a cing dingin Eden Huan nisuahna lamah a koih hi.
English: So he drove out the man; and he placed at the east of the garden of Eden Cherubims, and a flaming sword which turned every way, to keep the way of the tree of life.

## Chapter 4

**4:1**
Zolai: Tu-in mipa in ama zi Eve luppih a, amah gai-in Kain nei a, “ Topa’ huhna tawh mi khat ka ngah khin hi,” ci hi.
English: And Adam knew Eve his wife; and she conceived, and bare Cain, and said, I have gotten a man from the LORD .

**4:2**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a sanggampa Abel nei leuleu hi. Tu-in Abel, tuu kem pa hi a, Kain, lo khopa ahi hi.
English: And she again bare his brother Abel. And Abel was a keeper of sheep, but Cain was a tiller of the ground.

**4:3**
Zolai: Tua hun sungin Kain in lei pana piang gah piakna Topa’ tungah paipih a,
English: And in process of time it came to pass, that Cain brought of the fruit of the ground an offering unto the LORD .

**4:4**
Zolai: Abel in a tuuhon tacilte le a sa limcite paipih hi. Topa in Abel le ama piakna thusim a,
English: And Abel, he also brought of the firstlings of his flock and of the fat thereof. And the LORD had respect unto Abel and to his offering:

**4:5**
Zolai: ahih hangin Kain le ama piakna thusim lo hi. Tua ahih ciangin Kain heh mahmah a, a mai sia hi.
English: but unto Cain and to his offering he had not respect. And Cain was very wroth, and his countenance fell.

**4:6**
Zolai: Topa in Kain tungah, “Bang hangin nang heh a, bang hangin na mai sia ahi hiam?
English: And the LORD said unto Cain, Why art thou wroth? and why is thy countenance fallen?

**4:7**
Zolai: Limtakin hih lecin, nang hong kisang lo ding ahi hiam? Limtakin na hih kei le nang hong hih nuamin mawhna in hong buk a, nang hong uk nuam hi. Ahih hangin nang in tua mawhna na zawh ding ahi hi,” a ci hi.
English: If thou doest well, shalt thou not be accepted? and if thou doest not well, sin lieth at the door. And unto thee shall be his desire, and thou shalt rule over him.

**4:8**
Zolai: Kain in a sanggampa Abel kiangah, “Gamlakah vak ni,” ci hi. Amaute gamlakah a om ciangin Kain in a sanggampa Abel a that hi.
English: And Cain talked with Abel his brother: and it came to pass, when they were in the field, that Cain rose up against Abel his brother, and slew him.

**4:9**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa in Kain tungah, “Na sanggampa Abel koi-ah om ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah in, “Ka thei kei hi. Kei, ka sanggam a kem pa ka hi hiam?” ci hi.
English: And the LORD said unto Cain, Where is Abel thy brother? And he said, I know not: Am I my brother's keeper?

**4:10**
Zolai: Topa in, “Bang hangin hici gamtat na hi hiam? Na sanggampa’ sisan, leilak panin kei tungah hong kiko hi.
English: And he said, What hast thou done? the voice of thy brother's blood crieth unto me from the ground.

**4:11**
Zolai: Na sanggampa’ sisan a hup dingin a kam a ka leitang tungah tu-in nang hong kisamsiat hi.
English: And now art thou cursed from the earth, which hath opened her mouth to receive thy brother's blood from thy hand;

**4:12**
Zolai: Lo na khawh ciangin nang a dingin an hong piangsak nawn lo ding hi. Nang pen a galtai, leitung a a vakvai na hi ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: when thou tillest the ground, it shall not henceforth yield unto thee her strength; a fugitive and a vagabond shalt thou be in the earth.

**4:13**
Zolai: Kain in Topa’ tungah, “Keimah gim hong kipiakna, ka thuak zawh ding hi lo hi.
English: And Cain said unto the LORD , My punishment is greater than I can bear.

**4:14**
Zolai: En in, tuni-in nangmah in leitung panin kei nong hawlkhia a, nang kiang panin kei nong notkhia hi. Kei pen a galtai, leitungah a vakvai ka hi ding a, kei hong mu peuhmah in hong that ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: Behold, thou hast driven me out this day from the face of the earth; and from thy face shall I be hid; and I shall be a fugitive and a vagabond in the earth; and it shall come to pass, that every one that findeth me shall slay me.

**4:15**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa in ama kiangah, “Tua bang hi lo ding hi. Khatpeuh in Kain a thah le tua pa tungah a zah sagihin kithuk ding hi,” a ci hi. Amah a tuakpeuh in a thahkhak loh nadingin Topa in Kain’ tungah ciaptehna khat a koih hi.
English: And the LORD said unto him, Therefore whosoever slayeth Cain, vengeance shall be taken on him sevenfold. And the LORD set a mark upon Cain, lest any finding him should kill him.

**4:16**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa’ omna panin Kain paikhia-in Eden nisuahna lam Nod gam sungah a teng hi.
English: And Cain went out from the presence of the LORD , and dwelt in the land of Nod, on the east of Eden.

**4:17**
Zolai: Kain in a zi luppih a, amah gai-in Enok a nei hi. Kain in khuapi khat sat a, tua khuapi min dingin ama tapa’ min tamin Enok a phuak hi.
English: And Cain knew his wife; and she conceived, and bare Enoch: and he builded a city, and called the name of the city, after the name of his son, Enoch.

**4:18**
Zolai: Enok sung panin Irad suak a, Irad pen Mehujael’ pa ahi hi. Mehujael pen Methushael’ pa hi a, Methushael pen Lamek’ pa ahi hi.
English: And unto Enoch was born Irad: and Irad begat Mehujael: and Mehujael begat Methusael: and Methusael begat Lamech.

**4:19**
Zolai: Lamek in zi nih nei hi. A khat’ min Adah hi a, adang khat’ min Zillah ahi hi.
English: And Lamech took unto him two wives: the name of the one was Adah, and the name of the other Zillah.

**4:20**
Zolai: Adah in tapa Jabal nei hi. Amah pen puanbukte sungah tengin ganhing a neite’ pianna pupi ahi hi.
English: And Adah bare Jabal: he was the father of such as dwell in tents, and of such as have cattle.

**4:21**
Zolai: A sanggampa’ min Jubal hi a, laiza lasakna le tamngai tumte khempeuh’ pianna pupi ahi hi.
English: And his brother's name was Jubal: he was the father of all such as handle the harp and organ.

**4:22**
Zolai: Zillah in Tubalkain nei a, sumngo le sik nazat khempeuh a bawlte’ pianna pupi ahi hi. Tubalkain’ sanggamnu pen Naamah ahi hi.
English: And Zillah, she also bare Tubal-cain, an instructer of every artificer in brass and iron: and the sister of Tubal-cain was Naamah.

**4:23**
Zolai: Lamek in a zite kiangah, “Adah le Zillah aw, ka aw ngai un. Lamek’ zite aw, ka thugen ngai un. Kei hong liamsak manin mi khat, kei hong sat manin khanglai mi khat ka that khin hi.
English: And Lamech said unto his wives, Adah and Zillah, Hear my voice; Ye wives of Lamech, hearken unto my speech: For I have slain a man to my wounding, And a young man to my hurt.

**4:24**
Zolai: Kain a kithah manin a zah sagihin kithukkik ahihleh, Lamek a kithah manin a zah sawmsagihin kithukkik taktak ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: If Cain shall be avenged sevenfold, Truly Lamech seventy and sevenfold.

**4:25**
Zolai: Adam in a zi luppih leuleu hi. Amah in tapa khat nei a, a min Seth ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh, “Kain in Abel that ahih manin Abel’ tangin Pasian in kei a dingin naupang khat hong sehsak hi,” amah in ci hi.
English: And Adam knew his wife again; and she bare a son, and called his name Seth: For God, said she , hath appointed me another seed instead of Abel, whom Cain slew.

**4:26**
Zolai: Seth in zong tapa khat nei a, ama min Enosh ci hi. Tua hun a kipanin mite in Topa bia-in a min lawh ding kipan ta uh hi.
English: And to Seth, to him also there was born a son; and he called his name Enos: then began men to call upon the name of the LORD .

## Chapter 5

**5:1**
Zolai: Hih pen Adam’ suanlekhakte’ laibu ahi hi. Pasian in mi a piansakin, amah in Pasian tawh a kisunin a bawl hi.
English: This is the book of the generations of Adam. In the day that God created man, in the likeness of God made he him;

**5:2**
Zolai: Amah in numei le pasal a piangsak hi. Amaute a kipiansakin amah in amaute, “Mi,” ci a, amaute thupha a pia hi.
English: male and female created he them; and blessed them, and called their name Adam, in the day when they were created.

**5:3**
Zolai: Adam kum za le kum sawmthum a phak khit ciangin, amah a sun tapa khat nei a, Seth ci-in a min a phuak hi.
English: And Adam lived an hundred and thirty years, and begat a son in his own likeness, after his image; and called his name Seth:

**5:4**
Zolai: Seth a suah khit ciangin Adam kum zagiat sung nungta lai hi. Amah in tanu le tapa dang zong a nei hi.
English: and the days of Adam after he had begotten Seth were eight hundred years: and he begat sons and daughters:

**5:5**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Adam’ nuntak hun sungteng pen kum zakua le kum sawmthum hi a, tua ciangin amah si hi.
English: and all the days that Adam lived were nine hundred and thirty years: and he died.

**5:6**
Zolai: Seth kum za le kum nga a phak ciangin Enosh kici tapa khat a nei hi.
English: And Seth lived an hundred and five years, and begat Enos:

**5:7**
Zolai: Enosh a suah khit ciangin Seth kum zagiat le kum sawmthum nungta a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Seth lived after he begat Enos eight hundred and seven years, and begat sons and daughters:

**5:8**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Seth’ khan sungteng pen kum zakua le kum sawm le nih hi a, tua ciangin amah si hi.
English: and all the days of Seth were nine hundred and twelve years: and he died.

**5:9**
Zolai: Enosh kum sawmkua a phak ciangin, amah in Kenan kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Enos lived ninety years, and begat Cainan:

**5:10**
Zolai: Kenan a suah khit ciangin Enosh kum zagiat le kum sawm le nga nungta a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Enos lived after he begat Cainan eight hundred and fifteen years, and begat sons and daughters:

**5:11**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Enosh’ khan sungteng pen kum zakua le kum nga hi a, tua ciangin amah si hi.
English: and all the days of Enos were nine hundred and five years: and he died.

**5:12**
Zolai: Kenan kum sawmsagih a phak ciangin, Mahalalel kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Cainan lived seventy years, and begat Mahalaleel:

**5:13**
Zolai: Mahalalel’ suah khit ciangin Kenan kum zagiat le kum sawmli nungta a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Cainan lived after he begat Mahalaleel eight hundred and forty years, and begat sons and daughters:

**5:14**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Kenan’ khan sungteng pen kum zakua le kum sawm hi a, tua ciangin amah si hi.
English: and all the days of Cainan were nine hundred and ten years: and he died.

**5:15**
Zolai: Mahalalel kum sawmguk le kum nga a phak ciangin Jared kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Mahalaleel lived sixty and five years, and begat Jared:

**5:16**
Zolai: Jared’ suah khit ciangin Mahalalel kum zagiat le kum sawmthum nungta a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Mahalaleel lived after he begat Jared eight hundred and thirty years, and begat sons and daughters:

**5:17**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Mahalalel’ khan sungteng pen kum zagiat le kum sawmkua le nga hi a, tua ciangin amah si hi.
English: and all the days of Mahalaleel were eight hundred ninety and five years: and he died.

**5:18**
Zolai: Jared kum za le kum sawmguk le nih a phak ciangin Enok kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Jared lived an hundred sixty and two years, and he begat Enoch:

**5:19**
Zolai: Enok’ suah khit ciangin Jared kum zagiat nungta a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Jared lived after he begat Enoch eight hundred years, and begat sons and daughters:

**5:20**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Jared’ khan sungteng pen kum zakua le kum sawmguk le nih hi a, tua ciangin amah si hi.
English: and all the days of Jared were nine hundred sixty and two years: and he died.

**5:21**
Zolai: Enok kum sawmguk le kum nga a phak ciangin, Methuselah kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Enoch lived sixty and five years, and begat Methuselah:

**5:22**
Zolai: Methuselah’ suah khit ciangin kum zathum sung Enok le Pasian kikhawl a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Enoch walked with God after he begat Methuselah three hundred years, and begat sons and daughters:

**5:23**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Enok’ khan sungteng pen kum zathum le kum sawmguk le kum nga ahi hi.
English: and all the days of Enoch were three hundred sixty and five years:

**5:24**
Zolai: Enok pen Pasian tawh kikhawl hi. Enok kimu nawn lo hi; bang hang hiam cih leh Pasian in amah la hi.
English: and Enoch walked with God: and he was not; for God took him.

**5:25**
Zolai: Methuselah kum za le kum sawmgiat le kum sagih a phak ciangin Lamek kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Methuselah lived an hundred eighty and seven years, and begat Lamech:

**5:26**
Zolai: Lamek’ suah khit ciangin Methuselah kum zasagih le kum sawmgiat le nih nungta a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Methuselah lived after he begat Lamech seven hundred eighty and two years, and begat sons and daughters:

**5:27**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Methuselah’ khan sungteng pen kum zakua le kum sawmguk le kua hi a, tua ciangin amah si hi.
English: and all the days of Methuselah were nine hundred sixty and nine years: and he died.

**5:28**
Zolai: Lamek kum za le kum sawmgiat le nih a phak ciangin tapa khat nei a,
English: And Lamech lived an hundred eighty and two years, and begat a son:

**5:29**
Zolai: ama min Noah phuakin, “ Topa in a samsiatsa leitang panin hih pa in i nasepna le i gimnate-ah eite hong khahkhia ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: and he called his name Noah, saying, This same shall comfort us concerning our work and toil of our hands, because of the ground which the LORD hath cursed.

**5:30**
Zolai: Noah’ suah khit ciangin Lamek kum zanga le kum sawmkua le nga nungta a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: And Lamech lived after he begat Noah five hundred ninety and five years, and begat sons and daughters:

**5:31**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Lamek’ khan sungteng pen kum zasagih le kum sawmsagih le sagih hi a, tua ciangin amah si hi.
English: and all the days of Lamech were seven hundred seventy and seven years: and he died.

**5:32**
Zolai: Noah kum zanga a phak khit ciangin Shem, Ham, le Jafeth, tapa thum a nei hi.
English: And Noah was five hundred years old: and Noah begat Shem, Ham, and Japheth.

## Chapter 6

**6:1**
Zolai: Leitungah mite tam dingin hong kipanin, amau’ sung panin tanute hong suah ciangin,
English: And it came to pass, when men began to multiply on the face of the earth, and daughters were born unto them,

**6:2**
Zolai: vana om mite in leitung mite’ tanute hoihsa uh ahih manin a deih bangun amaute zi-in a la uh hi.
English: that the sons of God saw the daughters of men that they were fair; and they took them wives of all which they chose.

**6:3**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa in, “Mihingte sungah ka Kha om paisuak nawn lo ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh mihingte a mawh hi khinta a, kum za le kum sawmnih sung kisik nading hun kipia lai bek ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And the LORD said, My spirit shall not always strive with man, for that he also is flesh: yet his days shall be an hundred and twenty years.

**6:4**
Zolai: Vana om mite in leitung mihing tanute luppihin, amaute in ta a neih hun laitak hitaleh tua khit hitaleh, amau’ suanlekhak Nefilim a kici mite leitungah om hi. Hih mite pen tang lai-a mi thahat, mi minthangte ahi uh hi.
English: There were giants in the earth in those days; and also after that, when the sons of God came in unto the daughters of men, and they bare children to them, the same became mighty men which were of old, men of renown.

**6:5**
Zolai: Leitungah mihing a gitlohna a liatna le mihing lungsim ngaihsutna peuhmah a sia ahih ngitngetna thu Topa in mu hi.
English: And GOD saw that the wickedness of man was great in the earth, and that every imagination of the thoughts of his heart was only evil continually.

**6:6**
Zolai: Leitungah mihing a bawl pen Topa khial kisa a, tua thu in ama lungsim dahsak hi.
English: And it repented the LORD that he had made man on the earth, and it grieved him at his heart.

**6:7**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Topa in, “Ka piansaksa mihing, ganhing, a bokvak ganhingte le huih lak vasate, leitung panin ka phiatkhia ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih le amaute ka bawl ka khial hi,” a ci hi.
English: And the LORD said, I will destroy man whom I have created from the face of the earth; both man, and beast, and the creeping thing, and the fowls of the air; for it repenteth me that I have made them.

**6:8**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Noah in Topa’ maipha mu hi.
English: But Noah found grace in the eyes of the LORD .

**6:9**
Zolai: Noah’ tangthu hih bang ahi hi. Noah a thuman mi khat hi a, ama khangah paubaang lo hi. Noah pen Pasian tawh kikhawl hi.
English: These are the generations of Noah: Noah was a just man and perfect in his generations, and Noah walked with God.

**6:10**
Zolai: Noah in tapa thum, Shem, Ham, le Jafeth a nei hi.
English: And Noah begat three sons, Shem, Ham, and Japheth.

**6:11**
Zolai: Tu-in Pasian’ muhna-ah leitung sia a, leitungah ngongtatna kidim hi.
English: The earth also was corrupt before God, and the earth was filled with violence.

**6:12**
Zolai: Pasian in leitung en a, a kisiagawp mu hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh leitungah mi khempeuh a sia-in a gamta lo kuamah om lo hi.
English: And God looked upon the earth, and, behold, it was corrupt; for all flesh had corrupted his way upon the earth.

**6:13**
Zolai: Pasian in Noah’ kiangah, “Mi khempeuh beisak ding ka khentat zo hi; bang hang hiam cih leh amau’ hangin leitungah ngongtatna kidim hi. En in, leitung tawh amaute ka susia khawm ding hi.
English: And God said unto Noah, The end of all flesh is come before me; for the earth is filled with violence through them; and, behold, I will destroy them with the earth.

**6:14**
Zolai: Nang a dingin noah-taak sing tawh teembaw khat bawl in. Teembaw sungah a deite bawl inla, a sung le a pua kultal tui tawh zut in.
English: Make thee an ark of gopher wood; rooms shalt thou make in the ark, and shalt pitch it within and without with pitch.

**6:15**
Zolai: Na bawl nading dan hih bang ahi hi: Teembaw a sauna pi zali sawmnga, a zaina pi sawmsagih le nga, a sanna pi sawmli le nga hi ding hi.
English: And this is the fashion which thou shalt make it of: The length of the ark shall be three hundred cubits, the breadth of it fifty cubits, and the height of it thirty cubits.

**6:16**
Zolai: Teembaw a dingin kongkhak khat bawl inla, tua tung pi khat le alang ciangah zawh bawl in. A pangah teembaw kongkhak bulh in. A dawl nuainung, a dawl nihna le a dawl thumnate bawl in.
English: A window shalt thou make to the ark, and in a cubit shalt thou finish it above; and the door of the ark shalt thou set in the side thereof; with lower, second, and third stories shalt thou make it.

**6:17**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh, en in, leitungah a om nuntak husanna a nei khempeuh a susia dingin leitungah tuiciin ka tungsak ding hi. Leitung a om khempeuh si ding hi.
English: And, behold, I, even I, do bring a flood of waters upon the earth, to destroy all flesh, wherein is the breath of life, from under heaven; and every thing that is in the earth shall die.

**6:18**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nang tawh ka thuciamna ka kipsak ding hi. Teembaw sungah nang na hong pai ding hi. Nang, na tapate, na zi le na tapate’ zite tawh na paikhawm ding uh hi.
English: But with thee will I establish my covenant; and thou shalt come into the ark, thou, and thy sons, and thy wife, and thy sons' wives with thee.

**6:19**
Zolai: Nuntakna a nei khempeuh nang tawh a nungta dingin nam khatah nih ciat teembaw sungah na paipih ding hi. Tuate pen a nu le a pa hi ding hi.
English: And of every living thing of all flesh, two of every sort shalt thou bring into the ark, to keep them alive with thee; they shall be male and female.

**6:20**
Zolai: Vasate amau’ nam ciatin, ganhingte amau’ nam ciatin, leilakah a bokvak ganhingte peuhmah amau’ nam ciatin, a suakta dingin nam khatah nih ciat nang kiangah hong pai ding uh hi.
English: Of fowls after their kind, and of cattle after their kind, of every creeping thing of the earth after his kind, two of every sort shall come unto thee, to keep them alive.

**6:21**
Zolai: A kine an nam khempeuh zong la inla khol in. Tuate pen nang le amaute a dingin an ding ahi hi,” a ci hi.
English: And take thou unto thee of all food that is eaten, and thou shalt gather it to thee; and it shall be for food for thee, and for them.

**6:22**
Zolai: Noah zong tua bangmahin gamta a, Pasian’ thupiak khempeuh a hih hi.
English: Thus did Noah; according to all that God commanded him, so did he.

## Chapter 7

**7:1**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa in Noah kiangah, “Nang le na innkuanpih mi khempeuh teembaw sungah pai un. Bang hang hiam cih leh hih khang mite sung panin nang bek a thuman na hihna ka hong thei hi.
English: And the LORD said unto Noah, Come thou and all thy house into the ark; for thee have I seen righteous before me in this generation.

**7:2**
Zolai: Ganhing siangtho nupa kop sagih, ganhing a siang lo nupa kop khat,
English: Of every clean beast thou shalt take to thee by sevens, the male and his female: and of beasts that are not clean by two, the male and his female.

**7:3**
Zolai: huih lak vasate zong nupa kop sagih, leitungah amau’ nam a manthan loh nadingin la in.
English: Of fowls also of the air by sevens, the male and the female; to keep seed alive upon the face of all the earth.

**7:4**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ni sagih sungin sun sawmli le zan sawmli sung leitungah guah ka zusak ding hi. Ka bawlsa nuntakna a nei peuhmah leitung panin ka phiatkhia ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: For yet seven days, and I will cause it to rain upon the earth forty days and forty nights; and every living substance that I have made will I destroy from off the face of the earth.

**7:5**
Zolai: Noah in zong Topa’ thupiak khempeuh a hih hi.
English: And Noah did according unto all that the LORD commanded him.

**7:6**
Zolai: Leitungah tuiciin a tun lai-in Noah kum zaguk pha hi.
English: And Noah was six hundred years old when the flood of waters was upon the earth.

**7:7**
Zolai: Tuiciin a pelh dingin Noah, a tapate, a zi le a tapate’ zite teembaw sungah pai uh hi.
English: And Noah went in, and his sons, and his wife, and his sons' wives with him, into the ark, because of the waters of the flood.

**7:8**
Zolai: Ganhing siangthote, a siang lo ganhingte, vasate, leitung a a bokvak peuhmah,
English: Of clean beasts, and of beasts that are not clean, and of fowls, and of every thing that creepeth upon the earth,

**7:9**
Zolai: a nupa kopin Pasian in Noah a thupiaksa bangin teembaw sungah Noah tawh pai uh hi.
English: there went in two and two unto Noah into the ark, the male and the female, as God had commanded Noah.

**7:10**
Zolai: A ni sagih ni-in leitungah tuiciin tung hi.
English: And it came to pass after seven days, that the waters of the flood were upon the earth.

**7:11**
Zolai: Noah’ nuntak kum zaguk kum, a kha nihna, tua kha ni sawm le sagih ni-in vana om a thuk mahmah tuikhukte puakkhamin, vantung tawlette kihong hi.
English: In the six hundredth year of Noah's life, in the second month, the seventeenth day of the month, the same day were all the fountains of the great deep broken up, and the windows of heaven were opened.

**7:12**
Zolai: Sun sawmli le zan sawmli sung leitungah guah zu hi.
English: And the rain was upon the earth forty days and forty nights.

**7:13**
Zolai: Tua ni teekteekin Noah le a tapate Shem, Ham, Jafeth, le Noah’ zi le a tapate’ zi thumte, amau tawh teembaw sungah a tum uh hi.
English: In the selfsame day entered Noah, and Shem, and Ham, and Japheth, the sons of Noah, and Noah's wife, and the three wives of his sons with them, into the ark;

**7:14**
Zolai: Amaute le gamsa peuhmah amau’ nam ciat, innsa khempeuh amau’ nam ciat, leitungah a bokvak peuhmah amau’ nam ciat, le vasa peuhmah amau’ nam ciat, vasa namkim amau’ nam ciatin a tum uh hi.
English: they, and every beast after his kind, and all the cattle after their kind, and every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth after his kind, and every fowl after his kind, every bird of every sort.

**7:15**
Zolai: Nuntak husanna a nei khempeuh a nupa kop ciatin Noah tawh teembaw sungah a pai uh hi.
English: And they went in unto Noah into the ark, two and two of all flesh, wherein is the breath of life.

**7:16**
Zolai: Pasian in Noah tungah a thupiakna bangin nuntakna a nei khempeuh teembaw sungah a lut khit ciangin Topa in Noah kong a khaknelh hi.
English: And they that went in, went in male and female of all flesh, as God had commanded him: and the LORD shut him in.

**7:17**
Zolai: Leitungah tuiciin ni sawmli sung omden hi. Tui tam semsem a, teembaw laamto-in, leitung’ tungah khangin sangto lai hi.
English: And the flood was forty days upon the earth; and the waters increased, and bare up the ark, and it was lift up above the earth.

**7:18**
Zolai: Tui khangto-in leitungah tam mahmah hi. Tui tungah teembaw laam hi.
English: And the waters prevailed, and were increased greatly upon the earth; and the ark went upon the face of the waters.

**7:19**
Zolai: Leitungah tui khangkhang ahih manin mual lian a sangte khempeuh tuumcip hi.
English: And the waters prevailed exceedingly upon the earth; and all the high hills, that were under the whole heaven, were covered.

**7:20**
Zolai: Mual liante tungah tui omto lai a, tuate tungah pi sawmnih le nih thuk-in tuumcip hi.
English: Fifteen cubits upward did the waters prevail; and the mountains were covered.

**7:21**
Zolai: Leitungah a nungta khempeuh, vasate, innsate, gamsate, a hon honin leitungah a hon om ganhingte khempeuh le mi khempeuh a si uh hi.
English: And all flesh died that moved upon the earth, both of fowl, and of cattle, and of beast, and of every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth, and every man:

**7:22**
Zolai: Leitungah a om, nuntakna hu a nei peuhmah a si uh hi.
English: all in whose nostrils was the breath of life, of all that was in the dry land , died.

**7:23**
Zolai: Mihing, ganhing, a bokvakte le huih lak vasate, leitung a om nuntakna a nei peuhmah amah in phiatkhia hi. Leitung panin amaute kiphiatkhia hi. Noah le amah tawh teembaw sunga a omteng bek a suakta uh hi.
English: And every living substance was destroyed which was upon the face of the ground, both man, and cattle, and the creeping things, and the fowl of the heaven; and they were destroyed from the earth: and Noah only remained alive , and they that were with him in the ark.

**7:24**
Zolai: Ni za le ni sawmnga sung leitungah tui om hi.
English: And the waters prevailed upon the earth an hundred and fifty days.

## Chapter 8

**8:1**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Pasian in Noah le amah tawh teembaw sungah a om gamsate le innsate khempeuh a phawk hi. Pasian in leitungah huih nungsak a, tui a kiam hi.
English: And God remembered Noah, and every living thing, and all the cattle that was with him in the ark: and God made a wind to pass over the earth, and the waters asswaged;

**8:2**
Zolai: Tui thukte le vantung tawlette kikhak a, vantung pana guahte kikhawlsak hi.
English: the fountains also of the deep and the windows of heaven were stopped, and the rain from heaven was restrained;

**8:3**
Zolai: Leitung panin tuite kiamkiam hi. Ni za le ni sawmnga a phak ciangin tuite kiam khinta hi.
English: and the waters returned from off the earth continually: and after the end of the hundred and fifty days the waters were abated.

**8:4**
Zolai: Kha sagihna, tua kha ni sawm le sagih ni-in Ararat mualtungah teembaw kinga hi.
English: And the ark rested in the seventh month, on the seventeenth day of the month, upon the mountains of Ararat.

**8:5**
Zolai: A kha sawmna ciang dong tuite kiamkiam lai hi. Kha sawmna, tua kha ni khat ni-in mual dawnte kidawk hi.
English: And the waters decreased continually until the tenth month: in the tenth month , on the first day of the month, were the tops of the mountains seen.

**8:6**
Zolai: Ni sawmli a cin ni ciangin Noah in ama bawlsa teembaw tawlet hong a,
English: And it came to pass at the end of forty days, that Noah opened the window of the ark which he had made:

**8:7**
Zolai: va-ak khat khah hi. Leitung panin tuite a keu mateng leeng kawikawi hi.
English: and he sent forth a raven, which went forth to and fro, until the waters were dried up from off the earth.

**8:8**
Zolai: Tua ciangin, leitungah tuite a kiam khin nai hiam cih a theihna dingin amah in vakhu khat khah hi.
English: Also he sent forth a dove from him, to see if the waters were abated from off the face of the ground;

**8:9**
Zolai: Ahih hangin, leitung khempeuhah tuite omlai-in, a khawl nading mu lo ahih manin teembaw-ah hong ciahkik hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in a khut zanin a vakhu man a, teembaw sungah paipih hi.
English: but the dove found no rest for the sole of her foot, and she returned unto him into the ark, for the waters were on the face of the whole earth: then he put forth his hand, and took her, and pulled her in unto him into the ark.

**8:10**
Zolai: Amah in ni sagih sung ngakin, teembaw panin a vakhu khah leuleu hi.
English: And he stayed yet other seven days; and again he sent forth the dove out of the ark;

**8:11**
Zolai: Nitak ciangin ama kiangah a vakhu hong ciahkik a, oliv teh a tukkhiat thak khat a mukah petin hong tunpih hi. Tua ahih ciangin leitung panin tuite kiam khinta hi, ci-in Noah in a thei hi.
English: and the dove came in to him in the evening; and, lo, in her mouth was an olive leaf pluckt off: so Noah knew that the waters were abated from off the earth.

**8:12**
Zolai: Tua ciangin ni sagih sung ngak leuleu-in a vakhu khah hi. Tua vakhu pen ama kiangah hong ciahkik nawn lo hi.
English: And he stayed yet other seven days; and sent forth the dove; which returned not again unto him any more.

**8:13**
Zolai: Noah a khan kum zaguk le a kum khatna, a kha masa, tua kha ni masa ni-in leitung panin tuite keu hi. Noah in teembaw khuhna lakhia a, khuadak hi. Lei maitang na keu ta hi.
English: And it came to pass in the six hundredth and first year, in the first month , the first day of the month, the waters were dried up from off the earth: and Noah removed the covering of the ark, and looked, and, behold, the face of the ground was dry.

**8:14**
Zolai: A kha nihna, tua kha ni sawmnih le sagih ni-in leitung keu hi.
English: And in the second month, on the seven and twentieth day of the month, was the earth dried.

**8:15**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Pasian in Noah kiangah,
English: And God spake unto Noah, saying,

**8:16**
Zolai: “Nang le na zi, na tapate le na tapate’ zite, teembaw sung panin paikhia un.
English: Go forth of the ark, thou, and thy wife, and thy sons, and thy sons' wives with thee.

**8:17**
Zolai: Nang tawh a omkhawm nuntakna a nei khempeuh - vasate, ganhingte le leitung a a bokvak peuhmah - leitungah tampi suakin, pungin leitungah a tam theih nadingin paikhiatpih in,” a ci hi.
English: Bring forth with thee every living thing that is with thee, of all flesh, both of fowl, and of cattle, and of every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth; that they may breed abundantly in the earth, and be fruitful, and multiply upon the earth.

**8:18**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Noah paikhia a, a tapate le ama zi le a tapate’ zite mah tawh paikhia khawm hi.
English: And Noah went forth, and his sons, and his wife, and his sons' wives with him:

**8:19**
Zolai: Ganhing khempeuh, a bokvak khempeuh, vasa khempeuh, leitung a a gamtang khempeuh a innkuan kuanin teembaw panin a paikhia uh hi.
English: every beast, every creeping thing, and every fowl, and whatsoever creepeth upon the earth, after their kinds, went forth out of the ark.

**8:20**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Noah in Topa a’ ding biakna tau khat lam a, a siangtho ganhing khempeuh le a siangtho vasa khempeuh lak pan khat ciat la-in, biakna tau tungah meihal biakna a pia hi.
English: And Noah builded an altar unto the LORD ; and took of every clean beast, and of every clean fowl, and offered burnt offerings on the altar.

**8:21**
Zolai: Topa in a namtui gimnam a zak ciangin, a lungsim sungah, “Mihing’ gamtatna hangin leitang ka samsia kik ngei nawn kei ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh mihing’ lungsim ngaihsutna pen a tangval lai panin a gi lo hi mawk hi. Tu-a ka hih bangin nuntakna a nei khempeuh zong ka susia ngei nawn kei ding hi.
English: And the LORD smelled a sweet savour; and the LORD said in his heart, I will not again curse the ground any more for man's sake; for the imagination of man's heart is evil from his youth; neither will I again smite any more every thing living, as I have done.

**8:22**
Zolai: Leitung a omlai tengin, lo pawi hun le anlak hun, a vot le a sa, khuakhal le phalbi, sun le zan bei lo ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: While the earth remaineth, seedtime and harvest, and cold and heat, and summer and winter, and day and night shall not cease.

## Chapter 9

**9:1**
Zolai: Pasian in Noah le a tapate thupha pia a, amaute tungah, “Pung unla, tampi pha-in, leitung dim un.
English: And God blessed Noah and his sons, and said unto them, Be fruitful, and multiply, and replenish the earth.

**9:2**
Zolai: Note pen leitung ganhing khempeuh, huih lak vasa khempeuh, leilakah a bokvak khempeuh le tuipi ngasa khempeuh in hong kihta-in hong zahtak ding uh hi. Note’ khut sungah tuate hong kipia hi.
English: And the fear of you and the dread of you shall be upon every beast of the earth, and upon every fowl of the air, upon all that moveth upon the earth, and upon all the fishes of the sea; into your hand are they delivered.

**9:3**
Zolai: A nungta a gamtang peuhmah, note a dingin an hi ding hi. Kung hing khempeuh ka hong piak bangin na khempeuh zong note ka hong pia hi.
English: Every moving thing that liveth shall be meat for you; even as the green herb have I given you all things.

**9:4**
Zolai: A nuntakna ahi a sisan pen a sa tawh na ne khawm kei bek ding uh hi.
English: But flesh with the life thereof, which is the blood thereof, shall ye not eat.

**9:5**
Zolai: Mi khatpeuh in hong thah le ama tungah sihna dan ka pia ding hi. A hong that ganhing peuhmah ka that ding a, a mipihte a that mi peuhmah gim ka pia ding hi.
English: And surely your blood of your lives will I require; at the hand of every beast will I require it, and at the hand of man; at the hand of every man's brother will I require the life of man.

**9:6**
Zolai: Mi a that peuhmahte pen, midangte in amah that ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Pasian in ama lim bangin mi bawl hi.
English: Whoso sheddeth man's blood, by man shall his blood be shed: for in the image of God made he man.

**9:7**
Zolai: “Note, pungin khang unla, leitungah tampi tak piangkhia-in, tampi pha-in khang un,” a ci hi.
English: And you, be ye fruitful, and multiply; bring forth abundantly in the earth, and multiply therein.

**9:8**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Pasian in Noah le amah tawh a om a tapate kiangah,
English: And God spake unto Noah, and to his sons with him, saying,

**9:9**
Zolai: “En un, note le note’ khit a na suanlekhakte uh le,
English: And I, behold, I establish my covenant with you, and with your seed after you;

**9:10**
Zolai: note tawh a om nuntakna a nei peuhmah, vasate, innsate, note tawh a om leitung gamsa peuhmah, teembaw sung panin a paikhia zahzah peuhmah tawh ka thuciamna ka kipsak hi.
English: and with every living creature that is with you, of the fowl, of the cattle, and of every beast of the earth with you; from all that go out of the ark, to every beast of the earth.

**9:11**
Zolai: Nuntakna a nei khempeuh, tuiciin tawh susia kik ngei nawn loin, leitung a susia dingin tuiciin ka tunsakkik ngei nawn loh nadingin note tawh ka thuciamna ka kipsak hi,” a ci hi.
English: And I will establish my covenant with you; neither shall all flesh be cut off any more by the waters of a flood; neither shall there any more be a flood to destroy the earth.

**9:12**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Pasian in, “Hih pen, kei le note le note tawh a om nuntakna a nei khempeuh kikalah mailam khang tawntung ah thuciamna lim ahi hi.
English: And God said, This is the token of the covenant which I make between me and you and every living creature that is with you, for perpetual generations:

**9:13**
Zolai: Meii sungah ka sakhituihup ka kaisak a, tua pen kei le leitung kikalah thuciamna lim hi ding hi.
English: I do set my bow in the cloud, and it shall be for a token of a covenant between me and the earth.

**9:14**
Zolai: Vantungah meii kong kaisak ciangin meii sungah sakhituihup a kimuh leh,
English: And it shall come to pass, when I bring a cloud over the earth, that the bow shall be seen in the cloud:

**9:15**
Zolai: kei le note le nuntakna a nei khempeuh tawh ka thuciamna ka phawk ding hi. Tuite pen, nuntakna a nei khempeuh a susia ding tuiciin suakkik ngei nawn lo ding hi.
English: and I will remember my covenant, which is between me and you and every living creature of all flesh; and the waters shall no more become a flood to destroy all flesh.

**9:16**
Zolai: Meii sungah sakhituihup a om ciangin keimah in ka en ding a, kei le leitung a a om nuntakna a nei khempeuh tawh tawntung thuciamna ka phawk ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And the bow shall be in the cloud; and I will look upon it, that I may remember the everlasting covenant between God and every living creature of all flesh that is upon the earth.

**9:17**
Zolai: Pasian in Noah kiangah, “Hih pen, kei le leitung a a om nuntakna a nei khempeuh tawh ka kipsaksa thuciamna lim ahi hi,” a ci hi.
English: And God said unto Noah, This is the token of the covenant, which I have established between me and all flesh that is upon the earth.

**9:18**
Zolai: Teembaw sung panin a paikhia Noah’ tapate, Shem, Ham, le Jafeth ahi hi. Ham pen Kanaan’ pa ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Noah, that went forth of the ark, were Shem, and Ham, and Japheth: and Ham is the father of Canaan.

**9:19**
Zolai: Hih Noah’ tapa thumte panin leitung buppi mi tawh hong kidim hi.
English: These are the three sons of Noah: and of them was the whole earth overspread.

**9:20**
Zolai: Noah pen lo kho masa pa hi a, amah in leenggui lo khat a bawl hi.
English: And Noah began to be an husbandman, and he planted a vineyard:

**9:21**
Zolai: Amah in leenggahzu ne-in kham a, a puanbuk sungah bangmah silh loin a lum hi.
English: and he drank of the wine, and was drunken; and he was uncovered within his tent.

**9:22**
Zolai: Kanaan’ pa Ham in a pa guaktangin a omna mu a, a pualama om a sanggam nihte kiangah a gen hi.
English: And Ham, the father of Canaan, saw the nakedness of his father, and told his two brethren without.

**9:23**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Shem le Jafeth in puan khat la-in amau tegel’ liangko tuakah baang uh a, a nung leh lamun pai-in a pa uh’ guaktang omna a khuh uh hi. Amaute in maingat lo uh ahih manin a pa uh guaktang omna mu lo uh hi.
English: And Shem and Japheth took a garment, and laid it upon both their shoulders, and went backward, and covered the nakedness of their father; and their faces were backward, and they saw not their father's nakedness.

**9:24**
Zolai: Noah a zukhamna panin a pilvan’ ciangin ama tungah a tapa Ham’ gamtatna thei a,
English: And Noah awoke from his wine, and knew what his younger son had done unto him.

**9:25**
Zolai: amah in, “Kanaan in samsiatna ngah ta hen la, a sanggamte’ sila hi tahen.
English: And he said, Cursed be Canaan; A servant of servants shall he be unto his brethren.

**9:26**
Zolai: Topa ka Pasian in Shem thupha pia hen la, Kanaan, ama sila hisak hen.
English: And he said, Blessed be the LORD God of Shem; And Canaan shall be his servant.

**9:27**
Zolai: Pasian in Jafeth pungsak hen la, Shem’ puanbukte sungah amah tengsak hen. Kanaan ama sila hisak hen,” a ci hi.
English: God shall enlarge Japheth, And he shall dwell in the tents of Shem; And Canaan shall be his servant.

**9:28**
Zolai: Tuiciin a tun khit ciangin Noah kum zathum le kum sawmnga nungta hi.
English: And Noah lived after the flood three hundred and fifty years.

**9:29**
Zolai: Noah’ khan sungteng pen kum zakua le kum sawmnga hi a, tua ciangin amah a si hi.
English: And all the days of Noah were nine hundred and fifty years: and he died.

## Chapter 10

**10:1**
Zolai: Hihte pen Noah’ tapa Shem, Ham, le Jafeth-te’ suanlekhakte ahi hi. Tuiciin tun khit ciangin amau sung panin tapate hong piang hi.
English: Now these are the generations of the sons of Noah, Shem, Ham, and Japheth: and unto them were sons born after the flood.

**10:2**
Zolai: Jafeth’ tapate: Gomer, Magog, Madai, Javan, le Tiras ahi hi.
English: The sons of Japheth; Gomer, and Magog, and Madai, and Javan, and Tubal, and Meshech, and Tiras.

**10:3**
Zolai: Gomer’ tapate: Ashkenaz, Rifath, le Togarmah ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Gomer; Ashkenaz, and Riphath, and Togarmah.

**10:4**
Zolai: Javan’ tapate: Elishah, Tarshish, Kittim, le Dodanim ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Javan; Elishah, and Tarshish, Kittim, and Dodanim.

**10:5**
Zolai: Hihte pen tuipi gei-a teng mite’ pulepa ahi uh hi. Amaute’ leitangah amau’ kam pau ciat zangin, a beh, a minamin a om uh hi.
English: By these were the isles of the Gentiles divided in their lands; every one after his tongue, after their families, in their nations.

**10:6**
Zolai: Ham’ tapate: Kush, Egypt, Put, le Kanaan ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Ham; Cush, and Mizraim, and Phut, and Canaan.

**10:7**
Zolai: Kush’ tapate: Seba, Havilah, Sabtah, Raamah, le Sabteka ahi hi. Raamah’ tapate: Sheba le Dedan ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Cush; Seba, and Havilah, and Sabtah, and Raamah, and Sabtechah: and the sons of Raamah; Sheba, and Dedan.

**10:8**
Zolai: Kush in Nimrod kici tapa khat nei a, amah pen leitungah a vanglian masa mi ahi hi.
English: And Cush begat Nimrod: he began to be a mighty one in the earth.

**10:9**
Zolai: Amah pen Topa’ mai-ah a minthang sabengpa zong ahi hi. Tua ahih ciangin, “ Topa in Nimrod bangin a minthang sabengpa hong suaksak ta hen,” kici hi.
English: He was a mighty hunter before the LORD : wherefore it is said, Even as Nimrod the mighty hunter before the LORD .

**10:10**
Zolai: Ama kumpi gam kipatna Babel, Erek, le Akkad hi a, tuate khempeuh Shinar gam sungah om hi.
English: And the beginning of his kingdom was Babel, and Erech, and Accad, and Calneh, in the land of Shinar.

**10:11**
Zolai: Tua gam panin Assiria gam sungah amah pai-in Nineveh, Rehoboth-Ir, Kalah, le
English: Out of that land went forth Asshur, and builded Nineveh, and the city Rehoboth, and Calah,

**10:12**
Zolai: Nineveh le Kalah kikal-a om Resen khuapite a sat hi. Tua Kalah khuapi pen khuapi lian ahi hi.
English: and Resen between Nineveh and Calah: the same is a great city.

**10:13**
Zolai: Egypt pen Lud mite, Anam mite, Lehab mite, Naftuh mite,
English: And Mizraim begat Ludim, and Anamim, and Lehabim, and Naphtuhim,

**10:14**
Zolai: Pathru mite, Kasluh mite (Filistia mite’ pianna), le Kaftor mite’ pianna pupi ahi hi.
English: and Pathrusim, and Casluhim, (out of whom came Philistim,) and Caphtorim.

**10:15**
Zolai: Kanaan pen ama sung pan a suak masa Sidon, Heth,
English: And Canaan begat Sidon his firstborn, and Heth,

**10:16**
Zolai: le Jebus mite, Amor mite, Girgash mite,
English: and the Jebusite, and the Amorite, and the Girgasite,

**10:17**
Zolai: Hiv mite, Arki mite, Sin mite,
English: and the Hivite, and the Arkite, and the Sinite,

**10:18**
Zolai: Arvad mite, Zemari mite, le Hamath mite’ pianna pupi ahi hi. Tua khit ciangin Kanaan mite kizelthang hi.
English: and the Arvadite, and the Zemarite, and the Hamathite: and afterward were the families of the Canaanites spread abroad.

**10:19**
Zolai: Kanaan mite’ gam pen Sidon panin kipanin Gerar lam manawhin Gaza ciang dong ban a, Sodom lam panin Gomorrah, Admah, le Lasha gei-a Zeboiim ciang dong ban hi.
English: And the border of the Canaanites was from Sidon, as thou comest to Gerar, unto Gaza; as thou goest, unto Sodom, and Gomorrah, and Admah, and Zeboim, even unto Lasha.

**10:20**
Zolai: Hihte pen a innkuan, a kam pau, a leitang, a minamin Ham’ suanlekhakte ahi hi.
English: These are the sons of Ham, after their families, after their tongues, in their countries, and in their nations.

**10:21**
Zolai: Eber mi khempeuh’ pianna pupi, Jafeth’ u, Shem’ sung panin zong tate hong piang hi.
English: Unto Shem also, the father of all the children of Eber, the brother of Japheth the elder, even to him were children born.

**10:22**
Zolai: Shem’ tapate: Elam, Asshur, Arpakshad, Lud, le Aram ahi hi.
English: The children of Shem; Elam, and Asshur, and Arphaxad, and Lud, and Aram.

**10:23**
Zolai: Aram’ tapate: Uz, Hul, Gether, le Mash ahi hi.
English: And the children of Aram; Uz, and Hul, and Gether, and Mash.

**10:24**
Zolai: Arpakshad in Shelah kici tapa khat nei a, Shelah in Eber kici tapa khat mah nei hi.
English: And Arphaxad begat Salah; and Salah begat Eber.

**10:25**
Zolai: Eber’ sung panin tapa nih suak a, khat’ min pen Peleg ahi hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh ama hunin leitung kikhen hi. A sanggampa’ min pen Joktan ahi hi.
English: And unto Eber were born two sons: the name of one was Peleg; for in his days was the earth divided; and his brother's name was Joktan.

**10:26**
Zolai: Joktan pen Almodad, Shelef, Hazarmaveth, Jerah,
English: And Joktan begat Almodad, and Sheleph, and Hazarmaveth, and Jerah,

**10:27**
Zolai: Hadoram, Uzal, Diklah,
English: and Hadoram, and Uzal, and Diklah,

**10:28**
Zolai: Obal, Abimael, Sheba,
English: and Obal, and Abimael, and Sheba,

**10:29**
Zolai: Ofir, Havilah, le Jobab’ pianna pa ahi hi. Hihte khempeuh Joktan’ tapate ahi hi.
English: and Ophir, and Havilah, and Jobab: all these were the sons of Joktan.

**10:30**
Zolai: Amau’ tenna gam pen Mesha panin kipanin Sefar lamah nisuahna gam mualtung dong ban hi.
English: And their dwelling was from Mesha, as thou goest unto Sephar a mount of the east.

**10:31**
Zolai: Hihte pen a innkuan, a kam pau, a leitang, a minamin Shem’ suanlekhakte ahi hi.
English: These are the sons of Shem, after their families, after their tongues, in their lands, after their nations.

**10:32**
Zolai: Hihte pen Noah’ tapate innkuan, a khangsimna tawh kizui-in amau’ minam ahi hi. Tuiciin tun khit ciangin hihte tung panin leitungah minamte kizelthang hi.
English: These are the families of the sons of Noah, after their generations, in their nations: and by these were the nations divided in the earth after the flood.

## Chapter 11

**11:1**
Zolai: Tua laitakin leitung buppi in kampau khat le kammal tawmno bek nei hi.
English: And the whole earth was of one language, and of one speech.

**11:2**
Zolai: Amaute, nisuahna lamah lal uh a, Shinar gam sungah zanglei mun khat mu-in tua lai-ah a teng uh hi.
English: And it came to pass, as they journeyed from the east, that they found a plain in the land of Shinar; and they dwelt there.

**11:3**
Zolai: Amaute khatlekhat kiangah, “Hong pai un, leiseek seekin limtakin hal ni,” kici uh hi. Amaute in suang dingin leiseek nei uh a, a buan dingin kultal tui nei uh hi.
English: And they said one to another, Go to, let us make brick, and burn them throughly. And they had brick for stone, and slime had they for morter.

**11:4**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in, “Hong pai un, leitung buppi-ah eite i kithehthang gawp loh nadingin ei a dingin khuapi khat bawlin, a dawn in vantung a ban ding tausang khat lamin, eite’ minthan nading khat bawl ni,” ci uh hi.
English: And they said, Go to, let us build us a city and a tower, whose top may reach unto heaven; and let us make us a name, lest we be scattered abroad upon the face of the whole earth.

**11:5**
Zolai: Tua ciangin mihingte’ lamsa khuapi le tausangpi a en dingin Topa hong paisuk hi.
English: And the LORD came down to see the city and the tower, which the children of men builded.

**11:6**
Zolai: Topa in, “En un, amaute minam khat hi uh a, amaute khempeuh in kampau khat nei uh hi. Hih pen amau’ sep ding a kipatna bek ahi hi. Tu-in sep dinga amau’ vaihawmte amau a dingin hi thei nawn lo ding hi.
English: And the LORD said, Behold, the people is one, and they have all one language; and this they begin to do: and now nothing will be restrained from them, which they have imagined to do.

**11:7**
Zolai: Hong pai un, amaute khatlekhat’ thugen a kitheih loh nadingun eite paisukin amau’ kampau va kitukalhsak ni,” a ci hi.
English: Go to, let us go down, and there confound their language, that they may not understand one another's speech.

**11:8**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Topa in tua lai panin leitung khempeuhah amaute thehthang a, a khuapi bawl uh a tawp uh hi.
English: So the LORD scattered them abroad from thence upon the face of all the earth: and they left off to build the city.

**11:9**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin a min Babel kici hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in tua munah leitung khempeuh’ kampau kitukalhsak hi. Tua lai mun panin Topa in leitung khempeuhah amaute a thehthang hi.
English: Therefore is the name of it called Babel; because the LORD did there confound the language of all the earth: and from thence did the LORD scatter them abroad upon the face of all the earth.

**11:10**
Zolai: Hihte pen Shem’ suanlekhakte ahi hi. Shem kum zakhat a phak, tuiciin tun khit kum nih ciangin, amah in Arpakshad kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: These are the generations of Shem: Shem was an hundred years old, and begat Arphaxad two years after the flood:

**11:11**
Zolai: Arpakshad a suah khit ciangin Shem kum zakhat nungta lai a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Shem lived after he begat Arphaxad five hundred years, and begat sons and daughters.

**11:12**
Zolai: Arpakshad kum sawmthum le nga a phak khit ciangin, amah in Shelah kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Arphaxad lived five and thirty years, and begat Salah:

**11:13**
Zolai: Shelah a suah khit ciangin Arpakshad kum zali le kum sawmthum nungta lai a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Arphaxad lived after he begat Salah four hundred and three years, and begat sons and daughters.

**11:14**
Zolai: Shelah kum sawmthum a phak khit ciangin Eber kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Salah lived thirty years, and begat Eber:

**11:15**
Zolai: Eber’ suah khit ciangin Shelah kum zali le kum sawmthum nungta lai a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Salah lived after he begat Eber four hundred and three years, and begat sons and daughters.

**11:16**
Zolai: Eber kum sawmthum le li a phak khit ciangin amah in Peleg kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Eber lived four and thirty years, and begat Peleg:

**11:17**
Zolai: Peleg a suah khit ciangin Eber kum zali le kum sawmthum nungta lai a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Eber lived after he begat Peleg four hundred and thirty years, and begat sons and daughters.

**11:18**
Zolai: Peleg kum sawmthum a phak khit ciangin amah in Reu kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Peleg lived thirty years, and begat Reu:

**11:19**
Zolai: Reu a suah khit ciangin Peleg kum zanih le kum kua nungta lai a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Peleg lived after he begat Reu two hundred and nine years, and begat sons and daughters.

**11:20**
Zolai: Reu kum sawmthum le nih a phak khit ciangin amah in Serug kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Reu lived two and thirty years, and begat Serug:

**11:21**
Zolai: Serug a suah khit ciangin Reu kum zanih le kum sagih nungta lai a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Reu lived after he begat Serug two hundred and seven years, and begat sons and daughters.

**11:22**
Zolai: Serug kum sawmthum a phak khit ciangin amah in Nahor kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Serug lived thirty years, and begat Nahor:

**11:23**
Zolai: Nahor a suah khit ciangin Serug kum zanih nungta lai a, tanu le tapa dang nei lai hi.
English: and Serug lived after he begat Nahor two hundred years, and begat sons and daughters.

**11:24**
Zolai: Nahor kum sawmnih le kua a phak khit ciangin amah in Terah kici tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Nahor lived nine and twenty years, and begat Terah:

**11:25**
Zolai: Terah a suah khit ciangin Nahor kum za le sawm le kua nungta lai a, tanu le tapa dang neilai hi.
English: and Nahor lived after he begat Terah an hundred and nineteen years, and begat sons and daughters.

**11:26**
Zolai: Terah kum sawmsagih a phak khit ciangin amah in Abram, Nahor, le Haran a nei hi.
English: And Terah lived seventy years, and begat Abram, Nahor, and Haran.

**11:27**
Zolai: Tu-in Terah’ suanlekhakte hih bang ahi hi. Terah pen Abram, Nahor, le Haran’ pa hi a, Haran pen Lot’ pa ahi hi.
English: Now these are the generations of Terah: Terah begat Abram, Nahor, and Haran; and Haran begat Lot.

**11:28**
Zolai: Ama pa Terah a sih ma-in ama suahna gam ahi, Khaldea gam Ur khua-ah Haran si hi.
English: And Haran died before his father Terah in the land of his nativity, in Ur of the Chaldees.

**11:29**
Zolai: Abram le Nahor in zi nei uh hi. Abram’ zi min Sarai hi a, Nahor’ zi min Milkah hi a, Milkah pen Iskah’ pa Haran’ tanu ahi hi.
English: And Abram and Nahor took them wives: the name of Abram's wife was Sarai; and the name of Nahor's wife, Milcah, the daughter of Haran, the father of Milcah, and the father of Iscah.

**11:30**
Zolai: Tu-in Sarai ciing a, ta nei lo hi.
English: But Sarai was barren; she had no child.

**11:31**
Zolai: Terah in ama tapa Abram le Haran’ tapa, ama tupa ahi Lot, le a tapa Abram’ zi ahi a monu Sarai samin, Kanaan gam sungah a pai dingin Khaldea gam Ur khua panin amaute a paikhia khawm uh hi. Ahi zongin amaute Haran a tun uh ciangin tua munah a teng uh hi.
English: And Terah took Abram his son, and Lot the son of Haran his son's son, and Sarai his daughter in law, his son Abram's wife; and they went forth with them from Ur of the Chaldees, to go into the land of Canaan; and they came unto Haran, and dwelt there.

**11:32**
Zolai: Terah’ khansung kum zanih le kum nga hi a, Haran-ah Terah a si hi.
English: And the days of Terah were two hundred and five years: and Terah died in Haran.

## Chapter 12

**12:1**
Zolai: Topa in Abram kiangah, “Na gam, na beh, le na pa’ inn panin nang kong lah ding gamah pai in.
English: Now the LORD had said unto Abram, Get thee out of thy country, and from thy kindred, and from thy father's house, unto a land that I will shew thee:

**12:2**
Zolai: Thupha a ngah dingin minam lian khatin nang hong bawlin, thupha hong pia-in, na min kong liansak ding hi.
English: and I will make of thee a great nation, and I will bless thee, and make thy name great; and thou shalt be a blessing:

**12:3**
Zolai: Nang thupha hong piate thupha ka pia ding a, nang hong samsiate ka samsia ding hi. Nang’ thupha ngah bangin thupha a ngah nadingun leitung midang khempeuh in hong ngen ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: and I will bless them that bless thee, and curse him that curseth thee: and in thee shall all families of the earth be blessed.

**12:4**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa’ gensa bangin Abram pai a, Lot in zong a zui hi. Haran panin a paikhiatin Abram kum sawmsagih le nga a pha hi.
English: So Abram departed, as the LORD had spoken unto him; and Lot went with him: and Abram was seventy and five years old when he departed out of Haran.

**12:5**
Zolai: Abram in ama zi Sarai, a sanggampa’ tapa Lot, amau’ kaihkhopsa neihsa khempeuh, le Haran-a amau’ neih sila khempeuh samin, Kanaan gamah a pai dingin amaute ding khia uh a, tua gam a tung uh hi.
English: And Abram took Sarai his wife, and Lot his brother's son, and all their substance that they had gathered, and the souls that they had gotten in Haran; and they went forth to go into the land of Canaan; and into the land of Canaan they came.

**12:6**
Zolai: Abram in tua gam sung nawkin Shekhem mun, Moreh tawsaw phung dong a tung hi. Tua hunin tua lai-ah Kanaan mite teng lai hi.
English: And Abram passed through the land unto the place of Sichem, unto the plain of Moreh. And the Canaanite was then in the land.

**12:7**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abram’ tungah Topa kilang a, “Na suanlekhakte tungah hih leitang ka pia ding hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in ama tunga kilang Topa a dingin biakna tau khat a bawl hi.
English: And the LORD appeared unto Abram, and said, Unto thy seed will I give this land: and there builded he an altar unto the LORD , who appeared unto him.

**12:8**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Bethel panin nisuahna lam mualah amah kin kikin a puanbuk lam a, nitumna lamah Bethel, nisuahna lamah Ai om hi. Tua lai munah zong amah in Topa a dingin biakna tau khat bawl a, Topa’ tungah thu a ngen hi.
English: And he removed from thence unto a mountain on the east of Beth-el, and pitched his tent, having Beth-el on the west, and Hai on the east: and there he builded an altar unto the LORD , and called upon the name of the LORD .

**12:9**
Zolai: Abram in a khualzin zom lai a, Negeb gam lam manawhin a pai lai hi.
English: And Abram journeyed, going on still toward the south.

**12:10**
Zolai: Kanaan gam sungah kialpi tung hi. Tua kialpi nasia ahih manin tawlkhat sung a om dingin Egypt-ah Abram a paisuk hi.
English: And there was a famine in the land: and Abram went down into Egypt to sojourn there; for the famine was grievous in the land.

**12:11**
Zolai: Egypt gam a tum ding ciangin amah in a zi Sarai’ kiangah, “Nang pen nupi melhoih khat na hihna ka thei hi.
