English: And it came to pass, when he was come near to enter into Egypt, that he said unto Sarai his wife, Behold now, I know that thou art a fair woman to look upon:

**12:12**
Zolai: Egypt mite in nang hong muh ciangin amaute in, ‘Hih nu ama zi hi,’ ci ding uh hi. Tua ciangin amaute in kei hong that ding uh a, ahi zongin amaute in nang hong nungtasak ding uh hi.
English: therefore it shall come to pass, when the Egyptians shall see thee, that they shall say, This is his wife: and they will kill me, but they will save thee alive.

**12:13**
Zolai: Nang pen ka sanggamnu ci lehang, nangma hangin kei a dingin thu hong hoihzaw ding a, nangma hangin ka suakta thei kha ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: Say, I pray thee, thou art my sister: that it may be well with me for thy sake; and my soul shall live because of thee.

**12:14**
Zolai: Egypt gam sungah Abram a tun ciangin Egypt mite in tua nupi a mel hoihsa mahmah uh hi.
English: And it came to pass, that, when Abram was come into Egypt, the Egyptians beheld the woman that she was very fair.

**12:15**
Zolai: Faro’ uliante in amah a muh uh ciangin Faro’ kiangah amah phat uh hi. Faro’ inn sungah tua nupi kila hi.
English: The princes also of Pharaoh saw her, and commended her before Pharaoh: and the woman was taken into Pharaoh's house.

**12:16**
Zolai: Tua nu’ hangin amah in Abram limbawl mahmah hi. Amah in tuu, bawngtal, latal, pasal nasem, numei nasem, lanu, le kalaohte a pia hi.
English: And he entreated Abram well for her sake: and he had sheep, and oxen, and he asses, and menservants, and maidservants, and she asses, and camels.

**12:17**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa in Abram’ zi Sarai’ huhau-in Faro le a innkuanpihte gimna lianpi thuaksak hi.
English: And the LORD plagued Pharaoh and his house with great plagues because of Sarai Abram's wife.

**12:18**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Faro in Abram samin, “Bang hangin hih bangin kei hong bawl na hi hiam? Amah na zi ahihna bang hangin kei kiangah hong gen lo na hi hiam?
English: And Pharaoh called Abram, and said, What is this that thou hast done unto me? why didst thou not tell me that she was thy wife?

**12:19**
Zolai: Ka zi dingin amah ka lak theih nadingin, ‘Amah ka sanggamnu hi,’ bang hangin hong ci na hi hiam? Tu-in hih lai-ah na zi om hi. Amah la in la pai un,” a ci hi.
English: Why saidst thou, She is my sister? so I might have taken her to me to wife: now therefore behold thy wife, take her , and go thy way.

**12:20**
Zolai: Faro in amah tawh kisai-in a mite tungah thu a pia hi. Amaute in a zi le ama neih khempeuh tawh lampi-ah a khakhia uh hi.
English: And Pharaoh commanded his men concerning him: and they sent him away, and his wife, and all that he had.

## Chapter 13

**13:1**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Egypt panin Abram, a zi, ama neih khempeuh, le Lot zong tawh, Negeb gam lamah a paito hi.
English: And Abram went up out of Egypt, he, and his wife, and all that he had, and Lot with him, into the south.

**13:2**
Zolai: Abram in ganhing, ngun, le kham hau mahmah hi.
English: And Abram was very rich in cattle, in silver, and in gold.

**13:3**
Zolai: Amah Negeb gam pan kipanin Bethel ciang dong, a kipat cil-in a puanbuk omnasa mun Bethel le Ai kikal,
English: And he went on his journeys from the south even to Beth-el, unto the place where his tent had been at the beginning, between Beth-el and Hai;

**13:4**
Zolai: a masa-a biakna tau khat a bawlnasa munah khualzinin a paisuak hi. Tua lai munah Abram in Topa’ tungah thu a ngen hi.
English: unto the place of the altar, which he had made there at the first: and there Abram called on the name of the LORD .

**13:5**
Zolai: Abram tawh a paikhawm Lot in zong tuuhon, ganhon, le puanbukte nei hi.
English: And Lot also, which went with Abram, had flocks, and herds, and tents.

**13:6**
Zolai: Tua ahih manin mun khatah a tengkhawm dingin leitang in amau tegel vak zo lo hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amau’ gan neihsate tam mahmah ahih manin amau tegel tengkhawm thei lo uh a,
English: And the land was not able to bear them, that they might dwell together: for their substance was great, so that they could not dwell together.

**13:7**
Zolai: Abram’ gancingte le Lot’ gancingte kitawng thei zel hi. Tua hun laitakin Kanaan mite le Perez mite tua gamah teng lai uh hi.
English: And there was a strife between the herdmen of Abram's cattle and the herdmen of Lot's cattle: and the Canaanite and the Perizzite dwelled then in the land.

**13:8**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abram in Lot’ kiangah, “Nang le kei’ kikal, nang’ gancingte le kei’ gancingte’ kikalah kitotna omsak kei ni. Bang hang hiam cih leh eite beh khat ihi hi.
English: And Abram said unto Lot, Let there be no strife, I pray thee, between me and thee, and between my herdmen and thy herdmen; for we be brethren.

**13:9**
Zolai: Na mai-ah gam buppi om hi lo ahi hiam? Kei’ kiang panin nangmah paikhia tawm in. Nang in veilam na lak leh, kei taklamah ka pai ding hi. Tua ahih kei leh zong, nang in taklam na lak leh, kei veilamah ka pai ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: Is not the whole land before thee? separate thyself, I pray thee, from me: if thou wilt take the left hand, then I will go to the right; or if thou depart to the right hand, then I will go to the left.

**13:10**
Zolai: Lot zong khuadak a, Jordan gun kuam mun khempeuh in limtakin tui ngahin Topa’ huan hitaleh, Zoar lama Egypt gam tawh hitaleh kibang hi, ci-in mu hi. Hih pen Topa in Sodom le Gomorrah a suksiat hun ma ahi hi.
English: And Lot lifted up his eyes, and beheld all the plain of Jordan, that it was well watered every where, before the LORD destroyed Sodom and Gomorrah, even as the garden of the LORD , like the land of Egypt, as thou comest unto Zoar.

**13:11**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Lot in ama a dingin Jordan gun kuam khempeuh teel a, nisuahna lamah a pai hi. Tua ahih manin amaute kikhen tuak uh hi.
English: Then Lot chose him all the plain of Jordan; and Lot journeyed east: and they separated themselves the one from the other.

**13:12**
Zolai: Kuam sunga khuapite’ lakah Lot tengin, a puanbukte Sodom ciang dongah khinin a om laitakin Kanaan gam sungah Abram teng hi.
English: Abram dwelled in the land of Canaan, and Lot dwelled in the cities of the plain, and pitched his tent toward Sodom.

**13:13**
Zolai: Tua laitakin Sodom mite migi lo hi a, Topa’ tungah nakpitakin a khialte ahi hi.
English: But the men of Sodom were wicked and sinners before the LORD exceedingly.

**13:14**
Zolai: Ama kiang panin Lot a paikhiat khit ciangin Topa in Abram’ kiangah, “Khuadak to inla, nangma omna panin leilu lam, leitaw lam, nisuahna lam, le nitumna lam en in.
English: And the LORD said unto Abram, after that Lot was separated from him, Lift up now thine eyes, and look from the place where thou art northward, and southward, and eastward, and westward:

**13:15**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh na muh gam khempeuh nang le na suanlekhakte kong pia paisuak ding hi.
English: for all the land which thou seest, to thee will I give it, and to thy seed for ever.

**13:16**
Zolai: Na suanlekhakte, leitung leivui zahin tampi ka phasak ding hi. Mi khatpeuh in leitung leivui a sim theih leh na suanlekhakte zong kisim thei ding hi.
English: And I will make thy seed as the dust of the earth: so that if a man can number the dust of the earth, then shall thy seed also be numbered.

**13:17**
Zolai: Ding inla, gamdung gamvai kantanin pai in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nang’ tungah kong pia ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: Arise, walk through the land in the length of it and in the breadth of it; for I will give it unto thee.

**13:18**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Abram in a puanbuk khinin, Hebron gam sung, Mamre tawsawte gei-ah hong pai-in a teng hi. Tua lai munah Topa a dingin biakna tau khat a bawl hi.
English: Then Abram removed his tent, and came and dwelt in the plain of Mamre, which is in Hebron, and built there an altar unto the LORD .

## Chapter 14

**14:1**
Zolai: Shinar kumpipa Amrafel, Ellasar kumpipa Ariok, Elam kumpipa Khedorlaomer, le Goiim kumpipa Tidal-te’ hun lai-in,
English: And it came to pass in the days of Amraphel king of Shinar, Arioch king of Ellasar, Chedorlaomer king of Elam, and Tidal king of nations;

**14:2**
Zolai: hih kumpite in Sodom kumpipa Bera, Gomorrah kumpipa Birsha, Admah kumpipa Shinab, Zeboiim kumpipa Shemeber, le Bela (Zoar) kumpipa, kumpi ngate va sim uh hi.
English: that these made war with Bera king of Sodom, and with Birsha king of Gomorrah, Shinab king of Admah, and Shemeber king of Zeboiim, and the king of Bela, which is Zoar.

**14:3**
Zolai: Hih kumpi ngate in kipawlna bawlin Siddim Kuam (Ci Tuipi)-ah a galkapte uh gawm uh hi.
English: All these were joined together in the vale of Siddim, which is the salt sea.

**14:4**
Zolai: Amaute, kum sawm le nih sung Khedorlaomer’ khutnuai-ah om uh a, ahih hangin a kum sawm le thumna ciangin amaute in lehdo uh hi.
English: Twelve years they served Chedorlaomer, and in the thirteenth year they rebelled.

**14:5**
Zolai: A kum sawm le lina ciangin Khedorlaomer le amah tawh a kipawl kumpite hong pai-in sehnel gamgi Elparan ciang dongah Ashteroth Karnaim gam a Refaim, Ham gam a Zuzim, Shavehkiriathaim gam a Emim,
English: And in the fourteenth year came Chedorlaomer, and the kings that were with him, and smote the Rephaims in Ashteroth Karnaim, and the Zuzims in Ham, and the Emims in Shaveh Kiriathaim,

**14:6**
Zolai: le amau’ gam Seir Mual tunga Hori mite hong zo uh hi.
English: and the Horites in their mount Seir, unto El-paran, which is by the wilderness.

**14:7**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute kihei kikin Enmishpat (Kadesh) ah hong pai uh a, Amalek mite’ gam khempeuh le Hazazontamar gam a teng Amor mite zong zo uh hi.
English: And they returned, and came to En-mishpat, which is Kadesh, and smote all the country of the Amalekites, and also the Amorites, that dwelt in Hazezon-tamar.

**14:8**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Sodom kumpipa, Gomorrah kumpipa, Admah kumpipa, Zeboiim kumpipa, le Bela (Zoar) kumpipa kuankhia uh a, amaute kipawlin Siddim Kuam ah
English: And there went out the king of Sodom, and the king of Gomorrah, and the king of Admah, and the king of Zeboiim, and the king of Bela (the same is Zoar;) and they joined battle with them in the vale of Siddim;

**14:9**
Zolai: Ela kumpipa Khedorlaomer, Goiim kumpipa Tidal, Shinar kumpipa Amrafel, le Ellasar kumpipa Ariok tawh kido uh a, kumpi li kigawm le kumpi nga kigawm kido uh hi.
English: with Chedorlaomer the king of Elam, and with Tidal king of nations, and Amraphel king of Shinar, and Arioch king of Ellasar; four kings with five.

**14:10**
Zolai: Siddim Kuam pen kultal khukte tawh kidim a, Sodom le Gomorrah kumpite a tai uh ciangin pawlkhat tua khukte sungah kia uh a, a omlai teng mualtungah tai uh hi.
English: And the vale of Siddim was full of slimepits; and the kings of Sodom and Gomorrah fled, and fell there; and they that remained fled to the mountain.

**14:11**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin galte in Sodom le Gomorrah-te’ na khempeuh le a an khempeuh uh la-in a ciah uh hi.
English: And they took all the goods of Sodom and Gomorrah, and all their victuals, and went their way.

**14:12**
Zolai: Amaute in Sodom a, a teng Lot (Abram’ sanggampa’ tapa) le a na khempeuh zong la-in a paikhia uh hi.
English: And they took Lot, Abram's brother's son, who dwelt in Sodom, and his goods, and departed.

**14:13**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a suakta mi khat hong pai-in, Hebru mi Abram’ kiangah hong gen hi. Amah pen Eshkol le Aner’ sanggampa ahi hi. Amor mi hi a, Mamre tawsawte gei-ah teng hi. Hih mite pen Abram’ kipawlpihte ahi hi.
English: And there came one that had escaped, and told Abram the Hebrew; for he dwelt in the plain of Mamre the Amorite, brother of Eshcol, and brother of Aner: and these were confederate with Abram.

**14:14**
Zolai: Ama behpa salin a kimatna Abram in a zak ciangin, ama inn sunga a suak, a kihilhsa ama mi zathum le sawm le giatte makaihin Dan ciang dong a delhin a pai uh hi.
English: And when Abram heard that his brother was taken captive, he armed his trained servants , born in his own house, three hundred and eighteen, and pursued them unto Dan.

**14:15**
Zolai: Amah in zan hunin ama pawlte, amah le a nasemte, amaute a do dingin khenin amaute zo a, Damaskas leilu lam Hobah ciang dong a delh uh hi.
English: And he divided himself against them, he and his servants, by night, and smote them, and pursued them unto Hobah, which is on the left hand of Damascus.

**14:16**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in Lot le ama na khempeuh, numeite le a galmatte tawh a ciahpih kik hi.
English: And he brought back all the goods, and also brought again his brother Lot, and his goods, and the women also, and the people.

**14:17**
Zolai: Abram in Khedorlaomer kumpipa le a pawlte a zawhna panin a ciahkik ciangin amah a dawn dingin Sodom kumpipa Shaveh Kuam (Kumpipa’ Kuam)-ah na pai hi.
English: And the king of Sodom went out to meet him after his return from the slaughter of Chedorlaomer, and of the kings that were with him, at the valley of Shaveh, which is the king's dale.

**14:18**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jerusalem kumpipa Melkhizedek in an le leenggahzu hong pusuah hi. Amah pen Sang Pen Pasian’ siampi zong ahi hi.
English: And Melchizedek king of Salem brought forth bread and wine: and he was the priest of the most high God.

**14:19**
Zolai: Amah in thupha pia a, “Vantung le leitung a bawl, Sang Pen Pasian in Abram thupha pia hen!
English: And he blessed him, and said, Blessed be Abram of the most high God, possessor of heaven and earth:

**14:20**
Zolai: Na galte na khut sungah a hong pia Sang Pen Pasian in thupha ngah hen,” a ci hi. Abram in na khempeuh sawm-ah-khat ama tungah a pia hi.
English: and blessed be the most high God, which hath delivered thine enemies into thy hand. And he gave him tithes of all.

**14:21**
Zolai: Sodom kumpipa in Abram’ kiangah, “A mite hong pia inla, ahih hangin a nate nang a dingin la in,” a ci hi.
English: And the king of Sodom said unto Abram, Give me the persons, and take the goods to thyself.

**14:22**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Abram in Sodom kumpipa kiangah, “Vantung le leitung a bawl Sang Pen Topa Pasian tungah ka kiciam khinzo hi.
English: And Abram said to the king of Sodom, I have lift up mine hand unto the LORD , the most high God, the possessor of heaven and earth,

**14:23**
Zolai: Nangmah in, ‘Abram ka hausak hi,’ ci kha ding na hih manin mimkhau ahi a, khedap khau ahi a, nangma a’ ahi na khat peuhpeuh ahi zongin ka la kei ding hi.
English: that I will not take from a thread even to a shoelatchet, and that I will not take any thing that is thine, lest thou shouldest say, I have made Abram rich:

**14:24**
Zolai: Tangvalte’ neksate le kei tawh hong kuan mite’ tanh dingte lobuang bangmah ka la kei ding hi. Aner, Eshkol, le Mamre-te amau’ tanh ding pia in,” a ci hi.
English: save only that which the young men have eaten, and the portion of the men which went with me, Aner, Eshcol, and Mamre; let them take their portion.

## Chapter 15

**15:1**
Zolai: Hih thute khit ciangin mang sungah Topa’ thu Abram’ tungah hong tung a, “Abram aw, lau kei in. Keimah in lauhuaina panin nang ka hong hu ding a, na thaman lian mahmah ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: After these things the word of the LORD came unto Abram in a vision, saying, Fear not, Abram: I am thy shield, and thy exceeding great reward.

**15:2**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Abram in, “ Topa Pasian aw, bang hong pia ding na hi hiam? Ta nei loin ka omlai hi. Ka inn a luah ding pa pen Damaskas mi Eliezer ahi hi.
English: And Abram said, Lord GOD , what wilt thou give me, seeing I go childless, and the steward of my house is this Eliezer of Damascus?

**15:3**
Zolai: Ta nong pia kei a, ka inn sunga a suak sila in keima gamh a luah ding hi ta hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Abram said, Behold, to me thou hast given no seed: and, lo, one born in my house is mine heir.

**15:4**
Zolai: Tua ciangin ama tungah Topa’ thu hong tung a, “Hih mipa pen nangma gamhluah pa hi lo ding hi. Nangma tapa mahmah na gamhluah pa hi ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And, behold, the word of the LORD came unto him, saying, This shall not be thine heir; but he that shall come forth out of thine own bowels shall be thine heir.

**15:5**
Zolai: Amah in a pualamah paipih a, “Vantung lam enin aksite sim in; na sim thei hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Na suanlekhakte, tua mah bang ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he brought him forth abroad, and said, Look now toward heaven, and tell the stars, if thou be able to number them: and he said unto him, So shall thy seed be.

**15:6**
Zolai: Amah in Topa muang hi. Tua ahih manin ahi ding bangin Abram gamta hi, ci-in Topa in a ciamteh hi.
English: And he believed in the LORD ; and he counted it to him for righteousness.

**15:7**
Zolai: Tua ciangin ama kiangah, “Hih leitang na neih nadingin nangma tungah a hong pia dingin Khaldea gam Ur khua panin a hong paikhiatpih pa pen keimah na Topa ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said unto him, I am the LORD that brought thee out of Ur of the Chaldees, to give thee this land to inherit it.

**15:8**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah in, “Topa Pasian aw, keimah in tua leitang ka neih nading bangci theih ding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Lord GOD , whereby shall I know that I shall inherit it?

**15:9**
Zolai: Amah in, “Kum thum a pha bawngla khat, kum thum a pha keelnu khat, kum thum a pha tuutal khat, vakhu khat le kawl vakhu khanglai khat hong paipih in,” a ci hi.
English: And he said unto him, Take me an heifer of three years old, and a she goat of three years old, and a ram of three years old, and a turtledove, and a young pigeon.

**15:10**
Zolai: Amah in Pasian kiangah hihte khempeuh paipih a, tuate phel nih ciat suahin, phel khat pen a phel dang khat tungah a koih ciat hi. Ahih hangin vasate phelnih suah lo hi.
English: And he took unto him all these, and divided them in the midst, and laid each piece one against another: but the birds divided he not.

**15:11**
Zolai: Sasialne vasate tua sate tungah hong tuk suk ciangin Abram in tuate a hawlkhia hi.
English: And when the fowls came down upon the carcases, Abram drove them away.

**15:12**
Zolai: Ni a tum ciangin Abram a ihmut nak suah mahmah a, khua mial bekbak a, lau mahmah hi.
English: And when the sun was going down, a deep sleep fell upon Abram; and, lo, an horror of great darkness fell upon him.

**15:13**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa in Abram kiangah, “Na suanlekhakte amau’ leitang ahi lo munah tawlkhat sung omin, tua lai-ah amaute sila hi ding uh a, amaute kum zali sung kinengniam ding ahihna thu a kitel theihna thei in.
English: And he said unto Abram, Know of a surety that thy seed shall be a stranger in a land that is not their's, and shall serve them; and they shall afflict them four hundred years;

**15:14**
Zolai: Ahi zongin na a sepsak uh minamte’ tungah thukhenna ka tungsak ding a, tua khit ciangin neihsa tampi tawh amaute paikhia ding uh hi.
English: and also that nation, whom they shall serve, will I judge: and afterward shall they come out with great substance.

**15:15**
Zolai: Nang na hih leh, nuamtakin na pu na pate kiang na zuan ding a, khan kicingin hong kivui ding hi.
English: And thou shalt go to thy fathers in peace; thou shalt be buried in a good old age.

**15:16**
Zolai: Khang lina ciangin hih lai munah amaute hong paikik ding uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Amor mite’ mawhna kicing nai lo hi,” a ci hi.
English: But in the fourth generation they shall come hither again: for the iniquity of the Amorites is not yet full.

**15:17**
Zolai: Ni tumin khua a mial khit ciangin, en in, hih sate kikalah mei beel khu le a kuang meivak a pai hi.
English: And it came to pass, that, when the sun went down, and it was dark, behold a smoking furnace, and a burning lamp that passed between those pieces.

**15:18**
Zolai: Tua ni-in Topa in Abram tawh thuciamna khat bawl a, “Na suanlekhakte tungah hih leitang, Egypt gun panin a lian gunpi ahi Eufratis gun ciang dong,
English: In the same day the LORD made a covenant with Abram, saying, Unto thy seed have I given this land, from the river of Egypt unto the great river, the river Euphrates:

**15:19**
Zolai: Ken mite, Kenaz mite, Kadmon mite,
English: the Kenites, and the Kenizzites, and the Kadmonites,

**15:20**
Zolai: Hit mite, Perez mite, Refaim mite,
English: and the Hittites, and the Perizzites, and the Rephaims,

**15:21**
Zolai: Amor mite, Kanaan mite, Girgash mite, le Jebus mite’ leitang ka hong pia hi,” a ci hi.
English: and the Amorites, and the Canaanites, and the Girgashites, and the Jebusites.

## Chapter 16

**16:1**
Zolai: Tua hunin Abram’ zi Sarai in ta nei nai lo hi. Amah in Hagar min nei Egypt mi sila numei khat nei hi.
English: Now Sarai Abram's wife bare him no children: and she had an handmaid, an Egyptian, whose name was Hagar.

**16:2**
Zolai: Sarai in Abram’ kiangah, “Tu-in en in, Topa in ka ta neih ding hong khaktan hi. Ka sila numei’ kiangah lum in. Ama sung panin keimah in ta a nei ding ka hi kha ding hi,” a ci hi. Abram in Sarai’ thu mang hi.
English: And Sarai said unto Abram, Behold now, the LORD hath restrained me from bearing: I pray thee, go in unto my maid; it may be that I may obtain children by her. And Abram hearkened to the voice of Sarai.

**16:3**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin, Kanaan leitangah Abram kum sawm a ten khit ciangin Abram’ zi Sarai in Egypt mi a sila numei Hagar la-in a pasal Abram’ tungah zi-in a pia hi.
English: And Sarai Abram's wife took Hagar her maid the Egyptian, after Abram had dwelt ten years in the land of Canaan, and gave her to her husband Abram to be his wife.

**16:4**
Zolai: Amah in Hagar luppih a, Hagar gai hi. Amah a gai lam a kitheih ciangin kiphasakin a tonu simmawh bawl hi.
English: And he went in unto Hagar, and she conceived: and when she saw that she had conceived, her mistress was despised in her eyes.

**16:5**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Sarai in Abram’ kiangah, “Keima tungah a man lo a hong kibawlna nangma tungah hong tung ta hen! Nangma kawi dingin ka sila numei kong pia a, amah a gai khitna a kitheih ciangin kei hong simmawh bawl hi. Topa in nang le kei’ kikalah thu hong khen ta hen,” a ci hi.
English: And Sarai said unto Abram, My wrong be upon thee: I have given my maid into thy bosom; and when she saw that she had conceived, I was despised in her eyes: the LORD judge between me and thee.

**16:6**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Abram in Sarai’ kiangah, “En in, na sila numei, nangma khut sungah om hi. Na ut bangin ama tungah bawl in,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Sarai in amah gawt bawl a, Hagar zong a taikhia hi.
English: But Abram said unto Sarai, Behold, thy maid is in thy hand; do to her as it pleaseth thee. And when Sarai dealt hardly with her, she fled from her face.

**16:7**
Zolai: Topa’ vantungmi in Shur paina lampi-a cik ahi, sehnel gam a ciktui gei khatah amah a mu hi.
English: And the angel of the LORD found her by a fountain of water in the wilderness, by the fountain in the way to Shur.

**16:8**
Zolai: Amah in, “Sarai’ sila numei Hagar aw, koi pan hong pai a, koi-ah pai ding na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah in, “Ka tonu Sarai’ kiang panin a taikhia ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Hagar, Sarai's maid, whence camest thou? and whither wilt thou go? And she said, I flee from the face of my mistress Sarai.

**16:9**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa’ vantungmi in ama kiangah, “Na tonu’ kiangah ciahkik inla, ama tungah ki-ap in,” a ci hi.
English: And the angel of the LORD said unto her, Return to thy mistress, and submit thyself under her hands.

**16:10**
Zolai: Topa’ vantungmi in ama kiangah, “Na suanlekhakte nakpitakin tamsak ding ka hih manin amaute kisim zo lo ding hi,” zong ci lai hi.
English: And the angel of the LORD said unto her, I will multiply thy seed exceedingly, that it shall not be numbered for multitude.

**16:11**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa’ vantungmi in ama kiangah, “En in, nau na paii a, tapa khat na nei ding hi. Ama min Ishmael na phuak ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in nangma thuakna hong mu khin hi.
English: And the angel of the LORD said unto her, Behold, thou art with child, and shalt bear a son, and shalt call his name Ishmael; because the LORD hath heard thy affliction.

**16:12**
Zolai: Amah pen la a zual nai lo bang ding a, amah in mi khempeuh langpangin mi khempeuh in amah langpang ding hi. Ama behte khempeuh a langpangin om ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he will be a wild man; his hand will be against every man, and every man's hand against him; and he shall dwell in the presence of all his brethren.

**16:13**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin ama tungah thu a gen Topa pen, “Nang, a mu thei Pasian khat na hi hi,” a ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in, “Keimah in Pasian mu khin taktakin, amah ka muh khit ciangin hing lai hi lo ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And she called the name of the LORD that spake unto her, Thou God seest me: for she said, Have I also here looked after him that seeth me?

**16:14**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tua tuikhuk pen Beerlahairoi kici a, Kadesh le Bered kikalah om hi.
English: Wherefore the well was called Beer-lahai-roi; behold, it is between Kadesh and Bered.

**16:15**
Zolai: Hagar in Abram tawh tapa khat nei hi. Abram in Hagar’ sung panin a suak ama tapa’ min dingin Ishmael a phuak hi.
English: And Hagar bare Abram a son: and Abram called his son's name, which Hagar bare, Ishmael.

**16:16**
Zolai: Hagar in Abram tawh a neih Ishmael a suah ciangin Abram kum sawmgiat le guk a pha ta hi.
English: And Abram was fourscore and six years old, when Hagar bare Ishmael to Abram.

## Chapter 17

**17:1**
Zolai: Abram kum sawmkua le kua a phak ciangin ama tungah Topa kilang a, “Kei, Vanglian Pasian ka hi hi. Hoihtakin gamta inla, paubaang kei in.
English: And when Abram was ninety years old and nine, the LORD appeared to Abram, and said unto him, I am the Almighty God; walk before me, and be thou perfect.

**17:2**
Zolai: Nang tawh thuciamna ka bawl ding a, nang tampi tak kong phasak ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And I will make my covenant between me and thee, and will multiply thee exceedingly.

**17:3**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abram mai kunsuk hi. Pasian in ama kiangah,
English: And Abram fell on his face: and God talked with him, saying,

**17:4**
Zolai: “En in, nang tungah hih thuciamna kong bawl hi: Nang pen minam honpite’ pa na hi ding hi.
English: As for me, behold, my covenant is with thee, and thou shalt be a father of many nations.

**17:5**
Zolai: Na min Abram hi nawn lo ding a, Abraham hi ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh minam honpite’ pa-in nang kong bawl khin hi.
English: Neither shall thy name any more be called Abram, but thy name shall be Abraham; for a father of many nations have I made thee.

**17:6**
Zolai: Keimah in suanlekhak tampi kong neisak ding hi. Nang sung panin minamte ka piangsak ding a, nang sung panin kumpite hong piangkhia ding hi.
English: And I will make thee exceeding fruitful, and I will make nations of thee, and kings shall come out of thee.

**17:7**
Zolai: “Nang le nang’ khit cianga na suanlekhakte tungah Pasian hihna ding tawntung thuciam nadingin kei le nang’ khit cianga na suanlekhakte’ tungah amau’ khang tawntungin ka thuciamna ka kipsak ding hi.
English: And I will establish my covenant between me and thee and thy seed after thee in their generations for an everlasting covenant, to be a God unto thee, and to thy seed after thee.

**17:8**
Zolai: Nangma tung le nang’ khit cianga na suanlekhakte tungah tawlkhat na omna Kanaan leitang khempeuh na neih tawntung dingun kong pia ding a, kei pen amaute’ Pasian ka hi ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And I will give unto thee, and to thy seed after thee, the land wherein thou art a stranger, all the land of Canaan, for an everlasting possession; and I will be their God.

**17:9**
Zolai: Pasian in Abraham’ kiangah, “Nang le nang’ khit cianga na suanlekhakte in zong ka thuciamna na zuih ding uh nong thukim ding uh ahi hi.
English: And God said unto Abraham, Thou shalt keep my covenant therefore, thou, and thy seed after thee in their generations.

**17:10**
Zolai: Hih pen nang le nang’ khit cianga na suanlekhakte’ zuih ding keima thuciamna ahi hi: Note’ lak panin pasal peuhmah a vun ki-at ding hi.
English: This is my covenant, which ye shall keep, between me and you and thy seed after thee; Every man child among you shall be circumcised.

**17:11**
Zolai: Note’ vun dawn ki-at ding a, tua pen kei le note’ kikalah thuciamna lim khat hi ding hi.
English: And ye shall circumcise the flesh of your foreskin; and it shall be a token of the covenant betwixt me and you.

**17:12**
Zolai: Note’ lak panin ni giat a pha peuhmah pa a vun ki-at ding hi. Note’ khang tawntungin pasal peuhmah, note’ inn sunga suak hitaleh, note’ ta ahi lo, gamdang mi khatpeuh kiang panin na sum uh tawh na lei uh hitaleh
English: And he that is eight days old shall be circumcised among you, every man child in your generations, he that is born in the house, or bought with money of any stranger, which is not of thy seed.

**17:13**
Zolai: na inn sunga suak hitaleh, na sum tawh a kileipa hitaleh a vun ki-at tuak ding hi. Tua ahih ciangin tawntung thuciamna ahi keima thuciamna pen nomau’ satak sungah om ding hi.
English: He that is born in thy house, and he that is bought with thy money, must needs be circumcised: and my covenant shall be in your flesh for an everlasting covenant.

**17:14**
Zolai: A vun dawn a ki-at lo pasal peuhmah a mipihte kiang panin kihawlkhia ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in keima thuciamna palsat hi,” a ci hi.
English: And the uncircumcised man child whose flesh of his foreskin is not circumcised, that soul shall be cut off from his people; he hath broken my covenant.

**17:15**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Pasian in Abraham’ kiangah, “Na zi Sarai ahihleh, ama min Sarai na ci nawn kei ding a, ama min Sarah hi ding hi.
English: And God said unto Abraham, As for Sarai thy wife, thou shalt not call her name Sarai, but Sarah shall her name be .

**17:16**
Zolai: Amah thupha ka pia ding a, amah tawh tapa khat kong pia ding hi. Amah thupha ka pia ding a, amah, minamte’ nu hi ding hi. Mihingte’ kumpite ama sung pan hong piangkhia ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And I will bless her, and give thee a son also of her: yea, I will bless her, and she shall be a mother of nations; kings of people shall be of her.

**17:17**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abraham mai kun sukin nui a, amahmah tungah, “Kum za a pha pasal khat in ta nei ding ahi hiam? Kum sawmkua a pha Sarah in ta nei ding ahi hiam?” kici hi.
English: Then Abraham fell upon his face, and laughed, and said in his heart, Shall a child be born unto him that is an hundred years old? and shall Sarah, that is ninety years old, bear?

**17:18**
Zolai: Abraham in Pasian’ kiangah, “Ishmael hong nungtasak peuh lecin,” a ci hi.
English: And Abraham said unto God, O that Ishmael might live before thee!

**17:19**
Zolai: Pasian in, “Hi lo hi. Na zi Sarah in nang a dingin tapa khat nei ding a, ama min Isaac na phuak ding hi. Ama khit cianga a suanlekhakte a dingin tawntung thuciam nadingin ka thuciamna amah tawh ka kipsak ding hi.
English: And God said, Sarah thy wife shall bear thee a son indeed; and thou shalt call his name Isaac: and I will establish my covenant with him for an everlasting covenant, and with his seed after him.

**17:20**
Zolai: Ishmael a’ ding na ngetna ahihleh ka za khin hi. En in, amah thupha pia-in ka pungsak ding a, tampi tak ka phasak ding hi. Amah pen ulian sawm le nihte’ pa hi ding a, minam lian khatin ka bawl ding hi.
English: And as for Ishmael, I have heard thee: Behold, I have blessed him, and will make him fruitful, and will multiply him exceedingly; twelve princes shall he beget, and I will make him a great nation.

**17:21**
Zolai: Ahih hangin, kumkik tuhun ciangin Sarah’ sung panin nang a’ dinga hong suak ding Isaac tawh ka thuciamna ka kipsak ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: But my covenant will I establish with Isaac, which Sarah shall bear unto thee at this set time in the next year.

**17:22**
Zolai: Amah tawh a kiho a man khit ciangin Abraham’ kiang panin Pasian paikhia to hi.
English: And he left off talking with him, and God went up from Abraham.

**17:23**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abraham in a tapa Ishmael le ama sum tawh a lei hitaleh ama inn sunga suak hitaleh a sila, ama inn sunga om mite’ lak panin pasal khempeuh samin, Pasian in ama tunga a gensa bangin tua ni mahmahin amaute’ vun dawn a atsak hi.
English: And Abraham took Ishmael his son, and all that were born in his house, and all that were bought with his money, every male among the men of Abraham's house; and circumcised the flesh of their foreskin in the selfsame day, as God had said unto him.

**17:24**
Zolai: Ama vun dawn a ki-atin Abraham kum sawmkua le kua pha ta hi.
English: And Abraham was ninety years old and nine, when he was circumcised in the flesh of his foreskin.

**17:25**
Zolai: Ama vun dawn a ki-atin a tapa Ishmael kum sawm le thum a pha hi.
English: And Ishmael his son was thirteen years old, when he was circumcised in the flesh of his foreskin.

**17:26**
Zolai: Tua ni mahmahin Abraham le a tapa Ishmael a vun uh ki-at hi.
English: In the selfsame day was Abraham circumcised, and Ishmael his son.

**17:27**
Zolai: Ama inn sunga pasal khempeuh, inn sunga suak hitaleh gamdang mite’ tung panin sum tawh a kilei mite hitaleh, amah tawh a vun uh ki-at khawm hi.
English: And all the men of his house, born in the house, and bought with money of the stranger, were circumcised with him.

## Chapter 18

**18:1**
Zolai: Mamre tawsaw gei-a Abraham a omna-ah Topa hong kilang hi. Abraham a puanbuk kong gei-ah sun nisat laitakin tu-in a om laitakin
English: And the LORD appeared unto him in the plains of Mamre: and he sat in the tent door in the heat of the day;

**18:2**
Zolai: a khuadaktoh leh, ama mai-ah mi thum na ding hi. Amah in amaute a muh ciangin amaute a dawn dingin puanbuk kong panin va tai a, leilakah kunsukin,
English: and he lift up his eyes and looked, and, lo, three men stood by him: and when he saw them , he ran to meet them from the tent door, and bowed himself toward the ground,

**18:3**
Zolai: “Ka tote aw, nong hehpihna-un na sempa hong kheng kei un.
English: and said, My Lord, if now I have found favour in thy sight, pass not away, I pray thee, from thy servant:

**18:4**
Zolai: Na nasempa’ kiang hong tung khin na hih khit buangun na thahat kik nadingun an tawmkhat ka va lak kikal sungin tui tawmkhat lasakin na khe uh sil unla, sing nuai-ah khawl un; tua khit ciangin paisuak un,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amaute in, “Na cih bangin hong hih in,” a ci uh hi.
English: let a little water, I pray you, be fetched, and wash your feet, and rest yourselves under the tree:

**18:6**
Zolai: Tua ciangin puanbuk sunga Sarah kiangah Abraham pai mengmeng a, “Annel hoihte lawh thum hong bawl mengmeng inla, meek manin mohin hong bawl in,” a ci hi.
English: And Abraham hastened into the tent unto Sarah, and said, Make ready quickly three measures of fine meal, knead it , and make cakes upon the hearth.

**18:7**
Zolai: Abraham zong bawnghon lakah tai-in bawngno a dawng a hoih khat la a, manlang taka a na bawlpah a nasempa tungah a pia hi.
English: And Abraham ran unto the herd, and fetcht a calf tender and good, and gave it unto a young man; and he hasted to dress it.

**18:8**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in, bawngnawi-thaukhal, bawngnawi, le a minsa bawngsa la-in amau’ mai-ah a lui hi. Amaute in a nek laitakun sing nuai-ah amau’ kiangah amah a ding hi.
English: And he took butter, and milk, and the calf which he had dressed, and set it before them; and he stood by them under the tree, and they did eat.

**18:9**
Zolai: Amaute in ama kiangah, “Na zi Sarah koi-ah om ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Amah in, “Puanbuk sungah om hi,” a ci hi.
English: And they said unto him, Where is Sarah thy wife? And he said, Behold, in the tent.

**18:10**
Zolai: Amaute khat in, “Tuzawh kha kua khit ciangin kong paikik taktak ding a, na zi Sarah in tapa khat nei ding hi,” a ci hi. Sarah in ama nung puanbuk kongah na ngai hi.
English: And he said, I will certainly return unto thee according to the time of life; and, lo, Sarah thy wife shall have a son. And Sarah heard it in the tent door, which was behind him.

**18:11**
Zolai: Tu-in Abraham le Sarah teek ta uh a, a kum uh ham hi. Sarah a numei ngeina teng tawpta hi.
English: Now Abraham and Sarah were old and well stricken in age; and it ceased to be with Sarah after the manner of women.

**18:12**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Sarah amahmah nui-in, “Kei ka teek khit, ka topa zong a teek khitin tua bang hi thei nawn ding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: Therefore Sarah laughed within herself, saying, After I am waxed old shall I have pleasure, my lord being old also?

**18:13**
Zolai: Topa in Abraham’ tungah, “Bang hangin Sarah nui-in, ‘Tu-in kei teek ka hih ciangin ta nei takpi ding ka hi hiam?’ ci ahi hiam?
English: And the LORD said unto Abraham, Wherefore did Sarah laugh, saying, Shall I of a surety bear a child, which am old?

**18:14**
Zolai: Na khat peuhpeuh Topa a dingin haksa lua ahi hiam? A kisehsa tuzawh kha kua ciangin nang kiangah kong paikik ding a, Sarah in tapa khat nei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: Is any thing too hard for the LORD ? At the time appointed I will return unto thee, according to the time of life, and Sarah shall have a son.

**18:15**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Sarah in nialin, “Ka nui kei hi,” ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah lau hi. Amah in, “Hi lo hi, na nui mah hi,” a ci hi.
English: Then Sarah denied, saying, I laughed not; for she was afraid. And he said, Nay; but thou didst laugh.

**18:16**
Zolai: Tua ciangin tua mun panin mite paikhia a, amaute in Sodom lam en uh hi. Amau’ pai nading lampi-ah a kha dingin Abraham in amaute va zui hi.
English: And the men rose up from thence, and looked toward Sodom: and Abraham went with them to bring them on the way.

**18:17**
Zolai: Topa in a lungsimah, “Abraham a lian a thahat minam suakin, leitung minam khempeuh in ama thupha ngah bangin thupha a ngah nadingun hong ngen ding hi, ci-in thei ahih manin, tu-a ka hih ding thu Abraham’ tungah im ding ka hi hiam?
English: And the LORD said, Shall I hide from Abraham that thing which I do;

**18:19**
Zolai: Im kei ning. Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in Abraham’ tunga a ciamsa thu a tunsak theih nadingin ama khita a tate le a innkuanpihte in thuman le thutangin nasepna tawh Topa’ thupiakte a zuih theih nadingun a hilh dingin amah ka teel khin hi,” a ci hi.
English: For I know him, that he will command his children and his household after him, and they shall keep the way of the LORD , to do justice and judgment; that the LORD may bring upon Abraham that which he hath spoken of him.

**18:20**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa in, “Sodom le Gomorrah a kimawhsakna lianin, amaute’ khialhna nasia mahmah kici ahih manin,
English: And the LORD said, Because the cry of Sodom and Gomorrah is great, and because their sin is very grievous;

**18:21**
Zolai: kei tunga hong kigen bangin amaute gamta takpi uh hiam, ci-in a thei dingin ka paisuk ding hi. Tua bang ahih kei leh zong ke’n ka va thei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: I will go down now, and see whether they have done altogether according to the cry of it, which is come unto me; and if not, I will know.

**18:22**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tua panin mite kihei-in Sodom lamah pai uh a, ahi zongin Topa’ mai-ah Abraham ding lai hi.
English: And the men turned their faces from thence, and went toward Sodom: but Abraham stood yet before the LORD .

**18:23**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abraham in hong naihin, “Thuman mite, migilote tawh susia khawm takpi ding na hi hiam?
English: And Abraham drew near, and said, Wilt thou also destroy the righteous with the wicked?

**18:24**
Zolai: Tua khuapi sungah thuman mi sawmnga bang om leh, tua sunga om thuman mi sawmngate’ hangin khah loin tua khua susia teitei ding na hi hiam?
English: Peradventure there be fifty righteous within the city: wilt thou also destroy and not spare the place for the fifty righteous that are therein?

**18:25**
Zolai: Thuman mite, migilote tawh a kibat nadingin migilote tawh thuman mite thahkhawm ding, hi thei ding ahi hiam? Tua pen hi thei lo ding hi. Leitung khempeuh Thukhen pa a manin gamta lo ding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: That be far from thee to do after this manner, to slay the righteous with the wicked: and that the righteous should be as the wicked, that be far from thee: Shall not the Judge of all the earth do right?

**18:26**
Zolai: Topa in, “Sodom khuapi sungah thuman mi sawmnga ka muh leh, amaute’ hangin tua khua buppi ka khah ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And the LORD said, If I find in Sodom fifty righteous within the city, then I will spare all the place for their sakes.

**18:27**
Zolai: Abraham in thu gen leuleu a, “En in, leivui le vut bang ahi lel keimah in Topa’ tungah thu kong gen ngamna hong maisak in.
English: And Abraham answered and said, Behold now, I have taken upon me to speak unto the Lord, which am but dust and ashes:

**18:28**
Zolai: Thuman mi sawmnga sung panin nga om kei leh? Tua nga a om loh manin khuapi buppi na susia veve ding hiam?” a ci hi. Amah in, “Tua sungah sawmli le nga ka muh nakleh ka susia kei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: peradventure there shall lack five of the fifty righteous: wilt thou destroy all the city for lack of five? And he said, If I find there forty and five, I will not destroy it .

**18:29**
Zolai: Ama kiangah thu gen kikin, “Tua sungah sawmli bang kimu leh,” a ci hi. Amah in dawngin, “Sawmlite’ hangin ka hih kei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he spake unto him yet again, and said, Peradventure there shall be forty found there. And he said, I will not do it for forty's sake.

**18:30**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in, “Topa heh kei in, thu kong gen lai ding hi. Tua lai-ah sawmthum bang kimu leh,” ci hi. Amah in dawngin, “Sawmthum ka muh leh ka hih kei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said unto him , Oh let not the Lord be angry, and I will speak: Peradventure there shall thirty be found there. And he said, I will not do it , if I find thirty there.

**18:31**
Zolai: Amah in, “En in, Topa tungah thu kong gen ngam lailaina hong maisak in. Tua lai-ah sawmnih bang kimu leh,” a ci hi. Amah in dawngin, “Sawmnihte’ hangin ka susia kei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Behold now, I have taken upon me to speak unto the Lord: Peradventure there shall be twenty found there. And he said, I will not destroy it for twenty's sake.

**18:32**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in, “Topa heh kei in, hih khatvei bek thu hong gensak lai in. Tua lai-ah sawm bang kimu leh,” a ci hi. Amah in dawngin, “Sawmte’ hangin ka susia kei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Oh let not the Lord be angry, and I will speak yet but this once: Peradventure ten shall be found there. And he said, I will not destroy it for ten's sake.

**18:33**
Zolai: Abraham’ tungah a thugen ding a man khit ciangin ama pai nadingah Topa pai a, Abraham zong ama inn-ah a ciahkik hi.
English: And the LORD went his way, as soon as he had left communing with Abraham: and Abraham returned unto his place.

## Chapter 19

**19:1**
Zolai: Vantung mi nihte Sodom ah nitakin hong tung a, Sodom khua kulhkongpi-ah Lot na tu hi. Lot in amaute a muh ciangin, amaute a dawn dingin ding a, leilakah a mai ngatin kun a,
English: And there came two angels to Sodom at even; and Lot sat in the gate of Sodom: and Lot seeing them rose up to meet them; and he bowed himself with his face toward the ground;

**19:2**
Zolai: “Ka tote aw, kong thum hi. Na nasempa’ inn lamah hong kihei-in hong giak unla, na khete uh sil un. Tua ciangin zingsangin tho baihin na pai nading lam uhah pai pan un,” a ci hi. Amaute in, “Hi lo hi; khua lakah ka giak ding uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: and he said, Behold now, my lords, turn in, I pray you, into your servant's house, and tarry all night, and wash your feet, and ye shall rise up early, and go on your ways. And they said, Nay; but we will abide in the street all night.

**19:3**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah in amaute nakpitakin kun ahih manin ama lamah kihei uh a, ama inn-ah a lut uh hi. Amah in amaute a dingin an bawl a, silngo sawh loh anlum emsak a, amaute in a ne uh hi.
English: And he pressed upon them greatly; and they turned in unto him, and entered into his house; and he made them a feast, and did bake unleavened bread, and they did eat.

**19:4**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amaute’ lup ma-in Sodom khua mite, a moi a hamin mi khempeuh in a inn umcih uh hi.
English: But before they lay down, the men of the city, even the men of Sodom, compassed the house round, both old and young, all the people from every quarter:

**19:5**
Zolai: Amaute in Lot sam uh a, “Tu nitak a nang kiangah hong tung mite koi-ah om ahi hiam? Amau’ taw ka luk theih nadingun ko kiangah amaute hong paikhiatpih in,” a ci uh hi.
English: and they called unto Lot, and said unto him, Where are the men which came in to thee this night? bring them out unto us, that we may know them.

**19:6**
Zolai: Lot, kongkhak pua-ah mite kiangah pai-in kong lehkhak a,
English: And Lot went out at the door unto them, and shut the door after him,

**19:7**
Zolai: “Ka sanggamte aw, tua banga na gitloh gamtat loh nading uh kong thum hi.
English: and said, I pray you, brethren, do not so wickedly.

**19:8**
Zolai: En un, ta nungak nih ka nei hi. No kiangah amaute hong paikhiatpihsak unla, na ut bangun amaute tungah gamta un. Hih mite’ tungah bangmah gamta kei bek un. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute, keima innsung hong tungkhin uh ahih manin ka hut ding kisam hi,” a ci hi.
English: Behold now, I have two daughters which have not known man; let me, I pray you, bring them out unto you, and do ye to them as is good in your eyes: only unto these men do nothing; for therefore came they under the shadow of my roof.

**19:9**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amaute in, “Taikhia in. Kote kiangah hong peem pak a, tu-in nang thukhen hong kineih ding na hi hiam? Tu-in amaute sangin nang kong siatbawl zaw ding uh hi,” a ci uh hi. Tua ciangin amaute in nakpitakin Lot’ lam hong neh uh a, kongkhak a phukham zah dongin hong neh uh hi.
English: And they said, Stand back. And they said again , This one fellow came in to sojourn, and he will needs be a judge: now will we deal worse with thee, than with them. And they pressed sore upon the man, even Lot, and came near to break the door.

**19:10**
Zolai: Ahih hangin mi nihte in amau’ khut hong zanin innsung amau’ kiangah Lot paipihin kong khak uh hi.
English: But the men put forth their hand, and pulled Lot into the house to them, and shut to the door.

**19:11**
Zolai: Inn kongkhakah a om mi a lian a neute, amaute in a mit uh tawsak uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin kongkhak a zawtzawt hangun mu zo lo uh hi.
English: And they smote the men that were at the door of the house with blindness, both small and great: so that they wearied themselves to find the door.

**19:12**
Zolai: Tua ciangin mi nihte in Lot kiangah, “Hih lai-ah tanau dang na nei hiam? Makte, tapate, ahih kei leh khua sunga nang’ mi peuhpeuh hih mun panin paikhiatpih in.
English: And the men said unto Lot, Hast thou here any besides? son in law, and thy sons, and thy daughters, and whatsoever thou hast in the city, bring them out of this place:

**19:13**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh hih mite a kimawhsakna thu Topa’ tungah tung khin a, a susia dingin Topa in hong sawl khin ahih ciangin hih khua a susia ta ding ka hi uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: for we will destroy this place, because the cry of them is waxen great before the face of the LORD ; and the LORD hath sent us to destroy it.

**19:14**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Lot paikhia-in a tanute a tenpih dingte kiangah, “Manlangin hih khua panin paikhia un. Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in hih khuapi a susia ding hi ta hi,” a ci hi. Ahih hangin amah pen a mak dingte tungah a ciamnui bang lel hi.
English: And Lot went out, and spake unto his sons in law, which married his daughters, and said, Up, get you out of this place; for the LORD will destroy this city. But he seemed as one that mocked unto his sons in law.

**19:15**
Zolai: Zingsang khuavak ciangin vantung mite in, “Khuapi gimpiakna sungah kangtum kha ding na hih uh ciangin kinawh inla, hih lai-a om na zi le na tanute la in,” ci-in Lot sawl hamtang uh hi.
English: And when the morning arose, then the angels hastened Lot, saying, Arise, take thy wife, and thy two daughters, which are here; lest thou be consumed in the iniquity of the city.

**19:16**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah lungka-in omlai veve hi. Ahi zongin Topa in ama tungah hehpihna nei ahih manin, mite in amah le a zi le a tanu nihte a khut uh tawh manin, amaute in amah paikhiatpihin khua pualamah koih uh hi.
English: And while he lingered, the men laid hold upon his hand, and upon the hand of his wife, and upon the hand of his two daughters; the LORD being merciful unto him: and they brought him forth, and set him without the city.

**19:17**
Zolai: Amaute in a paikhiatpih khit uh ciangin, “Na nuntak nadingun tai un. Nunghei kei unla, kuam sungah zong khawl kei un. Note hong kangtum kha ding ahih manin mualtungah taito un,” a ci uh hi.
English: And it came to pass, when they had brought them forth abroad, that he said, Escape for thy life; look not behind thee, neither stay thou in all the plain; escape to the mountain, lest thou be consumed.

**19:18**
Zolai: Ahi zongin Lot in amaute tungah, “Hi lo hi, ka tote aw;
English: And Lot said unto them, Oh, not so, my Lord:

**19:19**
Zolai: en un, note’ muhna-ah na nasempa in maipha muzo a, ka nuntakna nong hutna uhah migitna lianpi kei tungah nong lak khin uh hi. Ahih hangin mualtung gamla ahih manin ka tun ma-in siatna in kei hong pha-in ka si ding hi.
English: behold now, thy servant hath found grace in thy sight, and thou hast magnified thy mercy, which thou hast shewed unto me in saving my life; and I cannot escape to the mountain, lest some evil take me, and I die:

**19:20**
Zolai: En un, gal-a om khuapi, tai nadingin nai a, khuapi neu khat ahi hi. Tua lai-ah hong taisak un - khuapi neu khat hi lo ahi hiam? tua hileh ka suakta ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: behold now, this city is near to flee unto, and it is a little one: Oh, let me escape thither, (is it not a little one?) and my soul shall live.

**19:21**
Zolai: Amah in ama kiangah, “En in, na gensa khuapi ka lumlet loh nading, hih maipha zong nang kong pia hi.
English: And he said unto him, See, I have accepted thee concerning this thing also, that I will not overthrow this city, for the which thou hast spoken.

**19:22**
Zolai: Kinawh inla, tua lai-ah tai in. Bang hang hiam cih leh tua lai-ah nang na tun mateng ke’n bangmah ka hih thei kei hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin tua khuapi min Zoar kici hi.
English: Haste thee, escape thither; for I cannot do any thing till thou be come thither. Therefore the name of the city was called Zoar.

**19:23**
Zolai: Zoar-ah Lot a tun ciangin tua lai-ah ni suak khinta hi.
English: The sun was risen upon the earth when Lot entered into Zoar.

**19:24**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa in vantung panin Sodom le Gomorrah khuate tungah kaat le meikuang zusak hi.
English: Then the LORD rained upon Sodom and upon Gomorrah brimstone and fire from the LORD out of heaven;

**19:25**
Zolai: Amah in tua khuapite, kuamte khempeuh, khuapite sunga mi tengte khempeuh le leitung a a po khempeuh a susia hi.
English: and he overthrew those cities, and all the plain, and all the inhabitants of the cities, and that which grew upon the ground.

**19:26**
Zolai: Ahih hangin a nunga om Lot’ zi nunghei a, amah ci khuam a suak hi.
English: But his wife looked back from behind him, and she became a pillar of salt.

**19:27**
Zolai: Topa’ mai-a a dinnasa munah zingsang tungin Abraham va pai hi.
English: And Abraham gat up early in the morning to the place where he stood before the LORD :

**19:28**
Zolai: Sodom le Gomorrah le kuamte khempeuh lam nga sukin khuadak a, leitang khu pen, meiphualpi khu bangin a kah to a mu hi.
English: and he looked toward Sodom and Gomorrah, and toward all the land of the plain, and beheld, and, lo, the smoke of the country went up as the smoke of a furnace.

**19:29**
Zolai: Pasian in kuam sunga khuapite a suksiat lai-in, amah in Abraham phawk a, amah in Lot’ tenna khuapite a suksiat ciangin tua bang a suksiatna sung panin Lot sawlkhia ahih manin a suakta ahi hi.
English: And it came to pass, when God destroyed the cities of the plain, that God remembered Abraham, and sent Lot out of the midst of the overthrow, when he overthrew the cities in the which Lot dwelt.

**19:30**
Zolai: Tu-in Zoar panin Lot paikhia to-in a tanu nihte tawh mualtungah a teng hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Zoar-ah a ten ding lau hi. Tua ahih ciangin a tanu nihte tawh suanghawm sung khatah a teng uh hi.
English: And Lot went up out of Zoar, and dwelt in the mountain, and his two daughters with him; for he feared to dwell in Zoar: and he dwelt in a cave, he and his two daughters.

**19:31**
Zolai: A u pen in a nau tungah, “I pa lah teek ta a, leitung ngeina bangin eite hong luppih ding pasal khat zong om lo hi.
English: And the firstborn said unto the younger, Our father is old, and there is not a man in the earth to come in unto us after the manner of all the earth:

**19:32**
Zolai: Hong pai in; i pa leenggahzu khamsak ni; i pa tawh suanlekhak i kizopsak theih nadingin amah tawh lumkhawm ni,” a ci hi.
English: come, let us make our father drink wine, and we will lie with him, that we may preserve seed of our father.

**19:33**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute in tua nitakin a pa uh leenggahzu khamsak uh hi. A unu pai-in a pa tawh lum hi. A tanu a luplam hitaleh a thawhlam hitaleh amah in phawk lo hi.
English: And they made their father drink wine that night: and the firstborn went in, and lay with her father; and he perceived not when she lay down, nor when she arose.

**19:34**
Zolai: A zing ciangin a u in a nau tungah, “En in, zan zanin i pa tawh ka lum hi. Tu nitakin zong amah leenggahzu khamsak leuleu ni. Tua ciangin nang pai inla, i pa tawh suanlekhak i kizopsak theih nadingin amah tawh lumkhawm in,” a ci hi.
English: And it came to pass on the morrow, that the firstborn said unto the younger, Behold, I lay yesternight with my father: let us make him drink wine this night also; and go thou in, and lie with him, that we may preserve seed of our father.

**19:35**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute in tua nitakin zong a pa uh leenggahzu khamsak uh hi. A nau pai-in amah tawh lum hi. A tanu a luplam hitaleh a thawhlam hitaleh amah in phawk lo hi.
English: And they made their father drink wine that night also: and the younger arose, and lay with him; and he perceived not when she lay down, nor when she arose.

**19:36**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Lot’ tanu tegel in a pa uh tawh naupaii uh hi.
English: Thus were both the daughters of Lot with child by their father.

**19:37**
Zolai: A u in tapa khat nei-in a min Moab phuak a, amah pen tuhuna Moab mite’ pianna pupi ahi hi.
English: And the firstborn bare a son, and called his name Moab: the same is the father of the Moabites unto this day.

**19:38**
Zolai: A nau in zong tapa khat nei-in a min Benammi phuak a, amah pen tu donga Ammon mite’ pianna pupi ahi hi.
English: And the younger, she also bare a son, and called his name Ben-ammi: the same is the father of the children of Ammon unto this day.

## Chapter 20

**20:1**
Zolai: Mamre panin Negeb gamah Abraham paisuk a, Kadesh le Shur kikal Gerar-ah tawlkhat sung a teng hi.
English: And Abraham journeyed from thence toward the south country, and dwelled between Kadesh and Shur, and sojourned in Gerar.

**20:2**
Zolai: Abraham in a zi Sarah pen, “Ka sanggamnu hi,” ci hi. Gerar kumpipa Abimelek in mi sawlin Sarah samsak hi.
English: And Abraham said of Sarah his wife, She is my sister: and Abimelech king of Gerar sent, and took Sarah.

**20:3**
Zolai: Ahih hangin zanin mang sungah Abimelek kiangah Pasian pai a, ama kiangah, “En in, na laksa numei’ hangin nang a si ding na hi hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah, mi khat’ zi ahi hi,” a ci hi.
English: But God came to Abimelech in a dream by night, and said to him, Behold, thou art but a dead man, for the woman which thou hast taken; for she is a man's wife.

**20:4**
Zolai: Ahi zongin Abimelek in amah zuan nai lo hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in, “Topa aw, nang in midik pa that ding na hi hiam?
English: But Abimelech had not come near her: and he said, Lord, wilt thou slay also a righteous nation?

**20:5**
Zolai: Amahmah in kei kiangah, ‘Amah, ka sanggamnu ahi hi,’ hong ci hi lo ahi hiam? A numei mahmah in zong, ‘Amah, ka sanggampa ahi hi,’ hong ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin lungsim kisuang hetloin a gamta ka hi a, khial ka kisa kei hi,” a ci hi.
English: Said he not unto me, She is my sister? and she, even she herself said, He is my brother: in the integrity of my heart and innocency of my hands have I done this.

**20:6**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Pasian in a mang sungin ama kiangah, “Hi hi, lungsim kisuanna om loin hih bangin na gamtatna thu ka thei a, kei tungah na khialh loh nadingin a hong kem pa kei mahmah ka hi hi. Tua ahih ciangin nang, amah kong lawngsak kei hi.
English: And God said unto him in a dream, Yea, I know that thou didst this in the integrity of thy heart; for I also withheld thee from sinning against me: therefore suffered I thee not to touch her.

**20:7**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tu-in mipa’ zi piakik in. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah, kamsang khat hi a, amah in nang a dingin thu hong ngetsak ding a, nang na nungta ding hi. Ahih hangin nang in tua numei na piakkik kei le nang le na mi khempeuh na sih taktak ding uh thei in,” a ci hi.
English: Now therefore restore the man his wife; for he is a prophet, and he shall pray for thee, and thou shalt live: and if thou restore her not, know thou that thou shalt surely die, thou, and all that are thine.

**20:8**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin zingsangin Abimelek tho baih a, a nasemte samin hih thute khempeuh amaute kiangah a gen hi. Amaute nak lau mahmah uh hi.
English: Therefore Abimelech rose early in the morning, and called all his servants, and told all these things in their ears: and the men were sore afraid.

**20:9**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abimelek in Abraham samin ama kiangah, “Bang hangin ko tungah hong hici gamtat na hi hiam? Kei le ka kumpi gam sungah khialhna lianpi khat nong tut nadingin nang’ tungah bang khialhna nei ka hi uh hiam? Hih dinga kilawm lo nate kei’ tungah nong hih hi,” a ci hi.
English: Then Abimelech called Abraham, and said unto him, What hast thou done unto us? and what have I offended thee, that thou hast brought on me and on my kingdom a great sin? thou hast done deeds unto me that ought not to be done.

**20:10**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abimelek in Abraham’ kiangah, “Hih banga na gamtat nadingin bang ngaihsun na hi hiam?” ci lai hi.
English: And Abimelech said unto Abraham, What sawest thou, that thou hast done this thing?

**20:11**
Zolai: Abraham in, “Hih lai munah Pasian zahtakna om het lo hi. Ka zi’ hangin amaute in kei hong that ding hi, ci-in ngaihsun kha ka hih manin hih bangin a gamta ka hi hi.
English: And Abraham said, Because I thought, Surely the fear of God is not in this place; and they will slay me for my wife's sake.

**20:12**
Zolai: Tua tham loin a taktakin amah ka sanggamnu mah ahi hi. Pa kikhat, nu tuam ka hi uh a, amah ka tenpih ahi hi.
English: And yet indeed she is my sister; she is the daughter of my father, but not the daughter of my mother; and she became my wife.

**20:13**
Zolai: Pasian in ka pa’ inn panin hong paikhiatsak ciangin ama kiangah, ‘Hih pen kei’ tunga nong hih ding na migitna ahi hi: I paina peuhpeuhah kei pen ka sanggampa hi, hong ci in,’ ka ci hi,” a ci hi.
English: And it came to pass, when God caused me to wander from my father's house, that I said unto her, This is thy kindness which thou shalt shew unto me; at every place whither we shall come, say of me, He is my brother.

**20:14**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abimelek in tuu le bawngtalte, sila numei le sila pasalte la-in Abraham pia a, ama tungah a zi Sarah a pia kik hi.
English: And Abimelech took sheep, and oxen, and menservants, and womenservants, and gave them unto Abraham, and restored him Sarah his wife.

**20:15**
Zolai: Abimelek in, “En in, ka leitang, na mai-ah om hi. Nangmah in hoih na sakna munah teng in,” a ci hi.
English: And Abimelech said, Behold, my land is before thee: dwell where it pleaseth thee.

**20:16**
Zolai: Sarah’ kiangah, “En in, na sanggampa tungah ngun tang tulkhat ka pia khin hi. Nang tawh a om mite khempeuh’ mai-ah nangma dikna a kilatna ahi hi. Mi khempeuh’ mai-ah nang a manin hong kibawl hi,” a ci hi.
English: And unto Sarah he said, Behold, I have given thy brother a thousand pieces of silver: behold, he is to thee a covering of the eyes, unto all that are with thee, and with all other: thus she was reproved.

**20:17**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abraham in Pasian’ tungah thu ngen a, Pasian in Abimelek a damsak hi. Amaute in ta a neih theih nadingin a zi le a sila numeite zong a damsak hi.
English: So Abraham prayed unto God: and God healed Abimelech, and his wife, and his maidservants; and they bare children .

**20:18**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Topa in Abraham’ zi Sarah’ hangin Abimelek’ innkuan’ naubu khempeuh khakcipsak khin hi.
English: For the LORD had fast closed up all the wombs of the house of Abimelech, because of Sarah Abraham's wife.

## Chapter 21

**21:1**
Zolai: A gensa bangin Topa in Sarah’ tungah thupha pia a, a gensa bangin Sarah’ tungah Topa in hih hi.
English: And the LORD visited Sarah as he had said, and the LORD did unto Sarah as he had spoken.

**21:2**
Zolai: Sarah gai a, ama tunga Pasian in a gensa hunin a teek zawhin Abraham tawh tapa khat nei hi.
English: For Sarah conceived, and bare Abraham a son in his old age, at the set time of which God had spoken to him.

**21:3**
Zolai: Abraham in Sarah tawh a neih ama tapa’ min dingin Isaac a phuak hi.
English: And Abraham called the name of his son that was born unto him, whom Sarah bare to him, Isaac.

**21:4**
Zolai: Pasian in ama tunga a thu piaksa bangin amah in ni giat a phak ciangin a tapa Isaac a vun a at hi.
English: And Abraham circumcised his son Isaac being eight days old, as God had commanded him.

**21:5**
Zolai: A tapa Isaac a suah ciangin Abraham kum za pha hi.
English: And Abraham was an hundred years old, when his son Isaac was born unto him.

**21:6**
Zolai: Sarah in, “Pasian in kei a dingin nuamin nuihzak nading hong bawlsak khin hi. A za peuhmah in nuamin hong nuihpih ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Sarah said, God hath made me to laugh, so that all that hear will laugh with me.

**21:7**
Zolai: Amah in, “Sarah in nau nawi pia ding ci-in kua in Abraham’ tungah gen ngei ding ahi hiam? Ahi zongin a teek khitin amah tawh tapa khat ka nei hi,” a ci hi.
English: And she said, Who would have said unto Abraham, that Sarah should have given children suck? for I have born him a son in his old age.

**21:8**
Zolai: Naupang khang a, nawi tawh hong kikhen ta hi. Isaac nawi tawh a kikhen ni ciangin Abraham in pawi lianpi khat bawl hi.
English: And the child grew, and was weaned: and Abraham made a great feast the same day that Isaac was weaned.

**21:9**
Zolai: Ahih hangin, Abraham tawh a neih Egypt mi Hagar’ tapa in ama tapa Isaac a ciamnuih bawlna Sarah in a mu hi.
English: And Sarah saw the son of Hagar the Egyptian, which she had born unto Abraham, mocking.

**21:10**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in Abraham’ kiangah, “Hih sila numei a tapa tawh lawnkhia in; bang hang hiam cih leh sila numei’ tapa in ka tapa Isaac tawh gamh luahkhawm thei lo ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: Wherefore she said unto Abraham, Cast out this bondwoman and her son: for the son of this bondwoman shall not be heir with my son, even with Isaac.

**21:11**
Zolai: Ama tapa’ hangin Abraham’ tungah thu nuam het lo hi.
English: And the thing was very grievous in Abraham's sight because of his son.

**21:12**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Pasian in Abraham’ tungah, “Tangvalpa le na sila numei’ hangin lungkim loin om kei in. Sarah in nang’ tunga hong gen peuhmah ama hong gen bangin gamta in. Bang hang hiam cih leh Isaac tawh na suanlekhakte’ min ki lo ding hi.
English: And God said unto Abraham, Let it not be grievous in thy sight because of the lad, and because of thy bondwoman; in all that Sarah hath said unto thee, hearken unto her voice; for in Isaac shall thy seed be called.

**21:13**
Zolai: Sila numei’ tapa zong nangma ta mah ahih manin, minam khatin ka bawl ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And also of the son of the bondwoman will I make a nation, because he is thy seed.

**21:14**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin zingsangin Abraham tho baihin an le tuithawl la-in Hagar pia a, ama liangko tungah naupang tawh suanin a sawlkhia hi. Amah paikhia a, Beersheba gam sungah a vak kawikawi hi.
English: And Abraham rose up early in the morning, and took bread, and a bottle of water, and gave it unto Hagar, putting it on her shoulder, and the child, and sent her away: and she departed, and wandered in the wilderness of Beer-sheba.

**21:15**
Zolai: Thawl sunga tui a bei ciangin amah in sawlbawk nuai khatah naupang lawn hi.
English: And the water was spent in the bottle, and she cast the child under one of the shrubs.

**21:16**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah pai-in a hoihkhop khat a gamla, thallot khat tan bangah a ta nungngatin a tusuk hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in, “Naupang’ sih hong musak kei in,” a ci hi. Amah nungngatin a tut laitakin naupang nakpi-in a kap hi.
English: And she went, and sat her down over against him a good way off, as it were a bowshot: for she said, Let me not see the death of the child. And she sat over against him , and lift up her voice, and wept.

**21:17**
Zolai: Pasian in naupang’ kahna aw a za hi. Pasian’ vantungmi in vantung panin Hagar sam a, ama kiangah, “Hagar aw, bang in hong lungkhamsak ahi hiam? Lau kei in. Bang hang hiam cih leh naupang a omna munah a kahna awging Pasian in za hi.
English: And God heard the voice of the lad; and the angel of God called to Hagar out of heaven, and said unto her, What aileth thee, Hagar? fear not; for God hath heard the voice of the lad where he is .

**21:18**
Zolai: Dingin naupang la inla, na khut tawh kip takin len in. Bang hang hiam cih leh minam lian khatin amah ka bawl ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: Arise, lift up the lad, and hold him in thine hand; for I will make him a great nation.

**21:19**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Pasian in ama mit haksak a, amah in tuikhuk khat a mu hi. Amah pai-in tui tawh tuithawl dimin naupang a dawnsak hi.
English: And God opened her eyes, and she saw a well of water; and she went, and filled the bottle with water, and gave the lad drink.

**21:20**
Zolai: Pasian in tua naupang ompih a, amah khangto hi. Amah gamlakah teng a, thallot siampa khat hong suak hi.
English: And God was with the lad; and he grew, and dwelt in the wilderness, and became an archer.

**21:21**
Zolai: Paran gam sungah amah teng hi. A nu in Egypt gam panin ama a’ ding zi khat a la hi.
English: And he dwelt in the wilderness of Paran: and his mother took him a wife out of the land of Egypt.

**21:22**
Zolai: Tua hun laitakin Abimelek le a galkap mangpa Fikol in Abraham’ kiangah, “Na sepna khempeuhah Pasian in nang hong ompih hi.
English: And it came to pass at that time, that Abimelech and Phichol the chief captain of his host spake unto Abraham, saying, God is with thee in all that thou doest:

**21:23**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tu-in kei hitaleh ka tate hitaleh ka suanlekhakte hitaleh tungah a man lopi-in hong bawl loin, nang tungah thuman tak tawh kong gamtat bangin keima tung le tawlkhat na omna leitang tungah nong gamtat nadingin Pasian tawh kei tungah hong kiciam in,” a ci hi.
English: now therefore swear unto me here by God that thou wilt not deal falsely with me, nor with my son, nor with my son's son: but according to the kindness that I have done unto thee, thou shalt do unto me, and to the land wherein thou hast sojourned.

**21:24**
Zolai: Abraham in, “Ka kiciam ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Abraham said, I will swear.

**21:25**
Zolai: Abimelek’ nasemte in a suhsa tuikhuk tawh kisai thu Abraham in a lungkim lohna Abimelek’ kiangah a gen ciangin,
English: And Abraham reproved Abimelech because of a well of water, which Abimelech's servants had violently taken away.

**21:26**
Zolai: Abimelek in, “Kua in hih hiam ka thei kei hi. Nang nong gen kei a, keimah in tuni dong ka za nai kei hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Abimelech said, I wot not who hath done this thing: neither didst thou tell me, neither yet heard I of it , but to day.

**21:27**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Abraham in tuu le bawngtalte la-in Abimelek pia a, tua mi nihte in thuciamna khat a bawl uh hi.
English: And Abraham took sheep and oxen, and gave them unto Abimelech; and both of them made a covenant.

**21:28**
Zolai: Abraham in a tuuhon sung panin tuununo sagih tuam koih hi.
English: And Abraham set seven ewe lambs of the flock by themselves.

**21:29**
Zolai: Abimelek in Abraham’ kiangah, “Hih na koihtuam tuununo sagihte bang a cihnopna ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Abimelech said unto Abraham, What mean these seven ewe lambs which thou hast set by themselves?

**21:30**
Zolai: Amah in, “Keimah in hih tuikhuk ka tawhna thu-ah nang in keima a dingin teci na hih theih nadingin nangmah in ka khutsung panin hih tuununo sagihte na la ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, For these seven ewe lambs shalt thou take of my hand, that they may be a witness unto me, that I have digged this well.

**21:31**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tua mun Beersheba kici hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amau tegel tua munah thu kiciam uh hi.
English: Wherefore he called that place Beer-sheba; because there they sware both of them.

**21:32**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute in Beersheba-ah thuciamna khat a bawl uh hi. Tua khit ciangin Abimelek le a galkap mangpa Fikol, Filistia mite’ leitangah ciahkik uh hi.
English: Thus they made a covenant at Beer-sheba: then Abimelech rose up, and Phichol the chief captain of his host, and they returned into the land of the Philistines.

**21:33**
Zolai: Abraham in Beersheba-ah makeng kung khat suan a, tua lai munah Tawntung Pasian, Topa a bia hi.
English: And Abraham planted a grove in Beer-sheba, and called there on the name of the LORD , the everlasting God.

**21:34**
Zolai: Filistia mite’ leitangah Abraham, sauveipi sung peemta-in a om hi.
English: And Abraham sojourned in the Philistines' land many days.

## Chapter 22

**22:1**
Zolai: Hih thute khit ciangin Pasian in Abraham ze-et a, ama kiangah, “Abraham,” a ci hi. Amah in, “Hiah om ing,” a ci hi.
English: And it came to pass after these things, that God did tempt Abraham, and said unto him, Abraham: and he said, Behold, here I am .

**22:2**
Zolai: Amah in, “Na it, na tapa neihsun Isaac, la inla Moriah gamah pai in. Tua lai mun a nang kiangah kong gen ding mual khat tungah meihal biakpiakna-in amah hong pia in,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Take now thy son, thine only son Isaac, whom thou lovest, and get thee into the land of Moriah; and offer him there for a burnt offering upon one of the mountains which I will tell thee of.

**22:3**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin zingsangin Abraham tho baih a, a la tutphah vawhin, ama nasem tangval nih le a tapa Isaac a paipih hi. Amah in meihal biakpiak nadingin sing ek a, ama tunga Pasian’ gensa munah a pai hi.
English: And Abraham rose up early in the morning, and saddled his ass, and took two of his young men with him, and Isaac his son, and clave the wood for the burnt offering, and rose up, and went unto the place of which God had told him.

**22:4**
Zolai: A ni thum ni ciangin Abraham khuadak to-in a gamla-ah tua mun a mu hi.
English: Then on the third day Abraham lifted up his eyes, and saw the place afar off.

**22:5**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abraham in a nasemte kiangah, “Hih lai-ah la tawh na om un. Kei le tangvalpa hua lamah pai-in Pasian ka va bia ding uh a, note kiangah ka hong paikik ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Abraham said unto his young men, Abide ye here with the ass; and I and the lad will go yonder and worship, and come again to you.

**22:6**
Zolai: Abraham in meihal biak nading sing la-in a tapa Isaac’ tungah suan a, amah in a khut sungah mei le temta a tawi hi. Tua bangin amau tegel paikhawm uh hi.
English: And Abraham took the wood of the burnt offering, and laid it upon Isaac his son; and he took the fire in his hand, and a knife; and they went both of them together.

**22:7**
Zolai: Isaac in a pa Abraham’ kiangah, “Pa aw,” a ci hi. Amah in, “Hiah om ing, ka ta,” a ci hi. Amah in, “En in, mei le sing om hi. Ahih hangin meihal biakpiak nading tuuno koi-ah om ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Isaac spake unto Abraham his father, and said, My father: and he said, Here am I, my son. And he said, Behold the fire and the wood: but where is the lamb for a burnt offering?

**22:8**
Zolai: Abraham in, “Pasian in meihal biakpiak nadingin ama a’ ding tuuno hong pia ding hi, ka ta aw,” a ci hi. Tua bangin amau tegel paikhawm uh hi.
English: And Abraham said, My son, God will provide himself a lamb for a burnt offering: so they went both of them together.

**22:9**
Zolai: Ama kiangah Pasian’ gensa mun a tun uh ciangin, Abraham in tua lai-ah biakna tau khat bawlin, a ngeina ding bangin sing koihin, a tapa Isaac henin biakna tau tunga sing tungah a koih hi.
English: And they came to the place which God had told him of; and Abraham built an altar there, and laid the wood in order, and bound Isaac his son, and laid him on the altar upon the wood.

**22:10**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abraham in a tapa a that dingin tem la hi.
English: And Abraham stretched forth his hand, and took the knife to slay his son.

**22:11**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa’ vantungmi in vantung panin, “Abraham, Abraham!” ci-in a sam hi. Amah in, “Hiah om ing,” a ci hi.
English: And the angel of the LORD called unto him out of heaven, and said, Abraham, Abraham: and he said, Here am I.

**22:12**
Zolai: Amah in, “Tangvalpa su kei in. Ama tungah bangmah hih kei in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nang in Pasian na zahtakna tu-in ka thei a, na tapa khat neihsun keima a dingin na humcip lohna ka mu hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Lay not thine hand upon the lad, neither do thou any thing unto him: for now I know that thou fearest God, seeing thou hast not withheld thy son, thine only son from me.

**22:13**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Abraham khuadak kawikawi a, khaumang lakah a ki-a a awk tuutal khat a nungah na om hi. Abraham pai-in tua tuutal kai a, ama tapa’ tangin meihal biakna-in a pia hi.
English: And Abraham lifted up his eyes, and looked, and behold behind him a ram caught in a thicket by his horns: and Abraham went and took the ram, and offered him up for a burnt offering in the stead of his son.

**22:14**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Abraham in tua mun pen, “ Topa in hong sik hi,” ci-in min phuak a, tuni dongin Topa’ mual tungah hong kisik hi, a kici hi.
English: And Abraham called the name of that place Jehovah-jireh: as it is said to this day, In the mount of the LORD it shall be seen.

**22:15**
Zolai: Topa’ vantungmi in vantung panin Abraham a nih veina sam a,
English: And the angel of the LORD called unto Abraham out of heaven the second time,

**22:16**
Zolai: “Kei mahmah ka kiciam hi, Topa in ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh nang in hih thu na bawl khin a, na tapa neihsun na humcip kei hi.
English: and said, By myself have I sworn, saith the LORD , for because thou hast done this thing, and hast not withheld thy son, thine only son :

**22:17**
Zolai: Nang thupha kong pia taktak ding a, na suanlekhakte vana aksite le tuipi gei-a sehnel bangin tampi ka phasak ding hi. Na suanlekhakte in amau’ galte’ khuapite luah ding uh a,
English: that in blessing I will bless thee, and in multiplying I will multiply thy seed as the stars of the heaven, and as the sand which is upon the sea shore; and thy seed shall possess the gate of his enemies;

**22:18**
Zolai: na suanlekhakte thupha ka piak bangin, leitung minam khempeuh in thupha a ngah nadingun hong ngen ding uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh nang in ka thu na mang hi,” a ci hi.
English: and in thy seed shall all the nations of the earth be blessed; because thou hast obeyed my voice.

**22:19**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a nasemte’ kiangah Abraham ciahkik a, Beersheba-ah paikhawm uh hi. Abraham Beersheba-ah a teng hi.
English: So Abraham returned unto his young men, and they rose up and went together to Beer-sheba; and Abraham dwelt at Beer-sheba.

**22:20**
Zolai: Hih thute’ khit ciangin Abraham’ kiangah, “En in, Milkah in zong na sanggampa Nahor tawh tate nei hi:
English: And it came to pass after these things, that it was told Abraham, saying, Behold, Milcah, she hath also born children unto thy brother Nahor;

**22:21**
Zolai: Uz a u pen hi. A sanggamte pen Buz, Aram’ pa Kemuel,
English: Huz his firstborn, and Buz his brother, and Kemuel the father of Aram,

**22:22**
Zolai: Khesed, Hazo, Pildash, Jidlaf, le Bethuel ahi hi,” kici hi.
English: and Chesed, and Hazo, and Pildash, and Jidlaph, and Bethuel.

**22:23**
Zolai: Bethuel pen Rebekah’ pa ahi hi. Milkah in Abraham’ sanggam Nahor tawh tapa giat nei hi.
English: And Bethuel begat Rebekah: these eight Milcah did bear to Nahor, Abraham's brother.

**22:24**
Zolai: Tua tham loin Reumah min nei a zineu in ta Tebah, Gaham, Tahash, le Maakah a nei hi.
English: And his concubine, whose name was Reumah, she bare also Tebah, and Gaham, and Thahash, and Maachah.

## Chapter 23

**23:1**
Zolai: Sarah kum za le kum sawmnih le sagih nungta a,
English: And Sarah was an hundred and seven and twenty years old: these were the years of the life of Sarah.

**23:2**
Zolai: Kanaan mite’ gam sung Kiriatharba (Hebron)-ah a si hi. Abraham dahin kap a, a vui nading vaihawm hi.
English: And Sarah died in Kirjath-arba; the same is Hebron in the land of Canaan: and Abraham came to mourn for Sarah, and to weep for her.

**23:3**
Zolai: Abraham in a misi nusia-in Hit mite kiangah va pai a,
English: And Abraham stood up from before his dead, and spake unto the sons of Heth, saying,

**23:4**
Zolai: “Kei pen note lakah khualmi hi-in peemta ka hi hi. Ka zi ka vui theih nadingin note’ lakah vui nading mun leitang hong pia un,” a ci hi.
English: I am a stranger and a sojourner with you: give me a possession of a buryingplace with you, that I may bury my dead out of my sight.

**23:5**
Zolai: Hit mite in Abraham dawngin,
English: And the children of Heth answered Abraham, saying unto him,

**23:6**
Zolai: “Topa aw, kote’ thu hong ngai in. Nang pen kote’ lakah a vanglian ulian khat na hi hi. Kote’ han na deih pen munah na zi vui in. Kote kuamah in nang a dingin a han it lo ding a, na zi vui ding hong khaktan lo ding hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: Hear us, my lord: thou art a mighty prince among us: in the choice of our sepulchres bury thy dead; none of us shall withhold from thee his sepulchre, but that thou mayest bury thy dead.

**23:7**
Zolai: Abraham dingin tua gammi ahi Hit mite’ lamah a kun hi.
English: And Abraham stood up, and bowed himself to the people of the land, even to the children of Heth.

**23:8**
Zolai: Amah in amaute’ kiangah, “Hih gamah ka zi ka vui ding nong deih uhleh, ka thu hong ngai un. Zohar’ tapa Efron in
English: And he communed with them, saying, If it be your mind that I should bury my dead out of my sight; hear me, and intreat for me to Ephron the son of Zohar,

**23:9**
Zolai: ama neih Makpelah leihawm kei tungah hong piak theih nadingin hong thumsak un. Tua pen ama lo nawlah om hi. Vui nading munin ka neihna dingin a man ding cing takin piakna tawh note’ muhna-ah kei tungah amah hong piasak un,” a ci hi.
English: that he may give me the cave of Machpelah, which he hath, which is in the end of his field; for as much money as it is worth he shall give it me for a possession of a buryingplace amongst you.

**23:10**
