Zolai: Tua laitakin Hit mite’ lakah Efron zong a om ahi hi. Khuapi kulhkongpi-ah a hong pai Hit mite khempeuh’ zakna-ah Hit mi Efron in Abraham dawng a,
English: And Ephron dwelt among the children of Heth: and Ephron the Hittite answered Abraham in the audience of the children of Heth, even of all that went in at the gate of his city, saying,

**23:11**
Zolai: “Hi lo hi, ka topa aw, hong ngai in. Nang’ tungah lo kong pia hi. Tua sunga leihawm zong nang’ tungah kong pia hi. Ka mipihte’ muhna-ah nang’ tungah kong pia hi. Na misi vui in,” a ci hi.
English: Nay, my lord, hear me: the field give I thee, and the cave that is therein, I give it thee; in the presence of the sons of my people give I it thee: bury thy dead.

**23:12**
Zolai: Tua ciangin tua gam mite’ mai-ah Abraham a kun hi.
English: And Abraham bowed down himself before the people of the land.

**23:13**
Zolai: Tua gam mite’ zakna-ah amah in Efron’ kiangah, “Lungsim takpi tawh na cih ahihleh hong ngai in. Lo man ding kong pia ding hi. Tua lai-ah ka misi ka vui theih nadingin kei’ tung panin a man hong sang in,” a ci hi.
English: And he spake unto Ephron in the audience of the people of the land, saying, But if thou wilt give it , I pray thee, hear me: I will give thee money for the field; take it of me, and I will bury my dead there.

**23:14**
Zolai: Efron in Abraham dawngin,
English: And Ephron answered Abraham, saying unto him,

**23:15**
Zolai: “Ka topa aw, ka thu hong ngai in. Leitang bek khat in ngun shekel zali man hi. Nang le kei’ kikalah bang thudang omnawn ahi hiam? Na misi vui in,” a ci hi.
English: My lord, hearken unto me: the land is worth four hundred shekels of silver; what is that betwixt me and thee? bury therefore thy dead.

**23:16**
Zolai: Efron’ cih bangin Abraham thukim hi. Abraham in Efron a dingin, Hit mite’ zakna-ah a min lawh zah, tua hun laitak a sumbukte’ lakah a kizang a gikzah tawh kizui-in ngun shekel zali a tehkhia hi.
English: And Abraham hearkened unto Ephron; and Abraham weighed to Ephron the silver, which he had named in the audience of the sons of Heth, four hundred shekels of silver, current money with the merchant.

**23:17**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Makpelah a Efron’ lo, Mamre nisuahna lamah a om, a sunga om leihawm le a lo, le tua mun khempeuhah a om lo sunga singte pen
English: And the field of Ephron, which was in Machpelah, which was before Mamre, the field, and the cave which was therein, and all the trees that were in the field, that were in all the borders round about, were made sure

**23:18**
Zolai: khuapi kulhkongpi-ah a kikhawm mite khempeuh’ mai, Hit mite’ omna-ah Abraham’ neih dingin kipia hi.
English: unto Abraham for a possession in the presence of the children of Heth, before all that went in at the gate of his city.

**23:19**
Zolai: Hih bangin a kihih khit ciangin, Kanaan gam sunga om Mamre (Hebron) nisuahna lamah a om Makpelah lo sunga leihawm sungah Abraham in a zi Sarah a vui hi.
English: And after this, Abraham buried Sarah his wife in the cave of the field of Machpelah before Mamre: the same is Hebron in the land of Canaan.

**23:20**
Zolai: Lo le a sunga om leihawmte si vui nading munin a neih dingin Abraham’ tungah Hit mite in a pia uh hi.
English: And the field, and the cave that is therein, were made sure unto Abraham for a possession of a buryingplace by the sons of Heth.

## Chapter 24

**24:1**
Zolai: Tu-in Abraham teekin a kum tam mahmah ta hi. Topa in na khempeuhah Abraham thupha pia hi.
English: And Abraham was old, and well stricken in age: and the LORD had blessed Abraham in all things.

**24:2**
Zolai: Abraham in ama neih khempeuh a uk, a inn sungah a upa pen a nasempa kiangah, “Ka phei nuai-ah na khut hong koih in.
English: And Abraham said unto his eldest servant of his house, that ruled over all that he had, Put, I pray thee, thy hand under my thigh:

**24:3**
Zolai: Nangmah in amau’ lakah ka tenna Kanaan mite’ tanute lak panin ka tapa’ zi ding la loin, keima gam le ka behte kiangah va pai-in ka tapa Isaac’ zi ding na lak nadingin vantung le leitung Pasian ahi Topa tawh nang kong kiciamsak ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: and I will make thee swear by the LORD , the God of heaven, and the God of the earth, that thou shalt not take a wife unto my son of the daughters of the Canaanites, among whom I dwell:

**24:5**
Zolai: Nasempa in ama kiangah, “A numei in hih gamah kei hong zui nuam kei khaleh nangma nong paikhiatna gamah na tapa ka paipih kik ding hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And the servant said unto him, Peradventure the woman will not be willing to follow me unto this land: must I needs bring thy son again unto the land from whence thou camest?

**24:6**
Zolai: Abraham in ama kiangah, “Tua lai-ah ka tapa na paipih kik loh ding thei in.
English: And Abraham said unto him, Beware thou that thou bring not my son thither again.

**24:7**
Zolai: Ka pa’ inn le ka suahna leitang panin kei hong la-in, kei kiangah thu hong genin kei tungah hong kiciam a, ‘Na suanlekhakte’ tungah hih leitang ka pia ding hi,’ a hong ci vantung Pasian, Topa in nangma mai-ah a vantungmi sawl ding a, tua lai mun panin nangmah in ka tapa a’ ding zi khat na la ding hi.
English: The LORD God of heaven, which took me from my father's house, and from the land of my kindred, and which spake unto me, and that sware unto me, saying, Unto thy seed will I give this land; he shall send his angel before thee, and thou shalt take a wife unto my son from thence.

**24:8**
Zolai: Ahih hangin a numei in nang hong zuih nop kei leh keima thuciamna panin nang na suakta ding hi. Bangbang hileh tua lai-ah ka tapa na paipih kik kei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And if the woman will not be willing to follow thee, then thou shalt be clear from this my oath: only bring not my son thither again.

**24:9**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin a nasempa in a topa Abraham’ phei nuai-ah a khut koih a, hih thu tawh kisai-in ama tungah a kiciam hi.
English: And the servant put his hand under the thigh of Abraham his master, and sware to him concerning that matter.

**24:10**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a nasempa in a topa’ kalaohte sawm la-in paikhia a, a topa’ tung panin letsong hoihnono a namkim la hi. Amah dingin Mesopotamia gam Nahor’ khuapi-ah a pai hi.
English: And the servant took ten camels of the camels of his master, and departed; for all the goods of his master were in his hand: and he arose, and went to Mesopotamia, unto the city of Nahor.

**24:11**
Zolai: Numeite’ nitak tuitawi hun laitakin khuapi pualam tuikhuk gei-ah amah in a kalaohte boksak hi.
English: And he made his camels to kneel down without the city by a well of water at the time of the evening, even the time that women go out to draw water .

**24:12**
Zolai: Amah in, “Ka topa Abraham’ Pasian, Topa aw, tuni-in ka maa hong vangsak in. Nang tungah thu kong ngen hi, ka topa Abraham’ tungah itna kip hong lak in.
English: And he said, O LORD God of my master Abraham, I pray thee, send me good speed this day, and shew kindness unto my master Abraham.

**24:13**
Zolai: En in, tuikhuk gei-ah kei ka ding a, khuapi nungakte tuitawi dingin hong pai uh hi.
English: Behold, I stand here by the well of water; and the daughters of the men of the city come out to draw water:

**24:14**
Zolai: Keimah in, ‘Tui ka dawn theih nadingin na beel hong nga suk in,’ ka cih ciangin, ‘Dawn in; na kalaohte zong tui ka pia ding hi,’ hong ci nu pen na nasempa Isaac a dingin na sehsa numei hisak in. Nangmah in ka topa tungah itna kip na lahna hih thu tawh ka thei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: and let it come to pass, that the damsel to whom I shall say, Let down thy pitcher, I pray thee, that I may drink; and she shall say, Drink, and I will give thy camels drink also: let the same be she that thou hast appointed for thy servant Isaac; and thereby shall I know that thou hast shewed kindness unto my master.

**24:15**
Zolai: Tua bangin a thunget a khit ma-in, Abraham’ sanggampa Nahor in a zi Milkah tawh a neih a tapa Bethuel’ tanu Rebekah a liangko tungah a tuibeel pua-in hong paikhia hi.
English: And it came to pass, before he had done speaking, that, behold, Rebekah came out, who was born to Bethuel, son of Milcah, the wife of Nahor, Abraham's brother, with her pitcher upon her shoulder.

**24:16**
Zolai: Tua nu pen kuamah tawh a lumkhawm nai lo, nungak, a ngaihbaang mahmah khat ahi hi. Amah tuikhukah paisukin a beel dim a, hong paito hi.
English: And the damsel was very fair to look upon, a virgin, neither had any man known her: and she went down to the well, and filled her pitcher, and came up.

**24:17**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah a dawntuah dingin nasempa tai a, “Dawn ding tui tawmkhat na beel sung panin hong pia dih in,” a ci hi.
English: And the servant ran to meet her, and said, Let me, I pray thee, drink a little water of thy pitcher.

**24:18**
Zolai: Amah in, “Dawn in, ka topa,” a ci hi. Tua nu in a khut tungah a beel niamsuksakin amah a dawnsak hi.
English: And she said, Drink, my lord: and she hasted, and let down her pitcher upon her hand, and gave him drink.

**24:19**
Zolai: Amah in tua mipa tui a dawnsak khit ciangin, “Na kalaohte in a kham matengun a dawn ding zong tui kong tawisak ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And when she had done giving him drink, she said, I will draw water for thy camels also, until they have done drinking.

**24:20**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in a tuikuang sungah a tui bungsuk pak a, tuitawi dingin tuikhukah tai-in a kalaohte khempeuh a dingin tui a tawi hi.
English: And she hasted, and emptied her pitcher into the trough, and ran again unto the well to draw water , and drew for all his camels.

**24:21**
Zolai: Topa in ama khualzinna mavangsak ding hiam, vangsak lo ding hiam, cih a theih nadingin mipa in daptakin tua nu na en hi.
English: And the man wondering at her held his peace, to wit whether the LORD had made his journey prosperous or not.

**24:22**
Zolai: Kalaohte in tui a dawn khit ciangin mipa in shekel lang a gik kham nakbah khat le shekel sawm a gik kham tau nih tua nu a dingin la-in pia a,
English: And it came to pass, as the camels had done drinking, that the man took a golden earring of half a shekel weight, and two bracelets for her hands of ten shekels weight of gold;

**24:23**
Zolai: “Kua’ tanu na hi hiam, hong gen in. Na pa’ inn-ah kote’ giah nading a awng ding hiam?” a ci hi.
English: and said, Whose daughter art thou? tell me, I pray thee: is there room in thy father's house for us to lodge in?

**24:24**
Zolai: Tua nu in ama kiangah, “Nahor le a zi Milkah’ tapa Bethuel’ tanu ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
English: And she said unto him, I am the daughter of Bethuel the son of Milcah, which she bare unto Nahor.

**24:25**
Zolai: Amah in, “Buhkung le gan-an a kicing ka nei uh a, giah nading mun zong ka nei uh hi,” ci thuah lai hi.
English: She said moreover unto him, We have both straw and provender enough, and room to lodge in.

**24:26**
Zolai: Mipa a lu kunin Topa bia a,
English: And the man bowed down his head, and worshipped the LORD .

**24:27**
Zolai: “Ka topa’ tungah a itna kip le a thumanna a pelh lo, ka topa Abraham’ Pasian, Topa in thupha ngah tahen. Kei ka hih leh, ka topa’ behte’ inn zuatna lampi-ah Topa in hong paipih hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Blessed be the LORD God of my master Abraham, who hath not left destitute my master of his mercy and his truth: I being in the way, the LORD led me to the house of my master's brethren.

**24:28**
Zolai: Tua ciangin nungaknu a inn-ah tai-in hih thute khempeuh a innkuanpihte tungah a gen hi.
English: And the damsel ran, and told them of her mother's house these things.

**24:29**
Zolai: Rebekah in Laban min nei sanggam pasal khat nei hi. Laban zong tuikhuka mipa kiangah a tai hi.
English: And Rebekah had a brother, and his name was Laban: and Laban ran out unto the man, unto the well.

**24:30**
Zolai: Amah in nakbah le a sanggamnu’ khut tunga taaute a muh ciang le, “Mipa in hih bangin kei tungah hong gen,” ci-in a sanggamnu Rebekah’ kam gen a zak ciangin, mipa kiangah a pai ahi hi. Tuikhuka kalaohte kiangah amah na ding hi.
English: And it came to pass, when he saw the earring and bracelets upon his sister's hands, and when he heard the words of Rebekah his sister, saying, Thus spake the man unto me; that he came unto the man; and, behold, he stood by the camels at the well.

**24:31**
Zolai: Amah in, “Hong pai in, Topa’ thupha piakpa aw; bang hangin a pua-ah ding na hi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh inn-ah na om nading mun ka bawl khin a, kalaohte a’ ding mun zong om hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Come in, thou blessed of the LORD ; wherefore standest thou without? for I have prepared the house, and room for the camels.

**24:32**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin inn sungah mipa hong pai hi. Laban in kalaoh vante suah a, kalaohte a dingin buhkung le gan-an pia a, amah le a kikholhpih mite’ khe sil nadingin tui zong a pia hi.
English: And the man came into the house: and he ungirded his camels, and gave straw and provender for the camels, and water to wash his feet, and the men's feet that were with him.

**24:33**
Zolai: Tua ciangin nek dingin a mai-ah an kilui hi. Ahih hangin amah in, “Ka thu ka gen khit matengin an ka ne kei ding hi,” a cih ciangin amah in, “Gen in,” a ci hi.
English: And there was set meat before him to eat: but he said, I will not eat, until I have told mine errand. And he said, Speak on.

**24:34**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in, “Kei pen Abraham’ nasem ka hi hi.
English: And he said, I am Abraham's servant.

**24:35**
Zolai: Topa in ka topa nakpitakin thupha pia a, amah a lian mahmah suak khin hi. Amah in ama tungah tuuhon, bawnghon, ngun le kham, nasem pasal le nasem numei, kalaoh le late tampi pia hi.
English: And the LORD hath blessed my master greatly; and he is become great: and he hath given him flocks, and herds, and silver, and gold, and menservants, and maidservants, and camels, and asses.

**24:36**
Zolai: Ka topa’ zi Sarah in a teek khitin ka topa tawh tapa khat nei hi. Amah in a neihsa khempeuh ama tungah pia hi.
English: And Sarah my master's wife bare a son to my master when she was old: and unto him hath he given all that he hath.

**24:37**
Zolai: Ka topa in kei hong kiciamsak a, ‘Nangmah in amau’ gamah ka tenna Kanaan numeite lak panin ka tapa’ zi ding la kei inla,
English: And my master made me swear, saying, Thou shalt not take a wife to my son of the daughters of the Canaanites, in whose land I dwell:

**24:38**
Zolai: ka pa’ innkuan mi le ka behte kiangah pai-in ka tapa a’ ding zi khat na la ding hi,’ hong ci hi.
English: but thou shalt go unto my father's house, and to my kindred, and take a wife unto my son.

**24:39**
Zolai: Keimah in ka topa kiangah, ‘A numei in kei hong zui nuam kei kha leh,’ ka ci hi.
English: And I said unto my master, Peradventure the woman will not follow me.

**24:40**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah in kei tungah, ‘A thu ka man’ Topa in nang tawh a vantungmi hong sawlin na maa hong vangsak ding hi. Nang in ka behte le ka pa’ inn panin ka tapa a’ ding zi khat na la ding hi.
English: And he said unto me, The LORD , before whom I walk, will send his angel with thee, and prosper thy way; and thou shalt take a wife for my son of my kindred, and of my father's house:

**24:41**
Zolai: Ka behte kiangah na pai ciangin amaute in nang hong piak kei leh ka thuciamna panin nang na suakta ding hi,’ hong ci hi.
English: then shalt thou be clear from this my oath, when thou comest to my kindred; and if they give not thee one , thou shalt be clear from my oath.

**24:42**
Zolai: “Tuni-in tuikhukah pai-in, ‘Ka topa Abraham’ Pasian, Topa aw, tu-a ka paina ka maa nong vansak ding le,
English: And I came this day unto the well, and said, O LORD God of my master Abraham, if now thou do prosper my way which I go:

**24:43**
Zolai: en in, tuikhuk gei-ah kei ka ding hi. Tuitawi dinga hong paikhia nungak tungah, “Na beel panin tui dawn ding tawmkhat hong pia in,” ka cih ciangin,
English: behold, I stand by the well of water; and it shall come to pass, that when the virgin cometh forth to draw water , and I say to her, Give me, I pray thee, a little water of thy pitcher to drink;

**24:44**
Zolai: “Dawn in, na kalaohte a’ ding zong kong tawisak ding hi,” hong ci nu pen, ka topa’ tapa a dingin Topa in a sehsa numei hisak in,’ ka ci hi.
English: and she say to me, Both drink thou, and I will also draw for thy camels: let the same be the woman whom the LORD hath appointed out for my master's son.

**24:45**
Zolai: “Ka lungsim sungah thu ka nget khit ma-in, a liangko tungah a tuibeel pua-in Rebekah hong paikhia ka mu hi. Amah tuikhukah paisukin tui hong tawi hi. Keimah in ama kiangah, ‘Tui hong dawnsak in,’ ka ci hi.
English: And before I had done speaking in mine heart, behold, Rebekah came forth with her pitcher on her shoulder; and she went down unto the well, and drew water: and I said unto her, Let me drink, I pray thee.

**24:46**
Zolai: Amah in a liangko panin a beel hong khiasuk pahin, ‘Dawn in, na kalaohte zong tui ka pia ding hi,’ hong ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin keimah in ka dawn a, amah in kalaohte zong tui a pia hi.
English: And she made haste, and let down her pitcher from her shoulder , and said, Drink, and I will give thy camels drink also: so I drank, and she made the camels drink also.

**24:47**
Zolai: Tua ciangin, ‘Kua’ tanu na hi hiam?’ ci-in ka dong hi. Amah in, ‘Nahor le a zi Milkah’ tapa Bethuel’ tanu ka hi hi,’ hong ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin a nak tungah nakbah ka batsak a, a khut tungah taaute ka butsak hi.
English: And I asked her, and said, Whose daughter art thou? And she said, The daughter of Bethuel, Nahor's son, whom Milcah bare unto him: and I put the earring upon her face, and the bracelets upon her hands.

**24:48**
Zolai: Tua ciangin ka lu kunin Topa ka bia a, a tapa a dingin ka topa’ behpa’ tanu a la dingin lampi manah kei a hong paipih, ka topa Abraham’ Pasian, Topa ka phat hi.
English: And I bowed down my head, and worshipped the LORD , and blessed the LORD God of my master Abraham, which had led me in the right way to take my master's brother's daughter unto his son.

**24:49**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tu-in, ka gamtat nading zia ka theih nadingin ka topa’ tungah hoihtak le thuman takin na gamtat ding uh le na gamtat loh ding uh hong gen un,” a ci hi.
English: And now if ye will deal kindly and truly with my master, tell me: and if not, tell me; that I may turn to the right hand, or to the left.

**24:50**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Laban le Bethuel in dawng a, “Hih thu pen Topa’ kiang panin hong pai thu ahi hi. A sia ahi zongin a pha ahi zongin nang tungah kong gen ding dang uh om lo hi.
English: Then Laban and Bethuel answered and said, The thing proceedeth from the LORD : we cannot speak unto thee bad or good.

**24:51**
Zolai: En in, Rebekah na mai-ah om hi. Amah la inla pai un. Topa’ gensa bangin na topa’ tapa’ zi hisak un,” a ci uh hi.
English: Behold, Rebekah is before thee, take her , and go, and let her be thy master's son's wife, as the LORD hath spoken.

**24:52**
Zolai: Abraham’ nasempa in amau’ kammalte a zak ciangin Topa’ mai leilakah a kunsuk hi.
English: And it came to pass, that, when Abraham's servant heard their words, he worshipped the LORD , bowing himself to the earth.

**24:53**
Zolai: Nasempa in ngun le kham kizepnate le puante hong suahkhia-in Rebekah a pia hi. A sanggampa le a nu zong a manpha kizepnate a pia hi.
English: And the servant brought forth jewels of silver, and jewels of gold, and raiment, and gave them to Rebekah: he gave also to her brother and to her mother precious things.

**24:54**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah le a nungzuite in an ne tui dawnin, tua lai-ah tua zan a giak uh hi. Amaute zingsangin a thawh uh ciangin amah in, “Ka topa’ kiangah hong ciahsakkik un,” a ci hi.
English: And they did eat and drink, he and the men that were with him, and tarried all night; and they rose up in the morning, and he said, Send me away unto my master.

**24:55**
Zolai: Ahi zongin a sanggampa le a nu in, “A tawm penin ni sawm bang, ko tawh numei hong omsak lai in; tua khit ciangin amah hong pai thei ding hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And her brother and her mother said, Let the damsel abide with us a few days, at the least ten; after that she shall go.

**24:56**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah in amaute kiangah, “ Topa in ka maa hong vangsak khin ahih nungsang kei hong zekaisak nawn kei un. Ka topa kiangah ka ciah theih nadingin hong paisak un,” a ci hi.
English: And he said unto them, Hinder me not, seeing the LORD hath prospered my way; send me away that I may go to my master.

**24:57**
Zolai: Amaute in, “A numei samin amah i dong ding hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And they said, We will call the damsel, and enquire at her mouth.

**24:58**
Zolai: Amaute in Rebekah samin ama kiangah, “Hih mipa na zui pah ding hiam?” a ci uh hi. Amah in, “Ka zui ding hi,” ci pah hi.
English: And they called Rebekah, and said unto her, Wilt thou go with this man? And she said, I will go.

**24:59**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute in a sanggamnu uh Rebekah le a cingnu, Abraham’ nasempa le a nungzuite tawh ciahkhiasak uh hi.
English: And they sent away Rebekah their sister, and her nurse, and Abraham's servant, and his men.

**24:60**
Zolai: Amaute in Rebekah thupha pia-in ama kiangah, “Kote’ sanggamnu aw, a tultul a thenthente’ nu hi ta in. Na suanlekhakte in amau a mudahte’ khuapite luah ta uh hen!” a ci uh hi.
English: And they blessed Rebekah, and said unto her, Thou art our sister, be thou the mother of thousands of millions, and let thy seed possess the gate of those which hate them.

**24:61**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Rebekah le a numeite dingin, kalaohte tungah tuangin mipa a zui uh hi. Tua bangin nasempa in Rebekah la-in a pai nading lamah a pai hi.
English: And Rebekah arose, and her damsels, and they rode upon the camels, and followed the man: and the servant took Rebekah, and went his way.

**24:62**
Zolai: Tua kikalin, Isaac, Beerlahairoi panin hong pai-in Negeb gamah na teng hi.
English: And Isaac came from the way of the well Lahai-roi; for he dwelt in the south country.

**24:63**
Zolai: Isaac, thu a lungngaingai dingin nitakin gamlakah a paikhia hi. Amah a khuadak le kalaohte hong pai a mu hi.
English: And Isaac went out to meditate in the field at the eventide: and he lifted up his eyes, and saw, and, behold, the camels were coming.

**24:64**
Zolai: Rebekah in Isaac a muh ciangin, kalaoh tung panin kumin
English: And Rebekah lifted up her eyes, and when she saw Isaac, she lighted off the camel.

**24:65**
Zolai: nasempa kiangah, “Hua lai-a mipa, eite hong dawn dingin gamlak a hong pai kua ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Nasempa in, “Ka topa hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in a kikhuhna puan la-in a kikhuh hi.
English: For she had said unto the servant, What man is this that walketh in the field to meet us? And the servant had said, It is my master: therefore she took a vail, and covered herself.

**24:66**
Zolai: Nasempa in Isaac kiangah a gamtatnasa khempeuh a gen hi.
English: And the servant told Isaac all things that he had done.

**24:67**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Isaac in a puanbuk sungah Rebekah paipih a, amah pen a zi a suak hi. Amah in tua nu a it hi. Tua ahih manin a nu’ sih khit ciangin Isaac in hehnepna a ngah hi.
English: And Isaac brought her into his mother Sarah's tent, and took Rebekah, and she became his wife; and he loved her: and Isaac was comforted after his mother's death .

## Chapter 25

**25:1**
Zolai: Abraham in Keturah min nei zi dang khat la hi.
English: Then again Abraham took a wife, and her name was Keturah.

**25:2**
Zolai: Amah in tua nu tawh ta Zimran, Jokshan, Medan, Midian, Ishbak, le Shuah nei hi.
English: And she bare him Zimran, and Jokshan, and Medan, and Midian, and Ishbak, and Shuah.

**25:3**
Zolai: Jokshan pen Sheba le Dedan’ pa ahi hi. Dedan’ tate: Asshurim, Lethusim, le Leummim ahi hi.
English: And Jokshan begat Sheba, and Dedan. And the sons of Dedan were Asshurim, and Letushim, and Leummim.

**25:4**
Zolai: Midian’ tate: Efah, Efer, Hanok, Abida, le Eldaah ahi hi. Hihte khempeuh, Keturah’ suanlekhakte ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Midian; Ephah, and Epher, and Hanoch, and Abidah, and Eldaah. All these were the children of Keturah.

**25:5**
Zolai: Abraham in a neih khempeuh Isaac a pia hi.
English: And Abraham gave all that he had unto Isaac.

**25:6**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Abraham in a zi dang tawh a tate tungah zong letsong pia a, ama nuntak lai mahin ama tapa Isaac kiang panin nisuahna lam gamah amaute a sawlkhia hi.
English: But unto the sons of the concubines, which Abraham had, Abraham gave gifts, and sent them away from Isaac his son, while he yet lived, eastward, unto the east country.

**25:7**
Zolai: Abraham, kum za le kum sawmsagih le nga a phak ciangin,
English: And these are the days of the years of Abraham's life which he lived, an hundred threescore and fifteen years.

**25:8**
Zolai: a hu tawpna sang a, a teek, kum tampi a pha, a khanghamin si a, ama mite tawh kivui khawm hi.
English: Then Abraham gave up the ghost, and died in a good old age, an old man, and full of years ; and was gathered to his people.

**25:9**
Zolai: Ama tapa Isaac le Ishmael in, Abraham in Hit mite’ tung panin a lei, Mamre nisuahna lamah a om, Hit mi Zohar’ tapa Efron’ lo sung, Makpelah leihawm sungah amah a vui uh hi. Tua lai munah a zi Sarah kiangah Abraham kivui hi.
English: And his sons Isaac and Ishmael buried him in the cave of Machpelah, in the field of Ephron the son of Zohar the Hittite, which is before Mamre;

**25:11**
Zolai: Abraham’ sih khit ciangin Pasian in a tapa Isaac thupha pia hi. Isaac, Beerlahairoi-ah a teng hi.
English: And it came to pass after the death of Abraham, that God blessed his son Isaac; and Isaac dwelt by the well Lahai-roi.

**25:12**
Zolai: Hihte pen, Abraham in Sarah’ sila numei ahi Egypt mi Hagar tawh a neih, Abraham’ tapa Ishmael’ suanlekhakte ahi hi.
English: Now these are the generations of Ishmael, Abraham's son, whom Hagar the Egyptian, Sarah's handmaid, bare unto Abraham:

**25:13**
Zolai: Hihte pen a suahna tawh kizui-in Ishmael’ tate’ min ahi hi: Ishmael’ ta upa pen Nebaioth hi a, tua ciangin Kedar, Adbeel, Mibsam,
English: and these are the names of the sons of Ishmael, by their names, according to their generations: the firstborn of Ishmael, Nebajoth; and Kedar, and Adbeel, and Mibsam,

**25:14**
Zolai: Mishma, Dumah, Massa,
English: and Mishma, and Dumah, and Massa,

**25:15**
Zolai: Hadad, Tema, Jetur, Nafish, le Kedemah ahi hi.
English: Hadar, and Tema, Jetur, Naphish, and Kedemah:

**25:16**
Zolai: Hihte pen a khua, a phual, a behin ulian sawm le nihte ahi Ishmael’ tate le amaute’ min ahi hi.
English: these are the sons of Ishmael, and these are their names, by their towns, and by their castles; twelve princes according to their nations.

**25:17**
Zolai: (Ishmael kum za le kum sawmthum le sagih a phak ciangin a hu tawpna sang-in si a, a behte tawh kivui khawm hi.)
English: And these are the years of the life of Ishmael, an hundred and thirty and seven years: and he gave up the ghost and died; and was gathered unto his people.

**25:18**
Zolai: Amaute, Egypt nisuahna, Assiria lam Havilah panin Shur dongah teng uh a, amau’ sanggamte khempeuh panin amau tuam ten uh hi.
English: And they dwelt from Havilah unto Shur, that is before Egypt, as thou goest toward Assyria: and he died in the presence of all his brethren.

**25:19**
Zolai: Hihte pen Abraham’ tapa Isaac’ suanlekhakte ahi hi. Abraham pen Isaac’ pa hi a,
English: And these are the generations of Isaac, Abraham's son: Abraham begat Isaac:

**25:20**
Zolai: Aram mi Laban’ sanggamnu, Paddanaram gam a Aram mi Bethuel’ tanu Rebekah zi-in a lak lai-in Isaac kum sawmli pha hi.
English: and Isaac was forty years old when he took Rebekah to wife, the daughter of Bethuel the Syrian of Padan-aram, the sister to Laban the Syrian.

**25:21**
Zolai: Isaac in Topa’ tungah a zi a dingin thu ngen hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah ciing hi. Topa in ama thungetna pia a, a zi Rebekah gai hi.
English: And Isaac intreated the LORD for his wife, because she was barren: and the LORD was intreated of him, and Rebekah his wife conceived.

**25:22**
Zolai: Ama sungah a naute kilaigawp hi. Amah in, “Hih bang ahihleh bang hangin nungta se ka hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin Topa kiangah thukan dingin amah pai hi.
English: And the children struggled together within her; and she said, If it be so, why am I thus? And she went to enquire of the LORD .

**25:23**
Zolai: Topa in ama kiangah, “Na gil sungah mi nam nih om a, nang’ sung pan a suak mihing nihte kikhen ding hi. Khat pen a khat sangin hat zaw ding a, a uzaw in a nauzaw’ na sem ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And the LORD said unto her, Two nations are in thy womb, And two manner of people shall be separated from thy bowels; And the one people shall be stronger than the other people; And the elder shall serve the younger.

**25:24**
Zolai: Amah a suah hun a tun ciangin, a gil sungah tapeeng om hi.
English: And when her days to be delivered were fulfilled, behold, there were twins in her womb.

**25:25**
Zolai: A masa pen a sanin hong suak a, a pumpi khempeuh mul a nei puan tawh kibang hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama min dingin Esau phuak uh hi.
English: And the first came out red, all over like an hairy garment; and they called his name Esau.

**25:26**
Zolai: Tua khit ciangin a sanggampa hong suakkhia a, ama khut in Esau’ khetul len hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama min dingin Jakob kiphuak hi. Amau’ suah ciangin Isaac kum sawmguk a pha hi.
English: And after that came his brother out, and his hand took hold on Esau's heel; and his name was called Jacob: and Isaac was threescore years old when she bare them.

**25:27**
Zolai: Tua naupangte a khan ciangin, Esau pen gam sung mi sabet siam khat hi a, Jakob ahihleh inn-ah om hithiatin a cingkam khat ahi hi.
English: And the boys grew: and Esau was a cunning hunter, a man of the field; and Jacob was a plain man, dwelling in tents.

**25:28**
Zolai: Isaac in Esau’ sa matsa nene ahih manin Esau mah itzaw a, ahi zongin Rebekah in Jakob itzaw hi.
English: And Isaac loved Esau, because he did eat of his venison: but Rebekah loved Jacob.

**25:29**
Zolai: Khatvei Jakob in meh huanin a om laitakin gamlak a sa betna panin phukhong vei-in Esau hong ciah hi.
English: And Jacob sod pottage: and Esau came from the field, and he was faint:

**25:30**
Zolai: Esau in Jakob kiangah, “Gilkialin phukhong vei ka hih manin tua na meh san tawmkhat hong nesak in,” a ci hi. (Tua ahih manin ama min Edom kici hi.)
English: and Esau said to Jacob, Feed me, I pray thee, with that same red pottage ; for I am faint: therefore was his name called Edom.

**25:31**
Zolai: Jakob in, “Na innluahza hong pia lecin ka meh kong pia ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob said, Sell me this day thy birthright.

**25:32**
Zolai: Esau in, “A si ding ka hita hi; kei a dingin innluahza bangin kimang ding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Esau said, Behold, I am at the point to die: and what profit shall this birthright do to me?

**25:33**
Zolai: Jakob in, “Kei’ tungah hong kiciam masa in,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama tungah Esau kiciam a, Jakob’ tungah a innluahza a zuak hi.
English: And Jacob said, Swear to me this day; and he sware unto him: and he sold his birthright unto Jacob.

**25:34**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in an le bemeh Esau a pia hi. Esau in zong an ne-in tui a dawn khit ciangin a pai nading a zuan hi. Tua ahih manin Esau in a innluahza tua ciang bang bekin a ngaihsun ahi hi.
English: Then Jacob gave Esau bread and pottage of lentiles; and he did eat and drink, and rose up, and went his way: thus Esau despised his birthright.

## Chapter 26

**26:1**
Zolai: Abraham’ hun lai-a kialpi banah, tu-in tua gam sungah kialpi dang khat tung hi. Filistia mite’ kumpipa Abimelek’ omna Gerar-ah Isaac pai hi.
English: And there was a famine in the land, beside the first famine that was in the days of Abraham. And Isaac went unto Abimelech king of the Philistines unto Gerar.

**26:2**
Zolai: Ama tungah Topa kilang a, “Egypt-ah paisuk kei inla, kong gen ding leitangah teng in.
English: And the LORD appeared unto him, and said, Go not down into Egypt; dwell in the land which I shall tell thee of:

**26:3**
Zolai: Hih leitangah tawlkhat om in. Nang tawh kong omkhawm ding a, thupha kong pia ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh nang le na suanlekhakte tungah hih leitangte kong pia ding a, na pa Abraham’ tungah ka thuciam ka tungsak ding hi.
English: sojourn in this land, and I will be with thee, and will bless thee; for unto thee, and unto thy seed, I will give all these countries, and I will perform the oath which I sware unto Abraham thy father;

**26:4**
Zolai: Na suanlekhakte vana aksi bangin tampi ka phasak ding a, na suanlekhakte tungah hih leitang khempeuh ka pia ding hi. Na suanlekhakte thupha ka piak bangin leitung minam khempeuh in thupha a ngah nadingun hong ngen ding uh hi.
English: and I will make thy seed to multiply as the stars of heaven, and will give unto thy seed all these countries; and in thy seed shall all the nations of the earth be blessed;

**26:5**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Abraham in ka thu mangin, ka sawlna, ka thupiakna, ka ngeina kip le ka thu zui hi,” a ci hi.
English: because that Abraham obeyed my voice, and kept my charge, my commandments, my statutes, and my laws.

**26:6**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Isaac, Gerar-ah teng hi.
English: And Isaac dwelt in Gerar:

**26:7**
Zolai: Tua mun mite in ama zi tawh kisai thu a dot uh ciangin amah in, “Ka sanggamnu hi,” a ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh, “Rebekah’ hangin tua gam mite in hong that kha ding ahih ciangin,” ci-in ngaihsun ahih manin, “Ka zi hi,” a cih ding lau hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah ngaihbaang hi.
English: And the men of the place asked him of his wife; and he said, She is my sister: for he feared to say, She is my wife; lest, said he , the men of the place should kill me for Rebekah; because she was fair to look upon.

**26:8**
Zolai: Tua lai-ah amah sauveipi a om khit ciangin, Filistia mite’ kumpipa Abimelek a tawlet panin khuadak a, Isaac in a zi Rebekah a noh laitak mu kha hi.
English: And it came to pass, when he had been there a long time, that Abimelech king of the Philistines looked out at a window, and saw, and, behold, Isaac was sporting with Rebekah his wife.

**26:9**
Zolai: Tua ahih manin Abimelek in Isaac samin, “En in, amah na zi ahi hi. Tua ahih ciangin bangci-in nang in, ‘Amah ka sanggamnu hi,’ ci thei na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Isaac in ama kiangah, ”‘Ama hangin si kha ding ka hih ciangin,’ ci-in ngaihsun ka hihna hang hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Abimelech called Isaac, and said, Behold, of a surety she is thy wife: and how saidst thou, She is my sister? And Isaac said unto him, Because I said, Lest I die for her.

**26:10**
Zolai: Abimelek in, “Ko tungah bangci-a hih bangin hong gamta na hi hiam? Mite khat peuhpeuh na zi tawh lumkhawm pak kha thei ding a, kote’ tungah mawhna hong tun na hi ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Abimelech said, What is this thou hast done unto us? one of the people might lightly have lien with thy wife, and thou shouldest have brought guiltiness upon us.

**26:11**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Abimelek in mi khempeuh thu zasak a, “Hih mipa ahi zongin a zi ahi zongin a sukha peuhmah kithat ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Abimelech charged all his people, saying, He that toucheth this man or his wife shall surely be put to death.

**26:12**
Zolai: Isaac in tua leitangah khai tuh a, tua kum mahin a zah zakhat la hi. Topa in amah thupha pia a,
English: Then Isaac sowed in that land, and received in the same year an hundredfold: and the LORD blessed him.

**26:13**
Zolai: a neihsa kibehlaplap ahih manin a hau mahmah khat a suak hi.
English: And the man waxed great, and went forward, and grew until he became very great:

**26:14**
Zolai: Amah in tuuhon le bawnghon, le innkuan mi tampi nei a, Filistia mite in amah eng uh hi.
English: for he had possession of flocks, and possession of herds, and great store of servants: and the Philistines envied him.

**26:15**
Zolai: (Ama pa Abraham’ hun lai-a a pa’ nasemte in a tawh tuikhuk khempeuh tu-in Filistia mite in hucipin lei vuk uh hi.)
English: For all the wells which his father's servants had digged in the days of Abraham his father, the Philistines had stopped them, and filled them with earth.

**26:16**
Zolai: Abimelek in Isaac kiangah, “Kote’ kiang panin paikhia in. Bang hang hiam cih leh kote sangin nang na vanglian zaw hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Abimelech said unto Isaac, Go from us; for thou art much mightier than we.

**26:17**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tua mun panin Isaac paikhia a, Gerar kuam sungah phual satin tua munah a teng hi.
English: And Isaac departed thence, and pitched his tent in the valley of Gerar, and dwelt there.

**26:18**
Zolai: Isaac in a pa Abraham’ hun lai-a a kitosa tuikhukte to pha kik hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Abraham’ sih khit ciangin Filistia mite in tuate vukcip uh hi. Amah in a pa’ phuahsa minte mah phuak kik hi.
English: And Isaac digged again the wells of water, which they had digged in the days of Abraham his father; for the Philistines had stopped them after the death of Abraham: and he called their names after the names by which his father had called them.

**26:19**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Isaac’ nasemte in tua kuam sung to-in tuikhuk a muh uh ciangin,
English: And Isaac's servants digged in the valley, and found there a well of springing water.

**26:20**
Zolai: Gerar gancingte le Isaac’ gancingte kitawng uh a, “Tui, ko a’ hi,” ci uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in tua tuikhuk Esek ci-in min a phuak hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute le amah kitawng uh hi.
English: And the herdmen of Gerar did strive with Isaac's herdmen, saying, The water is our's: and he called the name of the well Esek; because they strove with him.

**26:21**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in tuikhuk dang khat to uh a, tua tungtangah zong amaute kitawng leuleu uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in tua pen Sitnah ci-in min a phuak hi.
English: And they digged another well, and strove for that also: and he called the name of it Sitnah.

**26:22**
Zolai: Tua mun panin amah kinin tuikhuk dang khat to leuleu hi. Tua tungtangah amaute kitawng nawn lo uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in Rehoboth ci-in min a phuak hi. “Bang hang hiam cih leh tu-in Topa in eite a dingin omna hong bawlsak khin a, eite hih gamah i pung ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he removed from thence, and digged another well; and for that they strove not: and he called the name of it Rehoboth; and he said, For now the LORD hath made room for us, and we shall be fruitful in the land.

**26:23**
Zolai: Tua lai mun panin amah Beersheba-ah paito hi.
English: And he went up from thence to Beer-sheba.

**26:24**
Zolai: Tua zan mahin ama tungah Topa kilang a, “Kei pen na pa Abraham’ Pasian ka hi hi. Lau kei in; bang hang hiam cih leh ka nasempa Abraham’ huhau-in nang tawh kong om a, nang le na suanlekhakte thupha hong pia-in kong pungsak ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And the LORD appeared unto him the same night, and said, I am the God of Abraham thy father: fear not, for I am with thee, and will bless thee, and multiply thy seed for my servant Abraham's sake.

**26:25**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in tua lai munah biakna tau khat lamin Topa bia a, tua munah puanbuk a lam hi. Tua lai-ah Isaac’ nasemte in tuikhuk khat a to uh hi.
English: And he builded an altar there, and called upon the name of the LORD , and pitched his tent there: and there Isaac's servants digged a well.

**26:26**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Gerar panin Abimelek a thu lamlak pa Ahuzzath le a galkap mangpa Fikol tawh Isaac kiangah hong pai hi.
English: Then Abimelech went to him from Gerar, and Ahuzzath one of his friends, and Phichol the chief captain of his army.

**26:27**
Zolai: Isaac in amaute’ kiangah, “Note in kei hong mudahin note’ kiang panin hong hawlkhia na hih uh ciangin bang hangin kei’ kiangah hong hawh na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Isaac said unto them, Wherefore come ye to me, seeing ye hate me, and have sent me away from you?

**26:28**
Zolai: Amaute in, “Nang tawh Topa a omna teltakin ka mu uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin, kote in nang hong sukha loin, nang’ tungah bangmah hong hih loin, a hoihin gamta-in lungnuam takin kong sawl khiat mah bangun kote’ tungah nang in siatna nong bawl loh nadingin nang le kote’ kikalah kiciamna khat om hen la, nang tawh thuciamna khat bawl ni, a ci hi ung. Nang pen tu-in Topa’ thupha piak na hi hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And they said, We saw certainly that the LORD was with thee: and we said, Let there be now an oath betwixt us, even betwixt us and thee, and let us make a covenant with thee;

**26:30**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in amaute a dingin pawi khat bawl a, amaute in pawi an ne-in a dawn uh hi.
English: And he made them a feast, and they did eat and drink.

**26:31**
Zolai: Zingsangin amaute tho baih uh a, khatlekhat kiciamna a bawl uh hi. Isaac in amaute a lampi ding uhah kha a, ama kiang panin amaute lungnuam takin a paikhia uh hi.
English: And they rose up betimes in the morning, and sware one to another: and Isaac sent them away, and they departed from him in peace.

**26:32**
Zolai: Tua ni mahin Isaac’ nasemte hong pai-in amau’ tawhsa tuikhuk thu ama kiangah hong gen uh a, “Tui ka muzo uh hi,” hong ci uh hi.
English: And it came to pass the same day, that Isaac's servants came, and told him concerning the well which they had digged, and said unto him, We have found water.

**26:33**
Zolai: Amah in tua pen Shibah ci-in min phuak hi. Tua ahih ciangin tua khuapi min pen tuni dongin Beersheba kici hi.
English: And he called it Shebah: therefore the name of the city is Beer-sheba unto this day.

**26:34**
Zolai: Esau kum sawmli a phak ciangin, Hit mi Beeri’ tanu Judith le Hit mi Elon’ tanu Basemath zi-in la hi.
English: And Esau was forty years old when he took to wife Judith the daughter of Beeri the Hittite, and Bashemath the daughter of Elon the Hittite:

**26:35**
Zolai: A zi tegel in Isaac le Rebekah’ nuntakna haksasak uh hi.
English: which were a grief of mind unto Isaac and to Rebekah.

## Chapter 27

**27:1**
Zolai: Isaac teekin a mitte maangin khua a muh theih nawn loh ciangin a ta upa zaw Esau samin ama kiangah, “Ka tapa aw,” a ci hi. Amah in dawngin, “Hiah om ing,” a ci hi.
English: And it came to pass, that when Isaac was old, and his eyes were dim, so that he could not see, he called Esau his eldest son, and said unto him, My son: and he said unto him, Behold, here am I.

**27:2**
Zolai: Amah in, “En in, kei ka teek hi. Ka sih ding hun ka thei kei hi.
English: And he said, Behold now, I am old, I know not the day of my death:

**27:3**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tu-in, na hiamte ahi na thallawng le na thal la inla, gamlakah pai-in kei a dingin sa va beng in.
English: now therefore take, I pray thee, thy weapons, thy quiver and thy bow, and go out to the field, and take me some venison;

**27:4**
Zolai: Ka sih ma-in nang thupha kong piak theih nadingin kei’ duh bangin an lim hong bawl inla, ka nek dingin hong paipih in,” a ci hi.
English: and make me savoury meat, such as I love, and bring it to me, that I may eat; that my soul may bless thee before I die.

**27:5**
Zolai: Isaac in a tapa Esau a hopih laitakin Rebekah in na ngaisim hi. Sa bengin a ciahpih dingin Esau gamlakah a kuan ciangin,
English: And Rebekah heard when Isaac spake to Esau his son. And Esau went to the field to hunt for venison, and to bring it .

**27:6**
Zolai: Rebekah in a tapa Jakob kiangah, “Na sanggampa Esau’ tungah na pa’ thugen ka za a,
English: And Rebekah spake unto Jacob her son, saying, Behold, I heard thy father speak unto Esau thy brother, saying,

**27:7**
Zolai: ‘Ka sih ma-in Topa’ mai-ah nang thupha kong piak theih nadingin ka nek dingin na sa matsa hong paipih inla, kei a dingin an lim hong bawl in,’ ci hi.
English: Bring me venison, and make me savoury meat, that I may eat, and bless thee before the LORD before my death.

**27:8**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tu-in ka ta aw, kong thupiak bangin gamta in.
English: Now therefore, my son, obey my voice according to that which I command thee.

**27:9**
Zolai: Ama duh bangin na pa a dingin an lim ka bawl theih nadingin keelhon lakah va pai inla keelno a hoih nih hong paipih in.
English: Go now to the flock, and fetch me from thence two good kids of the goats; and I will make them savoury meat for thy father, such as he loveth:

**27:10**
Zolai: Na pa in a sih ma-in nang thupha hong piak theih nadingin a nek dingin na pa kiangah na va paipih ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: and thou shalt bring it to thy father, that he may eat, and that he may bless thee before his death.

**27:11**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Jakob in a nu Rebekah kiangah, “En in, ka sanggampa Esau pen mulnei mi hi a, kei pen cineel mi ka hi hi.
English: And Jacob said to Rebekah his mother, Behold, Esau my brother is a hairy man, and I am a smooth man:

**27:12**
Zolai: Ka pa in kei hong lawngkha leh, amah in ka khemna hong thei ding a, kei’ tungah thupha hi loin samsiatna hong tung zawsop ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: my father peradventure will feel me, and I shall seem to him as a deceiver; and I shall bring a curse upon me, and not a blessing.

**27:13**
Zolai: A nu in ama kiangah, “Nangma thuak ding samsiatna kei tungah hong tung ta hen, ka ta aw; ka thu hong mang peuh inla, pai-in keelnote kei’ kiangah hong puak in,” a ci hi.
English: And his mother said unto him, Upon me be thy curse, my son: only obey my voice, and go fetch me them .

**27:14**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah pai-in keelnote va la-in a nu kiangah paipih a, a pa’ duh bangin a nu in an lim a bawl hi.
English: And he went, and fetched, and brought them to his mother: and his mother made savoury meat, such as his father loved.

**27:15**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Rebekah in inn-a a kep, ama ta upa zaw Esau’ puan hoihpente la-in a ta nauzaw Jakob a silhsak hi.
English: And Rebekah took goodly raiment of her eldest son Esau, which were with her in the house, and put them upon Jacob her younger son:

**27:16**
Zolai: Amah in keelnote’ vun ama khut tung le a neelna mun a ngawng sanah silhsak a,
English: and she put the skins of the kids of the goats upon his hands, and upon the smooth of his neck:

**27:17**
Zolai: a bawlsa meh lim le an a tapa Jakob a pia hi.
English: and she gave the savoury meat and the bread, which she had prepared, into the hand of her son Jacob.

**27:18**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin a pa’ kiangah amah pai a, “Ka pa aw,” a ci hi. Amah in, “Hiah om ing, ka ta aw; kua na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And he came unto his father, and said, My father: and he said, Here am I; who art thou, my son?

**27:19**
Zolai: Jakob in a pa kiangah, “Na ta upa zaw Esau ka hi hi. Nong gen bangin ka hih khin hi. Kei thupha nong piak theih nadingin tu-in tuto inla, ka sa matsa ne in,” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob said unto his father, I am Esau thy firstborn; I have done according as thou badest me: arise, I pray thee, sit and eat of my venison, that thy soul may bless me.

**27:20**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Isaac in a tapa’ kiangah, “Ka ta aw, bangci-a hong hici manlan pak na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah in dawngin, “ Topa nangma Pasian in kei hong tuahphasak hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Isaac in Jakob kiangah,
English: And Isaac said unto his son, How is it that thou hast found it so quickly, my son? And he said, Because the LORD thy God brought it to me.

**27:21**
Zolai: “Ka ta aw, ka ta Esau taktak na hi hiam, na hi kei hiam kong lawn theih nadingin ka nai-ah hong pai in,” a ci hi.
English: And Isaac said unto Jacob, Come near, I pray thee, that I may feel thee, my son, whether thou be my very son Esau or not.

**27:22**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a pa Isaac’ kiangah Jakob pai a, amah lawngin, “A aw, Jakob’ aw hi, ahih hangin a khutte, Esau’ khut hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob went near unto Isaac his father; and he felt him, and said, The voice is Jacob's voice, but the hands are the hands of Esau.

**27:23**
Zolai: A khutte in a sanggampa Esau’ khut bangin mul nei ahih manin amah in thei lo hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in thupha pia dingin kithawi a,
English: And he discerned him not, because his hands were hairy, as his brother Esau's hands: so he blessed him.

**27:24**
Zolai: “Ka ta Esau taktak na hi hiam?” ci-in dongkik hi. Amah in dawngin, “Ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Art thou my very son Esau? And he said, I am .

**27:25**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in, “Ka tapa nangma sa matsa ne-in thupha kong piak theih nadingin ka kiangah hong paipih in,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in a kiangah paipih a, amah in a ne hi. Amah in leenggahzu paipihin, amah in a dawn hi.
English: And he said, Bring it near to me, and I will eat of my son's venison, that my soul may bless thee. And he brought it near to him, and he did eat: and he brought him wine, and he drank.

**27:26**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a pa Isaac in ama kiangah, “Ka kiangah hong pai inla hong nam in, ka ta aw,” a ci hi.
English: And his father Isaac said unto him, Come near now, and kiss me, my son.

**27:27**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah a nai-ah hong pai-in a pa a nam hi. Amah in a puan gimnamte nam a, amah thupha pia-in, “En in, ka tapa’ gimnam pen Topa in thupha a piak gamlak gimnam tawh kibang!
English: And he came near, and kissed him: and he smelled the smell of his raiment, and blessed him, and said, See, the smell of my son Is as the smell of a field which the LORD hath blessed:

**27:28**
Zolai: Pasian in na tungah vantung daitui hong pia hen la, na lote hoihsak tahen. An le leenggahzu tampi hong pia tahen.
English: Therefore God give thee of the dew of heaven, And the fatness of the earth, And plenty of corn and wine:

**27:29**
Zolai: Mite in nangma na hong sem hen la, minamte na mai-ah hong kun ta uh hen. Na sanggamte’ tungah topa hi inla, na sanggamte’ suanlekhakte, na mai-ah hong kun uh hen. Nang hong samsia peuhmah in samsiatna ngah hen la, thupha hong pia peuhmah in thupha ngah ta hen,” a ci hi.
English: Let people serve thee, And nations bow down to thee: Be lord over thy brethren, And let thy mother's sons bow down to thee: Cursed be every one that curseth thee, And blessed be he that blesseth thee.

**27:30**
Zolai: Isaac in Jakob thupha a piak a man khit, a pa Isaac’ omna panin Jakob a paikhiat khit phetin, a sa betna panin a sanggampa Esau hong tung hi.
English: And it came to pass, as soon as Isaac had made an end of blessing Jacob, and Jacob was yet scarce gone out from the presence of Isaac his father, that Esau his brother came in from his hunting.

**27:31**
Zolai: Amah in zong an lim bawlin a pa’ kiangah hong paipih hi. Amah in a pa’ kiangah, “Thupha nong piak theih nadingin na tapa’ sa matsa a ne dingin ka pa hong tho in,” a ci hi.
English: And he also had made savoury meat, and brought it unto his father, and said unto his father, Let my father arise, and eat of his son's venison, that thy soul may bless me.

**27:32**
Zolai: A pa Isaac in ama kiangah, “Kua na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah in dawngin, “Kei pen na tapa, a suak masa Esau ka hi hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Isaac his father said unto him, Who art thou? And he said, I am thy son, thy firstborn Esau.

**27:33**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Isaac nakpitakin lingin, “Tua ahihleh, nang’ hong pai ma-in sa matsa hong paipihin, a vekin ka nek khit, amah thupha ka piakpa kua ahi hiam? Thupha pia khin ka hih manin amah in thupha ngah ding hi” a ci hi.
English: And Isaac trembled very exceedingly, and said, Who? where is he that hath taken venison, and brought it me, and I have eaten of all before thou camest, and have blessed him? yea, and he shall be blessed.

**27:34**
Zolai: Esau in a pa’ kammalte a zak ciangin nakpi tak le nasia takin kikokhia-in a pa’ kiangah, “Kei thupha hong pia in, kei zong, aw ka pa!” a ci hi.
English: And when Esau heard the words of his father, he cried with a great and exceeding bitter cry, and said unto his father, Bless me, even me also, O my father.

**27:35**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah in, “Khemna tawh na sanggampa hong pai-in amah in na thupha lakhia khinta hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Thy brother came with subtilty, and hath taken away thy blessing.

**27:36**
Zolai: Esau in, “Amah Jakob kici mah hi lo ahi hiam? Amah in kei nihvei hong suankhia khin hi. Amah in ka innluahza hong sut hi. En in, tu-in amah in ka thupha hong sut leuleu hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Kei a dingin thupha siit lo na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Is not he rightly named Jacob? for he hath supplanted me these two times: he took away my birthright; and, behold, now he hath taken away my blessing. And he said, Hast thou not reserved a blessing for me?

**27:37**
Zolai: Isaac in Esau dawngin, “En in, amah nangma’ topa-in ka bawl khin a, a sanggamte khempeuh ama tungah nasemin ka pia khin a, an le leenggahzu tawh amah ka hingsak hi. Tua ahih ciangin ka ta aw, nang a dingin bang hih thei nawn ding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Isaac answered and said unto Esau, Behold, I have made him thy lord, and all his brethren have I given to him for servants; and with corn and wine have I sustained him: and what shall I do now unto thee, my son?

**27:38**
Zolai: Esau in a pa’ kiangah, “Pa aw, thupha khat beek nei nawn lo na hi hiam? Kei thupha hong pia in, kei zong, ka pa aw,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Esau a kap hi.
English: And Esau said unto his father, Hast thou but one blessing, my father? bless me, even me also, O my father. And Esau lifted up his voice, and wept.

**27:39**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a pa Isaac in, “En in, leitung pana piang an le leenggahzu na nei kei ding a, na lo a dingin vantung daituite na ngah kei ding hi.
English: And Isaac his father answered and said unto him, Behold, thy dwelling shall be the fatness of the earth, And of the dew of heaven from above;

**27:40**
Zolai: Na namsau tawh na nungta ding a, na sanggampa’ na na sem ding hi. Ahih hangin amah na langpan’ ciangin ama khutnuai panin na leengkhia ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And by thy sword shalt thou live, and shalt serve thy brother; And it shall come to pass when thou shalt have the dominion, That thou shalt break his yoke from off thy neck.

**27:41**
Zolai: A pa in amah thupha pia khin ahih manin tua thupha hangin tu-in Esau in Jakob mudah a, Esau in, “Ka pa’ sihna hangin dah nading hun hong nai ta hi. Tua khit ciangin ka sanggampa Jakob ka that ding hi,” ci-in ngaihsun hi.
English: And Esau hated Jacob because of the blessing wherewith his father blessed him: and Esau said in his heart, The days of mourning for my father are at hand; then will I slay my brother Jacob.

**27:42**
Zolai: Ahih hangin a tapa upa zaw Esau’ ngimna, Rebekah’ tungah kigen hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in a ta nauzaw Jakob samin ama kiangah, “En in, na sanggampa Esau in nangmah thah ding vaihawmna tawh amah kihehnem hi.
English: And these words of Esau her elder son were told to Rebekah: and she sent and called Jacob her younger son, and said unto him, Behold, thy brother Esau, as touching thee, doth comfort himself, purposing to kill thee.

**27:43**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tu-in ka ta aw, ka thu hong mang in. Haran-a ka sanggampa Laban’ kiangah va tai inla,
English: Now therefore, my son, obey my voice; and arise, flee thou to Laban my brother to Haran;

**27:44**
Zolai: na sanggampa’ hehna a dam mateng tua lai ama kiangah tawlkhat sung va om in.
English: and tarry with him a few days, until thy brother's fury turn away;

**27:45**
Zolai: Na sanggampa’ sinsona a daih mateng, ama tunga na gamtatna a mangngilh mateng va om in. Tua ciangin mi hong sawlin hih lai munah nang kong lasak ding hi. Bang hangin no tegel tawh nikhat thu-in kei kikhen ding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: until thy brother's anger turn away from thee, and he forget that which thou hast done to him: then I will send, and fetch thee from thence: why should I be deprived also of you both in one day?

**27:46**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Rebekah in Isaac kiangah, “Esau’ zi Hit numeite’ hangin ka lung gimin ka cimtak hi. Jakob in hih gam numeite khat ahi Hit numeite khat tenpih leh kei a dingin bang nuntak tham nawn ding ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Rebekah said to Isaac, I am weary of my life because of the daughters of Heth: if Jacob take a wife of the daughters of Heth, such as these which are of the daughters of the land, what good shall my life do me?

## Chapter 28

**28:1**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Isaac in Jakob sam a, amah thupha pia-in thuhilh a, “Nang in Kanaan numeite na tenpih kei ding hi.
English: And Isaac called Jacob, and blessed him, and charged him, and said unto him, Thou shalt not take a wife of the daughters of Canaan.

**28:2**
Zolai: Kithawi inla, na nu’ pa Bethuel’ inn, Paddanaram-ah pai in. Tua lai munah na nu’ sanggampa Laban’ tanute khat na zi dingin la in.
English: Arise, go to Padan-aram, to the house of Bethuel thy mother's father; and take thee a wife from thence of the daughters of Laban thy mother's brother.

**28:3**
Zolai: Nang, mihonpi khat na suah theih nadingin Vanglian Pasian in nang thupha hong pia-in, hong pungsakin, tampi hong phasak hen.
English: And God Almighty bless thee, and make thee fruitful, and multiply thee, that thou mayest be a multitude of people;

**28:4**
Zolai: Pasian in Abraham’ tunga a piak, tawlkhat sung na omna leitang na neih theih nadingin nang le na suanlekhakte tungah amah in Abraham’ thupha hong pia ta hen!” a ci hi.
English: and give thee the blessing of Abraham, to thee, and to thy seed with thee; that thou mayest inherit the land wherein thou art a stranger, which God gave unto Abraham.

**28:5**
Zolai: Tua bangin Isaac in Jakob sawlkhia hi. Jakob le Esau’ nu Rebekah’ sanggampa, Aram mi Bethuel’ tapa Laban’ omna Paddanaram-ah amah a pai hi.
English: And Isaac sent away Jacob: and he went to Padan-aram unto Laban, son of Bethuel the Syrian, the brother of Rebekah, Jacob's and Esau's mother.

**28:6**
Zolai: Isaac in Jakob thupha pia-in, zi la dingin Paddanaram-ah sawl a, thupha a piak kawmin amah thuhilhin, “Kanaan numeite na tenpih kei ding hi,” a cihna le,
English: When Esau saw that Isaac had blessed Jacob, and sent him away to Padan-aram, to take him a wife from thence; and that as he blessed him he gave him a charge, saying, Thou shalt not take a wife of the daughters of Canaan;

**28:7**
Zolai: Jakob in a nu le a pa’ thu mangin Paddanaram-ah a paina thu tu-in Esau in thei hi.
English: and that Jacob obeyed his father and his mother, and was gone to Padan-aram;

**28:8**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Kanaan numeite in a pa lungkimsak lo cih Esau in a theih ciangin,
English: and Esau seeing that the daughters of Canaan pleased not Isaac his father;

**28:9**
Zolai: Ishmael’ kiangah Esau pai-in, ama zi neihsa banah, Nebaioth’ sanggamnu, Abraham’ tapa Ishmael’ tanu Mahalath zi-in a la hi.
English: then went Esau unto Ishmael, and took unto the wives which he had Mahalath the daughter of Ishmael Abraham's son, the sister of Nebajoth, to be his wife.

**28:10**
Zolai: Jakob in Beersheba khua nusia-in Haran lamah a pai hi.
English: And Jacob went out from Beer-sheba, and went toward Haran.

**28:11**
Zolai: Amah mun khat tungin, ni tum khin ahih manin tua lai-ah tua zan a giak hi. Tua mun a suangte khat la-in, amah in lukhamin zang a, a ihmu dingin tua munah a lumsuk hi.
English: And he lighted upon a certain place, and tarried there all night, because the sun was set; and he took of the stones of that place, and put them for his pillows, and lay down in that place to sleep.

**28:12**
Zolai: Amah in mang man a, leitungah kahlei khat kiphutin, a kahlei dawn in van ban hi. Pasian’ vantung mite tua kahlei tungah kah to-in a kum suk a mu hi.
English: And he dreamed, and behold a ladder set up on the earth, and the top of it reached to heaven: and behold the angels of God ascending and descending on it.

**28:13**
Zolai: En in, tua sanah Topa ding a, “Kei pen na pa Abraham’ Pasian le Isaac’ Pasian, Topa ka hi hi. Nang le na suanlekhakte’ tungah tu-a na lupna leitang kong pia ding hi.
English: And, behold, the LORD stood above it, and said, I am the LORD God of Abraham thy father, and the God of Isaac: the land whereon thou liest, to thee will I give it, and to thy seed;

**28:14**
Zolai: Na suanlekhakte leilak leivui zah pha ding a, nitumna lam le nisuahna lam, leilu lam le leitaw lamah na kizelthang ding uh hi. Nang le na suanlekhakte thupha kong piak bangin leitung minam khempeuh in thupha a ngah nadingun hong ngen ding uh hi.
English: and thy seed shall be as the dust of the earth, and thou shalt spread abroad to the west, and to the east, and to the north, and to the south: and in thee and in thy seed shall all the families of the earth be blessed.

**28:15**
Zolai: En in, keimah in nang hong ompihin na paina peuhah kong kem ding a, hih leitangah nang kong paipih kik ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh nang’ tunga kong gensa thute ka hih khit matengin nang kong nusia kei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And, behold, I am with thee, and will keep thee in all places whither thou goest, and will bring thee again into this land; for I will not leave thee, until I have done that which I have spoken to thee of.

**28:16**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a ihmutna panin Jakob khang lo a, “Hih lai munah Topa om taktak hi; keimah in tua thu ka thei kei hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob awaked out of his sleep, and he said, Surely the LORD is in this place; and I knew it not.

**28:17**
Zolai: Amah lau a, “Hih mun bangzahin lauhuai ahi hiam! Hih pen Pasian’ inn lo adang hi lo a, hih pen vantung lutna kongpi ahi hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he was afraid, and said, How dreadful is this place! this is none other but the house of God, and this is the gate of heaven.

**28:18**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin zingsangin Jakob tho baih a, amah in lukhamin a zat suang la-in khuamin phut a, a tungah sathau a sung hi.
English: And Jacob rose up early in the morning, and took the stone that he had put for his pillows, and set it up for a pillar, and poured oil upon the top of it.

**28:19**
Zolai: Amah in tua mun Bethel ci hi. Ahih hangin a masa-in tua khua min pen Luz ahi hi.
English: And he called the name of that place Beth-el: but the name of that city was called Luz at the first.

**28:20**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in thuciamna khat bawlin, “Pasian in kei hong ompih a, hih ka paina lampi-ah kei hong kep a, nek ding an le silh ding puan hong piak a,
English: And Jacob vowed a vow, saying, If God will be with me, and will keep me in this way that I go, and will give me bread to eat, and raiment to put on,

**28:21**
Zolai: lungnuam takin ka pa’ inn-ah ka ciahkik leh, Topa pen keima Pasian hi ding a,
English: so that I come again to my father's house in peace; then shall the LORD be my God:

**28:22**
Zolai: khuamin ka phuhsa hih suang pen Pasian’ inn hi ding hi. Keima tungah nangmah in nong piak khempeuh sawm-ah-khat nang’ tungah kong pia kik ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: and this stone, which I have set for a pillar, shall be God's house: and of all that thou shalt give me I will surely give the tenth unto thee.

## Chapter 29

**29:1**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in a khualzinna zom a, nisuahna lam mite’ gam a tung hi.
English: Then Jacob went on his journey, and came into the land of the people of the east.

**29:2**
Zolai: A khuadak leh gamlakah tuikhuk khat a mu hi. Tua gei-ah tuuhon thum na lum hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh tua tuikhuk panin tuuhonte tui kipia hi. Tuikhuk gong hukna suang lian hi.
English: And he looked, and behold a well in the field, and, lo, there were three flocks of sheep lying by it; for out of that well they watered the flocks: and a great stone was upon the well's mouth.

**29:3**
Zolai: Tua lai munah tuuhonte khempeuh a kikaihkhop khit ciangin, tuucingte in tuikhuk gong panin a suang khukkhia uh a, tuute tui pia-in, tuikhuk gong ama omna ngei-ah a suang koih kik uh hi.
English: And thither were all the flocks gathered: and they rolled the stone from the well's mouth, and watered the sheep, and put the stone again upon the well's mouth in his place.

**29:4**
Zolai: Jakob in amaute kiangah, “Sanggamte aw, koi pana hong pai na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi. Amaute in, “Haran pan hi ung,” ci uh hi.
English: And Jacob said unto them, My brethren, whence be ye? And they said, Of Haran are we.

**29:5**
Zolai: Amah in amaute kiangah, “Nahor’ tapa Laban na thei uh hiam?” a ci hi. Amaute in, “Thei mah ung,” a ci uh hi.
English: And he said unto them, Know ye Laban the son of Nahor? And they said, We know him .

**29:6**
Zolai: Amah in amaute kiangah, “Amah a cidam hiam?” a ci hi. Amaute in, “Dam hi; en in, a tanu Rachel zong a tuuhon tawh hong pai!” a ci uh hi.
English: And he said unto them, Is he well? And they said, He is well: and, behold, Rachel his daughter cometh with the sheep.

**29:7**
Zolai: Amah in, “En un, ni sang lai a, gan kaihkhop hun nai lo hi. Tuute tui pia unla, pai-in an nesak lai un,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Lo, it is yet high day, neither is it time that the cattle should be gathered together: water ye the sheep, and go and feed them .

**29:8**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amaute in, “Tuute kikaikhawm a, tuikhuk gong panin a suang a kikhuk khiat mateng tui ka pia thei kei uh hi. A kikhuk khiat khit ciang bekin tuute tui ka pia thei pan uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And they said, We cannot, until all the flocks be gathered together, and till they roll the stone from the well's mouth; then we water the sheep.

**29:9**
Zolai: Tua bangin amaute tawh a kiho laitakin, Rachel a pa’ tuute tawh hong tung hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in tuate kem hi.
English: And while he yet spake with them, Rachel came with her father's sheep: for she kept them.

**29:10**
Zolai: Tu-in Jakob in a nu’ sanggampa Laban’ tanu Rachel le a nu’ sanggampa Laban’ tuute a muh ciangin paito-in tuikhuk gong panin a suang khukkhia a, a nu’ sanggampa Laban’ tuute tui a pia hi.
English: And it came to pass, when Jacob saw Rachel the daughter of Laban his mother's brother, and the sheep of Laban his mother's brother, that Jacob went near, and rolled the stone from the well's mouth, and watered the flock of Laban his mother's brother.

**29:11**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in Rachel nam a, a gingin kapkhia hi.
English: And Jacob kissed Rachel, and lifted up his voice, and wept.

**29:12**
Zolai: Jakob in Rachel’ kiangah amah pen a pa’ behte hi a, Rebekah’ tapa ahihna zong a kigen hi. Tua ciangin Rachel tai-in a pa’ kiangah a gen hi.
English: And Jacob told Rachel that he was her father's brother, and that he was Rebekah's son: and she ran and told her father.

**29:13**
Zolai: Laban in a sanggamnu’ tapa Jakob’ thu a zak ciangin amah a dawn dingin hong tai a, amah kawi-in nam a, a inn-ah a ciahpih hi. Jakob in Laban’ tungah a thute khempeuh gen a,
English: And it came to pass, when Laban heard the tidings of Jacob his sister's son, that he ran to meet him, and embraced him, and kissed him, and brought him to his house. And he told Laban all these things.

**29:14**
Zolai: Laban in ama kiangah, “Nang pen keima si keima sa na hi takpi hi,” a ci hi. Tua hi a, amah tawh kha khat a omkhawm hi.
English: And Laban said to him, Surely thou art my bone and my flesh. And he abode with him the space of a month.

**29:15**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Laban in Jakob’ kiangah, “Nang pen keima beh na hih ciangin, a man nei lopi-in kei’ na hong sem ding na hi hiam? Hong gen in; na thaman ding bang hi ding hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Laban said unto Jacob, Because thou art my brother, shouldest thou therefore serve me for nought? tell me, what shall thy wages be ?

**29:16**
Zolai: Tu-in Laban in tanu nih nei hi. A uzaw’ min Leah hi a, a nauzaw’ min Rachel ahi hi.
English: And Laban had two daughters: the name of the elder was Leah, and the name of the younger was Rachel.

**29:17**
Zolai: Leah’ mit-hah nem a, ahih hangin Rachel melhoihin ngaihbaang hi.
English: Leah was tender eyed; but Rachel was beautiful and well favoured.

**29:18**
Zolai: Jakob in Rachel ngai hi. Amah in, “Na tanu a nauzaw Rachel thalawh nadingin nangma na kum sagih kong sem ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob loved Rachel; and said, I will serve thee seven years for Rachel thy younger daughter.

**29:19**
Zolai: Laban in, “Midang tungah amah ka piak ding sangin nang’ tungah amah kong piak ding hoihzaw hi; kei kiangah om in,” a ci hi.
English: And Laban said, It is better that I give her to thee, than that I should give her to another man: abide with me.

**29:20**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Jakob in Rachel a ngah nadingin kum sagih sung na sem a, amah a itna hangin tua hunte ni tawmno khat tawh kibang a sa hi.
English: And Jacob served seven years for Rachel; and they seemed unto him but a few days, for the love he had to her.

**29:21**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in Laban kiangah, “Ka hun cingta ahih ciangin amah tawh ka lupkhawm theih nadingin ka zi hong pia in,” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob said unto Laban, Give me my wife, for my days are fulfilled, that I may go in unto her.

**29:22**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Laban in tua mun a mi khempeuh kaikhawmin pawi khat a bawl hi.
English: And Laban gathered together all the men of the place, and made a feast.

**29:23**
Zolai: Ahih hangin a nitak ciangin amah in a tanu Leah la-in Jakob kiangah paipih hi. Amah in tua nu luppih hi.
English: And it came to pass in the evening, that he took Leah his daughter, and brought her to him; and he went in unto her.

**29:24**
Zolai: (Laban in ama numei nasem Zilpah a tanu Leah tungah a nasem numei dingin a pia hi.)
English: And Laban gave unto his daughter Leah Zilpah his maid for an handmaid.

**29:25**
Zolai: A zingsang ciangin, Leah na hi mawk hi. Jakob in Laban kiangah, “Bangci a kei hong hici bawl na hi hiam? Rachel ngah nadingin na na hong sem hi lo ka hi hiam? Tua ahihleh bang hangin kei hong khem na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And it came to pass, that in the morning, behold, it was Leah: and he said to Laban, What is this thou hast done unto me? did not I serve with thee for Rachel? wherefore then hast thou beguiled me?

**29:26**
Zolai: Laban in, “A u’ ma-in a nauzaw piak ding ko’ gamah ngeina hi lo hi.
English: And Laban said, It must not be so done in our country, to give the younger before the firstborn.

**29:27**
Zolai: Hih nu a dingin nipikal khat sung pawi beisak phot inla, adang kum sagih ka na nong sepsak thamanin a khat pen zong kong pia ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: Fulfil her week, and we will give thee this also for the service which thou shalt serve with me yet seven other years.

**29:28**
Zolai: Jakob zong tua bangmahin gamta a, tua nu’ pawi hun sung beisak phot hi. Tua ciangin Laban in a tanu Rachel zong a zi dingin a pia hi.
English: And Jacob did so, and fulfilled her week: and he gave him Rachel his daughter to wife also.

**29:29**
Zolai: (Laban in ama nasem numei Bilhah a tanu Rachel’ tungah a nasem numei dingin a pia hi.)
English: And Laban gave to Rachel his daughter Bilhah his handmaid to be her maid.

**29:30**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Jakob in Rachel zong luppih a, amah in Leah sangin Rachel itzaw hi. Laban’ na adang kum sagih sung a semlai hi.
English: And he went in also unto Rachel, and he loved also Rachel more than Leah, and served with him yet seven other years.

**29:31**
Zolai: Topa in Leah a kimuhdahna a theih ciangin, amah in a naubu honsak hi; ahih hangin Rachel ciing hi.
English: And when the LORD saw that Leah was hated, he opened her womb: but Rachel was barren.

**29:32**
Zolai: Leah gai-in tapa khat nei a, amah in a min Reuben a phuak hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in, “ Topa in ka thuakna hong muzo hi; tu-in ka pasal in kei hong it taktak ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Leah conceived, and bare a son, and she called his name Reuben: for she said, Surely the LORD hath looked upon my affliction; now therefore my husband will love me.

**29:33**
Zolai: Amah gai kikin tapa khat nei a, amah in, “Keimah hong kimuhdahna thu Topa in za khin ahih manin, amah in hih tapa zong hong pia hi,” ci hi. Amah in a min Simeon a phuak hi.
English: And she conceived again, and bare a son; and said, Because the LORD hath heard that I was hated, he hath therefore given me this son also: and she called his name Simeon.

**29:34**
Zolai: Amah gai leuleu-in tapa khat nei a, “Amah tawh tapa thum nei ta ka hih manin tu-in ka pasal in kei hong pawl ding hi,” ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama min Levi a phuak hi.
English: And she conceived again, and bare a son; and said, Now this time will my husband be joined unto me, because I have born him three sons: therefore was his name called Levi.

**29:35**
Zolai: Amah gai leuleu-in tapa khat nei a, “Tuhunin Topa ka phat ding hi,” ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in a min Judah a phuak hi. Tua ciangin a ta neih a tawp hi.
English: And she conceived again, and bare a son: and she said, Now will I praise the LORD : therefore she called his name Judah; and left bearing.

## Chapter 30

**30:1**
Zolai: Rachel in Jakob tawh ta a neih lohna a kimuh ciangin, amah in a sanggamnu eng hi. Amah in Jakob kiangah, “Ta hong pia in, tua ahih kei leh si ning!” a ci hi.
English: And when Rachel saw that she bare Jacob no children, Rachel envied her sister; and said unto Jacob, Give me children, or else I die.

**30:2**
Zolai: Rachel’ tungah Jakob heh mahmah a, amah in, “Nang’ tungah ta hong pia lo Pasian’ munah om ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob's anger was kindled against Rachel: and he said, Am I in God's stead, who hath withheld from thee the fruit of the womb?

**30:3**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in, “Hih lai-ah ka nasem numei Bilhah om hi. Ka phei tungah ka tawi ding ta hong neih nading, le ama sung panin suanlekhak ka neih theih nadingin amah tawh lumkhawm in,” a ci hi.
English: And she said, Behold my maid Bilhah, go in unto her; and she shall bear upon my knees, that I may also have children by her.

**30:4**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin a nasem numei Bilhah ama tungah zi-in a pia hi. Jakob in tua nu luppih hi.
English: And she gave him Bilhah her handmaid to wife: and Jacob went in unto her.

**30:5**
Zolai: Bilhah gai-in Jakob tawh tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Bilhah conceived, and bare Jacob a son.

**30:6**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Rachel in, “Pasian in kei’ thu a hoihin hong khen zo a, amah in ka aw zong za zo-in tapa khat hong pia hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in a min Dan a phuak hi.
English: And Rachel said, God hath judged me, and hath also heard my voice, and hath given me a son: therefore called she his name Dan.

**30:7**
Zolai: Rachel’ nasem numei Bilhah gai kikin Jakob tawh tapa a nihna nei hi.
English: And Bilhah Rachel's maid conceived again, and bare Jacob a second son.

**30:8**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Rachel in, “Nakpi takin hanciamna tawh ka sanggamnu ka zo hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama min Naftali a phuak hi.
English: And Rachel said, With great wrestlings have I wrestled with my sister, and I have prevailed: and she called his name Naphtali.

**30:9**
Zolai: Leah in ta neih a tawplam a kimuh ciangin, amah in a nasem numei Zilpah la-in Jakob’ tungah zi-in a pia hi.
English: When Leah saw that she had left bearing, she took Zilpah her maid, and gave her Jacob to wife.

**30:10**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Leah’ nasem numei Zilpah in Jakob tawh tapa khat nei hi.
English: And Zilpah Leah's maid bare Jacob a son.

**30:11**
Zolai: Leah in, “Kaam pha!” ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama min Gad a phuak hi.
English: And Leah said, A troop cometh: and she called his name Gad.

**30:12**
Zolai: Leah’ nasem numei Zilpah in Jakob tawh tapa a nihna nei hi.
English: And Zilpah Leah's maid bare Jacob a second son.

**30:13**
Zolai: Leah in, “Kei lungdam ing! Bang hang hiam cih leh numei dangte in kei a lungdam hong ci ding uh hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama min Asher a phuak hi.
English: And Leah said, Happy am I, for the daughters will call me blessed: and she called his name Asher.

**30:14**
Zolai: Mangbuh lak hun laitakin gamlakah Reuben pai-in zawl-ai kungte va mu a, tuate a nu Leah’ kiangah a ciahpih hi. Tua ciangin Rachel in Leah kiangah, “Na tapa’ zawl-ai kungte kimkhat kei hong hawm in, hong thum ing,” a ci hi.
English: And Reuben went in the days of wheat harvest, and found mandrakes in the field, and brought them unto his mother Leah. Then Rachel said to Leah, Give me, I pray thee, of thy son's mandrakes.

**30:15**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Leah in, “Ka pasal nong suh thuneu sa na hi hiam? Ka tapa’ zawl-ai kungte zong hong sut lai ding na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Rachel in, “Tua ahihleh na tapa’ zawl-ai man dingin tuzanin amah, nang tawh hong lumkhawm thei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And she said unto her, Is it a small matter that thou hast taken my husband? and wouldest thou take away my son's mandrakes also? And Rachel said, Therefore he shall lie with thee to night for thy son's mandrakes.

**30:16**
Zolai: Nitakin lo panin Jakob hong ciah ciangin, amah a dawn dingin Leah paikhia a, “Kei’ kiangah hong lum in. Bang hang hiam cih leh ka tapa’ zawl-ai kungte tawh nang kong cial zo hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin tua zan amah tawh a lumkhawm hi.
English: And Jacob came out of the field in the evening, and Leah went out to meet him, and said, Thou must come in unto me; for surely I have hired thee with my son's mandrakes. And he lay with her that night.

**30:17**
Zolai: Pasian in Leah’ thu ngai a, amah gai-in Jakob tawh tapa a ngana a nei hi.
English: And God hearkened unto Leah, and she conceived, and bare Jacob the fifth son.

**30:18**
Zolai: Leah in, “Ka nasem numei ka pasal tungah pia ka hih manin Pasian in ka thacial hong pia hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama min Issakhar a phuak hi.
English: And Leah said, God hath given me my hire, because I have given my maiden to my husband: and she called his name Issachar.

**30:19**
Zolai: Leah gai kik a, Jakob tawh tapa a gukna a nei hi.
English: And Leah conceived again, and bare Jacob the sixth son.

**30:20**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Leah in, “Pasian in moken’ hoih kei hong guan hi. Tu-in ka pasal in kei hong pahtawi ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah tawh tapa guk ka nei khin hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama min Zebulun a phuak hi.
English: And Leah said, God hath endued me with a good dowry; now will my husband dwell with me, because I have born him six sons: and she called his name Zebulun.

**30:21**
Zolai: Tua khit ciangin amah in tanu khat nei a, a min Dinah a phuak hi.
English: And afterwards she bare a daughter, and called her name Dinah.

**30:22**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Pasian in Rachel phawk a, Pasian in ama thu ngai-in a naubu honsak hi.
English: And God remembered Rachel, and God hearkened to her, and opened her womb.

**30:23**
Zolai: Amah gai-in tapa khat nei a, “Pasian in kei hong kikona teng lakhia khinta hi,” a ci hi.
English: And she conceived, and bare a son; and said, God hath taken away my reproach:

**30:24**
Zolai: Amah in a min Josef phuak a, “ Topa in tapa khat hong pia beh hen!” a ci hi.
English: and she called his name Joseph; and said, The LORD shall add to me another son.

**30:25**
Zolai: Rachel in Josef a neih khit ciangin, Jakob in Laban’ kiangah, “Keima inn le ka gamah ka ciahkik theih nadingin kei hong sawl in.
English: And it came to pass, when Rachel had born Joseph, that Jacob said unto Laban, Send me away, that I may go unto mine own place, and to my country.

**30:26**
Zolai: Nang’ tunga kong thalawhsa ka zite le ka tate hong pia inla, hong paisak in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nangma na kong sepsaksa na thei hi,” a ci hi.
English: Give me my wives and my children, for whom I have served thee, and let me go: for thou knowest my service which I have done thee.

**30:27**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Laban in ama kiangah, “Kei, thu hong gensak dih in. Topa in nangma hangin kei thupha hong piakna ka thei hi.
English: And Laban said unto him, I pray thee, if I have found favour in thine eyes, tarry: for I have learned by experience that the LORD hath blessed me for thy sake.

**30:28**
Zolai: Na thaman ding hong gen lecin kong pia ding hi,” a ci hi.
