English: And he said, Appoint me thy wages, and I will give it .

**30:29**
Zolai: Jakob in ama kiangah, “Nangma na kong sepsak khitna le keima kep sungin na ganhingte tampi a phakna nangmahmah in na thei hi.
English: And he said unto him, Thou knowest how I have served thee, and how thy cattle was with me.

**30:30**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh kei kong pai ma-in nang in tawm bek na nei a, tu-in tampi takin a khang hi. Ka sepna peuhah Topa in nang thupha hong pia hi. Ahih hangin tu-in keima innkuan a’ ding cik ciangin ke’n vaihawm ding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: For it was little which thou hadst before I came , and it is now increased unto a multitude; and the LORD hath blessed thee since my coming: and now when shall I provide for mine own house also?

**30:31**
Zolai: Amah in, “Nang bang hong pia ding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi. Jakob in, “Bangmah dang nong pia kei ding hi. Hih bangin nong hih nakleh na tuuhonte vak kikin ka kem ding hi.
English: And he said, What shall I give thee? And Jacob said, Thou shalt not give me any thing: if thou wilt do this thing for me, I will again feed and keep thy flock.

**30:32**
Zolai: Tuni-in na tuuhonte khempeuh lakah hong paisak inla, tua sung panin tuu a puang le a gial khempeuh, le tuuno a vom khempeuh le keel lak panin a gial le a puang khempeuh hong khenkhiasak in; tuate keima thaman hi ding hi.
English: I will pass through all thy flock to day, removing from thence all the speckled and spotted cattle, and all the brown cattle among the sheep, and the spotted and speckled among the goats: and of such shall be my hire.

**30:33**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin nang’ tung pana ka thaman a en dingin nong pai ciangin ka thumanna na hong nung muh ding hi. Keel lakah a puang lo le a gial lo peuhmah le tuuno lakah a vom lo peuhmah, kei kiangah a kimuh zenzen leh, guk-in kiseh pah ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: So shall my righteousness answer for me in time to come, when it shall come for my hire before thy face: every one that is not speckled and spotted among the goats, and brown among the sheep, that shall be counted stolen with me.

**30:34**
Zolai: Laban in, “Hoih hi! Na cihsa bangin hisak ni,” a ci hi.
English: And Laban said, Behold, I would it might be according to thy word.

**30:35**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Laban in tua ni-in keeltal a dung gial le a bem gialte, keelpi a puang le a gialte, a tungah a kang mun a om khempeuh le tuuno a vom khempeuh la khia-in, ama tapate’ kep dingin tuate a koih hi.
English: And he removed that day the he goats that were ringstraked and spotted, and all the she goats that were speckled and spotted, and every one that had some white in it, and all the brown among the sheep, and gave them into the hand of his sons.

**30:36**
Zolai: Jakob’ kiang panin ni thum paina gamlapi-ah tua ganhonte a paipih hi. Jakob in Laban’ ganhon a omlai teng an a vak hi.
English: And he set three days' journey betwixt himself and Jacob: and Jacob fed the rest of Laban's flocks.

**30:37**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in poplar kung, almond kung, le hiangpa kungte tung pan ciangkhut ding a thak satin la a, a ciangkhutte a kang mun a om dingin kheh a, a ciangkang kangte kidawksak hi.
English: And Jacob took him rods of green poplar, and of the hazel and chesnut tree; and pilled white strakes in them, and made the white appear which was in the rods.

**30:38**
Zolai: Amah in a khehsa ciangkangte tuiluang, tuipiakna tuikuang, tuuhonte tui dawn dingin a hong paina mun, tuuhonte’ mai-ah a koih hi. Amaute tui dawn dingin hong pai uh ciangin a nu le a pa omkhawm uh ahih manin,
English: And he set the rods which he had pilled before the flocks in the gutters in the watering troughs when the flocks came to drink, that they should conceive when they came to drink.

**30:39**
Zolai: tuuhonte tua ciangkangte’ mai-ah omkhawm uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin tuuhonte in a dung gial, a puang le a gial ta nei uh hi.
English: And the flocks conceived before the rods, and brought forth cattle ringstraked, speckled, and spotted.

**30:40**
Zolai: Jakob in tuunote khenkhia a, tuuhonte’ maitang pen a dung gialte le Laban’ tuuhon sunga a vomte khempeuh’ lam ngasak hi. Amah in ama a’ honte a tuamin koihkhia-in, Laban’ tuuhonte tawh koihkhawm lo hi.
English: And Jacob did separate the lambs, and set the faces of the flocks toward the ringstraked, and all the brown in the flock of Laban; and he put his own flocks by themselves, and put them not unto Laban's cattle.

**30:41**
Zolai: Tuuhon sung panin a thahat zawte a huk ciangin, amaute tua ciangkangte lakah a gai theih nadingin Jakob in tuuhonte’ muhna, tuiluang sungah a ciangkangte a koih hi.
English: And it came to pass, whensoever the stronger cattle did conceive, that Jacob laid the rods before the eyes of the cattle in the gutters, that they might conceive among the rods.

**30:42**
Zolai: Ahih hangin tuuhon a ginalote’ mai-ah tua ciangkangte koih lo hi. Tua ahih ciangin a ginalo zawte Laban a’ hi a, a thahat zawte Jakob-a’ ahi hi.
English: But when the cattle were feeble, he put them not in: so the feebler were Laban's, and the stronger Jacob's.

**30:43**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Jakob a hauhna nakpitakin khang a, tuuhon lianpi, nasem numei, nasem pasal, kalaoh, le late a nei hi.
English: And the man increased exceedingly, and had much cattle, and maidservants, and menservants, and camels, and asses.

## Chapter 31

**31:1**
Zolai: Laban’ tapate in, “Jakob in i pa-a’ khempeuh la khin a, i pa’ neihsa tung panin amah in hih hauhna ngah hi,” a cihna thu tu-in Jakob in za hi.
English: And he heard the words of Laban's sons, saying, Jacob hath taken away all that was our father's; and of that which was our father's hath he gotten all this glory.

**31:2**
Zolai: Laban in nidang bangin maipha tawh amah a don lohna Jakob in mu hi.
English: And Jacob beheld the countenance of Laban, and, behold, it was not toward him as before.

**31:3**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Topa in Jakob’ kiangah, “Na pate le na behte’ gamah ciahkik in, nang kong ompih ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And the LORD said unto Jacob, Return unto the land of thy fathers, and to thy kindred; and I will be with thee.

**31:4**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Jakob in mi sawlin ama tuuhon a omna gamlakah Rachel le Leah samsakin
English: And Jacob sent and called Rachel and Leah to the field unto his flock,

**31:5**
Zolai: amaute kiangah, “Na pa un nidang bangin maipha tawh kei hong don lohna ka mu hi. Ahih hangin ka pa’ Pasian in kei hong ompih hi.
English: and said unto them, I see your father's countenance, that it is not toward me as before; but the God of my father hath been with me.

**31:6**
Zolai: Ka tha neih khempeuh tawh na pa’ na ka sepna na thei uh hi.
English: And ye know that with all my power I have served your father.

**31:7**
Zolai: Ahi zongin na pa un kei hong khemin, ka thaman sawmvei khelkhin a, ahih hangin kei hong gimsak ding Pasian in phal lo hi.
English: And your father hath deceived me, and changed my wages ten times; but God suffered him not to hurt me.

**31:8**
Zolai: Amah in, ‘A gialte na thaman hi ding hi,’ ci leh tua ciangin tuuhon khempeuh in a gial ta hong nei hi. Amah in, ‘A dung gialte na thaman hi ding hi,’ ci leh tua ciangin tuuhon khempeuh in a dung gial ta hong nei hi.
English: If he said thus, The speckled shall be thy wages; then all the cattle bare speckled: and if he said thus, The ringstraked shall be thy hire; then bare all the cattle ringstraked.

**31:9**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in na pa’ ganhing khempeuh la khia-in tuate keima tungah hong piazo hi.
English: Thus God hath taken away the cattle of your father, and given them to me.

**31:10**
Zolai: “Ganhonte ta nei dingin a kikholh hunin ka khuadak to a, a honte’ tunga a diang keeltal khempeuh a dung gial, a bem gial, a puangin a omna ka mangin ka mu hi.
English: And it came to pass at the time that the cattle conceived, that I lifted up mine eyes, and saw in a dream, and, behold, the rams which leaped upon the cattle were ringstraked, speckled, and grisled.

**31:11**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Pasian’ vantungmi in ka mang sungah, ‘Jakob,’ hong ci a, ke’n, ‘Hiah om ing!’ ka ci hi.
English: And the angel of God spake unto me in a dream, saying , Jacob: And I said, Here am I.

**31:12**
Zolai: Amah in, ‘Khuadak to inla en in, a honte’ tunga a diang keelte khempeuh dung gial, bem gialin puang uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Laban in nang’ tunga hong bawlna ka mu khin hi.
English: And he said, Lift up now thine eyes, and see, all the rams which leap upon the cattle are ringstraked, speckled, and grisled: for I have seen all that Laban doeth unto thee.

**31:13**
Zolai: Kei pen, nang in khuam khat sathau nuhin kei’ tungah thuciamna nong bawlna mun Bethel Pasian ka hi hi. Tu-in kithawi inla, hih gam panin paikhia-in, na suahna gamah ciahkik in,’ hong ci hi,” a ci hi.
English: I am the God of Beth-el, where thou anointedst the pillar, and where thou vowedst a vow unto me: now arise, get thee out from this land, and return unto the land of thy kindred.

**31:14**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Rachel le Leah in amah dawngin, “I pa’ inn sungah ei’ tanh ding ahi a, ei’ luah ding ahi zongin bang om ahi hiam?
English: And Rachel and Leah answered and said unto him, Is there yet any portion or inheritance for us in our father's house?

**31:15**
Zolai: Amah in eite gamdangmi bangin hong ngaihsun hi lo ahi hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in eite hong zuak khin a, eite a’ ding hong kipia sum amah in zang mang khin hi.
English: Are we not counted of him strangers? for he hath sold us, and hath quite devoured also our money.

**31:16**
Zolai: I pa’ tung panin Pasian in a lakkhiatsa neihsa khempeuh eite le i tate a’ ahi hi. Tua ahih ciangin tu-in, nang’ tunga Pasian’ hong cih peuhpeuh hih in,” a ci uh hi.
English: For all the riches which God hath taken from our father, that is our's, and our children's: now then, whatsoever God hath said unto thee, do.

**31:17**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Jakob kithawi-in a tapate le a zite kalaohte tungah a tuangsak hi.
English: Then Jacob rose up, and set his sons and his wives upon camels;

**31:18**
Zolai: Amah in a ganhing khempeuh, a ngahsa a bawng khempeuh, Paddanaram gam sunga a ngah ama neihsa ganhing khempeuh, a pa Isaac’ omna Kanaan gamah a paipih dingin a hawlkhia hi.
English: and he carried away all his cattle, and all his goods which he had gotten, the cattle of his getting, which he had gotten in Padan-aram, for to go to Isaac his father in the land of Canaan.

**31:19**
Zolai: Laban a tuumul met dingin a paikhia hi a, Rachel in a pa’ innsung pasian-te na gu hi.
English: And Laban went to shear his sheep: and Rachel had stolen the images that were her father's.

**31:20**
Zolai: Jakob in Aram mi Laban khem a, tai ding a sawmna amah in gen lo hi.
English: And Jacob stole away unawares to Laban the Syrian, in that he told him not that he fled.

**31:21**
Zolai: Amah a neihsa khempeuh tawh tai-in, Eufratis gun kantan a, Gilead gam mualtung lam a manawh hi.
English: So he fled with all that he had; and he rose up, and passed over the river, and set his face toward the mount Gilead.

**31:22**
Zolai: Jakob tai hi, ci-in a ni thum ni-in Laban’ tungah a kigen ciangin,
English: And it was told Laban on the third day that Jacob was fled.

**31:23**
Zolai: amah in a behte zawnin ni sagih sung amah delh a, Gilead gam mualtungah amah pha dekdek uh hi.
English: And he took his brethren with him, and pursued after him seven days' journey; and they overtook him in the mount Gilead.

**31:24**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Aram mi Laban kiangah zanin mang sungah Pasian hong pai-in ama kiangah, “Jakob’ tungah a pha hitaleh a sia hitaleh kam khat beek na pau loh nadingin kidawm in,” a ci hi.
English: And God came to Laban the Syrian in a dream by night, and said unto him, Take heed that thou speak not to Jacob either good or bad.

**31:25**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Laban in Jakob pha hi. Tu-in Jakob in mualtung khatah a puanbuk na lam a, Laban le a behte in Gilead gam mualtungah phual a sat uh hi.
English: Then Laban overtook Jacob. Now Jacob had pitched his tent in the mount: and Laban with his brethren pitched in the mount of Gilead.

**31:26**
Zolai: Laban in Jakob kiangah, “Nang in kei hong khemin, galmat bangin ka tanute bang hangin paikhiatpih na hi hiam?
English: And Laban said to Jacob, What hast thou done, that thou hast stolen away unawares to me, and carried away my daughters, as captives taken with the sword?

**31:27**
Zolai: Bang hangin tai simin kei hong khem a, hong gen lo na hi hiam? Tuaci gamtat kei lecin, lungdamna le lasakna, khuang le laiza tawh kong kha ding hi.
English: Wherefore didst thou flee away secretly, and steal away from me; and didst not tell me, that I might have sent thee away with mirth, and with songs, with tabret, and with harp?

**31:28**
Zolai: Bang hangin ka tapate le ka tanute mangpha khakna hong namsak lo na hi hiam? Tu-in na hai gamtat khin hi.
English: And hast not suffered me to kiss my sons and my daughters? thou hast now done foolishly in so doing.

**31:29**
Zolai: Nang kong siatsak ding keima thu ahi hi. Ahih hangin na pa’ Pasian in zan zanin kei kiangah thu hong gen a, ‘Jakob tungah a pha hitaleh a sia hitaleh na gen ding kidawm in,’ hong ci hi.
English: It is in the power of my hand to do you hurt: but the God of your father spake unto me yesternight, saying, Take thou heed that thou speak not to Jacob either good or bad.

**31:30**
Zolai: Tu-in nang in na pa’ inn nakpitakin lunggulh na hih manin na paikhia khinta hi. Ahih hangin bang hangin ka pasian-te gu na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And now, though thou wouldest needs be gone, because thou sore longedst after thy father's house, yet wherefore hast thou stolen my gods?

**31:31**
Zolai: Jakob in Laban dawngin, “Kei’ kiang panin na tanute thahat thu-in nong suh khak ding ka launa hang ahi hi.
English: And Jacob answered and said to Laban, Because I was afraid: for I said, Peradventure thou wouldest take by force thy daughters from me.

**31:32**
Zolai: Na pasian-te na muhna mi peuhpeuh kithat tahen! I behte’ muhna-ah nang a’ ahi na khat peuhpeuh kei’ neihsa lakah a om leh kawkkhia-in la in,” a ci hi. Rachel in Laban’ pasian-te a na guklam Jakob in thei kha lo hi.
English: With whomsoever thou findest thy gods, let him not live: before our brethren discern thou what is thine with me, and take it to thee. For Jacob knew not that Rachel had stolen them.

**31:33**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Laban, Jakob’ puanbuk, Leah’ puanbuk, le nasem numei nihte’ puanbuk sungah pai a, ahih hangin amah in tuate mu lo hi. Leah’ puanbuk panin amah paikhia-in Rachel’ puanbuk sungah a lut hi.
English: And Laban went into Jacob's tent, and into Leah's tent, and into the two maidservants' tents; but he found them not. Then went he out of Leah's tent, and entered into Rachel's tent.

**31:34**
Zolai: Rachel in innsung pasian-te na gu a, kalaoh tutphah sungah koihin, tuate’ tungah na tu hi. Laban in puanbuk sungteng khempeuh zawt a, ahih hangin tuate mu lo hi.
English: Now Rachel had taken the images, and put them in the camel's furniture, and sat upon them. And Laban searched all the tent, but found them not.

**31:35**
Zolai: Amah in a pa kiangah, “Nang’ mai-ah hong ding thei lo ka hih manin ka topa heh kei in; bang hang hiam cih leh numei ngeina nin ka nei hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in mundang khempeuh zong a, ahih hangin a innsung pasian-te mu zo lo hi.
English: And she said to her father, Let it not displease my lord that I cannot rise up before thee; for the custom of women is upon me. And he searched, but found not the images.

**31:36**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob a heh suak a, Laban mawhsakin, “Ka mawhna bang ahi hiam? Nasia takin kei nong delh nadingin ka khialhna bang ahi hiam?
English: And Jacob was wroth, and chode with Laban: and Jacob answered and said to Laban, What is my trespass? what is my sin, that thou hast so hotly pursued after me?

**31:37**
Zolai: Ka van khempeuh na thawi khit hangin na innsung nate mu na hi hiam? Ei tegel kikalah amaute in thu a khen theih nadingin keima behte le nangma behte’ mai-ah, na muh a om leh hong koihkhia in.
English: Whereas thou hast searched all my stuff, what hast thou found of all thy household stuff? set it here before my brethren and thy brethren, that they may judge betwixt us both.

**31:38**
Zolai: Hih kum sawmnih sung nang kiangah kong om khin hi. Na tuupi le na keelpite tatolh nai lo a, na tuuhonte’ sung pan tuutal sa ka ne kei hi.
English: This twenty years have I been with thee; thy ewes and thy she goats have not cast their young, and the rams of thy flock have I not eaten.

**31:39**
Zolai: Gamlak ganhingte’ balzante, nang’ kiangah kong puak kei hi. Tua banga supnate kei mahmah in ka thuak hi. Sun-a kigu hitaleh zan a kigu hitaleh kei nong lohsak hi.
English: That which was torn of beasts I brought not unto thee; I bare the loss of it; of my hand didst thou require it, whether stolen by day, or stolen by night.

**31:40**
Zolai: Kei pen tu-a bang ka hi hi. Sunin a sa in hong kang a, zanin a vot in hong tawp a, ka ihmu ngei kei hi.
English: Thus I was; in the day the drought consumed me, and the frost by night; and my sleep departed from mine eyes.

**31:41**
Zolai: Hih kum sawmnih sung na inn sungah kong om khin hi. Na tanu nihte, kum sawm le li sung kong thalawh a, na tuuhonte, kum guk sung kong thalawh a, nangmah in ka thaman sawmvei na kheel hi.
English: Thus have I been twenty years in thy house; I served thee fourteen years for thy two daughters, and six years for thy cattle: and thou hast changed my wages ten times.

**31:42**
Zolai: Ka pa’ Pasian, Abraham’ Pasian, le Isaac’ Zahtak pa in kei hong ompih lo hileh, tu-in nangmah in khut hawmguakin kei nong sawlkhia taktak ding hi. Pasian in ka thuakna le ka nasepna mu a, zan zanin nang hong thuhilh hi,” a ci hi.
English: Except the God of my father, the God of Abraham, and the fear of Isaac, had been with me, surely thou hadst sent me away now empty. God hath seen mine affliction and the labour of my hands, and rebuked thee yesternight.

**31:43**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Laban in dawngin Jakob kiangah, “Tanute pen keima tanu hi; naupangte zong keima naupang hi; tuuhonte, keima tuuhon hi a, na muh khempeuh keima-a’ ahi hi. Ahih hangin tuni-in hih ka tanute hitaleh amau’ sung pana piang naupangte’ tung hitaleh ke’n bang cih thei ding ka hi hiam?
English: And Laban answered and said unto Jacob, These daughters are my daughters, and these children are my children, and these cattle are my cattle, and all that thou seest is mine: and what can I do this day unto these my daughters, or unto their children which they have born?

**31:44**
Zolai: Tu-in hong pai in, nang le kei in thuciamna khat bawl ni; suangcian khat bawlin nang le kei’ kikalah teci hisak ni,” a ci hi.
English: Now therefore come thou, let us make a covenant, I and thou; and let it be for a witness between me and thee.

**31:45**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Jakob in suang khat la-in khuamin a phut hi.
English: And Jacob took a stone, and set it up for a pillar.

**31:46**
Zolai: Jakob in a behte kiangah, “Suang khawm un,” ci a, amaute in suang la-in suangcian khat a bawl uh hi. Tua suangcian gei-ah amaute in an a ne khawm uh hi.
English: And Jacob said unto his brethren, Gather stones; and they took stones, and made an heap: and they did eat there upon the heap.

**31:47**
Zolai: Laban in, Jegarsahadutha, ci hi. Ahih hangin Jakob in, Galeed, ci hi.
English: And Laban called it Jegar-sahadutha: but Jacob called it Galeed.

**31:48**
Zolai: Laban in, “Hih suangcian pen tuni-in nang le kei’ kikalah teci ahi hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in, Galeed, ci-in min phuak a,
English: And Laban said, This heap is a witness between me and thee this day. Therefore was the name of it called Galeed;

**31:49**
Zolai: a khuam pen Mizpah, ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Laban in, “Eite khatlekhat i tuam om ciangin Topa in nang le kei’ kikalah hong encik tahen.
English: and Mizpah; for he said, The LORD watch between me and thee, when we are absent one from another.

**31:50**
Zolai: Ka tanute na bawl siat a, ka tanute’ banah zi na lak beh leh, eite tawh kuamah a om loh hangin nang le kei’ kikalah, Pasian, teci ahihna phawk in,” a ci hi.
English: If thou shalt afflict my daughters, or if thou shalt take other wives beside my daughters, no man is with us; see, God is witness betwixt me and thee.

**31:51**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Laban in Jakob’ kiangah, “Nang le kei’ kikalah ka phuhsa hih suangcian mu in.
English: And Laban said to Jacob, Behold this heap, and behold this pillar, which I have cast betwixt me and thee;

**31:52**
Zolai: Siatna a bawl dingin keimah in hih suangcian khengin nang kiangah kong pai loh nading, nang zong hih suangcian le khuam khengin kei kiangah nong pai loh nadingin hih suangcian le suangkhuam, teci ahi hi.
English: this heap be witness, and this pillar be witness, that I will not pass over this heap to thee, and that thou shalt not pass over this heap and this pillar unto me, for harm.

**31:53**
Zolai: Abraham’ Pasian le Nahor’ Pasian, amau’ pate’ Pasian in eite’ kikalah thu khen ta hen,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin Jakob in ama pa Isaac’ Zahtak pa tawh a kiciam hi.
English: The God of Abraham, and the God of Nahor, the God of their father, judge betwixt us. And Jacob sware by the fear of his father Isaac.

**31:54**
Zolai: Jakob in mualtungah biakpiakna pia-in an ne dingin a behte a sam hi. Amaute in an ne uh a, zan tawntung mualtungah a om uh hi.
English: Then Jacob offered sacrifice upon the mount, and called his brethren to eat bread: and they did eat bread, and tarried all night in the mount.

**31:55**
Zolai: Zingsang tungin Laban tho-in, a tute le a tanute namin amaute thupha a piak khit ciangin paikhia-in a inn-ah a ciahkik hi.
English: And early in the morning Laban rose up, and kissed his sons and his daughters, and blessed them: and Laban departed, and returned unto his place.

## Chapter 32

**32:1**
Zolai: Jakob zong ama lampi-ah paisuak a, Pasian’ vantung mite in amah na dawn hi.
English: And Jacob went on his way, and the angels of God met him.

**32:2**
Zolai: Jakob in amaute a muh ciangin amah in, “Hihte, Pasian’ galkapte!,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin tua mun pen Mahanaim, ci-in min a phuak hi.
English: And when Jacob saw them, he said, This is God's host: and he called the name of that place Mahanaim.

**32:3**
Zolai: Jakob in Edom gam, Seir leitangah a om a sanggampa Esau kiangah kamtaite ma sawl a,
English: And Jacob sent messengers before him to Esau his brother unto the land of Seir, the country of Edom.

**32:4**
Zolai: amaute hilhin, “Note in ka topa Esau kiangah hih bangin na ci ding uh hi: Na nasempa Jakob in, ‘Laban’ kiangah peemta-in tu ciang dong ka om hi.
English: And he commanded them, saying, Thus shall ye speak unto my lord Esau; Thy servant Jacob saith thus, I have sojourned with Laban, and stayed there until now:

**32:5**
Zolai: Keimah in bawngtal, la, tuuhon, nasem pasal, le nasem numeite ka nei hi. Na mai-ah maipha ka muh theih nadingin ka topa tungah a gen dingin kong sawl hi, ci hi’, ci un,” a ci hi.
English: and I have oxen, and asses, flocks, and menservants, and womenservants: and I have sent to tell my lord, that I may find grace in thy sight.

**32:6**
Zolai: Kamtaite, Jakob kiangah hong ciahkik uh a, “Na sanggampa Esau kiangah ka va pai uh hi. Nangmah a dawn dingin amah hong pai a, amah tawh mihing zali om hi,” ci-in hong gen uh hi.
English: And the messengers returned to Jacob, saying, We came to thy brother Esau, and also he cometh to meet thee, and four hundred men with him.

**32:7**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob nakpitakin lau-in lungkham hi. Amah in ama kianga om mite, tuuhonte, bawnghonte, le kalaohte pawl nihin khen a,
English: Then Jacob was greatly afraid and distressed: and he divided the people that was with him, and the flocks, and herds, and the camels, into two bands;

**32:8**
Zolai: “Pawlkhatah Esau pai-in a suksiat leh a pawlkhat suakta ding hi,” ci-in a ngaihsun hi.
English: and said, If Esau come to the one company, and smite it, then the other company which is left shall escape.

**32:9**
Zolai: Jakob in, “Ka pu Abraham’ Pasian le ka pa Isaac’ Pasian, keima kiangah, ‘Na gam le na behte kiangah ciahkik in; nang’ tungah hoihna kong bawl ding hi,’ hong ci Topa aw,
English: And Jacob said, O God of my father Abraham, and God of my father Isaac, the LORD which saidst unto me, Return unto thy country, and to thy kindred, and I will deal well with thee:

**32:10**
Zolai: kei pen na itna kip khempeuh lak pan a neupen le na nasempa tunga nong lahsa na thumannate khempeuh tawh ka kilawm kei hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh ka ciangkhut guak tawh hih Jordan ka kantan a, ahi zongin tu-in pawl nih ka cing khinta hi.
English: I am not worthy of the least of all the mercies, and of all the truth, which thou hast shewed unto thy servant; for with my staff I passed over this Jordan; and now I am become two bands.

**32:11**
Zolai: Ka sanggampa Esau’ khutsung pan kei hong khahkhia in, kong thum hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah hong pai-in kote khempeuh, nute, naupangte tawh hong thah khit khak ding ka lau hi.
English: Deliver me, I pray thee, from the hand of my brother, from the hand of Esau: for I fear him, lest he will come and smite me, and the mother with the children.

**32:12**
Zolai: Ahih hangin nangmah in, ‘Na tungah hoihna kong bawl ding a, na suanlekhakte tuipi sehnel zahin a honpi a kisim thei loin ka bawl ding hi,’ nong ci hi,” a ci hi.
English: And thou saidst, I will surely do thee good, and make thy seed as the sand of the sea, which cannot be numbered for multitude.

**32:13**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah tua zanin tua lai-ah giak a, ama neih sung panin a sanggampa Esau a’ ding letsong
English: And he lodged there that same night; and took of that which came to his hand a present for Esau his brother;

**32:14**
Zolai: keelpi zanih le keeltal sawmnih, tuupi zanih le tuutal sawmnih,
English: two hundred she goats, and twenty he goats, two hundred ewes, and twenty rams,

**32:15**
Zolai: kalaoh nawisuk sawmthum le a note, bawngpi sawmli le bawngtal sawm, lapi sawmnih le latal sawm a la hi.
English: thirty milch camels with their colts, forty kine, and ten bulls, twenty she asses, and ten foals.

**32:16**
Zolai: Amah in hihte a nasemte’ khut sungah amau’ hon ciatin pia a, ama nasemte kiangah, “Ka mai-ah na paisuak unla, hon khat le hon khat kikal kihalsak un,” a ci hi.
English: And he delivered them into the hand of his servants, every drove by themselves; and said unto his servants, Pass over before me, and put a space betwixt drove and drove.

**32:17**
Zolai: Amah in a masa pente tungah thu hilh a, “Ka sanggampa Esau in note hong dawnin, ‘Kua-a’ na hi uh hiam? Koi pana hong pai na hi uh hiam? Na mai uha om hihte kua-a’ ahi hiam?’ ci-in hong dot ciangin
English: And he commanded the foremost, saying, When Esau my brother meeteth thee, and asketh thee, saying, Whose art thou? and whither goest thou? and whose are these before thee?

**32:18**
Zolai: note in, ‘Na nasempa Jakob-a’ ahi hi. Hihte pen ka topa Esau’ tungah letsongin hong kipuak ahi hi. Tua tham loin amah ka nung uhah om hi,’ ci un,” a ci hi.
English: Then thou shalt say, They be thy servant Jacob's; it is a present sent unto my lord Esau: and, behold, also he is behind us.

**32:19**
Zolai: Amah in tua mah bangin a nihna, a thumna, le ganhing honte a zuite khempeuh kiangah, “Amah tawh na kituah uh ciangin Esau’ kiangah a kibangmahin na gen ding uh hi.
English: And so commanded he the second, and the third, and all that followed the droves, saying, On this manner shall ye speak unto Esau, when ye find him.

**32:20**
Zolai: Note in, ‘Tua tham loin na nasempa Jakob ka nung uhah om hi,’ na ci ding uh hi,” a ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah in, “Ka mai-ah a pai letsong tawh amah ka lungdamsak zo kha ding a, tua khit ciangin ama maipha ka mu ding hi. Amah in kei hong sang kha ding hi,” ci-in a ngaihsun hi.
English: And say ye moreover, Behold, thy servant Jacob is behind us. For he said, I will appease him with the present that goeth before me, and afterward I will see his face; peradventure he will accept of me.

**32:21**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin letsong a piak dingte, ama mai-ah paisak a, amah ahihleh tua zanin giahphual ah a giak lai hi.
English: So went the present over before him: and himself lodged that night in the company.

**32:22**
Zolai: Tua zan mahin amah tho-in a zi nihte, a nasem numei nihte, le a ta sawm le khatte la-in, Jabbok ngahmun a kantan hi.
English: And he rose up that night, and took his two wives, and his two womenservants, and his eleven sons, and passed over the ford Jabbok.

**32:23**
Zolai: Amah in amaute la-in lui galkhatah puak a, tua mah bangin a neih khempeuh zong a galkahsak hi.
English: And he took them, and sent them over the brook, and sent over that he had.

**32:24**
Zolai: Jakob amah guak bek omlai a, zingsang khuavak dong mi khat in amah a lai hi.
English: And Jacob was left alone; and there wrestled a man with him until the breaking of the day.

**32:25**
Zolai: Tua mipa in Jakob a zawh lohna a theih ciangin amah in a khelkom sung suksak hi. Tua bangin amah tawh a kilaina-in Jakob’ khelguh a kilawi hi.
English: And when he saw that he prevailed not against him, he touched the hollow of his thigh; and the hollow of Jacob's thigh was out of joint, as he wrestled with him.

**32:26**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in, “Khua vak ta ahih ciangin hong khah in,” a ci hi. Ahih hangin Jakob in, “Kei, thupha nong piak kei leh kong khah kei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Let me go, for the day breaketh. And he said, I will not let thee go, except thou bless me.

**32:27**
Zolai: Amah in, “Na min bang ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amah in, “Jakob,” ci hi.
English: And he said unto him, What is thy name? And he said, Jacob.

**32:28**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in, “Na min Jakob, kici nawn loin Israel, kici ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Pasian le mite tawh na kilai khinzo a, na zo hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Thy name shall be called no more Jacob, but Israel: for as a prince hast thou power with God and with men, and hast prevailed.

**32:29**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in amah dongin, “Na min hong gen in, hong thum ing,” a ci hi. Ahih hangin amah in, “Bang hanga ka min hong dong na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua lai-ah amah in Jakob thupha a pia hi.
English: And Jacob asked him , and said, Tell me , I pray thee, thy name. And he said, Wherefore is it that thou dost ask after my name? And he blessed him there.

**32:30**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Jakob in tua mun pen Peniel, ci-in min a phuak hi. “Bang hang hiam cih leh maitang kituahin Pasian ka mu khin a, ahi zongin kei hong kihing khawi lai hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob called the name of the place Peniel: for I have seen God face to face, and my life is preserved.

**32:31**
Zolai: A khelpi’ hangin amah bai kawmin Peniel a kantan laitakin ni hong suak hi.
English: And as he passed over Penuel the sun rose upon him, and he halted upon his thigh.

**32:32**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tuni dongin Israel mite in khelkom tunga a om khel thagui ne lo uh hi. Amah in Jakob’ khelkom, a khel thagui tung a sukna hang ahi hi.
English: Therefore the children of Israel eat not of the sinew which shrank, which is upon the hollow of the thigh, unto this day: because he touched the hollow of Jacob's thigh in the sinew that shrank.

## Chapter 33

**33:1**
Zolai: Jakob khuadak a, Esau tawh mihing zali hong pai a mu hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in Leah, Rachel, le nasem numei nihte’ lakah a naupangte a khen hi.
English: And Jacob lifted up his eyes, and looked, and, behold, Esau came, and with him four hundred men. And he divided the children unto Leah, and unto Rachel, and unto the two handmaids.

**33:2**
Zolai: Amah in nasem numeite le a tate a masa penin, tua ciangin Leah le a tate, tua ciangin Rachel le Josef a nunung penin a koih hi.
English: And he put the handmaids and their children foremost, and Leah and her children after, and Rachel and Joseph hindermost.

**33:3**
Zolai: Amah ahihleh amaute’ mai-ah pai-in, a sanggampa’ kiang nai a tun matengin leilak lamah sagihvei a kun hi.
English: And he passed over before them, and bowed himself to the ground seven times, until he came near to his brother.

**33:4**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah a dawn dingin Esau hong tai-in, amah ngawng kawi a, pomcipin nam a, amaute a kap uh hi.
English: And Esau ran to meet him, and embraced him, and fell on his neck, and kissed him: and they wept.

**33:5**
Zolai: Esau khuadak to-in nupite le naupangte a muh ciangin amah in, “Nang tawh a om hihte kua ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Jakob in, “Pasian in hehpihna tawh na nasempa a piak tate ahi hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he lifted up his eyes, and saw the women and the children; and said, Who are those with thee? And he said, The children which God hath graciously given thy servant.

**33:6**
Zolai: Tua ciangin nasem numeite in hong naih uh a, amau le a tate hong kun uh hi.
English: Then the handmaidens came near, they and their children, and they bowed themselves.

**33:7**
Zolai: Leah le a tate in zong tua bangmahin hong naihin a kun uh hi. A nunung penin Josef le Rachel in hong naihin a kun uh hi.
English: And Leah also with her children came near, and bowed themselves: and after came Joseph near and Rachel, and they bowed themselves.

**33:8**
Zolai: Esau in, “Ka kituahpih hih a honte khempeuh bang na cihnopna ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Jakob in dawngin, “Ka topa’ maipha zon nading,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, What meanest thou by all this drove which I met? And he said, These are to find grace in the sight of my lord.

**33:9**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Esau in, “A kicing nei ing, sanggam aw; nang’ neihte nangma a dingin kem in,” a ci hi.
English: And Esau said, I have enough, my brother; keep that thou hast unto thyself.

**33:10**
Zolai: Jakob in, “Hi lo hi, nang’ tungah hong thum ing. Na muhna-ah maipha ngah ka hih leh ka khutsung panin ka letsongte hong sang in. Bang hang hiam cih leh hih banga maipha tawh kei nong sanna, na maitang ka muh ding pen Pasian’ maitang muh tawh kibang taktak hi.
English: And Jacob said, Nay, I pray thee, if now I have found grace in thy sight, then receive my present at my hand: for therefore I have seen thy face, as though I had seen the face of God, and thou wast pleased with me.

**33:11**
Zolai: Nang’ kianga hong kipaipih ka letsong nong san nadingin hong thum ing. Bang hang hiam cih leh Pasian in kei hong hehpih mahmah a, a kicing ka nei hi,” a ci hi. Tua bangin amah in kun teitei ahih manin Esau in zong a sang hi.
English: Take, I pray thee, my blessing that is brought to thee; because God hath dealt graciously with me, and because I have enough. And he urged him, and he took it .

**33:12**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Esau in, “Tu-in paikhawm ni. Na mai-ah kei ka pai ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Let us take our journey, and let us go, and I will go before thee.

**33:13**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Jakob in ama kiangah, “Naupangte a hat lohna ka topa in na thei hi. Tuuhonte le bawngte, a nongek neite ka lungphamawh hi. Ni khat sung kinak hawl lua leh ganhonte khempeuh si ding uh hi.
English: And he said unto him, My lord knoweth that the children are tender, and the flocks and herds with young are with me: and if men should overdrive them one day, all the flock will die.

**33:14**
Zolai: Na nasempa’ mai-ah ka topa na pai inla, Seir-ah ka topa’ kiang kong tun matengin ka mai-a om ganhingte’ thahatna le naupangte’ hatna tawh kituakin damdamin kong makaih ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: Let my lord, I pray thee, pass over before his servant: and I will lead on softly, according as the cattle that goeth before me and the children be able to endure, until I come unto my lord unto Seir.

**33:15**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Esau in, “Kei tawh a om mite pawlkhat, nang’ kiangah hong nusia ning,” a ci hi. Ahih hangin amah in, “A kisapna bang om ahi hiam? Ka topa’ muhna-ah kei maipha hong ngahsak in,” a ci hi.
English: And Esau said, Let me now leave with thee some of the folk that are with me. And he said, What needeth it? let me find grace in the sight of my lord.

**33:16**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Esau in tua ni-in ama lampi zui-in Seir-ah a ciahkik hi.
English: So Esau returned that day on his way unto Seir.

**33:17**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Jakob, Sukkoth lamah pai a, ama a’ ding inn le a ganhingte a’ ding hampheng a lam hi. Tua ahih ciangin tua mun a min Sukkoth, kici hi.
English: And Jacob journeyed to Succoth, and built him an house, and made booths for his cattle: therefore the name of the place is called Succoth.

**33:18**
Zolai: Paddanaram panin hong pai lampi, Kanaan gam sunga om Shekhem khuapi-ah lungmuang takin Jakob hong tung a, a khuapi kiangah phual a sat hi.
English: And Jacob came to Shalem, a city of Shechem, which is in the land of Canaan, when he came from Padan-aram; and pitched his tent before the city.

**33:19**
Zolai: Amah in Shekhem’ pa Hamor’ innkuante’ tung panin a puanbuk lamnasa leitang dangka zakhat tawh a lei hi.
English: And he bought a parcel of a field, where he had spread his tent, at the hand of the children of Hamor, Shechem's father, for an hundred pieces of money.

**33:20**
Zolai: Tua lai-ah amah in biakna tau khat bawl a, El-Elohe-Israel, ci-in min a phuak hi.
English: And he erected there an altar, and called it El-elohe-Israel.

## Chapter 34

**34:1**
Zolai: Ni khat, Jakob le Leah’ tanu Dinah tua gam numeite kiangah va hawh hi.
English: And Dinah the daughter of Leah, which she bare unto Jacob, went out to see the daughters of the land.

**34:2**
Zolai: Hiv mi Hamor’ tapa Shekhem, tua gam ulianpa in amah a muh ciangin, amah manin luppih a, amah siasak hi.
English: And when Shechem the son of Hamor the Hivite, prince of the country, saw her, he took her, and lay with her, and defiled her.

**34:3**
Zolai: Amah in Jakob’ tanu Dinah hoihsa mahmah ahih manin itin kamkhum takin hopih hi.
English: And his soul clave unto Dinah the daughter of Jacob, and he loved the damsel, and spake kindly unto the damsel.

**34:4**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Shekhem in a pa Hamor’ kiangah, “Hih numei ka zi dingin hong laksak in,” a ci hi.
English: And Shechem spake unto his father Hamor, saying, Get me this damsel to wife.

**34:5**
Zolai: Tu-in Jakob in a tanu Dinah a kisiatsakna za hi. Ahih hangin a tate, a ganhingte tawh gamlakah om ahih manin amaute hong tun matengin Jakob in bangmah gen loin om hi.
English: And Jacob heard that he had defiled Dinah his daughter: now his sons were with his cattle in the field: and Jacob held his peace until they were come.

**34:6**
Zolai: Shekhem’ pa Hamor, Jakob tawh a kimu dingin ama kiangah va pai hi.
English: And Hamor the father of Shechem went out unto Jacob to commune with him.

**34:7**
Zolai: Jakob’ tapate in tua thu a zak uh ciangin gamlak panin hong ciah uh hi. Amaute lungkim loin heh mahmah uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Jakob’ tanu tawh a lupkhop manin amah in Israel mite’ sungah a kilawm lo hai gamtatna hong tun hi.
English: And the sons of Jacob came out of the field when they heard it: and the men were grieved, and they were very wroth, because he had wrought folly in Israel in lying with Jacob's daughter; which thing ought not to be done.

**34:8**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Hamor in amaute tawh thu gen a, “Ka tapa Shekhem in na tanu ngai mahmah hi. A tenpih dingin nong piak nadingin kong thum hi.
English: And Hamor communed with them, saying, The soul of my son Shechem longeth for your daughter: I pray you give her him to wife.

**34:9**
Zolai: Kote tawh kitenna hong bawl un. Na tanute uh kote’ tungah hong pia unla, no a dingin ka tanute uh la un.
English: And make ye marriages with us, and give your daughters unto us, and take our daughters unto you.

**34:10**
Zolai: Kote’ lakah nong teng ding uh hi. No a dingin leitang hong kipia ding hi. Ka gam sung uhah tengin sum bawl unla, neihsa lam un,” a ci hi.
English: And ye shall dwell with us: and the land shall be before you; dwell and trade ye therein, and get you possessions therein.

**34:11**
Zolai: Shekhem in a numei’ pa le a numei’ sanggamte’ kiangah, “Note’ mai-ah maipha hong musak unla, kei’ tunga nong cih peuhpeuh uh kong pia ding hi.
English: And Shechem said unto her father and unto her brethren, Let me find grace in your eyes, and what ye shall say unto me I will give.

**34:12**
Zolai: Kei kiang panin moman le letsong tampi hong ngen un. Kei’ tunga nong nget zahzah uh kong pia ding hi. Zi dingin a numei hong pia hoh un,” ci thuah lai hi.
English: Ask me never so much dowry and gift, and I will give according as ye shall say unto me: but give me the damsel to wife.

**34:13**
Zolai: Shekhem in a sanggamnu uh Dinah siasak khin ahih manin Jakob’ tapate in Shekhem le a pa Hamor khemna tawh dawng uh hi.
English: And the sons of Jacob answered Shechem and Hamor his father deceitfully, and said, because he had defiled Dinah their sister:

**34:14**
Zolai: Amaute in amau kiangah, “Vun ki-at lopa’ tungah ka sanggamnu uh ka piak ding uh ka ngaihsun thei kei uh hi. Tua bangin pia le ung ko a dingin mindaina hi ding hi.
English: and they said unto them, We cannot do this thing, to give our sister to one that is uncircumcised; for that were a reproach unto us:

**34:15**
Zolai: Hih bangin nong gamtat uhleh ka thukim bek ding uh hi: Note’ sung panin pasal khempeuh vun ki-at le-uhcin kote mah bang na suak ding uh hi.
English: but in this will we consent unto you: If ye will be as we be , that every male of you be circumcised;

**34:16**
Zolai: Tua ciangin ka tanute uh note’ tungah hong pia-in, na tanute uh kote a dingin kong la ding uh a, note tawh kote hong tengin mikhat i suak ding hi.
English: then will we give our daughters unto you, and we will take your daughters to us, and we will dwell with you, and we will become one people.

**34:17**
Zolai: Ahih hangin note in ka thu uh hong ngai loin, vun na ki-at kei uh le, ka tanu uh ka la ding uh a, kote ka paikhia ding uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: But if ye will not hearken unto us, to be circumcised; then will we take our daughter, and we will be gone.

**34:18**
Zolai: Amau’ thugente in Hamor le Hamor’ tapa Shekhem lungdamsak hi.
English: And their words pleased Hamor, and Shechem Hamor's son.

**34:19**
Zolai: Tangvalpa in Jakob’ tanu deih ahih manin tua banga a gamtat ding zekai lo hi. Amah pen, a kipahtawi a thupi pen khat ahi hi.
English: And the young man deferred not to do the thing, because he had delight in Jacob's daughter: and he was more honourable than all the house of his father.

**34:20**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Hamor le a tapa Shekhem, amau’ khua kulhpi kongpi-ah hong pai-in a khuapih mite uh kiangah thu gen a,
English: And Hamor and Shechem his son came unto the gate of their city, and communed with the men of their city, saying,

**34:21**
Zolai: “Hih mite, eite’ tungah hong nop mahmah uh hi. I gam sungah tengsakin sum bawlsak ni. Bang hang hiam cih leh en un, amau a’ ding a kicing dingin i leitang a zai hi. Amau’ tanute zi-in tenpih ni. Eite’ tanute zong amau pia ni.
English: These men are peaceable with us; therefore let them dwell in the land, and trade therein; for the land, behold, it is large enough for them; let us take their daughters to us for wives, and let us give them our daughters.

**34:22**
Zolai: Hih thu khat bek tawh eite tawh tenkhop ding, mikhat suah ding amau thukim uh hi. Amaute vun a ki-at bangin eite’ lakah pasal khempeuh vun ki-at ding ahi hi.
English: Only herein will the men consent unto us for to dwell with us, to be one people, if every male among us be circumcised, as they are circumcised.

**34:23**
Zolai: Amau’ bawngte, amaute’ neihsate, le amau’ ganhingte khempeuh ei a’ ding hi lo ahi hiam? Amaute tawh eite thukim hoh ni. Tua hileh amaute, eite tawh hong tengkhawm ding uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: Shall not their cattle and their substance and every beast of their's be our's? only let us consent unto them, and they will dwell with us.

**34:24**
Zolai: Khuapi kulhkongpi-ah a pai mi khempeuh in Hamor le a tapa Shekhem’ thu a mang uh hi. Khuapi kulhkongpi-ah a hong pai pasal khempeuh a vun ki-at uh hi.
English: And unto Hamor and unto Shechem his son hearkened all that went out of the gate of his city; and every male was circumcised, all that went out of the gate of his city.

**34:25**
Zolai: A ni thum ni, amaute meima vei-in a om laitakun Jakob’ tapa nihte Simeon le Levi, Dinah’ sanggamte in amau’ namsau la-in theihkholh lohin khuapi va sim uh a, pasal khempeuh a that uh hi.
English: And it came to pass on the third day, when they were sore, that two of the sons of Jacob, Simeon and Levi, Dinah's brethren, took each man his sword, and came upon the city boldly, and slew all the males.

**34:26**
Zolai: Amaute in Hamor le a tapa Shekhem, namsau tawh that uh a, Shekhem’ innsung panin Dinah lakhia-in a paikhia uh hi.
English: And they slew Hamor and Shechem his son with the edge of the sword, and took Dinah out of Shechem's house, and went out.

**34:27**
Zolai: Jakob tapa dangte in a kithat mite’ tungtawnin khuapi susia uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh a sanggamnu uh kisiasak hi.
English: The sons of Jacob came upon the slain, and spoiled the city, because they had defiled their sister.

**34:28**
Zolai: Amaute in a tuuhonte le a bawnghonte, a late le khuapi sunga om peuhmah, le lo sunga om peuhmah a laksak uh hi.
English: They took their sheep, and their oxen, and their asses, and that which was in the city, and that which was in the field,

**34:29**
Zolai: Amau’ neihsa khempeuh, a naupangte khempeuh, a zite khempeuh, le inn sunga om na khempeuh laksak uh a, amau’ neihsa a suaksak uh hi.
English: and all their wealth, and all their little ones, and their wives took they captive, and spoiled even all that was in the house.

**34:30**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in Simeon le Levi’ kiangah, “Hih leitangah a teng, Kanaan mite le Perez mite tungah kei a muhdahhuai-in nong bawlna uh tawh kei’ tungah haksatna nong tun uh hi. Kei’ pawl mite tawm hi. Amaute kei’ langah hong kikaikhawmin kei hong sim leh, kei le ka innkuanpihte hong susia ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob said to Simeon and Levi, Ye have troubled me to make me to stink among the inhabitants of the land, among the Canaanites and the Perizzites: and I being few in number, they shall gather themselves together against me, and slay me; and I shall be destroyed, I and my house.

**34:31**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amaute in, “Amah in ka sanggamnu uh numei paktat bangin a bawl ding kilawm ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
English: And they said, Should he deal with our sister as with an harlot?

## Chapter 35

**35:1**
Zolai: Pasian in Jakob kiangah, “Kithawi-in Bethel-ah paito inla, tua lai-ah teng in. Na sanggampa Esau’ kiang panin na tai hun lai-a nang’ tungah a hong kilang Pasian a dingin biakna tau khat bawl in,” a ci hi.
English: And God said unto Jacob, Arise, go up to Beth-el, and dwell there: and make there an altar unto God, that appeared unto thee when thou fleddest from the face of Esau thy brother.

**35:2**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Jakob in a innkuanpihte le amah tawh a omte khempeuh kiangah, “Note lakah a om gamdang pasian-te koihkhia unla, nomau kisiansuahin, na puante uh khek un.
English: Then Jacob said unto his household, and to all that were with him, Put away the strange gods that are among you, and be clean, and change your garments:

**35:3**
Zolai: Ka lungkham hunin hong huhin, ka paina khempeuhah a hong ompih Pasian a dingin biakna tau khat ka bawl theih nadingin eite kipanin Bethel-ah paito ni,” a ci hi.
English: and let us arise, and go up to Beth-el; and I will make there an altar unto God, who answered me in the day of my distress, and was with me in the way which I went.

**35:4**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute in Jakob’ tungah amau’ neih gamdang pasian khempeuh le a bil uha om bilbahte a pia uh hi. Jakob in Shekhem khua gei-a tawsaw nuai-ah tuate a seel hi.
English: And they gave unto Jacob all the strange gods which were in their hand, and all their earrings which were in their ears; and Jacob hid them under the oak which was by Shechem.

**35:5**
Zolai: Jakob le a tapate khualzinin a pai laitakun amau’ kiima om khuapite’ tungah Pasian’ kiang panin lauhuaina lianpi khat tung ahih manin amaute in Jakob le a tapate delh lo uh hi.
English: And they journeyed: and the terror of God was upon the cities that were round about them, and they did not pursue after the sons of Jacob.

**35:6**
Zolai: Kanaan gam sunga om Luz (Bethel)-ah Jakob le amah tawh a om mi khempeuh tung uh a,
English: So Jacob came to Luz, which is in the land of Canaan, that is , Beth-el, he and all the people that were with him.

**35:7**
Zolai: tua lai-ah amah in biakna tau khat lamin, tua mun Elbethel, ci-in min a phuak hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh a sanggampa kiang panin a tai lai-in tua munah ama tungah Pasian mahmah kilang hi.
English: And he built there an altar, and called the place El-beth-el: because there God appeared unto him, when he fled from the face of his brother.

**35:8**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Rebekah a cingnu Deborah si a, Bethel khang tawsaw nuai-ah amah kivui hi. Tua ahih ciangin tua mun min pen Allonbakuth, kici hi.
English: But Deborah Rebekah's nurse died, and she was buried beneath Beth-el under an oak: and the name of it was called Allon-bachuth.

**35:9**
Zolai: Paddanaram panin amah hong pai ciangin Jakob’ tungah Pasian kilang kik a, amah thupha a pia hi.
English: And God appeared unto Jacob again, when he came out of Padan-aram, and blessed him.

**35:10**
Zolai: Pasian in ama kiangah, “Na min Jakob ahi hi. Ahi zongin tu-a kipanin nangma min pen Jakob kici nawn lo ding a, Israel, hong kici ding hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama min Israel, kici hi.
English: And God said unto him, Thy name is Jacob: thy name shall not be called any more Jacob, but Israel shall be thy name: and he called his name Israel.

**35:11**
Zolai: Pasian in ama kiangah, “Kei pen Vanglian Pasian ka hi hi: Pung inla, tampi pha in. Minam khat le minamte honkhat nang’ sung panin piang ding a, nang’ sung panin kumpite zong piang ding hi.
English: And God said unto him, I am God Almighty: be fruitful and multiply; a nation and a company of nations shall be of thee, and kings shall come out of thy loins;

**35:12**
Zolai: Abraham le Isaac tunga ka piak leitang nangma tungah kong pia ding a, nang’ khit cianga na suanlekhakte’ tungah tua leitang ka pia ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: and the land which I gave Abraham and Isaac, to thee I will give it, and to thy seed after thee will I give the land.

**35:13**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah tawh a kihona mun ama kiang panin Pasian paikhia to hi.
English: And God went up from him in the place where he talked with him.

**35:14**
Zolai: Jakob in amah tawh a kihona munah suang khuam khat phut a, amah in tua tungah leenggahzu tawh biakpiakna a sungkhia hi. Tua tungah sathau zong a sung hi.
English: And Jacob set up a pillar in the place where he talked with him, even a pillar of stone: and he poured a drink offering thereon, and he poured oil thereon.

**35:15**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Jakob in, Pasian in amah a hopihna mun a min Bethel, a ci hi.
English: And Jacob called the name of the place where God spake with him, Beth-el.

**35:16**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Bethel panin amaute ding khia uh a, Efrath panin a gamla sim lai mun a tun laitakun Rachel a nausuah hun tung a, amah nakpi takin a gim hi.
English: And they journeyed from Beth-el; and there was but a little way to come to Ephrath: and Rachel travailed, and she had hard labour.

**35:17**
Zolai: Amah a gim mahmah laitakin naudom nu in ama kiangah, “Lunghimawh kei in. Tu-in tapa dang khat na nei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And it came to pass, when she was in hard labour, that the midwife said unto her, Fear not; thou shalt have this son also.

**35:18**
Zolai: Amah a bei laitakin amah in a min dingin Benoni, a ci hi. Ahih hangin a pa in ama min Benjamin, ci-in a phuak hi.
English: And it came to pass, as her soul was in departing, (for she died) that she called his name Ben-oni: but his father called him Benjamin.

**35:19**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Rachel si-in, Efrath (Bethlehem) paina lampi-ah kivui a,
English: And Rachel died, and was buried in the way to Ephrath, which is Beth-lehem.

**35:20**
Zolai: Jakob in ama han tungah mualsuang khat a phut hi. Tua pen tuni dongin tua lai mahah a om Rachel’ han mualsuang khuam ahi hi.
English: And Jacob set a pillar upon her grave: that is the pillar of Rachel's grave unto this day.

**35:21**
Zolai: Israel in a khualzin zomlai a, Eder tausang galkhatah a puanbuk a lam hi.
English: And Israel journeyed, and spread his tent beyond the tower of Edar.

**35:22**
Zolai: Tua gamah Israel a ten laitakin Reuben in a pa’ zineu Bilhah luppih hi. Israel in tua thu za-in heh mahmah hi. Tu-in Jakob’ tapate, sawm le nih ahi hi.
English: And it came to pass, when Israel dwelt in that land, that Reuben went and lay with Bilhah his father's concubine: and Israel heard it . Now the sons of Jacob were twelve:

**35:23**
Zolai: Leah’ tapate: Reuben (Jakob’ ta u pen), Simeon, Levi, Judah, Issakhar, le Zebulun ahi hi.
English: the sons of Leah; Reuben, Jacob's firstborn, and Simeon, and Levi, and Judah, and Issachar, and Zebulun:

**35:24**
Zolai: Rachel’ tapate: Josef le Benjamin ahi hi.
English: the sons of Rachel; Joseph, and Benjamin:

**35:25**
Zolai: Rachel’ nasem numei Bilhah’ tapate: Dan le Naftali ahi hi.
English: and the sons of Bilhah, Rachel's handmaid; Dan, and Naphtali:

**35:26**
Zolai: Leah’ nasem numei Zilpah’ tapate: Gad le Asher ahi hi. Hihte pen Paddanaram gamah ama sunga suak Jakob’ tapa sawm le nihte ahi hi.
English: and the sons of Zilpah, Leah's handmaid; Gad, and Asher: these are the sons of Jacob, which were born to him in Padan-aram.

**35:27**
Zolai: Abraham le Isaac tawlkhat a omna Mamre, ahih kei leh Kiriatharba (Hebron)-a a pa Isaac a omna-ah Jakob hong pai hi.
English: And Jacob came unto Isaac his father unto Mamre, unto the city of Arbah, which is Hebron, where Abraham and Isaac sojourned.

**35:28**
Zolai: Tu-in Isaac’ khansung, kum za le kum sawmgiat ahi hi.
English: And the days of Isaac were an hundred and fourscore years.

**35:29**
Zolai: Isaac in a nunung pen a hu sang hi. Amah a teek, kum tampi a pha-in si a, ama mite’ kiangah kigawm hi. Ama tapa Esau le Jakob in amah a vui uh hi.
English: And Isaac gave up the ghost, and died, and was gathered unto his people, being old and full of days: and his sons Esau and Jacob buried him.

## Chapter 36

**36:1**
Zolai: Hihte pen Esau (Edom) suanlekhakte ahi hi.
English: Now these are the generations of Esau, who is Edom.

**36:2**
Zolai: Esau in Kanaan numeite zi-in la hi. Hit mi Elon’ tanu Adah, Hiv mi Zibeon’ tapa Anah’ tanu Oholibamah,
English: Esau took his wives of the daughters of Canaan; Adah the daughter of Elon the Hittite, and Aholibamah the daughter of Anah the daughter of Zibeon the Hivite;

**36:3**
Zolai: le Nebaioth’ sanggamnu, Ishmael’ tanu Basemath ahi hi.
English: and Bashemath Ishmael's daughter, sister of Nebajoth.

**36:4**
Zolai: Adah in Esau tawh Elifaz nei a, Basemath in Reuel nei hi.
English: And Adah bare to Esau Eliphaz; and Bashemath bare Reuel;

**36:5**
Zolai: Oholibamah in Jeush, Jalam, le Korah nei hi. Hihte pen Kanaan gam sunga a neih Esau’ tapate ahi hi.
English: and Aholibamah bare Jeush, and Jaalam, and Korah: these are the sons of Esau, which were born unto him in the land of Canaan.

**36:6**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Esau in a zite, a tapate, a tanute, le ama innkuan sunga mi khempeuh; a bawngte, a ganhingte khempeuh; le Kanaan gam sunga a lam a neihsa khempeuh la-in a sanggampa Jakob kiang panin gamdang khatah paikhia hi.
English: And Esau took his wives, and his sons, and his daughters, and all the persons of his house, and his cattle, and all his beasts, and all his substance, which he had got in the land of Canaan; and went into the country from the face of his brother Jacob.

**36:7**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ten khop theih dingin amau’ neihsate tam lua a, a ganhingte uh hangin tawlkhat a omna uh leitang in amaute vak zo lo hi.
English: For their riches were more than that they might dwell together; and the land wherein they were strangers could not bear them because of their cattle.

**36:8**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Seir mualtung gamah Esau teng hi. Esau’ min dang khat pen Edom ahi hi.
English: Thus dwelt Esau in mount Seir: Esau is Edom.

**36:9**
Zolai: Hihte pen Seir mualtung gam a Edom mite’ pupi Esau’ suanlekhakte ahi hi.
English: And these are the generations of Esau the father of the Edomites in mount Seir:

**36:10**
Zolai: Esau’ tapate: Esau’ zi Adah’ tapa Elifaz, Esau’ zi Basemath’ tapa Reuel ahi hi.
English: these are the names of Esau's sons; Eliphaz the son of Adah the wife of Esau, Reuel the son of Bashemath the wife of Esau.

**36:11**
Zolai: Elifaz’ tapate: Teman, Omar, Zefo, Gatam, le Kenaz ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Eliphaz were Teman, Omar, Zepho, and Gatam, and Kenaz.

**36:12**
Zolai: (Timna pen Esau’ tapa Elifaz’ zineu hi a, amah in Elifaz tawh Amalek nei hi.) Hihte pen Esau’ zi Adah’ tapate ahi hi.
English: And Timna was concubine to Eliphaz Esau's son; and she bare to Eliphaz Amalek: these were the sons of Adah Esau's wife.

**36:13**
Zolai: Reuel’ tapate: Nahath, Zerah, Shammah, le Mizzah ahi hi. Hihte pen Esau’ zi Basemath’ tapate ahi hi.
English: And these are the sons of Reuel; Nahath, and Zerah, Shammah, and Mizzah: these were the sons of Bashemath Esau's wife.

**36:14**
Zolai: Esau’ zi, Zibeon’ tapa Anah’ tanu Oholibamah tapate: Jeush, Jalam, le Korah ahi hi.
English: And these were the sons of Aholibamah, the daughter of Anah the daughter of Zibeon, Esau's wife: and she bare to Esau Jeush, and Jaalam, and Korah.

**36:15**
Zolai: Esau’ suante hih bang ahi hi. Esau’ ta masa Elifaz’ tate: Teman, Omar, Zefo, Kenaz,
English: These were dukes of the sons of Esau: the sons of Eliphaz the firstborn son of Esau; duke Teman, duke Omar, duke Zepho, duke Kenaz,

**36:16**
Zolai: Korah, Gatam, le Amalek ahi hi. Hihte pen Edom gam sungah Elifaz’ suante hi a, Esau’ zi Adah’ sunga piangte ahi hi.
English: duke Korah, duke Gatam, and duke Amalek: these are the dukes that came of Eliphaz in the land of Edom; these were the sons of Adah.

**36:17**
Zolai: Esau’ tapa Reuel’ tapate: Nahath, Zerah, Shammah, le Mizzah hi a, Edom gam sungah a om Reuel’ suante ahi hi. Amaute pen Esau’ zi Basemath’ sung panin a piangte ahi hi.
English: And these are the sons of Reuel Esau's son; duke Nahath, duke Zerah, duke Shammah, duke Mizzah: these are the dukes that came of Reuel in the land of Edom; these are the sons of Bashemath Esau's wife.

**36:18**
Zolai: Esau’ zi Oholibamah’ tapate: Jeush, Jalam, le Korah ahi hi. Hihte pen Esau’ zi, Anah’ tanu Oholibamah’ sung panin a piangte ahi hi.
English: And these are the sons of Aholibamah Esau's wife; duke Jeush, duke Jaalam, duke Korah: these were the dukes that came of Aholibamah the daughter of Anah, Esau's wife.

**36:19**
Zolai: Hihte pen Esau (Edom) suante hi a, amaute’ sung pan beh lutangte ahi uh hi.
English: These are the sons of Esau, who is Edom, and these are their dukes.

**36:20**
Zolai: Tua gam a teng Hori mi Seir’ tapate: Lotan, Shobal, Zibeon, Anah,
English: These are the sons of Seir the Horite, who inhabited the land; Lotan, and Shobal, and Zibeon, and Anah,

**36:21**
Zolai: Dishon, Ezer, le Dishan hi a, Edom gam sunga Seir’ suante ahi Hori mite’ sung pan beh lutang ahi uh hi.
English: and Dishon, and Ezer, and Dishan: these are the dukes of the Horites, the children of Seir in the land of Edom.

**36:22**
Zolai: Lotan’ tapate: Hori le Heman ahi hi. Lotan’ sanggamnu Timna ahi hi.
English: And the children of Lotan were Hori and Hemam; and Lotan's sister was Timna.

**36:23**
Zolai: Shobal’ tapate: Alvan, Manahath, Ebal, Shefo, le Onam ahi hi.
English: And the children of Shobal were these; Alvan, and Manahath, and Ebal, Shepho, and Onam.

**36:24**
Zolai: Zibeon’ tapate: Ai-ah le Anah ahi hi. Amah pen a pa Zibeon’ late a cin laitakin gamlakah a sa ciktui a mu pa Anah ahi hi.
English: And these are the children of Zibeon; both Ajah, and Anah: this was that Anah that found the mules in the wilderness, as he fed the asses of Zibeon his father.

**36:25**
Zolai: Anah’ tate: Dishon le Anah’ tanu Oholibamah ahi hi.
English: And the children of Anah were these; Dishon, and Aholibamah the daughter of Anah.

**36:26**
Zolai: Dishon’ tapate: Hemdan, Eshban, Ithran, le Kheran ahi hi.
English: And these are the children of Dishon; Hemdan, and Eshban, and Ithran, and Cheran.

**36:27**
Zolai: Ezer’ tapate: Bilhan, Zaavan, le Akan ahi hi.
English: The children of Ezer are these; Bilhan, and Zaavan, and Akan.

**36:28**
Zolai: Dishan’ tapate: Uz le Aran ahi hi.
English: The children of Dishan are these; Uz, and Aran.

**36:29**
Zolai: Hori mite’ beh lutangte: Lotan, Shobal, Zibeon, Anah,
English: These are the dukes that came of the Horites; duke Lotan, duke Shobal, duke Zibeon, duke Anah,

**36:30**
Zolai: Dishon, Ezer, le Dishan ahi hi. Hihte pen Seir gam sungah amau’ beh ciatin Hori mite’ sung pan beh lutang ahi uh hi.
English: duke Dishon, duke Ezer, duke Dishan: these are the dukes that came of Hori, among their dukes in the land of Seir.

**36:31**
Zolai: Hihte pen Israel mite tungah kumpi khat beek in a uk ma-in Edom gam sunga kumpite ahi hi.
English: And these are the kings that reigned in the land of Edom, before there reigned any king over the children of Israel.

**36:32**
Zolai: Beor’ tapa Bela in Edom gam sung uk a, ama khuapi min Dinhabah ahi hi.
English: And Bela the son of Beor reigned in Edom: and the name of his city was Dinhabah.

**36:33**
Zolai: Bela si a, Bozrah khua mi Zerah’ tapa Jobab in ama tangin a uk hi.
English: And Bela died, and Jobab the son of Zerah of Bozrah reigned in his stead.

**36:34**
Zolai: Jobab si a, Teman mite’ gammi Husham in ama tangin a uk hi.
English: And Jobab died, and Husham of the land of Temani reigned in his stead.

**36:35**
Zolai: Husham si a, Moab gam sungah Midian mite a zo Bedad’ tapa Hadad in ama tangin uk a, ama khuapi min Avith ahi hi.
English: And Husham died, and Hadad the son of Bedad, who smote Midian in the field of Moab, reigned in his stead: and the name of his city was Avith.

**36:36**
Zolai: Hadad si a, Masrekah khua mi Samlah in ama tangin uk hi.
English: And Hadad died, and Samlah of Masrekah reigned in his stead.

**36:37**
Zolai: Samlah si a, Eufratis gun gei-a Rehoboth khua mi Shaul in ama tangin a uk hi.
English: And Samlah died, and Saul of Rehoboth by the river reigned in his stead.

**36:38**
Zolai: Shaul si a, Akbor’ tapa Baalhanan in ama tangin a uk hi.
English: And Saul died, and Baal-hanan the son of Achbor reigned in his stead.

**36:39**
Zolai: Akbor’ tapa Baalhanan si a, Hadar in ama tangin uk a, ama khuapi min Pau ahi hi. Ama zi’ min Mehetabel hi a, Mezahab’ tanu Matred, Matred tanu Mehetabel ahi hi.
English: And Baal-hanan the son of Achbor died, and Hadar reigned in his stead: and the name of his city was Pau; and his wife's name was Mehetabel, the daughter of Matred, the daughter of Mezahab.

**36:40**
Zolai: Amau’ innkuan le a tenna, amau’ min tawh kizui-in, Esau’ suan sung pan minamte’ min: Timna, Alvah, Jetheth,
English: And these are the names of the dukes that came of Esau, according to their families, after their places, by their names; duke Timnah, duke Alvah, duke Jetheth,

**36:41**
Zolai: Oholibamah, Elah, Pinon,
English: duke Aholibamah, duke Elah, duke Pinon,

**36:42**
Zolai: Kenaz, Teman, Mibzar,
English: duke Kenaz, duke Teman, duke Mibzar,

**36:43**
Zolai: Magdiel, le Iram ahi hi. Hihte in amau’ neih, amau’ tenna leitang min dingin amau’ min mah vawh pah uh a, Esau’ suan, Edom mi a kicite ahi uh hi.
English: duke Magdiel, duke Iram: these be the dukes of Edom, according to their habitations in the land of their possession: he is Esau the father of the Edomites.

## Chapter 37

**37:1**
Zolai: A pa tawlkhat a tenna Kanaan gamah Jakob teng hi.
English: And Jacob dwelt in the land wherein his father was a stranger, in the land of Canaan.

**37:2**
Zolai: Jakob innkuante’ tangthu hih bang ahi hi. Josef kum sawm le sagih pha ahih manin a sanggamte tawh tuuhon cing hi. A pa’ zite Bilhah le Zilpah’ tapate tawh tangval ahi uh hi. Josef in a pa uh kiangah amaute’ siat gamtatnate a gen hi.
English: These are the generations of Jacob. Joseph, being seventeen years old, was feeding the flock with his brethren; and the lad was with the sons of Bilhah, and with the sons of Zilpah, his father's wives: and Joseph brought unto his father their evil report.

**37:3**
Zolai: Tu-in Israel in a ta dangte khat peuhpeuh sangin Josef itzaw hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh a teek khitin a neih a tapa ahi hi. Amah in ama a dingin puantualpi bansau khat a bawlsak hi.
English: Now Israel loved Joseph more than all his children, because he was the son of his old age: and he made him a coat of many colours.

**37:4**
Zolai: Ahih hangin a pa un a sanggamte khempeuh sangin amah a itzawkna a sanggamte in a muh uh ciangin, amaute in Josef mudah uh a, nuamtakin amah hopih thei lo uh hi.
English: And when his brethren saw that their father loved him more than all his brethren, they hated him, and could not speak peaceably unto him.

**37:5**
Zolai: Tu-in Josef in mang khat man a, amah in a sanggamte’ lakah a gen ciangin amaute in amah muhdah semsemna-in nei uh hi.
English: And Joseph dreamed a dream, and he told it his brethren: and they hated him yet the more.

**37:6**
Zolai: Amah in amaute kiangah, “Keima mat hih mang ngai un:
English: And he said unto them, Hear, I pray you, this dream which I have dreamed:

**37:7**
Zolai: Eite in lo lai-ah buhlom i hen a, keima buhlom tho-in ding tang hi. Tua kiimah note’ buhlom kikhawm a, keima buhlom mai-ah kun uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: for, behold, we were binding sheaves in the field, and, lo, my sheaf arose, and also stood upright; and, behold, your sheaves stood round about, and made obeisance to my sheaf.

**37:8**
Zolai: A sanggamte in ama kiangah, “Kote’ tungah nang in hong uk ding a, kote’ tungah ukna aana nei ding na hi hiam?” a ci uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin amaute in a mangte le a thugente’ hangin amah mudah semsem uh hi.
English: And his brethren said to him, Shalt thou indeed reign over us? or shalt thou indeed have dominion over us? And they hated him yet the more for his dreams, and for his words.

**37:9**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in mang dang khat man a, tua mang a sanggamte kiangah genin, “Mang dang khat ka man hi. Ni, kha, le aksi sawm le khatte kei’ mai-ah hong kun uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he dreamed yet another dream, and told it his brethren, and said, Behold, I have dreamed a dream more; and, behold, the sun and the moon and the eleven stars made obeisance to me.

**37:10**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah in a pa le a sanggamte’ kiangah a gen ciangin a pa in amah taii-in, “Nangma mat hih mang a bangci mang ahi hiam? Kei le na nu le na sanggamte, nangma mai leilakah a kun dingin hong pai ding ka hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And he told it to his father, and to his brethren: and his father rebuked him, and said unto him, What is this dream that thou hast dreamed? Shall I and thy mother and thy brethren indeed come to bow down ourselves to thee to the earth?

**37:11**
Zolai: A sanggamte in amah haza uh a, ahih hangin a pa in hih thute a ciamteh hi.
English: And his brethren envied him; but his father observed the saying.

**37:12**
Zolai: Khatvei a pa uh’ tuuhonte a cing dingin Shekhem gei-ah a sanggamte a pai hi.
English: And his brethren went to feed their father's flock in Shechem.

**37:13**
Zolai: Israel in Josef kiangah, “Na sanggamte in Shekhem-ah tuuhon cing uh hi lo ahi hiam? Hong pai in, amau’ kiangah hong sawl ning,” a ci hi. Amah in a kiangah, “Hiah om ing,” a ci hi.
English: And Israel said unto Joseph, Do not thy brethren feed the flock in Shechem? come, and I will send thee unto them. And he said to him, Here am I .

**37:14**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in, “Tu-in va pai inla, na sanggamte le tuuhonte a cidam hiam va thei inla, kei kiangah thu hong zasakkik in,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in Hebron kuam panin Josef sawl a, Shekhem-ah amah va tung hi.
English: And he said to him, Go, I pray thee, see whether it be well with thy brethren, and well with the flocks; and bring me word again. So he sent him out of the vale of Hebron, and he came to Shechem.

**37:15**
Zolai: Gamlakah a vak kawikawina mi khat in mu a, “Bang zongzong na hi hiam?” ci-in a dong hi.
English: And a certain man found him, and, behold, he was wandering in the field: and the man asked him, saying, What seekest thou?

**37:16**
Zolai: “Ka sanggamte a zong ka hi hi. Amaute in koi lai-ah tuuhon cing uh hiam, hong gen in, hong thum ing,” amah in ci hi.
English: And he said, I seek my brethren: tell me, I pray thee, where they feed their flocks .

**37:17**
Zolai: Mipa in, “Amaute paikhia zo uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh, ‘Dothan-ah pai ni,’ a cih uh ka za hi,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin a sanggamte’ nungah Josef pai a, Dothan-ah amaute a mu hi.
English: And the man said, They are departed hence; for I heard them say, Let us go to Dothan. And Joseph went after his brethren, and found them in Dothan.

**37:18**
Zolai: Amaute in gamlapi-ah amah na mu uh a, amaute’ nai-ah amah hong tun ma-in amaute in amah thah ding na vaihawm uh hi.
English: And when they saw him afar off, even before he came near unto them, they conspired against him to slay him.

**37:19**
Zolai: Amaute khatlekhat in, “Hih lai-ah mangman pa hong pai hi.
English: And they said one to another, Behold, this dreamer cometh.

**37:20**
Zolai: Tu-in hong pai un. Amah thatin dum sung khatah lawn ni. Tua ciangin gamsa khat in amah netum khin hi, i ci ding hi. A mangte bang a suak hiam i mu ding hi,” a kici uh hi.
English: Come now therefore, and let us slay him, and cast him into some pit, and we will say, Some evil beast hath devoured him: and we shall see what will become of his dreams.

**37:21**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Reuben in tua thu a zak ciangin, “Amah that kei ni,” ci-in, amau’ khutsung panin amah honkhia hi.
English: And Reuben heard it , and he delivered him out of their hands; and said, Let us not kill him.

**37:22**
Zolai: A pa’ kiang a tunpihkik theih nadingin amau’ khutsung pan a hotkhiat theih nadingin Reuben in amaute’ kiangah, “Amah that kei un. Hih gamlak dum sungah amah lawn un. Ahih hangin amah bangmah cih kei un,” a ci hi.
English: And Reuben said unto them, Shed no blood, but cast him into this pit that is in the wilderness, and lay no hand upon him; that he might rid him out of their hands, to deliver him to his father again.

**37:23**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin, a sanggamte’ kiangah Josef hong tun ciangin, ama silh lai a puantualpi bansau a hawkkhiatsak uh hi.
English: And it came to pass, when Joseph was come unto his brethren, that they stript Joseph out of his coat, his coat of many colours that was on him;

**37:24**
Zolai: Amaute in Josef la-in dum sung khatah a lawn uh hi. A dum pen a hawm hi a, a sungah tui om lo hi.
English: and they took him, and cast him into a pit: and the pit was empty, there was no water in it.

**37:25**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute an ne dingin tu uh hi. A khuadak uhleh Gilead panin Ishmael mite a kalaohte uh tawh singnai, lingsi, le myrrh paknamtui pua-in Egypt-ah puaksuk dingin a pai mu uh hi.
English: And they sat down to eat bread: and they lifted up their eyes and looked, and, behold, a company of Ishmeelites came from Gilead with their camels bearing spicery and balm and myrrh, going to carry it down to Egypt.

**37:26**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Judah in a sanggamte kiangah, “I sanggampa thatin amah i thahna im lehang bang meetna om ahi hiam?
English: And Judah said unto his brethren, What profit is it if we slay our brother, and conceal his blood?

**37:27**
Zolai: Hong pai un, Ishmael mite kiangah amah zuak ni. Amah bangmah cih kei ni. Bang hang hiam cih leh amah i sanggampa, eima cilesa ahi hi,” a ci hi. A sanggamte in ama thu mang hi.
English: Come, and let us sell him to the Ishmeelites, and let not our hand be upon him; for he is our brother and our flesh. And his brethren were content.

**37:28**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Midian mi sumbawlte in hong nawk hi. Amaute in Josef kai to-in dum sung panin domkhia to uh a, Ishmael mite tungah ngun shekel sawmnihin amah zuak uh a, amaute in Egypt-ah Josef a paipih uh hi.
English: Then there passed by Midianites merchantmen; and they drew and lifted up Joseph out of the pit, and sold Joseph to the Ishmeelites for twenty pieces of silver: and they brought Joseph into Egypt.

**37:29**
Zolai: Reuben dumah paikikin dum sungah Josef a om lohna a muh ciangin amah in a puan balkek a,
English: And Reuben returned unto the pit; and, behold, Joseph was not in the pit; and he rent his clothes.

**37:30**
Zolai: a sanggamte kiangah ciahkikin, “Tangvalpa om nawn lo hi. Kei bangci ding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And he returned unto his brethren, and said, The child is not; and I, whither shall I go?

**37:31**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in Josef’ puan la-in, keel khat go uh a, a sisan sungah a puan diah uh hi.
English: And they took Joseph's coat, and killed a kid of the goats, and dipped the coat in the blood;

**37:32**
Zolai: Amaute in a puantualpi bansau a pa uh kiangah puak uh a, “Hih puan ka mu uh hi. Na tapa’ puan hi hiam, hi lo hiam tu-in thei in,” a ci uh hi.
English: and they sent the coat of many colours, and they brought it to their father; and said, This have we found: know now whether it be thy son's coat or no.

**37:33**
Zolai: Amah in Josef’ puan ahihlam thei a, “Ka tapa’ puan ahi hi. Gamsa khatpeuh in amah netum khinzo hi ding hi. Josef kibalnen gawp ahihna up loh nading om lo hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he knew it, and said, It is my son's coat; an evil beast hath devoured him; Joseph is without doubt rent in pieces.

**37:34**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in ama puan balkekin, a kawngah puanhampi teng a, a tapa’ hangin ni tampi sung a kap hi.
English: And Jacob rent his clothes, and put sackcloth upon his loins, and mourned for his son many days.

**37:35**
Zolai: A tapate le a tanute khempeuh in amah hehnem uh a, ahih hangin amah hehnep zawhin om lo a, “Hi lo hi. A kapsa-in ka tapa kiang Leinuai-ah ka pai ding hi,” a ci hi. Tua bangin ama hangin a pa kap hi.
English: And all his sons and all his daughters rose up to comfort him; but he refused to be comforted; and he said, For I will go down into the grave unto my son mourning. Thus his father wept for him.

**37:36**
Zolai: Tua kikal sungin Midian mite in Egypt gam sunga inncing mang, Faro’ nuai-ah ulian ahi Potifar’ tungah Josef na zuak uh hi.
English: And the Midianites sold him into Egypt unto Potiphar, an officer of Pharaoh's, and captain of the guard.

## Chapter 38

**38:1**
Zolai: Tua hun laitakin Judah a sanggamte kiang panin paisukin, Adullam mi Hirah min nei mi khat tawh omkhawm hi.
English: And it came to pass at that time, that Judah went down from his brethren, and turned in to a certain Adullamite, whose name was Hirah.

**38:2**
Zolai: Tua lai-ah Judah in Kanaan mi Shua’ tanu mu hi. Amah in tua nu tenpihin luppih a,
English: And Judah saw there a daughter of a certain Canaanite, whose name was Shuah; and he took her, and went in unto her.

**38:3**
Zolai: tua nu gai-in tapa khat nei a, amah in a min Er a phuak hi.
English: And she conceived, and bare a son; and he called his name Er.

**38:4**
Zolai: Tua nu gai leuleu-in tapa khat nei a, tua nu in a min Onan a phuak hi.
English: And she conceived again, and bare a son; and she called his name Onan.

**38:5**
Zolai: Tua nu in tapa khat nei leuleu-in a min Shelah a phuak hi. Tua nu in amah tawh Shelah a neih laitakin Khezib-ah amah a om hi.
English: And she yet again conceived, and bare a son; and called his name Shelah: and he was at Chezib, when she bare him.

**38:6**
Zolai: Judah in a tapa masa Er a dingin zi khat la a, tua nu’ min Tamar ahi hi.
English: And Judah took a wife for Er his firstborn, whose name was Tamar.

**38:7**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Judah’ ta masa Er pen Topa’ muhna-ah hoih lo a, Topa in amah that hi.
English: And Er, Judah's firstborn, was wicked in the sight of the LORD ; and the LORD slew him.

**38:8**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Judah in Onan kiangah, “Na sanggampa’ zi tawh lumkhawm inla, tua nu’ tungah pasal’ sanggamte’ tavuan sem inla, na sanggampa a dingin ta nei in,” a ci hi.
English: And Judah said unto Onan, Go in unto thy brother's wife, and marry her, and raise up seed to thy brother.

**38:9**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Onan in tate pen ama a’ ahih loh ding thei hi. Tua ahih ciangin a sanggampa’ zi tawh a lupkhawm ciangin a sanggampa’ tungah ta pia kha ding ahih manin a natui leilakah buasak hi.
English: And Onan knew that the seed should not be his; and it came to pass, when he went in unto his brother's wife, that he spilled it on the ground, lest that he should give seed to his brother.

**38:10**
Zolai: Ama gamtatna Topa’ muhna-ah lungkimhuai lo a, Topa in amah zong a that hi.
English: And the thing which he did displeased the LORD : wherefore he slew him also.

**38:11**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Judah in a monu Tamar’ tungah, “Ka tapa Shelah a gol mateng na pa’ inn-ah meigongnu-in va om in,” a ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh a sanggamte mah bangin amah zong si kha ding ci-in lau hi. Tua ahih ciangin Tamar pai-in a pa’ inn-ah a om hi.
English: Then said Judah to Tamar his daughter in law, Remain a widow at thy father's house, till Shelah my son be grown: for he said, Lest peradventure he die also, as his brethren did . And Tamar went and dwelt in her father's house.

**38:12**
Zolai: Tua hun sungin Judah’ zi, Shua’ tanu si hi. Judah a dahna hun a ven’ ciangin a lawm Hirah tawh Timnah-a ama tuumul a mette kiangah paito hi.
English: And in process of time the daughter of Shuah Judah's wife died; and Judah was comforted, and went up unto his sheepshearers to Timnath, he and his friend Hirah the Adullamite.

**38:13**
Zolai: “Na teekpa a tuute mul met dingin Timnah-ah paito hi,” ci-in Tamar’ kiangah a kigen ciangin,
English: And it was told Tamar, saying, Behold thy father in law goeth up to Timnath to shear his sheep.

**38:14**
Zolai: a meigong numei puan suahkhia-in, a kituamna silhin amah kituam a, Timnah paina lampi gei-a Enaim paina munah na tu hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Shelah a khang cing khin ahihna amah in thei a, ahi zongin amah tawh kitengsak nai lo hi.
English: And she put her widow's garments off from her, and covered her with a vail, and wrapped herself, and sat in an open place, which is by the way to Timnath; for she saw that Shelah was grown, and she was not given unto him to wife.

**38:15**
Zolai: Judah in tua nu a muh ciangin amah in a mai tuam ahih manin numei paktat dingin ngaihsun hi.
English: When Judah saw her, he thought her to be an harlot; because she had covered her face.

**38:16**
Zolai: Lampi gei-a tua nu’ kiangah amah pai a, “Hong pai in, lumkhawm ni,” a ci hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh tua nu pen a monu ahihlam thei lo hi. Tua nu in, “I lupkhop man dingin kei bang hong pia ding na hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And he turned unto her by the way, and said, Go to, I pray thee, let me come in unto thee; (for he knew not that she was his daughter in law.) And she said, What wilt thou give me, that thou mayest come in unto me?

**38:17**
Zolai: Amah in dawngin, “Keelhon panin keelno khat hong puak ning,” a ci hi. Tua nu in, “Nong puak mateng khapna khat nong pia ding hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And he said, I will send thee a kid from the flock. And she said, Wilt thou give me a pledge, till thou send it?

**38:18**
