Zolai: Amah in, “Bang khapna nang hong pia ding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua nu in dawngin, “Na min gelhna le na khauhual le na khutsunga om na ciangkhut,” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin amah in tua nu tungah tuate pia-in, amah luppih a, amah tawh tua nu a gai hi.
English: And he said, What pledge shall I give thee? And she said, Thy signet, and thy bracelets, and thy staff that is in thine hand. And he gave it her, and came in unto her, and she conceived by him.

**38:19**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah dingin paikhia a, a kikhuhna puan suahkhia-in meigong numei ahihna puan a silh hi.
English: And she arose, and went away, and laid by her vail from her, and put on the garments of her widowhood.

**38:20**
Zolai: Numei’ khutsung panin a khapna a lakik dingin Judah in Adullam mi a lawmpa a ganno tawh a sawl ciangin, amah in tua nu mu zo lo hi.
English: And Judah sent the kid by the hand of his friend the Adullamite, to receive his pledge from the woman's hand: but he found her not.

**38:21**
Zolai: Amah in tua lai mun mite dong a, “Lam gei Enaim a om numei paktat nu koi-ah om ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amaute in, “Hih lai-ah numei paktat om ngei lo hi,” na ci uh hi.
English: Then he asked the men of that place, saying, Where is the harlot, that was openly by the way side? And they said, There was no harlot in this place .

**38:22**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Judah kiangah amah ciahkikin, “Amah ka mu kei hi. Tua lai mun mite in, ‘Hih lai-ah numei paktat om ngei lo hi,’ zong hong ci uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he returned to Judah, and said, I cannot find her; and also the men of the place said, that there was no harlot in this place .

**38:23**
Zolai: Judah in dawngin, “Eite hong kinuihsan kha ding ahih ciangin a nate ama a dingin kem mai hen. Hih ganno ka puak a, nang in tua nu na muh lohna na thei hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Judah said, Let her take it to her, lest we be shamed: behold, I sent this kid, and thou hast not found her.

**38:24**
Zolai: Tua zawh kha thum ciangin Judah tungah, “Na monu Tamar paktatin gamta hi. Tua tham loin paktatna tawh naupaii hi,” ci-in kigen hi. Judah in, “Amah paikhiatpih un; amah kihaltum hen,” a ci hi.
English: And it came to pass about three months after, that it was told Judah, saying, Tamar thy daughter in law hath played the harlot; and also, behold, she is with child by whoredom. And Judah said, Bring her forth, and let her be burnt.

**38:25**
Zolai: Amah a kipaikhiatpih laitakin amah in a teekpa kiangah kam khak a, “Hih nate a nei pa tawh nau ka nei hi,” a ci hi. Tua nu in, “Ciamteh in, hong thum ing, min gelhna le khauhual le ciangkhut, hih nate kua-a’ ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: When she was brought forth, she sent to her father in law, saying, By the man, whose these are, am I with child: and she said, Discern, I pray thee, whose are these, the signet, and bracelets, and staff.

**38:26**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Judah in tua nate thei a, “Ka tapa Shelah tawh gawm lo ka hih ciangin, tua numei, kei sangin thuman zaw hi,” a ci hi. Tua nu tawh amah lumkhawm kik nawn lo hi.
English: And Judah acknowledged them , and said, She hath been more righteous than I; because that I gave her not to Shelah my son. And he knew her again no more.

**38:27**
Zolai: Tua nu a suah hun a tun ciangin a naubu sungah nih om hi.
English: And it came to pass in the time of her travail, that, behold, twins were in her womb.

**38:28**
Zolai: Nausuak dingin a nat ciangin, khat in a khut dawksak hi. Naudom nu in khausan khat la-in a khut tungah khih a, “Hih pen hong pai masa,” ci pah hi.
English: And it came to pass, when she travailed, that the one put out his hand: and the midwife took and bound upon his hand a scarlet thread, saying, This came out first.

**38:29**
Zolai: Ahih hangin a khut a dawh tum kik laitakin, en in, a sanggampa hong suakkhia hi. Amah in, “Nang a dingin a vang nangmahmah in bawltawm!” a ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin ama min Perez kiphuak hi.
English: And it came to pass, as he drew back his hand, that, behold, his brother came out: and she said, How hast thou broken forth? this breach be upon thee: therefore his name was called Pharez.

**38:30**
Zolai: Tua khit ciangin a khut tunga khausan tawh a sanggampa hong suakkhia a, ama min Zerah kiphuak hi.
English: And afterward came out his brother, that had the scarlet thread upon his hand: and his name was called Zarah.

## Chapter 39

**39:1**
Zolai: Tu-in Egypt-ah Josef kipaipih suk a, tua lai-a a paipih Ishmael mite tung panin Egypt mi, inncing mangpa, Faro’ nuai-a mangpa Potifar in amah na lei hi.
English: And Joseph was brought down to Egypt; and Potiphar, an officer of Pharaoh, captain of the guard, an Egyptian, bought him of the hands of the Ishmeelites, which had brought him down thither.

**39:2**
Zolai: Topa in Josef ompih a, amah nasep a zo mi khat suak hi. Amah, Egypt mi a topa’ inn sungah om a,
English: And the LORD was with Joseph, and he was a prosperous man; and he was in the house of his master the Egyptian.

**39:3**
Zolai: Topa in amah a ompihna le Topa in ama khut sungah a hih khempeuh a mavansakna a topa in mu hi.
English: And his master saw that the LORD was with him, and that the LORD made all that he did to prosper in his hand.

**39:4**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Josef in ama mai-ah maipha ngahin ama na sem a, amah in a innsung ukpa-in bawlin a neih khempeuh a uk dingin a koih hi.
English: And Joseph found grace in his sight, and he served him: and he made him overseer over his house, and all that he had he put into his hand.

**39:5**
Zolai: Amah in a innsung uk leh a neih khempeuh a ukin a bawl a kipan Topa in Josef’ hangin Egypt mipa’ innkuan thupha pia hi. Innsung hitaleh lo sung hitaleh a neih khempeuh tungah Topa’ thupha om hi.
English: And it came to pass from the time that he had made him overseer in his house, and over all that he had, that the LORD blessed the Egyptian's house for Joseph's sake; and the blessing of the LORD was upon all that he had in the house, and in the field.

**39:6**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in a neih khempeuh Josef’ khut sungah ap hi. Josef nei khin ahih manin amau nupa sungthu lobuang thudangte lunghihmawh dingin ngaihsun lo hi. Tu-in Josef ngaihbaangin a mel hoih hi.
English: And he left all that he had in Joseph's hand; and he knew not ought he had, save the bread which he did eat. And Joseph was a goodly person, and well favoured.

**39:7**
Zolai: Tawlkhat khit ciangin a topa’ zi in Josef zawl mit a, “Kei tawh hong lumkhawm in,” a ci hi.
English: And it came to pass after these things, that his master's wife cast her eyes upon Joseph; and she said, Lie with me.

**39:8**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah in nialin a topa’ zi kiangah, “En in, kei hong nei ahih manin ka topa in inn sungah bangmah lunghihmawhna nei lo a, ama neih khempeuh ka khut sungah hong koih khin hi.
English: But he refused, and said unto his master's wife, Behold, my master wotteth not what is with me in the house, and he hath committed all that he hath to my hand;

**39:9**
Zolai: Hih inn sungah kei sangin amah lianzaw lo hi. Nang, ama zi na hih manin, nang lobuang kei kiang panin amah in a kep tuam bangmah om lo hi. Tua ahih ciangin bangci-in hih gitlohna lianpi bawlin Pasian’ tungah khial ding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: there is none greater in this house than I; neither hath he kept back any thing from me but thee, because thou art his wife: how then can I do this great wickedness, and sin against God?

**39:10**
Zolai: Amah in ni khat khit ni khat Josef a zol hangin, amah tawh lupkhop ding hitaleh omkhop ding hitaleh amah in tua nu’ thu ngai lo hi.
English: And it came to pass, as she spake to Joseph day by day, that he hearkened not unto her, to lie by her, or to be with her.

**39:11**
Zolai: Ahih hangin ni khat, amah a nasep sem dingin inn sungah pai a, inn sungah innsung mite khat zong a om loh laitakin,
English: And it came to pass about this time, that Joseph went into the house to do his business; and there was none of the men of the house there within.

**39:12**
Zolai: tua nu in a puan-in amah man a, “Kei tawh hong lumkhawm hoh in,” a ci hi. Ahih hangin amah in tua nu’ khut sungah a puan nusia-in tai-in tua inn panin a paikhia hi.
English: And she caught him by his garment, saying, Lie with me: and he left his garment in her hand, and fled, and got him out.

**39:13**
Zolai: Tua nu in, amah in a khut sungah puan nusia-in inn panin a taikhiatna a muh ciangin,
English: And it came to pass, when she saw that he had left his garment in her hand, and was fled forth,

**39:14**
Zolai: ama innsung mite samin amaute kiangah, “En un, amah in eite hong no dingin Hebru mi khat eite’ lakah hong paipih hi. Kei tawh a lumkhawm dingin amah hong sungtang a, nakpitakin kei ka kiko hi.
English: that she called unto the men of her house, and spake unto them, saying, See, he hath brought in an Hebrew unto us to mock us; he came in unto me to lie with me, and I cried with a loud voice:

**39:15**
Zolai: Ka aw sangsakin ka kikona a zak ciangin amah in ka kiangah a puan nusia a, tai-in inn panin paikhia hi,” a ci hi.
English: and it came to pass, when he heard that I lifted up my voice and cried, that he left his garment with me, and fled, and got him out.

**39:16**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Josef’ topa inn-ah hong ciah mateng amah in a kiangah a puan koih hi.
English: And she laid up his garment by her, until his lord came home.

**39:17**
Zolai: Tua nu in ama kiangah tua thu mah gen a, “Kote kianga nong paipih Hebru mi nasempa keimah a no dingin hong sungtang hi.
English: And she spake unto him according to these words, saying, The Hebrew servant, which thou hast brought unto us, came in unto me to mock me:

**39:18**
Zolai: Ahih hangin ka aw sangsakin ka kiko phetin amah in a puan kei kiangah nusia-in inn panin taikhia hi,” a ci hi.
English: and it came to pass, as I lifted up my voice and cried, that he left his garment with me, and fled out.

**39:19**
Zolai: “Na nasempa in kei hong bawlna dan hih bang hi,” ci-in a zi in ama kianga a genna a topa in a zak ciangin nak heh mahmah hi.
English: And it came to pass, when his master heard the words of his wife, which she spake unto him, saying, After this manner did thy servant to me; that his wrath was kindled.

**39:20**
Zolai: Josef’ topa in amah manin kumpipa’ thongkiate a kikhumna thong sungah amah koih a, tua thong sungah amah om hi.
English: And Joseph's master took him, and put him into the prison, a place where the king's prisoners were bound: and he was there in the prison.

**39:21**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Topa in Josef ompihin ama tungah itna kip lak a, thong kem pa’ muhna-ah amah maipha a pia hi.
English: But the LORD was with Joseph, and shewed him mercy, and gave him favour in the sight of the keeper of the prison.

**39:22**
Zolai: Thong kem pa in thong sunga thongkia mi khempeuh Josef’ et dingin ap a, tua lai-a a kisem khempeuh ama hih ahi hi.
English: And the keeper of the prison committed to Joseph's hand all the prisoners that were in the prison; and whatsoever they did there, he was the doer of it .

**39:23**
Zolai: Topa in amah ompih ahih manin Josef’ etna sunga om peuhmah thong kem pa in don lo hi. Ama hih peuhmah Topa in daupaisak hi.
English: The keeper of the prison looked not to any thing that was under his hand; because the LORD was with him, and that which he did, the LORD made it to prosper.

## Chapter 40

**40:1**
Zolai: Tua zawh tawlkhat khit ciangin, Egypt kumpipa’ an piapa le a anhuan pa in Egypt kumpipa ahi amau’ topa hehsak uh hi.
English: And it came to pass after these things, that the butler of the king of Egypt and his baker had offended their lord the king of Egypt.

**40:2**
Zolai: An piapi pa le anhuan pipa ahi, ama nuai-a mangte nih tungah Faro heh a,
English: And Pharaoh was wroth against two of his officers, against the chief of the butlers, and against the chief of the bakers.

**40:3**
Zolai: Josef a kikhumna thong sung, inncing mangpa’ inn sungah amah in amaute a koih hi.
English: And he put them in ward in the house of the captain of the guard, into the prison, the place where Joseph was bound.

**40:4**
Zolai: Inncing mangpa in amaute Josef kemsak a, amah in amaute’ na sem hi. Kikhumna sungah amaute tawlkhat om uh hi.
English: And the captain of the guard charged Joseph with them, and he served them: and they continued a season in ward.

**40:5**
Zolai: Zan khat amau tegel in mang man uh hi. Thong sunga a om an piapa le anhuan pa, amau’ mang a tuam tuak, a mang khiatna zong a tuam tuak mah ahi hi.
English: And they dreamed a dream both of them, each man his dream in one night, each man according to the interpretation of his dream, the butler and the baker of the king of Egypt, which were bound in the prison.

**40:6**
Zolai: Zingsang ciangin amaute kiangah Josef pai-in amaute a muh ciangin, amaute na lungkham uh hi.
English: And Joseph came in unto them in the morning, and looked upon them, and, behold, they were sad.

**40:7**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin a topa’ inn sunga amah tawh a kikhumin a om Faro’ nuai-a mangte amah in dong a, “Bang hangin tuni-in maimial na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And he asked Pharaoh's officers that were with him in the ward of his lord's house, saying, Wherefore look ye so sadly to day?

**40:8**
Zolai: Amaute in ama kiangah, “Mang ka man uh a, tuate a khiathei ding om lo hi,” na ci uh hi. Josef in amaute kiangah, “Mang khiat theihnate Pasian’ hong piak hi lo ahi hiam? Kei kiangah hong gen un, hong thum ing,” a ci hi.
English: And they said unto him, We have dreamed a dream, and there is no interpreter of it. And Joseph said unto them, Do not interpretations belong to God? tell me them , I pray you.

**40:9**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin an piapi pa in Josef kiangah a mang gen a, “Ka mangin ka mai-ah leenggui khat om a,
English: And the chief butler told his dream to Joseph, and said to him, In my dream, behold, a vine was before me;

**40:10**
Zolai: tua leenggui tungah hiang thum om hi. A sel phetin pakkhia pah a, a bomte leenggah suakin min pah hi.
English: and in the vine were three branches: and it was as though it budded, and her blossoms shot forth; and the clusters thereof brought forth ripe grapes:

**40:11**
Zolai: Ka khut sungah Faro’ hai ka tawi hi. Keimah in leenggahte loin Faro’ hai sungah ka suk a, Faro’ khut tungah a hai ka pia hi,” a ci hi.
English: and Pharaoh's cup was in my hand: and I took the grapes, and pressed them into Pharaoh's cup, and I gave the cup into Pharaoh's hand.

**40:12**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Josef in ama kiangah, “A khiatna hih bang ahi hi. Hiang thumte, ni thum ahi hi.
English: And Joseph said unto him, This is the interpretation of it: The three branches are three days:

**40:13**
Zolai: Ni thum sungin Faro in nang hong khah ding a, na za-ah nang hong koih kik ding hi. Ama an piapa na hih lai-a mah bangin ama khut tungah Faro’ hai na pia ding hi.
English: yet within three days shall Pharaoh lift up thine head, and restore thee unto thy place: and thou shalt deliver Pharaoh's cup into his hand, after the former manner when thou wast his butler.

**40:14**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kei hong phawk in. Nang tungah thu hong hoih ciangin kei tungah hehpihna hong bawl in, kong thum hi. Faro’ tungah kei’ thu genin, hih inn panin kei hong lakhia in.
English: But think on me when it shall be well with thee, and shew kindness, I pray thee, unto me, and make mention of me unto Pharaoh, and bring me out of this house:

**40:15**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Hebru mite’ gam panin kei hong kigukhia a, hih lai-ah zong amaute in thong mial sungah kei hong koih nadingin bangmah ka gamta kei hi,” a ci hi.
English: for indeed I was stolen away out of the land of the Hebrews: and here also have I done nothing that they should put me into the dungeon.

**40:16**
Zolai: An huanpipa in a khiatna a hoihlam hi, ci-in a muh ciangin, amah in Josef kiangah, “Kei zong mang khat ka man hi: Ka lu tungah mohlawh thum om a,
English: When the chief baker saw that the interpretation was good, he said unto Joseph, I also was in my dream, and, behold, I had three white baskets on my head:

**40:17**
Zolai: a lawh tungnung pen sungah an huansa namkim Faro a dingin om hi. Ahih hangin ka lu tunga lawh sung panin vasate in ne uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: and in the uppermost basket there was of all manner of bakemeats for Pharaoh; and the birds did eat them out of the basket upon my head.

**40:18**
Zolai: Josef in dawngin, “A khiatna hih bang ahi hi: Lawh thumte, ni thum ahi hi.
English: And Joseph answered and said, This is the interpretation thereof: The three baskets are three days:

**40:19**
Zolai: Ni thum sungin Faro in nang hong lakhia-in na lu hong tan ding a, sing tung khatah nang hong khai ding hi. Vasate in na sa ne ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: yet within three days shall Pharaoh lift up thy head from off thee, and shall hang thee on a tree; and the birds shall eat thy flesh from off thee.

**40:20**
Zolai: A ni thum ni, Faro’ suah ni hunin, amah in a nasemte khempeuh a dingin pawi khat kham a, an piapi pa le an huanpipa lakhia hi.
English: And it came to pass the third day, which was Pharaoh's birthday, that he made a feast unto all his servants: and he lifted up the head of the chief butler and of the chief baker among his servants.

**40:21**
Zolai: Amah in an piapi pa an piak nasepah koihkik a, amah in Faro’ khut sungah a hai pia hi.
English: And he restored the chief butler unto his butlership again; and he gave the cup into Pharaoh's hand:

**40:22**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Josef’ khiat mah bangin an huanpipa a khailum hi.
English: but he hanged the chief baker: as Joseph had interpreted to them.

**40:23**
Zolai: Ahi zongin an piapi pa in Josef phawk nawn lo a, amah mangngilh ta hi.
English: Yet did not the chief butler remember Joseph, but forgat him.

## Chapter 41

**41:1**
Zolai: Tua zawh kum nih bit khit ciangin Faro in mang man a, amah Nail gun gei-ah ding hi.
English: And it came to pass at the end of two full years, that Pharaoh dreamed: and, behold, he stood by the river.

**41:2**
Zolai: Nail gun sung panin bawngpi a zol a thau sagih hong paikhia a, amaute in phai lopate ne uh hi.
English: And, behold, there came up out of the river seven well favoured kine and fatfleshed; and they fed in a meadow.

**41:3**
Zolai: Amaute’ khit ciangin Nail gun sung pan mahin a gulhgawng a gawng bawngpi dang sagih hong paikhia a, Nail gun gei-a bawngpi dangte kiangah ding uh hi.
English: And, behold, seven other kine came up after them out of the river, ill favoured and leanfleshed; and stood by the other kine upon the brink of the river.

**41:4**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a gulhgawng bawngpi gawng sagihte in a zol a thau bawngpi sagihte netum uh hi. Tua ciangin Faro khang lo hi.
English: And the ill favoured and leanfleshed kine did eat up the seven well favoured and fat kine. So Pharaoh awoke.

**41:5**
Zolai: Tua ciangin ihmu-in a nih veina mang man hi. A taksa a hoih buhvui sagih kung khat tungah vui hi.
English: And he slept and dreamed the second time: and, behold, seven ears of corn came up upon one stalk, rank and good.

**41:6**
Zolai: Tuate’ khit ciangin nisuahna huih in a theemsak a hawm vui sagih hong pokhia hi.
English: And, behold, seven thin ears and blasted with the east wind sprung up after them.

**41:7**
Zolai: A vui hawmte in a taksa a dim vui sagihte valhtum uh hi. Tua ciangin Faro khang lo a, tua pen a mang na hi hi.
English: And the seven thin ears devoured the seven rank and full ears. And Pharaoh awoke, and, behold, it was a dream.

**41:8**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin zingsangin a lungkham hi. Amah in mi sawlin Egypt mitphial siamte khempeuh le a mipil khempeuh samsak hi. Faro in amaute’ kiangah a mang gen a, ahih hangin Faro’ tungah a khiatna a gen thei kuamah om lo hi.
English: And it came to pass in the morning that his spirit was troubled; and he sent and called for all the magicians of Egypt, and all the wise men thereof: and Pharaoh told them his dream; but there was none that could interpret them unto Pharaoh.

**41:9**
Zolai: Tua ciangin an piapi pa in Faro’ kiangah, “Tuni-in ka khialhnate ka phawkkik hi.
English: Then spake the chief butler unto Pharaoh, saying, I do remember my faults this day:

**41:10**
Zolai: Faro, ama nasemte tungah heh a, kei le an huanpipa, inncing mangpa’ inn sungah hong khum lai-in
English: Pharaoh was wroth with his servants, and put me in ward in the captain of the guard's house, both me and the chief baker:

**41:11**
Zolai: amah le keimah in zan khat sungin mang ka man uh a, a mangte in a khiatna tuam ciat nei hi.
English: and we dreamed a dream in one night, I and he; we dreamed each man according to the interpretation of his dream.

**41:12**
Zolai: Inncing mangpa’ nasem ahi Hebru mi tangval khat tua lai-ah kote tawh om hi. Ama kiangah ka gen uh ciangin, amah in ka mangte uh hong khiatsak a, ka mang uh tawh a kizui tuakin a khiatna hong gen hi.
English: And there was there with us a young man, an Hebrew, servant to the captain of the guard; and we told him, and he interpreted to us our dreams; to each man according to his dream he did interpret.

**41:13**
Zolai: Amah in kote tungah a khiatna hong gen bangin hong tung hi. Kei pen ka za-ah hong kikoih kik a, anhuan pa kikhailum hi,” a ci hi.
English: And it came to pass, as he interpreted to us, so it was; me he restored unto mine office, and him he hanged.

**41:14**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Faro in mi sawlin Josef samsak a, amaute in manlang takin thongmial sung panin amah a paikhiatpih uh hi. Amah in a mul kiatin a puan a khek khit ciangin, Faro’ mai-ah hong pai hi.
English: Then Pharaoh sent and called Joseph, and they brought him hastily out of the dungeon: and he shaved himself , and changed his raiment, and came in unto Pharaoh.

**41:15**
Zolai: Faro in Josef kiangah, “Mang khat ka man a, a khiatna a gen thei kuamah om lo hi. Nang in mang na zak ciangin a khiatna gen thei, ci-in hong kigenna ka za hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Pharaoh said unto Joseph, I have dreamed a dream, and there is none that can interpret it: and I have heard say of thee, that thou canst understand a dream to interpret it.

**41:16**
Zolai: Josef in Faro dawngin, “Kei’ pilna tawh mang a khiathei ka hi kei hi. Pasian in Faro’ tungah a hoihlamin dawnna hong pia ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Joseph answered Pharaoh, saying, It is not in me: God shall give Pharaoh an answer of peace.

**41:17**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Faro in Josef kiangah, “Ka mangin Nail gun gei-ah ka ding hi.
English: And Pharaoh said unto Joseph, In my dream, behold, I stood upon the bank of the river:

**41:18**
Zolai: A thau a zol bawngpi sagih Nail gun panin hong paikhia a, phai lopate ne uh hi.
English: and, behold, there came up out of the river seven kine, fatfleshed and well favoured; and they fed in a meadow:

**41:19**
Zolai: Tuate’ khit ciangin a hehpihhuai a gulhgawng, Egypt gam sung khempeuhah tua bang ka muh ngei loh bawngpi dang sagih hong pai hi.
English: and, behold, seven other kine came up after them, poor and very ill favoured and leanfleshed, such as I never saw in all the land of Egypt for badness:

**41:20**
Zolai: A gawng a gulhgawng bawngpite in a masa a thau bawngpi sagihte netum uh hi.
English: and the lean and the ill favoured kine did eat up the first seven fat kine:

**41:21**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amaute in tuate a nek khit uh ciangin, a nek khitlam uh kuamah in thei lo hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh amaute pen a tunga mah bangin gulhgawng lai veve uh hi. Tua ciangin ka khang lo hi.
English: and when they had eaten them up, it could not be known that they had eaten them; but they were still ill favoured, as at the beginning. So I awoke.

**41:22**
Zolai: Tua ciangin ka mang mahin kung khat tungah a dim a hoih buhvui sagih a vuikhia zong ka mu hi.
English: And I saw in my dream, and, behold, seven ears came up in one stalk, full and good:

**41:23**
Zolai: Tuate’ khit ciangin nisuahna huihpi in a keusak a hawm, a theem vui sagih hong po a,
English: and, behold, seven ears, withered, thin, and blasted with the east wind, sprung up after them:

**41:24**
Zolai: a vui hawmte in a vui hoih sagihte valhtum uh hi. Mitphial siamte kiangah ka gen a, ahih hangin kei kiangah hong gentel thei khat beek om lo hi,” a ci hi.
English: and the thin ears devoured the seven good ears: and I told this unto the magicians; but there was none that could declare it to me.

**41:25**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Josef in Faro’ kiangah, “Faro’ mang tegel pen khat ahi hi. Pasian in ama bawl ding, Faro’ tungah hong kilangsak khin hi.
English: And Joseph said unto Pharaoh, The dream of Pharaoh is one: God hath shewed Pharaoh what he is about to do.

**41:26**
Zolai: A hoih bawngpi sagihte, kum sagih hi a, a hoih buhvui sagihte zong kum sagih mah ahi hi. A mang khiatna a kibang ahi hi.
English: The seven good kine are seven years; and the seven good ears are seven years: the dream is one.

**41:27**
Zolai: Tuate’ khit ciangin a hong paikhia, a gawng a gulhgawng bawngpi sagihte, kum sagih hi a, nisuahna huihpi in a theemsak buhvui sagihte zong kialpi kum sagih mah ahi hi.
English: And the seven thin and ill favoured kine that came up after them are seven years; and the seven empty ears blasted with the east wind shall be seven years of famine.

**41:28**
Zolai: Faro’ kianga kong gen bangin Pasian in ama hih ding, Faro’ tungah hong lak khin ahi hi.
English: This is the thing which I have spoken unto Pharaoh: What God is about to do he sheweth unto Pharaoh.

**41:29**
Zolai: Egypt gam sung khempeuhah kum sagih sung hauhna hong tung ding a,
English: Behold, there come seven years of great plenty throughout all the land of Egypt:

**41:30**
Zolai: ahih hangin tua khit ciangin kialpi kum sagih sung hong tungin, hauhna ngeisa khempeuh Egypt gam sungah kimangngilh ding hi. Kialpi in gam sung netum ding a,
English: and there shall arise after them seven years of famine; and all the plenty shall be forgotten in the land of Egypt; and the famine shall consume the land;

**41:31**
Zolai: nasia mahmah ding ahih manin, tua hong tung ding kialpi’ huhau-in gam sungah hauhna kithei lo ding hi.
English: and the plenty shall not be known in the land by reason of that famine following; for it shall be very grievous.

**41:32**
Zolai: Faro’ mang nih a phakna pen tua thu Pasian’ sehsa hi, a cihnopna hi a, Pasian in tomno sungin hong tungsak ding hi.
English: And for that the dream was doubled unto Pharaoh twice; it is because the thing is established by God, and God will shortly bring it to pass.

**41:33**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tu-in Faro in thu ngaihsun siam mipil khat tengkhia inla, Egypt gam sung a uk dingin amah koih in.
English: Now therefore let Pharaoh look out a man discreet and wise, and set him over the land of Egypt.

**41:34**
Zolai: Faro in gam sungah vaihawm ulian seh inla, a kihauh kum sagih sungin Egypt gam leitang pana piang sung panin nga-ah khat la in.
English: Let Pharaoh do this , and let him appoint officers over the land, and take up the fifth part of the land of Egypt in the seven plenteous years.

**41:35**
Zolai: Hong tung ding kum hoih sunga an khempeuh amaute khawmsak inla, khuapite sungah an nek dingin Faro’ ukna nuai-ah antangte kholin, amaute kemsak in.
English: And let them gather all the food of those good years that come, and lay up corn under the hand of Pharaoh, and let them keep food in the cities.

**41:36**
Zolai: Kialpi hangin gam sung a siatloh nadingin Egypt gam sungah a hong tung ding kum sagih kialpi dal nadingin a kikoihcing an hi ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And that food shall be for store to the land against the seven years of famine, which shall be in the land of Egypt; that the land perish not through the famine.

**41:37**
Zolai: Hih a thugen pen Faro le a nasemte khempeuh in hoihsa uh hi.
English: And the thing was good in the eyes of Pharaoh, and in the eyes of all his servants.

**41:38**
Zolai: Faro in a nasemte kiangah, “Ama sungah Pasian Kha a omna, hih bang midang mu ding ihi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Pharaoh said unto his servants, Can we find such a one as this is , a man in whom the Spirit of God is ?

**41:39**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Faro in Josef kiangah, “Pasian in hihte khempeuh nang hong lak khin ahih manin, nang bangin thu ngaihsun siam le a pil midang om lo hi.
English: And Pharaoh said unto Joseph, Forasmuch as God hath shewed thee all this, there is none so discreet and wise as thou art:

**41:40**
Zolai: Nang pen ka inn sungah ulian na hi ding a, nangma thupiak bangin ka mite khempeuh gamta ding uh hi. Kumpi tokhom tawh kisai-in kei pen nang sangin ka lian zaw ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: thou shalt be over my house, and according unto thy word shall all my people be ruled: only in the throne will I be greater than thou.

**41:41**
Zolai: Faro in Josef’ kiangah, “Egypt gam khempeuh a uk dingin nang kong koih khinzo hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Pharaoh said unto Joseph, See, I have set thee over all the land of Egypt.

**41:42**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Faro in a min gelhna zungbuh ama khut tung panin suahkhia-in Josef’ khutah bulh a, puan hoih mahmah tawh amah zemin, a ngawngah kham khainiang khat oksak hi.
English: And Pharaoh took off his ring from his hand, and put it upon Joseph's hand, and arrayed him in vestures of fine linen, and put a gold chain about his neck;

**41:43**
Zolai: Ama leeng nihna tungah Josef tuangsak a, ama mai-ah uliante kiko a, “Khukdin’ un!” ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin Egypt gam khempeuh a ukin amah koih hi.
English: and he made him to ride in the second chariot which he had; and they cried before him, Bow the knee: and he made him ruler over all the land of Egypt.

**41:44**
Zolai: Tua tham loin Faro in Josef kiangah, “Kei pen Faro ka hi hi. Nangma thukim lohin Egypt gam sung khempeuhah kuamah in a khut a khe nangawn uh liik lo ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Pharaoh said unto Joseph, I am Pharaoh, and without thee shall no man lift up his hand or foot in all the land of Egypt.

**41:45**
Zolai: Faro in Josef’ min Zafenath-paneah a phuak hi. Amah in On khua siampipa Potifera’ tanu Asenath tawh kitengsak hi. Tua ahih ciangin Egypt gam sungah Josef zin kawikawi hi.
English: And Pharaoh called Joseph's name Zaphnath-paaneah; and he gave him to wife Asenath the daughter of Poti-pherah priest of On. And Joseph went out over all the land of Egypt.

**41:46**
Zolai: Egypt kumpipa Faro’ nasemin a tum hunin Josef kum sawmthum pha hi. Faro’ omna panin Josef paikhia a, Egypt gam sung khempeuhah zin hi.
English: And Joseph was thirty years old when he stood before Pharaoh king of Egypt. And Joseph went out from the presence of Pharaoh, and went throughout all the land of Egypt.

**41:47**
Zolai: A kihauh kum sagih sungin leitang in tampi piangsak a,
English: And in the seven plenteous years the earth brought forth by handfuls.

**41:48**
Zolai: Egypt gamah tampi a om laitakin amah in tua kum sagih sunga ante khempeuh khawm a, khuapite sungah an khol hi. A kiima lote panin khuapi simah amah in an khol hi.
English: And he gathered up all the food of the seven years, which were in the land of Egypt, and laid up the food in the cities: the food of the field, which was round about every city, laid he up in the same.

**41:49**
Zolai: A teh ding a khawl dong zahin Josef in tuipi gei sehnel zahin antang tampi khol hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh kiteh khin zo lo hi.
English: And Joseph gathered corn as the sand of the sea, very much, until he left numbering; for it was without number.

**41:50**
Zolai: Kialpi kum hong tun ma-in Josef in On khua siampipa Potifera’ tanu Asenath tawh tapa nih nei hi.
English: And unto Joseph were born two sons before the years of famine came, which Asenath the daughter of Poti-pherah priest of On bare unto him.

**41:51**
Zolai: Josef in a ta masa Manasseh a phuak hi. Amah in, “Pasian in ka haksatna khempeuh le ka pa’ innkuan khempeuh a mangngilhin hong bawl hi,” ci hi.
English: And Joseph called the name of the firstborn Manasseh: For God, said he , hath made me forget all my toil, and all my father's house.

**41:52**
Zolai: A nihna pen amah in Efraim a phuak hi. “Ka thuakna gam sungah kei a pungin hong bawl hi,” ci hi.
English: And the name of the second called he Ephraim: For God hath caused me to be fruitful in the land of my affliction.

**41:53**
Zolai: Egypt gam sunga a om kum sagih sung hauhna hun bei ta hi.
English: And the seven years of plenteousness, that was in the land of Egypt, were ended.

**41:54**
Zolai: Josef’ gensa bangin kum sagih kialpi hong kipan hi. Gamdang khempeuhah kialpi tung a, ahih hangin Egypt gam sung tengah an om hi.
English: And the seven years of dearth began to come, according as Joseph had said: and the dearth was in all lands; but in all the land of Egypt there was bread.

**41:55**
Zolai: Egypt gam khempeuh a kial ciangin, an ngenin mite Faro’ tungah kiko uh hi. Faro in Egypt mite khempeuh tungah, “Josef’ kiangah pai un. Note’ tunga ama hong cih bangin gamta un,” a ci hi.
English: And when all the land of Egypt was famished, the people cried to Pharaoh for bread: and Pharaoh said unto all the Egyptians, Go unto Joseph; what he saith to you, do.

**41:56**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin gam khempeuhah kialpi a tunkim ciangin Josef in ankholna innte khempeuh hongin, Egypt mite tungah a zuak hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Egypt gamah kialpi nasia mahmah hi.
English: And the famine was over all the face of the earth: And Joseph opened all the storehouses, and sold unto the Egyptians; and the famine waxed sore in the land of Egypt.

**41:57**
Zolai: Tua tham loin, leitung khempeuhah kialpi nasia ahih manin, antang lei dingin Josef’ kiangah leitung mi khempeuh hong pai uh hi.
English: And all countries came into Egypt to Joseph for to buy corn ; because that the famine was so sore in all lands.

## Chapter 42

**42:1**
Zolai: Egypt-ah an a omna thu Jakob in a theih ciangin a tate kiangah, “Bang hangin khatlekhat ki-enen mawk na hi uh hiam?
English: Now when Jacob saw that there was corn in Egypt, Jacob said unto his sons, Why do ye look one upon another?

**42:2**
Zolai: Egypt-ah an om hi, ci-in ka za hi. Eite si loin i nuntak nadingin paisuk unla, ei a’ ding an va lei un,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Behold, I have heard that there is corn in Egypt: get you down thither, and buy for us from thence; that we may live, and not die.

**42:3**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Egypt-ah an lei dingin Josef’ sanggamte sawm paisuk uh hi.
English: And Joseph's ten brethren went down to buy corn in Egypt.

**42:4**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Jakob in Josef’ sanggampa Benjamin, a sanggamte tawh paisak lo hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh ama tungah siatna tung kha ding, ci-in lau hi.
English: But Benjamin, Joseph's brother, Jacob sent not with his brethren; for he said, Lest peradventure mischief befall him.

**42:5**
Zolai: Kanaan gam sungah kial tung ahih manin a hong pai dangte tawh Israel’ tapate an lei dingin hong paikhawm uh hi.
English: And the sons of Israel came to buy corn among those that came: for the famine was in the land of Canaan.

**42:6**
Zolai: Tu-in Josef pen tua gam a ukpa hi a, gammi khempeuh tungah an a zuakpa amah ahi hi. Josef’ sanggamte hong pai-in, a maitang uh leilam ngatin ama mai-ah hong kun uh hi.
English: And Joseph was the governor over the land, and he it was that sold to all the people of the land: and Joseph's brethren came, and bowed down themselves before him with their faces to the earth.

**42:7**
Zolai: Josef in a sanggamte a muh ciangin thei a, ahih hangin amah in midang bangin bawlin amaute tungah khauh pau hi. “Koi pana hong pai na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi. Amaute in, “An lei dingin Kanaan gam panin hong pai hi ung,” ci uh hi.
English: And Joseph saw his brethren, and he knew them, but made himself strange unto them, and spake roughly unto them; and he said unto them, Whence come ye? And they said, From the land of Canaan to buy food.

**42:8**
Zolai: Josef in a sanggamte thei a, ahih hangin a sanggamte in amah thei lo uh hi.
English: And Joseph knew his brethren, but they knew not him.

**42:9**
Zolai: Josef in a mangin amaute a mat khitna a phawk hi. Amah in amaute kiangah, “Note, thukan na hi uh a, hih gam thaneemna a en dingin hong pai na hi uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Joseph remembered the dreams which he dreamed of them, and said unto them, Ye are spies; to see the nakedness of the land ye are come.

**42:10**
Zolai: Amaute in Josef kiangah, “Hi lo hi, topa aw; an lei dingin na nasemte a hong pai hi ung.
English: And they said unto him, Nay, my lord, but to buy food are thy servants come.

**42:11**
Zolai: Kote khempeuh mi khat’ ta ka hi uh hi. Kote, a thutak ka hi uh a, na nasemte thukan hi lo uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: We are all one man's sons; we are true men , thy servants are no spies.

**42:12**
Zolai: Amah in amaute kiangah, “Hi lo hi, hih gam ginat lohna a en dingin hong pai na hi uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said unto them, Nay, but to see the nakedness of the land ye are come.

**42:13**
Zolai: Amaute in, “Ko, nangma nasemte, sanggam pasal sawm le nih ka hi uh a, Kanaan gam sungah mi khat’ ta ka hi uh hi. A moi pen tu laitakin ka pa uh tawh om a, khat pen om nawn lo hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And they said, Thy servants are twelve brethren, the sons of one man in the land of Canaan; and, behold, the youngest is this day with our father, and one is not.

**42:14**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Josef in amaute kiangah, “Note’ tunga kong gen bangin a man mah ahi hi. Note, thukan na hi uh hi.
English: And Joseph said unto them, That is it that I spake unto you, saying, Ye are spies:

**42:15**
Zolai: Hih thu tawh note hong kithei ding hi: Faro a nungta ahih mah bangin na sanggam moi pen uh hih lai-ah hong pai kei leh hih lai mun panin note na paikhia thei nawn kei ding uh hi.
English: hereby ye shall be proved: By the life of Pharaoh ye shall not go forth hence, except your youngest brother come hither.

**42:16**
Zolai: Note’ sungah thuman om hiam, ci-in a kimuh nading, na thugente uh a kitel nadingin note thong sungah na om laitakun note khat kisawl unla, na sanggampa uh hong paipihsak un. Tua ahih kei leh Faro a nungta ahih mah bangin note, thukan na hi taktak uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: Send one of you, and let him fetch your brother, and ye shall be kept in prison, that your words may be proved, whether there be any truth in you: or else by the life of Pharaoh surely ye are spies.

**42:17**
Zolai: Amah in thong sungah ni thum sung amaute a koih hi.
English: And he put them all together into ward three days.

**42:18**
Zolai: A ni thum ni-in Josef in amaute kiangah, “Keimah in Pasian zahtak ka hih manin hih bangin gamta un. Tua hileh na nungta ding uh hi.
English: And Joseph said unto them the third day, This do, and live; for I fear God:

**42:19**
Zolai: Note, thuman mi na hih uhleh thong sungah na sanggamte uh khat omsak lai unla, a dangte pai-in na innkuan uh a gilkialte a dingin an pua unla,
English: if ye be true men , let one of your brethren be bound in the house of your prison: go ye, carry corn for the famine of your houses:

**42:20**
Zolai: na sanggam moi pen uh kei kiangah hong paipih un. Tua ciangin na kam gente uh kitel ding a, note na si kei ding uh hi,” a ci hi. Amaute tua bangmahin gamta uh hi.
English: but bring your youngest brother unto me; so shall your words be verified, and ye shall not die. And they did so.

**42:21**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute khatlekhat in, “A taktakin i sanggampa tawh kisai-in eite i mawh hi. Amah in eite kiangah hong thum napi-in eite in a thu i ngaih loh ciangin amah a lungkhamna i mu hi. Tua thu hangin hih bang lungkhamna eite tungah hong tung hi,” kici uh hi.
English: And they said one to another, We are verily guilty concerning our brother, in that we saw the anguish of his soul, when he besought us, and we would not hear; therefore is this distress come upon us.

**42:22**
Zolai: Reuben in amaute dawng a, “Tangvalpa tungah khial kei un, ci-in note tungah hong gen hi lo ka hi hiam? Ahih hangin ka thu nong mang kei uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin tu-in ama sihna thaman eite’ tungah hong tung ahi hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Reuben answered them, saying, Spake I not unto you, saying, Do not sin against the child; and ye would not hear? therefore, behold, also his blood is required.

**42:23**
Zolai: Amaute’ kikalah kamphen khat om ahih manin Josef in amau’ paute a tellam amaute in thei lo uh hi.
English: And they knew not that Joseph understood them ; for he spake unto them by an interpreter.

**42:24**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute’ kiang panin Josef kihei-in a kap sim hi. Tua ciangin amaute kiangah hong paikikin amaute hopih hi. Amah in amau’ kiang panin Simeon la-in amau’ muhna-ah amah a hen hi.
English: And he turned himself about from them, and wept; and returned to them again, and communed with them, and took from them Simeon, and bound him before their eyes.

**42:25**
Zolai: Amau’ ipte antang tawh dipsakin, a van sung uhah amau’ sum ciat koih kikin, lampi-a a nek ding uh an a piak nading Josef in thu a pia hi. Tua bangmahin amau a dingin kihihsak hi.
English: Then Joseph commanded to fill their sacks with corn, and to restore every man's money into his sack, and to give them provision for the way: and thus did he unto them.

**42:26**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in a late uh antang suanin a paikhia uh hi.
English: And they laded their asses with the corn, and departed thence.

**42:27**
Zolai: Amaute khat in a giahna panun a la gan-an pia dingin a van a suah le, a van gongah a sum mu hi.
English: And as one of them opened his sack to give his ass provender in the inn, he espied his money; for, behold, it was in his sack's mouth.

**42:28**
Zolai: Amah in a sanggamte kiangah, “Ka sum kikoih kik hi. Hih lai-ah ka van gongah na om!” a ci hi. Hih thu hangin amaute lungsi uh a, lingin amaute khatlekhat ki-en uh a, “Pasian in eite hih bangin hong bawl a bangci thu ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.
English: And he said unto his brethren, My money is restored; and, lo, it is even in my sack: and their heart failed them , and they were afraid, saying one to another, What is this that God hath done unto us?

**42:29**
Zolai: Kanaan gamah a pa uh Jakob kiang a tun uh ciangin, amaute’ tunga thupiang khempeuh gen uh a,
English: And they came unto Jacob their father unto the land of Canaan, and told him all that befell unto them; saying,

**42:30**
Zolai: “Mipa, tua gam topa kote’ tungah hong khauh pau-in, tua gam thukanin kote hong ngaihsun hi.
English: The man, who is the lord of the land, spake roughly to us, and took us for spies of the country.

**42:31**
Zolai: Ahih hangin kote in ama kiangah, ‘Kote thuman mi ka hi uh a, kote thukan ka hi kei uh hi.
English: And we said unto him, We are true men ; we are no spies:

**42:32**
Zolai: Kote pen ka pa uh’ tapa, sanggam pasal sawm le nih ka hi uh hi. Khat pen om nawn lo a, tu laitakin a moipen Kanaan gamah ka pa uh tawh om hi,’ ka ci uh hi.
English: we be twelve brethren, sons of our father; one is not, and the youngest is this day with our father in the land of Canaan.

**42:33**
Zolai: Tua ciangin tua gam topa in kote kiangah, ‘Note thuman mi na hihna uh hih tawh ka thei ding hi: Na sanggamte uh khat kei kiangah nusia unla, na innkuan gilkialte a dingin antang la unla, ciahkik un.
English: And the man, the lord of the country, said unto us, Hereby shall I know that ye are true men ; leave one of your brethren here with me, and take food for the famine of your households, and be gone:

**42:34**
Zolai: Na sanggam moi pen uh kei kiangah hong paipih un. Tua hileh note thukan hi loin thuman mi na hihna uh ka thei ding a, note kiangah na sanggampa uh hong khahin, hih gam sungah omin na na sem thei ding uh hi,’ hong ci hi,” ci-in a gen uh hi.
English: and bring your youngest brother unto me: then shall I know that ye are no spies, but that ye are true men: so will I deliver you your brother, and ye shall traffick in the land.

**42:35**
Zolai: Amau’ vante a suah ciangun, a milipun a sumte uh a van sung ciat uhah na om hi. Amaute le a pa un amaute’ sum kihente a muh uh ciangin, lungkham uh hi.
English: And it came to pass as they emptied their sacks, that, behold, every man's bundle of money was in his sack: and when both they and their father saw the bundles of money, they were afraid.

**42:36**
Zolai: A pa uh Jakob in amaute kiangah, “Ka tate tawh kei nong kikhensak zo uh hi: Josef om nawn lo, Simeon om nawn lo, tu-in note in Benjamin na la ding uh hi. Hihte khempeuh kei’ tungah hong tung khin hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob their father said unto them, Me have ye bereaved of my children: Joseph is not, and Simeon is not, and ye will take Benjamin away: all these things are against me.

**42:37**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Reuben in a pa kiangah, “Na kiangah amah kong paipih kik kei leh ka tapa nihte that in. Kei hong ap in, nang kiangah amah kong ciahpih kik ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Reuben spake unto his father, saying, Slay my two sons, if I bring him not to thee: deliver him into my hand, and I will bring him to thee again.

**42:38**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah in, “A sanggampa si a, amah bek om ahih manin ka tapa in note hong zuisuk lo ding hi. Note’ pai nading na khualzinna uhah ama tungah siatna tung kha zenzen le, khangham khit nungin dahlua-in ka si ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, My son shall not go down with you; for his brother is dead, and he is left alone: if mischief befall him by the way in the which ye go, then shall ye bring down my gray hairs with sorrow to the grave.

## Chapter 43

**43:1**
Zolai: Tu-in gam sungah kialpi hong nasia semsem hi.
English: And the famine was sore in the land.

**43:2**
Zolai: Egypt gam panin a puak uh antang amaute in a gaih khit uh ciangin, a pa un amaute kiangah, “Paikik unla, eite a’ ding an tawmkhat va lei un,” a ci hi.
English: And it came to pass, when they had eaten up the corn which they had brought out of Egypt, their father said unto them, Go again, buy us a little food.

**43:3**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Judah in ama kiangah, “Mipa in thupi takin kote hong hilhkhol a, ‘Na sanggampa uh tawh nong ton kei uhleh ka mai na mu kei ding uh hi,’ hong ci hi.
English: And Judah spake unto him, saying, The man did solemnly protest unto us, saying, Ye shall not see my face, except your brother be with you.

**43:4**
Zolai: Ka sanggampa uh hong zuisak lecin kote paisukin nang a’ ding an ka va lei ding uh hi.
English: If thou wilt send our brother with us, we will go down and buy thee food:

**43:5**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah nong zuihsak kei leh kote ka paisuk kei ding uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh mipa in kote kiangah, ‘Na sanggampa uh tawh nong ton kei uhleh ka mai na mu kei ding uh hi,’ hong ci hi,” a ci hi.
English: but if thou wilt not send him , we will not go down: for the man said unto us, Ye shall not see my face, except your brother be with you.

**43:6**
Zolai: Israel in, “Mipa kiangah sanggam dang khat nei ung, ci-in genin bang hangin kei hong hici bawlsiat na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Israel said, Wherefore dealt ye so ill with me, as to tell the man whether ye had yet a brother?

**43:7**
Zolai: Amaute in dawngin, “Mipa in kote’ thu le ka sanggamte uh thu limtakin hong dong a, ‘Na pa uh a nungta lai hiam? Sanggam dang na nei uh hiam?’ hong ci hi. Hong dotnate ka dawnna-un ama kiangah a gen ka hi uh hi. ‘Na sanggampa uh hong tonpih suk un,’ amah in hong cih ding lam kote in bangci theihkholh ding ka hi uh hiam?” a ci uh hi.
English: And they said, The man asked us straitly of our state, and of our kindred, saying, Is your father yet alive? have ye another brother? and we told him according to the tenor of these words: could we certainly know that he would say, Bring your brother down?

**43:8**
Zolai: Judah in a pa Israel kiangah, “Tangvalpa hong zuisak in; nang le kote le i tate si loin i nuntak theih nadingin kote ka va pai ding uh hi.
English: And Judah said unto Israel his father, Send the lad with me, and we will arise and go; that we may live, and not die, both we, and thou, and also our little ones.

**43:9**
Zolai: Kei pen ama a dingin a kikham ka hi ding a, kei’ khutsung panin amah nong kal ding hi. Keimah in nang kiangah amah hong ciahpihkik loin na mai-ah kong koihkik kei leh, tua mawhna kei hong thuaksak tawntung in.
English: I will be surety for him; of my hand shalt thou require him: if I bring him not unto thee, and set him before thee, then let me bear the blame for ever:

**43:10**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh zekai lo hi lehang tu-in nihvei i tungkik khinta ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: for except we had lingered, surely now we had returned this second time.

**43:11**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a pa uh Israel in amaute kiangah, “A tuaci bang ding ahihleh hih bangin gamta un: Gam sunga singgah limci pente pua unla, mipa’ tungah letsongin lingsi tawm, khuaizu tawm, singnai, myrrh paknamtui, pistakhio gah, le almond gahte puak suk un.
English: And their father Israel said unto them, If it must be so now, do this; take of the best fruits in the land in your vessels, and carry down the man a present, a little balm, and a little honey, spices, and myrrh, nuts, and almonds:

**43:12**
Zolai: Na sum uh a zah nih pua un. Na van gong uhah a kikoihkik sumte puakik un, a kikhial hi kha ding hi.
English: and take double money in your hand; and the money that was brought again in the mouth of your sacks, carry it again in your hand; peradventure it was an oversight:

**43:13**
Zolai: Na sanggampa uh zong samin ding unla, mipa kiangah paikik un.
English: take also your brother, and arise, go again unto the man:

**43:14**
Zolai: Amah in na sanggampa uh le Benjamin hong ciahsakkik theihna dingin Vanglian Pasian in mipa’ mai-ah note hehpihna hong pia tahen. Ka tate tawh ka kikhen leh a kikhen ka hi ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: and God Almighty give you mercy before the man, that he may send away your other brother, and Benjamin. If I be bereaved of my children , I am bereaved.

**43:15**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute in letsong la-in, sum a zah nih pua-in, Benjamin zong tonpih uh hi. Amaute dingin Egypt-ah paisuk uh a, Josef’ mai-ah a ding uh hi.
English: And the men took that present, and they took double money in their hand, and Benjamin; and rose up, and went down to Egypt, and stood before Joseph.

**43:16**
Zolai: Josef in amaute tawh Benjamin a muh ciangin, amah in a innsung nasempa’ kiangah, “Mite inn sungah paipih inla, gan khat go-in bawl in. Bang hang hiam cih leh hih mite in sun ciangin kei tawh an ne ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And when Joseph saw Benjamin with them, he said to the ruler of his house, Bring these men home, and slay, and make ready; for these men shall dine with me at noon.

**43:17**
Zolai: Josef’ sawl bangin mipa in sem a, Josef’ inn-ah mite paipih hi.
English: And the man did as Joseph bade; and the man brought the men into Joseph's house.

**43:18**
Zolai: Josef’ inn-ah kipaipih ahih manin lau uh a, amaute in, “Eite sila-in hong bawlin i late a mat theih nading, eite’ tungah thu hong zongin eite hong hih theih nadingin, a masa lai-a i van sunga sum kikoihte’ hangin eite hong kipaipih hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And the men were afraid, because they were brought into Joseph's house; and they said, Because of the money that was returned in our sacks at the first time are we brought in; that he may seek occasion against us, and fall upon us, and take us for bondmen, and our asses.

**43:19**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Josef’ innsung nasempa’ kiangah amaute paito uh a, inn kongkhakah amah tawh kiho-in,
English: And they came near to the steward of Joseph's house, and they communed with him at the door of the house,

**43:20**
Zolai: “Aw, topa aw, an lei dingin khatvei kong pai uh hi.
English: and said, O sir, we came indeed down at the first time to buy food:

**43:21**
Zolai: Ka giahna mun uh ka tun uh ciangin ka vante uh ka hong uh a, ka sumte uh a cingin ka van sung ciat uhah na omkik hi. Tua ahih ciangin kote in tua sumte kong puakik uh a,
English: and it came to pass, when we came to the inn, that we opened our sacks, and, behold, every man's money was in the mouth of his sack, our money in full weight: and we have brought it again in our hand.

**43:22**
Zolai: an lei nadingin sum dang zong kong pua thuah uh hi. Ka van sung uhah kua in sum koih ahi hiam ka thei kei uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And other money have we brought down in our hands to buy food: we cannot tell who put our money in our sacks.

**43:23**
Zolai: Amah in dawng a, “Nuam takin om unla lau kei un. Na Pasian uh, note’ pa’ Pasian in note a dingin na van sung uhah sum koih hi ding hi. Keimah in note’ sum a cingin ka ngah khin hi,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amah in amaute’ kiangah Simeon paikhiatpih hi.
English: And he said, Peace be to you, fear not: your God, and the God of your father, hath given you treasure in your sacks: I had your money. And he brought Simeon out unto them.

**43:24**
Zolai: Mipa in Josef’ inn-ah amaute paipihin, amaute tui pia-in, amaute in a khe uh sil khinin, amah in amaute’ late gan-an a piak khit ciangin,
English: And the man brought the men into Joseph's house, and gave them water, and they washed their feet; and he gave their asses provender.

**43:25**
Zolai: amaute in tua lai-ah Josef tawh an ne ding uh ci-in za uh ahih manin sunin Josef hong pai ciangin a piak ding uh letsong bawlkhol uh hi.
English: And they made ready the present against Joseph came at noon: for they heard that they should eat bread there.

**43:26**
Zolai: Inn-ah Josef hong pai ciangin amau’ puak letsongte innsung ama kiangah paipih uh a, ama mai leilakah kun uh hi.
English: And when Joseph came home, they brought him the present which was in their hand into the house, and bowed themselves to him to the earth.

**43:27**
Zolai: Amah in amau’ omzia dong a, “Na gen uh puteek, na pa uh a dam hiam? Amah a nungta lai hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And he asked them of their welfare, and said, Is your father well, the old man of whom ye spake? Is he yet alive?

**43:28**
Zolai: Amaute in, “Nangma nasem ka pa uh dam hi. Amah nungta lai hi,” a ci uh hi. Amaute in a lu uh kun uh a, zahtakna a bawl uh hi.
English: And they answered, Thy servant our father is in good health, he is yet alive. And they bowed down their heads, and made obeisance.

**43:29**
Zolai: Amah khuadak to a, a nu’ tapa Benjamin mu a, “Hih pa, kei kianga nong gen uh na sanggam moi pen uh ahi hiam? Pasian in nang hong hehpih hen, ka ta!” a ci hi.
English: And he lifted up his eyes, and saw his brother Benjamin, his mother's son, and said, Is this your younger brother, of whom ye spake unto me? And he said, God be gracious unto thee, my son.

**43:30**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a lungsimah a sanggampa ngai lua ahih manin Josef manlangin paikhia a, a kah nading mun a zong hi. Amah a inndei sungah pai-in tua lai-ah va kap sim hi.
English: And Joseph made haste; for his bowels did yearn upon his brother: and he sought where to weep; and he entered into his chamber, and wept there.

**43:31**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in a mai phiatin hong paikhia hi. Amah ki-ip tawmin, “An hong pia un,” a ci hi.
English: And he washed his face, and went out, and refrained himself, and said, Set on bread.

**43:32**
Zolai: Amaute in Josef amah guakin nesakin, amaute a tuam mahin nesak a, amah tawh a ne Egypt mite in a tuam mahin ne uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih le Egypt mite in Hebru mite tawh an nekhawm lo uh hi. Tua banga nekkhawm ding pen Egypt mite a dingin a kihhuai ahi hi.
English: And they set on for him by himself, and for them by themselves, and for the Egyptians, which did eat with him, by themselves: because the Egyptians might not eat bread with the Hebrews; for that is an abomination unto the Egyptians.

**43:33**
Zolai: Ama mai-ah amaute a suakmasa a suah hun tawh kizui leh a moipen a khangnona tawh kizui-in tu uh hi. Lamdangsakna tawh amaute khatlekhat ki-en uh hi.
English: And they sat before him, the firstborn according to his birthright, and the youngest according to his youth: and the men marvelled one at another.

**43:34**
Zolai: Josef’ sabuai tung panin amau’ tanh ciat kipia-in, ahih hangin Benjamin’ tanh pen amaute-a’ zah nga pha hi. Tua ahih ciangin amaute in an ne tui dawnin amah tawh lungdam uh hi.
English: And he took and sent messes unto them from before him: but Benjamin's mess was five times so much as any of their's. And they drank, and were merry with him.

## Chapter 44

**44:1**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in a innsung nasempa thu pia a, “Hih mite’ van sungah amau’ puakzawh zahzah an guang inla, amau’ sum ciat a van gong ciat uhah koih in.
English: And he commanded the steward of his house, saying, Fill the men's sacks with food, as much as they can carry, and put every man's money in his sack's mouth.

**44:2**
Zolai: Ka ngun hai pen an lei nadinga a sum tawh a moipen’ van gongah koihsak in,” a ci hi. Amah in Josef’ gen bangin a hih hi.
English: And put my cup, the silver cup, in the sack's mouth of the youngest, and his corn money. And he did according to the word that Joseph had spoken.

**44:3**
Zolai: Zingsang khuavak phetin a late uh tawh mite kisawlkhia hi.
English: As soon as the morning was light, the men were sent away, they and their asses.

**44:4**
Zolai: Amaute a pai khit, ahih hangin khuapi panin a nai lai-in, Josef in ama innsung nasempa kiangah, “Kithawi inla, mite va delh in. Amaute na phak ciangin amaute kiangah, ‘Bang hangin a hoih pen a sia tawh hong thuk na hi uh hiam? Bang hangin ka topa’ ngun hai gu na hi uh hiam?
English: And when they were gone out of the city, and not yet far off, Joseph said unto his steward, Up, follow after the men; and when thou dost overtake them, say unto them, Wherefore have ye rewarded evil for good?

**44:5**
Zolai: Ka topa in hih hai sung panin dawnin, hih tawh amah in thu thei hi lo ahi hiam? Hih bangin na gamtat manun na khial uh hi,’ va ci in,” a ci hi.
English: Is not this it in which my lord drinketh, and whereby indeed he divineth? ye have done evil in so doing.

**44:6**
Zolai: Amah in amaute a phak ciangin amaute kiangah hih thute a gen hi.
English: And he overtook them, and he spake unto them these same words.

**44:7**
Zolai: Amaute in ama kiangah, “Bang hangin ka topa in thu hih bang hong gen na hi hiam? Na nasemte, tua banga gamta ding hi dek peuhmah lo hi.
English: And they said unto him, Wherefore saith my lord these words? God forbid that thy servants should do according to this thing:

**44:8**
Zolai: En in, ka van gong uha ka muh uh sumte, Kanaan gam panin nang kiangah kong puak kik uh hi. Tua ahih teh na topa’ inn panin ngun hitaleh kham hitaleh bangci guk ding ka hi uh hiam?
English: behold, the money, which we found in our sacks' mouths, we brought again unto thee out of the land of Canaan: how then should we steal out of thy lord's house silver or gold?

**44:9**
Zolai: Na nasemte’ sung pan tua hai a kimuhna penpen kithat hen; kote zong ka topa’ sila ka hi ding uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: With whomsoever of thy servants it be found, both let him die, and we also will be my lord's bondmen.

**44:10**
Zolai: Amah in, “Na cih bang uh hi ta hen: A kimuhna penpen pa ka sila hi ding a, no a dangteng mawh na baang kei ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, Now also let it be according unto your words: he with whom it is found shall be my servant; and ye shall be blameless.

**44:11**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a milipin a van uh leilakah ngasuk uh a, a milipin a van uh suah hi.
English: Then they speedily took down every man his sack to the ground, and opened every man his sack.

**44:12**
Zolai: Amah in zong a, a hampen panin kipanin a moipen tawh tawp a, Benjamin’ van sungah a hai kimu hi.
English: And he searched, and began at the eldest, and left at the youngest: and the cup was found in Benjamin's sack.

**44:13**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amaute in a puan uh balkekin, a late uh a van suan ciatin, khuapi-ah hong kileh kik uh hi.
English: Then they rent their clothes, and laded every man his ass, and returned to the city.

**44:14**
Zolai: Judah le a sanggamte, Josef’ inn-ah a tun ciangin, amah tua lai mahah na omlai hi. Ama mai leilakah amaute kun uh hi.
English: And Judah and his brethren came to Joseph's house; for he was yet there: and they fell before him on the ground.

**44:15**
Zolai: Josef in amaute kiangah, “Note’ gamtatna a bangci gamtat ahi hiam? Kei bang ahi mi in thu ka theihna thei lo na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Joseph said unto them, What deed is this that ye have done? wot ye not that such a man as I can certainly divine?

**44:16**
Zolai: Judah in, “Ka topa tungah hong bangci gen ding ka hi uh hiam? Bang thu gen ding ka hi uh hiam? Tua ahih kei leh ko bangci kiphel theih ding ka hi uh hiam? Pasian in na nasemte’ mawhna mukhia hi. En in, kote le hai a kimuhna pa zong, ka topa’ sila ka hi uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Judah said, What shall we say unto my lord? what shall we speak? or how shall we clear ourselves? God hath found out the iniquity of thy servants: behold, we are my lord's servants, both we, and he also with whom the cup is found.

**44:17**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amah in, “Tua bangin hi dek lo ding hi. Hai a kimuhna mipa bek ka sila hi ding hi. No a dangte ahihleh, na pa’ kiang uhah nuamtakin ciah un,” a ci hi.
English: And he said, God forbid that I should do so: but the man in whose hand the cup is found, he shall be my servant; and as for you, get you up in peace unto your father.

**44:18**
Zolai: Tua ciangin ama kiangah Judah hong paito-in, “Ka topa aw, hong thum ing. Na nasempa, nang tungah kam khat thu hong gensak inla, na nasempa tungah na hehna hong sosak kei in. Bang hang hiam cih leh nang pen Faro mahmah tawh a kibang na hi hi.
English: Then Judah came near unto him, and said, Oh my lord, let thy servant, I pray thee, speak a word in my lord's ears, and let not thine anger burn against thy servant: for thou art even as Pharaoh.

**44:19**
Zolai: Ka topa in a nasemte nong dong a, ‘Pa hitaleh sanggam pasal dang hitaleh na nei uh hiam?’ nong ci hi.
English: My lord asked his servants, saying, Have ye a father, or a brother?

**44:20**
Zolai: Kote in ka topa uh kiangah, ‘Kote in a teek pa khat le a teek zawhin a neih sanggam pasal moilai khat ka nei uh hi. Ama sanggampa si a, a nu’ tate sung pan amah bek omlai hi. A pa in amah it mahmah hi,’ kong ci uh hi.
English: And we said unto my lord, We have a father, an old man, and a child of his old age, a little one; and his brother is dead, and he alone is left of his mother, and his father loveth him.

**44:21**
Zolai: Tua ciangin nangmah in na nasemte kiangah, ‘Ka mit tawh amah ka muh theih nadingin kei kiangah amah hong tonpih suk un,’ nong ci hi.
English: And thou saidst unto thy servants, Bring him down unto me, that I may set mine eyes upon him.

**44:22**
Zolai: Kote in ka topa uh kiangah, ‘Tangvalpa in a pa nusia thei lo ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh a pa nusia leh a pa si ding hi,’ kong ci uh hi.
English: And we said unto my lord, The lad cannot leave his father: for if he should leave his father, his father would die.

**44:23**
Zolai: Tua ciangin nangmah in na nasemte kiangah, ‘Note tawh na sanggam uh a moipen hong paisuk khop kei leh ka mai nong mu nawn kei ding uh hi,’ nong ci hi.
English: And thou saidst unto thy servants, Except your youngest brother come down with you, ye shall see my face no more.

**44:24**
Zolai: “Tua ahih ciangin na nasem ka pa uh kiangah ka ciahkik uh ciangin ka topa’ thugente ama kiangah ka gen uh hi.
English: And it came to pass when we came up unto thy servant my father, we told him the words of my lord.

**44:25**
Zolai: Ka pa un, ‘Paikikin eite a’ ding an tawm va lei un,’ hong cih ciangin
English: And our father said, Go again, and buy us a little food.

**44:26**
Zolai: kote in, ‘Ka paisuk kei ding uh hi. Ka sanggam moipen uh ko tawh hong paikhawm leh ka paisuk bek ding uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh ka sanggam moipen uh ko tawh hong pai kei leh mipa’ mai ka mu kei ding uh hi,’ ka ci uh hi.
English: And we said, We cannot go down: if our youngest brother be with us, then will we go down: for we may not see the man's face, except our youngest brother be with us.

**44:27**
Zolai: Tua ciangin na nasem ka pa un kote kiangah, ‘Ka zi in kei tawh tapa nih a neih na thei uh hi.
English: And thy servant my father said unto us, Ye know that my wife bare me two sons:

**44:28**
Zolai: Khat in kei hong nusia khin a, amah kibalzan khin taktak hi, ka ci hi. Tua hun a kipan amah ka mu nawn kei hi.
English: and the one went out from me, and I said, Surely he is torn in pieces; and I saw him not since:

**44:29**
Zolai: Hih a khat zong kei kiang panin na lak uh a, ama tungah siatna a tun leh, dahna tawh ka sam kangte Leinuai-ah na paipih suk ding uh hi,’ hong ci hi.
English: and if ye take this also from me, and mischief befall him, ye shall bring down my gray hairs with sorrow to the grave.

**44:30**
Zolai: “Tua ahih ciangin tu-in, na nasem ka pa uh kiangah ka ciah uh ciangin, tangvalpa kote tawh hong ciah kei leh, ama lungsim khempeuh tangvalpa’ tungah om ahih manin,
English: Now therefore when I come to thy servant my father, and the lad be not with us; seeing that his life is bound up in the lad's life;

**44:31**
Zolai: kote tawh tangvalpa a ciah lohna a muh ciangin amah si ding hi. Na nasemte in na nasem ka pa uh’ sam kangte dahna tawh Leinuai-ah ka paipih ding uh hi.
English: it shall come to pass, when he seeth that the lad is not with us , that he will die: and thy servants shall bring down the gray hairs of thy servant our father with sorrow to the grave.

**44:32**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh na nasem keimah pen tangvalpa a dingin ka pa’ tungah a kikham ka hi a, ‘Nang kiangah amah kong ciahpih kik kei leh tua mawhsakna nangma muhna-ah ka nuntak tawntungin ka thuak ding hi,’ ka ci hi.
English: For thy servant became surety for the lad unto my father, saying, If I bring him not unto thee, then I shall bear the blame to my father for ever.

**44:33**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin tu-in kong thum hi. Ka topa’ sila dingin tangvalpa’ tangin na nasempa hong omsak inla, a sanggamte tawh tangvalpa ciahkiksak in.
English: Now therefore, I pray thee, let thy servant abide instead of the lad a bondman to my lord; and let the lad go up with his brethren.

**44:34**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh tangvalpa kei tawh hong ton kei leh ka pa kiangah bangci ciahkik thei ding ka hi hiam? Ka pa’ tungah a tung ding siatna ka thuakzo kei ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: For how shall I go up to my father, and the lad be not with me? lest peradventure I see the evil that shall come on my father.

## Chapter 45

**45:1**
Zolai: Tua ciangin ama kianga dingte khempeuh’ mai-ah Josef ki-ipzo nawn lo a, “Ka kiang panin mi khempeuh paikhia un,” ci-in a kiko hi. Tua ahih manin Josef a sanggamte tungah amah a kipulak ciangin kuamah dang om lo hi.
English: Then Joseph could not refrain himself before all them that stood by him; and he cried, Cause every man to go out from me. And there stood no man with him, while Joseph made himself known unto his brethren.

**45:2**
Zolai: Amah a gingin kapkhia ahih manin Egypt mite in za a, Faro’ innkuante in zong za uh hi.
English: And he wept aloud: and the Egyptians and the house of Pharaoh heard.

**45:3**
Zolai: Josef in a sanggamte kiangah, “Kei, Josef ka hi hi. I pa a nungta lai hiam?” a ci hi. Ahih hangin a sanggamte maizum uh ahih manin amah dawng thei lo uh hi.
English: And Joseph said unto his brethren, I am Joseph; doth my father yet live? And his brethren could not answer him; for they were troubled at his presence.

**45:4**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Josef in a sanggamte kiangah, “Ka nai-ah hong pai un, hong thum ing,” a ci hi. Amaute a nai-ah hong pai uh hi. Amah in, “Kei pen Egypt-ah nong zuak uh na sanggampa uh Josef ka hi hi.
English: And Joseph said unto his brethren, Come near to me, I pray you. And they came near. And he said, I am Joseph your brother, whom ye sold into Egypt.

**45:5**
Zolai: Hih lai-ah kei nong zuak manun tu-in lungkham kei un. Nomau tungah kiheh tawm kei un. Bang hang hiam cih leh nuntakna a hu dingin note’ mai-ah Pasian in kei hong sawl hi.
English: Now therefore be not grieved, nor angry with yourselves, that ye sold me hither: for God did send me before you to preserve life.

**45:6**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh gam sungah kum nih sung kialpi tungzo hi. Lo khawh loh, an lak loh ding kum nga omlai hi.
English: For these two years hath the famine been in the land: and yet there are five years, in the which there shall neither be earing nor harvest.

**45:7**
Zolai: Note a dingin leitungah a omlai mi a hingsak ding le note a dingin a suakta mi tampi a kem dingin note’ mai-ah Pasian in kei hong sawl hi.
English: And God sent me before you to preserve you a posterity in the earth, and to save your lives by a great deliverance.

**45:8**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin hih lai-ah a hong sawl mi pen note na hi kei uh a, Pasian ahi hi. Amah in Faro’ khutnuai-ah a ulian penin kei hong bawlin, ama innsung khempeuh’ topa le Egypt gam khempeuh a ukpa-in kei hong bawlkhin hi.
English: So now it was not you that sent me hither, but God: and he hath made me a father to Pharaoh, and lord of all his house, and a ruler throughout all the land of Egypt.

**45:9**
Zolai: “Manlangin i pa kiangah va ciahto unla ama kiangah, ‘Na tapa Josef in hih bangin ci hi: Pasian in Egypt gam khempeuh’ topa-in kei hong bawl khin hi. Ka kiangah hong paisuk hen, zekai kei hen.
English: Haste ye, and go up to my father, and say unto him, Thus saith thy son Joseph, God hath made me lord of all Egypt: come down unto me, tarry not:

**45:10**
Zolai: Goshen leitangah na teng ding a, nang le na tate’ tate le na tuuhonte le na bawnghonte le na neih khempeuh tawh, nang pen kei tawh a kinai-in na om ding hi.
English: and thou shalt dwell in the land of Goshen, and thou shalt be near unto me, thou, and thy children, and thy children's children, and thy flocks, and thy herds, and all that thou hast:

**45:11**
Zolai: Hong tung ding kialpi kum nga omlai ahih manin tua lai-ah nang kong vak ding hi. Tua hi kei le nang le na innkuanpihte le na neih khempeuh in zawnna na ngah ding uh hi, ci hi,’ va ci un.
English: and there will I nourish thee; for yet there are five years of famine; lest thou, and thy household, and all that thou hast, come to poverty.

**45:12**
Zolai: “Note’ kianga thu hong gen pen keima kam ahihna tu-in note’ mitin nong mu uh a, ka sanggampa Benjamin’ mit in zong hong mu hi.
English: And, behold, your eyes see, and the eyes of my brother Benjamin, that it is my mouth that speaketh unto you.

**45:13**
Zolai: Egypt-ah keima liatna khempeuh le note’ muhsa khempeuh, i pa’ kiangah na gen ding uh hi. Manlang unla, hih lai-ah i pa hong paisukpih un,” a ci hi.
English: And ye shall tell my father of all my glory in Egypt, and of all that ye have seen; and ye shall haste and bring down my father hither.

**45:14**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a sanggampa Benjamin ngawng kawi-in a kap hi. Benjamin in zong amah ngawng kawi-in a kap hi.
English: And he fell upon his brother Benjamin's neck, and wept; and Benjamin wept upon his neck.

**45:15**
Zolai: Tua ciangin a kah kawmin a sanggamte khempeuh ngawng kawi-in a nam hi. Tua khit ciangin a sanggamte in amah hopih uh hi.
English: Moreover he kissed all his brethren, and wept upon them: and after that his brethren talked with him.

**45:16**
Zolai: “Josef’ sanggamte hong pai,” cihna thu Faro’ inn sungah a kizak ciangin, tua thu in Faro le a nasemte lungdamsak mahmah hi.
English: And the fame thereof was heard in Pharaoh's house, saying, Joseph's brethren are come: and it pleased Pharaoh well, and his servants.

**45:17**
Zolai: Faro in Josef kiangah, “Na sanggamte kiangah, ‘Hih bangin gamta un: Na ganhingte uh van suan unla, Kanaan gamah ciahkik un.
English: And Pharaoh said unto Joseph, Say unto thy brethren, This do ye; lade your beasts, and go, get you unto the land of Canaan;

**45:18**
Zolai: I pa le na innkuanpihte uh va la unla, kei kiangah hong pai un. Egypt gam a hoihpen mun note kong pia ding a, note in gam hoih sunga piangte na ne ding uh hi,’ ci in.
English: and take your father and your households, and come unto me: and I will give you the good of the land of Egypt, and ye shall eat the fat of the land.

**45:19**
Zolai: Amaute zong thu pia inla, ‘Hih bangin gamta un: Na tate le na zite uh a dingin Egypt panin leeng la unla, i pa hong paipih un.
English: Now thou art commanded, this do ye; take you wagons out of the land of Egypt for your little ones, and for your wives, and bring your father, and come.

**45:20**
Zolai: Egypt gam khempeuh a hoih penna nomau-a’ ahih ciangin na vante uh ngaihsutin nei kei un,’ ci in,” a ci hi.
English: Also regard not your stuff; for the good of all the land of Egypt is your's.

**45:21**
Zolai: Israel’ tapate tua bangmahin gamta uh hi. Josef in Faro’ thupiak mah bangin amaute leeng pia a, lampi-a a nek ding uh an zong a pia hi.
English: And the children of Israel did so: and Joseph gave them wagons, according to the commandment of Pharaoh, and gave them provision for the way.

**45:22**
Zolai: Amah in amaute khempeuh tungah puan hoih silh khat ciat a pia hi. Ahih hangin Benjamin’ tungah ngun shekel zathum le puan hoih silh nga a pia hi.
English: To all of them he gave each man changes of raiment; but to Benjamin he gave three hundred pieces of silver, and five changes of raiment.

**45:23**
Zolai: Amah in a pa kiangah a nuai-ate a khak hi: Egypt na hoihte a pua la sawm; antang, anlum, le lampi-a a pa’ nek ding an a pua lapi sawm a puak hi.
English: And to his father he sent after this manner ; ten asses laden with the good things of Egypt, and ten she asses laden with corn and bread and meat for his father by the way.

**45:24**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in a sanggamte sawlkhia a, amaute a paikhiat ciangin amah in amaute kiangah, “Lampi-ah kitawng kei un,” a ci hi.
English: So he sent his brethren away, and they departed: and he said unto them, See that ye fall not out by the way.

**45:25**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute Egypt panin paito uh a, a pa uh Jakob kiang Kanaan gamah ciah uh hi.
English: And they went up out of Egypt, and came into the land of Canaan unto Jacob their father,

**45:26**
Zolai: Amaute in ama kiangah, “Josef nungta lai a, amah pen Egypt gam khempeuh a ukpa na hi hi,” hong ci uh hi. Amah in amaute’ thugen um lo ahih ciangin a lung si hi.
English: and told him, saying, Joseph is yet alive, and he is governor over all the land of Egypt. And Jacob's heart fainted, for he believed them not.

**45:27**
Zolai: Ahih hangin amaute’ tunga Josef’ gen kammalte ama kiangah a gen ciang leh Josef in amah puak nadinga a khak leengte a muh ciangin, a pa uh Jakob’ lungsim hingkik hi.
English: And they told him all the words of Joseph, which he had said unto them: and when he saw the wagons which Joseph had sent to carry him, the spirit of Jacob their father revived:

**45:28**
Zolai: Israel in, “Phazo hi. Ka tapa Josef nungta lai hi. Ka sih ma-in pai-in amah ka mu ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: and Israel said, It is enough; Joseph my son is yet alive: I will go and see him before I die.

## Chapter 46

**46:1**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Israel, a neih khempeuh tawh a khualzin kipanin Beersheba tung a, a pa Isaac’ Pasian tungah biakpiakna a bawl hi.
English: And Israel took his journey with all that he had, and came to Beer-sheba, and offered sacrifices unto the God of his father Isaac.

**46:2**
Zolai: Pasian in Israel tungah zanin thu gen a, “Jakob, Jakob,” ci hi. Amah in, “Hiah om ing,” ci hi.
English: And God spake unto Israel in the visions of the night, and said, Jacob, Jacob. And he said, Here am I.

**46:3**
Zolai: Tua ciangin amah in, “Kei pen na pa’ Pasian ahi, Pasian ka hi hi. Egypt-ah paisuk ding lau kei in. Bang hang hiam cih leh minam lian khatin tua lai-ah nang kong bawl ding hi.
English: And he said, I am God, the God of thy father: fear not to go down into Egypt; for I will there make of thee a great nation:

**46:4**
Zolai: Egypt-ah nang tawh kong paisuk ding a, tua ciangin zong keimah in nang kong paipihto kik ding hi. Josef’ khut sungah na si ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: I will go down with thee into Egypt; and I will also surely bring thee up again: and Joseph shall put his hand upon thine eyes.

**46:5**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Beersheba panin Jakob ding khia hi. Israel’ tapate in a pa uh Jakob, a tate uh, le a zite uh, amah puak nadinga Faro in a khak leeng sungah a pua uh hi.
English: And Jacob rose up from Beer-sheba: and the sons of Israel carried Jacob their father, and their little ones, and their wives, in the wagons which Pharaoh had sent to carry him.

**46:6**
Zolai: Amaute in zong Kanaan gam sunga a lam uh a ganhingte uh le a nate uh la-in, Jakob le ama suanlekhakte ahi,
English: And they took their cattle, and their goods, which they had gotten in the land of Canaan, and came into Egypt, Jacob, and all his seed with him:

**46:7**
Zolai: a tapate, ama tapate’ tapate, a tanute, a tapate’ tanute tawh Egypt-ah a pai uh hi. Amah in a suanlekhakte khempeuh Egypt-ah a paipih hi.
English: his sons, and his sons' sons with him, his daughters, and his sons' daughters, and all his seed brought he with him into Egypt.

**46:8**
Zolai: Tu-in hihte pen Israel’ suanlekhak, Egypt-ah a pai Jakob le a tate’ min ahi hi. Jakob’ ta u pen Reuben
English: And these are the names of the children of Israel, which came into Egypt, Jacob and his sons: Reuben, Jacob's firstborn.

**46:9**
Zolai: le Reuben’ tapate: Hanok, Pallu, Hezron, le Karmi ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Reuben; Hanoch, and Phallu, and Hezron, and Carmi.

**46:10**
Zolai: Simeon’ tapate: Jemuel, Jamin, Ohad, Jakhin, Zohar, le Kanaan numei’ tapa Shaul ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Simeon; Jemuel, and Jamin, and Ohad, and Jachin, and Zohar, and Shaul the son of a Canaanitish woman.

**46:11**
Zolai: Levi’ tapate: Gershon, Kohath, le Merari ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Levi; Gershon, Kohath, and Merari.

**46:12**
Zolai: Judah’ tapate: Er, Onan, Shelah, Perez, le Zerah ahi hi. (Ahih hangin Er le Onan Kanaan gamah si hi.) Perez’ tapate: Hezron le Hamul ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Judah; Er, and Onan, and Shelah, and Pharez, and Zarah: but Er and Onan died in the land of Canaan. And the sons of Pharez were Hezron and Hamul.

**46:13**
Zolai: Issakhar’ tapate: Tola, Puvah, Job, le Shimron ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Issachar; Tola, and Phuvah, and Job, and Shimron.

**46:14**
Zolai: Zebulun’ tapate: Sered, Elon, le Jahleel ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Zebulun; Sered, and Elon, and Jahleel.

**46:15**
Zolai: (Hihte pen Paddanaram-ah Leah tawh a neih Jakob’ suante hi a, a tanu Dinah tawh zong ahi hi. Numei le pasal a vekpi-in sawmthum le thum ahi hi.)
English: These be the sons of Leah, which she bare unto Jacob in Padan-aram, with his daughter Dinah: all the souls of his sons and his daughters were thirty and three.

**46:16**
Zolai: Gad’ tapate: Zifion, Haggi, Shuni, Ezbon, Eri, Arodi, le Areli ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Gad; Ziphion, and Haggi, Shuni, and Ezbon, Eri, and Arodi, and Areli.

**46:17**
Zolai: Asher’ tapate: Imnah, Ishvah, Ishvi, Beriah, le a sanggamnu uh Serah ahi hi. Beriah’ tapate: Heber le Malkhiel ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Asher; Jimnah, and Ishuah, and Isui, and Beriah, and Serah their sister: and the sons of Beriah; Heber, and Malchiel.

**46:18**
Zolai: (Hihte pen Laban in a tanu Leah tungah a piak Zilpah’ tapate ahi hi. Amah in Jakob tawh hihte nei a, mi sawm le guk ahi hi.)
English: These are the sons of Zilpah, whom Laban gave to Leah his daughter, and these she bare unto Jacob, even sixteen souls.

**46:19**
Zolai: Jakob’ zi Rachel’ tapate: Josef le Benjamin ahi hi.
English: The sons of Rachel Jacob's wife; Joseph, and Benjamin.

**46:20**
Zolai: Josef in Egypt gamah On khua siampipa Potifera’ tanu Asenath tawh Manasseh le Efraim nei hi.
