English: And unto Joseph in the land of Egypt were born Manasseh and Ephraim, which Asenath the daughter of Poti-pherah priest of On bare unto him.

**46:21**
Zolai: Benjamin’ tapate: Bela, Bekher, Ashbel, Gera, Naaman, Ehi, Rosh, Muppim, Huppim, le Ard ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Benjamin were Belah, and Becher, and Ashbel, Gera, and Naaman, Ehi, and Rosh, Muppim, and Huppim, and Ard.

**46:22**
Zolai: (Hihte pen Rachel tawh a neih Jakob’ suante hi a, a vekpi-in mi sawm le li ahi hi.)
English: These are the sons of Rachel, which were born to Jacob: all the souls were fourteen.

**46:23**
Zolai: Dan’ tapa Hushim ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Dan; Hushim.

**46:24**
Zolai: Naftali’ tapate: Jahzeel, Guni, Jezer, le Shillem ahi hi.
English: And the sons of Naphtali; Jahzeel, and Guni, and Jezer, and Shillem.

**46:25**
Zolai: (Hihte pen Laban in a tanu Rachel’ tungah a piak Bilhah in Jakob tawh a neih tapate hi a, a vekpi-in mi sagih ahi hi.)
English: These are the sons of Bilhah, which Laban gave unto Rachel his daughter, and she bare these unto Jacob: all the souls were seven.

**46:26**
Zolai: Egypt gamah a pai Jakob-a’ ahi ama suanlekhak, Jakob’ tate’ zite a kisim loin, a vekpi-in mi sawmguk le guk ahi hi.
English: All the souls that came with Jacob into Egypt, which came out of his loins, besides Jacob's sons' wives, all the souls were threescore and six;

**46:27**
Zolai: Josef in Egypt gamah a neih a tapate nih ahi hi. Egypt gamah a pai Jakob’ innkuan khempeuh sawmsagih ahi hi.
English: and the sons of Joseph, which were born him in Egypt, were two souls: all the souls of the house of Jacob, which came into Egypt, were threescore and ten.

**46:28**
Zolai: Jakob in ama mai Goshen-ah amah lam a lak dingin Josef kiangah Judah ma sawl hi. Amaute Goshen gamah hong pai uh hi.
English: And he sent Judah before him unto Joseph, to direct his face unto Goshen; and they came into the land of Goshen.

**46:29**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Josef in a leengte kithawisakin Goshen-ah a pa Israel a dawn dingin a paito hi. A pa a muh phetin ngawng kawi-in tawlkhat sung a kap hi.
English: And Joseph made ready his chariot, and went up to meet Israel his father, to Goshen, and presented himself unto him; and he fell on his neck, and wept on his neck a good while.

**46:30**
Zolai: Israel in Josef kiangah, “Na maitang mu khinin nang na nuntak lai thei ka hih manin tu-in ka si zongin phamawh nawn lo hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Israel said unto Joseph, Now let me die, since I have seen thy face, because thou art yet alive.

**46:31**
Zolai: Josef in a sanggamte le a pa’ innkuanpihte kiangah, “Kei paito-in Faro’ kiangah ka va gen ding a, ama tungah, ‘Kanaan gam a om ka sanggamte le ka pa’ innkuanpihte kei kiangah hong pai hi.
English: And Joseph said unto his brethren, and unto his father's house, I will go up, and shew Pharaoh, and say unto him, My brethren, and my father's house, which were in the land of Canaan, are come unto me;

**46:32**
Zolai: Amaute pen tuucing ahih manin gan kemte ahi uh hi. Amaute in a tuuhonte uh le a bawnghonte uh le a neih khempeuh uh hong paipih uh hi,’ ka va ci ding hi.
English: and the men are shepherds, for their trade hath been to feed cattle; and they have brought their flocks, and their herds, and all that they have.

**46:33**
Zolai: Faro in note hong samin note kiangah, ‘Na nasep uh bang ahi hiam?’ hong cih ciangin,
English: And it shall come to pass, when Pharaoh shall call you, and shall say, What is your occupation?

**46:34**
Zolai: Goshen leitangah na ten theih nadingun note in, ‘Kote hitaleh ka pate uh hitaleh ko na nasemte pen ka neu lai uh a kipan tuhun dongin gankemte ka hi uh hi,’ na ci ding uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Egypt mite a dingin tuucing peuhmah a kihhuai ahi hi,” a ci hi.
English: That ye shall say, Thy servants' trade hath been about cattle from our youth even until now, both we, and also our fathers: that ye may dwell in the land of Goshen; for every shepherd is an abomination unto the Egyptians.

## Chapter 47

**47:1**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Josef pai-in Faro’ kiangah, “Ka pa le ka sanggamte a tuuhon uh le a bawnghon uh le a neih khempeuh uh tawh Kanaan gam panin hong pai uh a, amaute tu-in Goshen gamah om uh hi,” ci-in a gen hi.
English: Then Joseph came and told Pharaoh, and said, My father and my brethren, and their flocks, and their herds, and all that they have, are come out of the land of Canaan; and, behold, they are in the land of Goshen.

**47:2**
Zolai: A sanggamte’ lak panin amah in mi nga la-in Faro’ kiangah va paipih hi.
English: And he took some of his brethren, even five men, and presented them unto Pharaoh.

**47:3**
Zolai: Faro in a sanggamte kiangah, “Na nasep uh bang ahi hiam?” a ci hi. Amaute in Faro’ kiangah, “Ka pate uh mah bangin na nasem kote pen gankemte ka hi uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And Pharaoh said unto his brethren, What is your occupation? And they said unto Pharaoh, Thy servants are shepherds, both we, and also our fathers.

**47:4**
Zolai: Amaute in Faro kiangah, “Hih gamah tawlkhat a om dingin kong pai uh hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh Kanaan gamah kialpi nasia lua ahih manin tua lai-ah na nasemte’ tuuhonte a’ ding lonona om nawn lo hi. Tu-in kong thum uh hi. Goshen gamah na nasemte hong tengsak in,” a ci uh hi.
English: They said moreover unto Pharaoh, For to sojourn in the land are we come; for thy servants have no pasture for their flocks; for the famine is sore in the land of Canaan: now therefore, we pray thee, let thy servants dwell in the land of Goshen.

**47:5**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Faro in Josef kiangah, “Na pa le na sanggamte na kiangah hong tung khin hi.
English: And Pharaoh spake unto Joseph, saying, Thy father and thy brethren are come unto thee:

**47:6**
Zolai: Egypt leitang khempeuh nangma thu ahi hi. Na pa le na sanggamte lei hoihna penah tengsak in. Goshen leitangah amaute tengsak in. Amaute’ lakah a hih thei mi na muh leh ka ganhingte a kem dingin koih in,” a ci hi.
English: the land of Egypt is before thee; in the best of the land make thy father and brethren to dwell; in the land of Goshen let them dwell: and if thou knowest any men of activity among them, then make them rulers over my cattle.

**47:7**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Josef in a pa Jakob tumpihin Faro’ mai-ah koih a, Jakob in Faro thupha a pia hi.
English: And Joseph brought in Jacob his father, and set him before Pharaoh: and Jacob blessed Pharaoh.

**47:8**
Zolai: Faro in Jakob kiangah, “Na nuntak kum bangzah pha ta ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Pharaoh said unto Jacob, How old art thou?

**47:9**
Zolai: Jakob in Faro kiangah, “Tawlkhat sung ka nuntak hun pen kum za le kum sawmthum ahi hi. Ka nuntak hun tom sungah siatna bekbek om a, ka pate tawlkhat a omsung uh a nuntak hunte ban nai lo hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Jacob said unto Pharaoh, The days of the years of my pilgrimage are an hundred and thirty years: few and evil have the days of the years of my life been, and have not attained unto the days of the years of the life of my fathers in the days of their pilgrimage.

**47:10**
Zolai: Jakob in Faro thupha pia-in tua lai panin a paikhia hi.
English: And Jacob blessed Pharaoh, and went out from before Pharaoh.

**47:11**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Faro’ thupiaksa bangin Josef in leitang a hoihpen, Rameses leitang, Egypt gam sungah neihsa pia-in a pa le a sanggamte a tengsak hi.
English: And Joseph placed his father and his brethren, and gave them a possession in the land of Egypt, in the best of the land, in the land of Rameses, as Pharaoh had commanded.

**47:12**
Zolai: Josef in a pa, a sanggamte, le a pa’ innkuante khempeuh a ne ding zah tawh kizui-in an a pia hi.
English: And Joseph nourished his father, and his brethren, and all his father's household, with bread, according to their families.

**47:13**
Zolai: Tu-in kialpi nasia mahmah ahih manin gam khempeuhah an om nawn lo a, kialpi hangin Egypt mite le Kanaan mite vulgawp uh hi.
English: And there was no bread in all the land; for the famine was very sore, so that the land of Egypt and all the land of Canaan fainted by reason of the famine.

**47:14**
Zolai: Amaute in antang a leina hangin, Egypt gam sung le Kanaan gam sunga sum khempeuh Josef in ngah khin hi. Josef in Faro’ inn-ah tua sumte paipih hi.
English: And Joseph gathered up all the money that was found in the land of Egypt, and in the land of Canaan, for the corn which they bought: and Joseph brought the money into Pharaoh's house.

**47:15**
Zolai: Egypt gam sung le Kanaan gam sunga sum a bei khit ciangin Egypt mite khempeuh Josef kiangah hong pai-in, “Kote an hong pia in. Bang hangin na muhna-ah si ding ka hi uh hiam? Bang hang hiam cih leh ka sum uh beita hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And when money failed in the land of Egypt, and in the land of Canaan, all the Egyptians came unto Joseph, and said, Give us bread: for why should we die in thy presence? for the money faileth.

**47:16**
Zolai: Josef in dawngin, “Na ganhingte uh hong pia un. Na sum uh bei ahihleh na ganhingte uh khekna-in an kong pia ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Joseph said, Give your cattle; and I will give you for your cattle, if money fail.

**47:17**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute in Josef kiangah a ganhingte uh paipih uh hi. Josef in sakolte, tuuhonte, bawnghonte, le late a khekna-in amaute an a pia hi. A ganhingte uh khekna-in Josef in tua kum sung amaute an a pia hi.
English: And they brought their cattle unto Joseph: and Joseph gave them bread in exchange for horses, and for the flocks, and for the cattle of the herds, and for the asses: and he fed them with bread for all their cattle for that year.

**47:18**
Zolai: Tua kum a bei, a kum kik ciangin amaute Josef kiangah hong pai-in, “Ka sum uh a bei khitna ka topa uh tungah kong im kei ding uh hi. Ganhing honte ka topa a’ ahi hi. Ka pumpi uh le ka leitang uh cih simloh ka topa’ muhna-ah bangmah dang om nawn lo hi.
English: When that year was ended, they came unto him the second year, and said unto him, We will not hide it from my lord, how that our money is spent; my lord also hath our herds of cattle; there is not ought left in the sight of my lord, but our bodies, and our lands:

**47:19**
Zolai: Bang hangin kote si-in ka leitang uh nangma muhna-ah maimawk ding ahi hiam? Kote le ka leitang uh an tawh hong lei in. Kote, Faro’ sila ka hi ding uh a, ka leitang uh zong ama a’ hi ding hi. Leitang mawkval loin, kote si loin ka hin theih nadingun khaici hong pia in,” a ci uh hi.
English: wherefore shall we die before thine eyes, both we and our land? buy us and our land for bread, and we and our land will be servants unto Pharaoh: and give us seed, that we may live, and not die, that the land be not desolate.

**47:20**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Josef in Egypt gam khempeuh Faro a dingin a lei hi. Kialpi nasia lua ahih manin Egypt mi khempeuh in a lote uh a zuak uh hi. Leitang khempeuh Faro-a’ suak khin hi.
English: And Joseph bought all the land of Egypt for Pharaoh; for the Egyptians sold every man his field, because the famine prevailed over them: so the land became Pharaoh's.

**47:21**
Zolai: Mihingte ahihleh, Egypt mongkhat panin a mongkhat dongin amah in sila-in bawl hi.
English: And as for the people, he removed them to cities from one end of the borders of Egypt even to the other end thereof.

**47:22**
Zolai: Siampite’ leitang bek amah in lei lo hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh siampite in Faro’ tung panin a kiciangtan zah an ngah uh a, amaute tungah Faro in a piak tawh amaute nungtazo uh ahih ciangin amaute in a leitang uh zuak lo uh hi.
English: Only the land of the priests bought he not; for the priests had a portion assigned them of Pharaoh, and did eat their portion which Pharaoh gave them: wherefore they sold not their lands.

**47:23**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Josef in mite kiangah, “En un, tuni-in note le na leitang uh Faro a dingin kong lei hi. Tu-in hih lai-ah no a dingin khaici om a, note in leitang tungah na vawh ding uh hi.
English: Then Joseph said unto the people, Behold, I have bought you this day and your land for Pharaoh: lo, here is seed for you, and ye shall sow the land.

**47:24**
Zolai: Anlak ciangin Faro’ tungah nga-ah khat na pia ding uh a, nga-ah li pen lo-ah khaici ding, note le na innkuanpihte uh le na tate uh’ an dingin na tang ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And it shall come to pass in the increase, that ye shall give the fifth part unto Pharaoh, and four parts shall be your own, for seed of the field, and for your food, and for them of your households, and for food for your little ones.

**47:25**
Zolai: Amaute in, “Nang in ka nuntakna uh nong honkhia khinzo hi. Ka topa uh lungdam hen; kote pen Faro’ sila ka hi ding uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And they said, Thou hast saved our lives: let us find grace in the sight of my lord, and we will be Pharaoh's servants.

**47:26**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Faro in nga-ah khat nei ding hi cihna, tuni donga a om, Egypt leitang tawh kisai-in Josef in ngeina kip khatin a bawl hi. Siampite’ leitang bek Faro-a’ suak lo hi.
English: And Joseph made it a law over the land of Egypt unto this day, that Pharaoh should have the fifth part ; except the land of the priests only, which became not Pharaoh's.

**47:27**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Egypt gam sung Goshen leitangah Israel-te teng uh hi. Tua lai-ah amaute in neihsa ngah uh a, pungin tampi tak pha uh hi.
English: And Israel dwelt in the land of Egypt, in the country of Goshen; and they had possessions therein, and grew, and multiplied exceedingly.

**47:28**
Zolai: Egypt gamah Jakob kum sawm le sagih nungta lai ahih manin ama khan kum za le kum sawmli le sagih ahi hi.
English: And Jacob lived in the land of Egypt seventeen years: so the whole age of Jacob was an hundred forty and seven years.

**47:29**
Zolai: Israel a sih ding hun a nai ciangin, amah in a tapa Josef samin ama kiangah, “Tu-in na muhna-ah maipha ka ngah leh, ka phei nuai-ah na khut hong koih inla, thumantak le citakin kei nong bawl ding thu hong ciam in. Egypt-ah kei hong vui kei inla,
English: And the time drew nigh that Israel must die: and he called his son Joseph, and said unto him, If now I have found grace in thy sight, put, I pray thee, thy hand under my thigh, and deal kindly and truly with me; bury me not, I pray thee, in Egypt:

**47:30**
Zolai: ka pate tawh hong sial khawm in. Egypt panin kei hong puakhia in la, amau’ kivuina munah kei hong vui in,” a ci hi. Amah in dawngin, “Na gen bangin ka gamta ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: but I will lie with my fathers, and thou shalt carry me out of Egypt, and bury me in their buryingplace. And he said, I will do as thou hast said.

**47:31**
Zolai: Amah in, “Kei’ tungah hong kiciam in,” a ci hi. Amah zong a pa’ tungah a kiciam hi. Tua ciangin Israel lungdamin a lupna lukhungah amahmah a kunsuk hi.
English: And he said, Swear unto me. And he sware unto him. And Israel bowed himself upon the bed's head.

## Chapter 48

**48:1**
Zolai: Tua zawh a sawt loin, “Na pa a ci na hi,” ci-in Josef kiangah kigen ahih ciangin amah in a tapa nihte Manasseh le Efraim a paipih hi.
English: And it came to pass after these things, that one told Joseph, Behold, thy father is sick: and he took with him his two sons, Manasseh and Ephraim.

**48:2**
Zolai: Jakob kiangah, “Na tapa Josef na kiangah hong pai hi,” ci-in kigen hi. Tua ciangin Israel in a tha sanin a lupna tungah a tu hi.
English: And one told Jacob, and said, Behold, thy son Joseph cometh unto thee: and Israel strengthened himself, and sat upon the bed.

**48:3**
Zolai: Jakob in Josef kiangah, “Kanaan gam Luz-ah Vanglian Pasian kei tungah hong kilangin kei thupha hong pia a,
English: And Jacob said unto Joseph, God Almighty appeared unto me at Luz in the land of Canaan, and blessed me,

**48:4**
Zolai: kei kiangah, ‘En in, nang hong pungsakin, mihing hon khatin hong bawlin, nang’ khit cianga na suanlekhakte’ tungah a neih tawntung dingun hih leitang ka pia ding hi,’ hong ci hi.
English: and said unto me, Behold, I will make thee fruitful, and multiply thee, and I will make of thee a multitude of people; and will give this land to thy seed after thee for an everlasting possession.

**48:5**
Zolai: “Tu-in, Egypt-ah nang kiangah kong pai ma-in Egypt gam sungah nang’ sung panin a suak na tapa nihte keima-a’ ahi hi. Reuben le Simeon-te mah bangin Efraim le Manasseh zong keima a’ hi ding hi.
English: And now thy two sons, Ephraim and Manasseh, which were born unto thee in the land of Egypt before I came unto thee into Egypt, are mine; as Reuben and Simeon, they shall be mine.

**48:6**
Zolai: Amaute’ khit cianga nang sung panin a suak tate pen nangma a’ hi ding hi. Amau’ gamh luahna-ah amau’ sanggamte’ min tawh amaute ki lo khawm ding hi.
English: And thy issue, which thou begettest after them, shall be thine, and shall be called after the name of their brethren in their inheritance.

**48:7**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh Paddan panin ka pai lai-in, Efrath tun ma diak, Kanaan gam lamkalah ka dah nadingin ka zi Rachel hong si hi. Efrath (Bethlehem) paina lampi-ah amah ka vui hi,” a ci hi.
English: And as for me, when I came from Padan, Rachel died by me in the land of Canaan in the way, when yet there was but a little way to come unto Ephrath: and I buried her there in the way of Ephrath; the same is Beth-lehem.

**48:8**
Zolai: Israel in Josef’ tapate a muh ciangin amah in, “Hihte kua ahi hiam?” a ci hi.
English: And Israel beheld Joseph's sons, and said, Who are these?

**48:9**
Zolai: Josef in a pa’ kiangah, “Pasian in hih lai-ah kei hong piak ka tapate ahi hi,” a ci hi. Amah in, “Kong thum hi; amaute thupha ka piak theih nadingin ka kiangah hong paipih in,” a ci hi.
English: And Joseph said unto his father, They are my sons, whom God hath given me in this place . And he said, Bring them, I pray thee, unto me, and I will bless them.

**48:10**
Zolai: Tu-in Israel’ mitte a khanghamna hangin maang a, amah in khua mu thei lo hi. Tua ahih ciangin Josef in ama kiangah amaute paipih hi. Amah in amaute namin a kawi hi.
English: Now the eyes of Israel were dim for age, so that he could not see. And he brought them near unto him; and he kissed them, and embraced them.

**48:11**
Zolai: Israel in Josef kiangah, “Na maitang a hong mu kik dingin ka kingaihsun kei hi. Tua hi napi, Pasian in na tate zong kei hong musak hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Israel said unto Joseph, I had not thought to see thy face: and, lo, God hath shewed me also thy seed.

**48:12**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Josef in amaute a khuk panin lakhia-in amahmah lei lam nga-in a kun hi.
English: And Joseph brought them out from between his knees, and he bowed himself with his face to the earth.

**48:13**
Zolai: Josef in amau tegel la-in, Efraim’ taklam khut, Israel’ veilam khutah, Manasseh’ veilam khut, Israel’ taklam khutah a paipih hi.
English: And Joseph took them both, Ephraim in his right hand toward Israel's left hand, and Manasseh in his left hand toward Israel's right hand, and brought them near unto him.

**48:14**
Zolai: Israel in a taklam khut zanin a nauzaw Efraim’ lu tungah nga a, Manasseh a ta upa ahih manin, a khut kipaihpehsakin Manasseh’ lu tungah a veilam khut a nga hi.
English: And Israel stretched out his right hand, and laid it upon Ephraim's head, who was the younger, and his left hand upon Manasseh's head, guiding his hands wittingly; for Manasseh was the firstborn.

**48:15**
Zolai: Amah in Josef thupha pia-in, “Ka pate Abraham le Isaac in a na a sep Pasian, tuni dongin ka nuntak tawntung ah lam hong pi Pasian,
English: And he blessed Joseph, and said, God, before whom my fathers Abraham and Isaac did walk, the God which fed me all my life long unto this day,

**48:16**
Zolai: siatna khempeuh panin kei hong tankhia vantungmi in hih tangvalte thupha pia hen la, amaute sungah keima min le ka pa Abraham le Isaac’ min kizomsak hen la, leitungah amaute mi honpi khatin khangsak ta hen!” a ci hi.
English: the Angel which redeemed me from all evil, bless the lads; and let my name be named on them, and the name of my fathers Abraham and Isaac; and let them grow into a multitude in the midst of the earth.

**48:17**
Zolai: A pa in a taklam khut Efraim’ lu tungah a koih Josef in a muh ciangin, tua in amah lungkim lo sak hi. Efraim’ lu panin Manasseh’ lu tungah koih dingin amah in a pa’ khut a la hi.
English: And when Joseph saw that his father laid his right hand upon the head of Ephraim, it displeased him: and he held up his father's hand, to remove it from Ephraim's head unto Manasseh's head.

**48:18**
Zolai: Josef in a pa kiangah, “Hi lo hi, pa aw; hih pen a suak masa ahi hi. Na taklam khut ama lu tungah koih in,” a ci hi.
English: And Joseph said unto his father, Not so, my father: for this is the firstborn; put thy right hand upon his head.

**48:19**
Zolai: Ahih hangin a pa in nial a, “Ka thei hi, ka ta aw; ka thei hi. Amah zong mi khat suak ding a, amah zong lian ding hi. Ahi zongin amah sangin a naupa lianzaw ding a, a suanlekhakte, minam lianpi khat suak ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And his father refused, and said, I know it , my son, I know it: he also shall become a people, and he also shall be great: but truly his younger brother shall be greater than he, and his seed shall become a multitude of nations.

**48:20**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in tua ni-in amaute thupha pia a, “Note, Israel sungah thupha na hi ding uh a, ‘Pasian in Efraim le Manasseh bangin note hong bawl hen,’ kici ding hi,” a ci hi. Tua bangin Jakob in Manasseh’ mai-ah Efraim a koih hi.
English: And he blessed them that day, saying, In thee shall Israel bless, saying, God make thee as Ephraim and as Manasseh: and he set Ephraim before Manasseh.

**48:21**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Israel in Josef kiangah, “En in, kei a si ding ka hi ta hi. Ahih hangin Pasian in nang hong ompih ding a, na pate’ leitangah nang hong paipih kik ding hi.
English: And Israel said unto Joseph, Behold, I die: but God shall be with you, and bring you again unto the land of your fathers.

**48:22**
Zolai: Tua tham loin, ka namsau le ka thal tawh Amor mite’ khut tung panin ka lak mualpang khat, na sanggamte’ tung sangin nang’ tungah kong piazaw hi,” a ci hi.
English: Moreover I have given to thee one portion above thy brethren, which I took out of the hand of the Amorite with my sword and with my bow.

## Chapter 49

**49:1**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in a tapate sam a, “A hong tung ding hunte-ah note’ tunga hong tung ding thu kong gen theih nadingin note hong kikhawm un.
English: And Jacob called unto his sons, and said, Gather yourselves together, that I may tell you that which shall befall you in the last days.

**49:2**
Zolai: “Jakob’ tapate aw, hong kikhawmin za unla, na pa Israel’ thugen ngai un.
English: Gather yourselves together, and hear, ye sons of Jacob; And hearken unto Israel your father.

**49:3**
Zolai: “Reuben, nang pen ka ta upa, ka vangliatna le ka tacil na hi a, a kiphasak pen, a vanglian pen na hi hi.
English: Reuben, thou art my firstborn, my might, and the beginning of my strength, The excellency of dignity, and the excellency of power:

**49:4**
Zolai: Tuihual bangin na kip kei ding a, na tungtuang kei ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh ka zi na luppih a, ka lupna na mindaisak hi.
English: Unstable as water, thou shalt not excel; Because thou wentest up to thy father's bed; Then defiledst thou it: he went up to my couch.

**49:5**
Zolai: “Simeon le Levi, unau hi a, a hiam uh ngongtat nadingin a zang uh hi.
English: Simeon and Levi are brethren; Instruments of cruelty are in their habitations.

**49:6**
Zolai: Amau’ kikhopna-ah ka kihel kei ding a, amau’ pawl tawh ka kizom kei ding hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh a heh manun mi that uh a, kiphatsakna lungsim tawh amaute in mawlpih dingin bawngtalte’ zagui a sattat uh hi.
English: O my soul, come not thou into their secret; Unto their assembly, mine honour, be not thou united: For in their anger they slew a man, And in their selfwill they digged down a wall.

**49:7**
Zolai: Amau’ sinsona lauhuai a, amau’ hehna kihtakhuai hi. Samsiatna ngah ta uh hen! Jakob suante sungah amaute ka khenthang ding a, Israel sungah amaute ka thehthang ding hi.
English: Cursed be their anger, for it was fierce; And their wrath, for it was cruel: I will divide them in Jacob, And scatter them in Israel.

**49:8**
Zolai: “Judah aw, na sanggamte in nang hong phat ding hi. Na galte’ gawl na meek ding a, na sanggamte na mai-ah hong kun ding uh hi.
English: Judah, thou art he whom thy brethren shall praise: Thy hand shall be in the neck of thine enemies; Thy father's children shall bow down before thee.

**49:9**
Zolai: Judah pen humpinelkai tawh kibang a, a sa matsa a nek khit ciangin a kua-ah a ciahkik tawh kibang hi. Humpinelkai bangin kizia-in a lumsuk hi. Kua in amah phawng ngam ding hiam?
English: Judah is a lion's whelp: From the prey, my son, thou art gone up: He stooped down, he couched as a lion, And as an old lion; who shall rouse him up?

**49:10**
Zolai: Judah in kumpi ciangkhut len tawntung ding a, a suan a khakte in zong ukna aana nei tawntung ding hi. Minam dangte in ama tungah siah puak ding a, zahtakna tawh ama mai-ah kun ding uh hi.
English: The sceptre shall not depart from Judah, Nor a lawgiver from between his feet, Until Shiloh come; And unto him shall the gathering of the people be .

**49:11**
Zolai: A sakolno leenggui-ah khih a, a lano leenggui limci penah khih hi. Amah in a puante leenggahzu sungah sawp a, a puansilhte leenggahtui san sungah a sawp hi.
English: Binding his foal unto the vine, And his ass's colt unto the choice vine; He washed his garments in wine, And his clothes in the blood of grapes:

**49:12**
Zolai: Leenggahzu a neknekna-in a mit san gega a, bawngnawi a neknekna-in a ha pak hi.
English: His eyes shall be red with wine, And his teeth white with milk.

**49:13**
Zolai: “Zebulun, tuipi gei-ah teng ding hi. Amah, teembaw khawlna mun suak ding a, Sidon ciang dongah a gamgi om ding hi.
English: Zebulun shall dwell at the haven of the sea; And he shall be for an haven of ships; And his border shall be unto Zidon.

**49:14**
Zolai: “Issakhar, a hat la tawh kibang a, vangik nih kikalah a lum hi.
English: Issachar is a strong ass Couching down between two burdens:

**49:15**
Zolai: A tawlngakna mun hoihsa a, a leitang noptuak sa hi. Tua ahih ciangin van pua dingin a liangko niamsak a, sila bangin na kisemsak hi.
English: And he saw that rest was good, And the land that it was pleasant; And bowed his shoulder to bear, And became a servant unto tribute.

**49:16**
Zolai: “Dan in Israel minam dangte mah bangin a mite thu khen ding hi.
English: Dan shall judge his people, As one of the tribes of Israel.

**49:17**
Zolai: Dan pen lampi-ah gulpi hi ding a, sul gei-ah gulgu nei hi ding hi. Sakol’ khetul petin a tuang pa a nungkiat hi.
English: Dan shall be a serpent by the way, An adder in the path, That biteth the horse heels, So that his rider shall fall backward.

**49:18**
Zolai: “Nong hotkhiat ding ka ngak hi, Topa.
English: I have waited for thy salvation, O LORD .

**49:19**
Zolai: “Gad pen a buluhte in buluh ding a, ahih hangin amah in amaute sulzuih kik ding hi.
English: Gad, a troop shall overcome him: But he shall overcome at the last.

**49:20**
Zolai: “Asher’ lo-ah an tampi piang ding a, amah in kumpi anlimte bawl ding hi.
English: Out of Asher his bread shall be fat, And he shall yield royal dainties.

**49:21**
Zolai: “Naftali, a kikhah sakhipi hi a, sakhino suakkhiasak hi.
English: Naphtali is a hind let loose: He giveth goodly words.

**49:22**
Zolai: “Josef, a gah pha hiang ahi hi. Ciktui gei-a om a gah pha hiang hi a, a hiangte kulh tungah zaam hi.
English: Joseph is a fruitful bough, Even a fruitful bough by a well; Whose branches run over the wall:

**49:23**
Zolai: Thal tawite in nakpitakin amah simin, amah thal tawh kap uh a, nasia takin gimsak uh hi.
English: The archers have sorely grieved him, And shot at him , and hated him:

**49:24**
Zolai: Ahih hangin ama thal ling loin om a, a khutte kizaptelsak hi. Jakob’ Vanglian Pa’ khut (Israel Suangpi, Tuucingpa’ min),
English: But his bow abode in strength, And the arms of his hands were made strong By the hands of the mighty God of Jacob; (From thence is the shepherd, the stone of Israel:)

**49:25**
Zolai: nang hong huh ding na pa’ Pasian in tunga om vantung thuphate, nuai-a tuithukna sunga om thuphate, khawilevulh le tuletate, nangma tungah hong pia hi.
English: Even by the God of thy father, who shall help thee; And by the Almighty, who shall bless thee With blessings of heaven above, Blessings of the deep that lieth under, Blessings of the breasts, and of the womb:

**49:26**
Zolai: Na pa’ thuphate pen tawntung mual liante’ thupha, tawntung mual neute sangin vanglian zaw hi. Tua thuphate Josef’ lu tungah hong tung hen la, a sanggamte’ kiang panin a kituam koihpa’ tungah hong tung tahen.
English: The blessings of thy father Have prevailed above the blessings of my progenitors Unto the utmost bound of the everlasting hills: They shall be on the head of Joseph, And on the crown of the head of him that was separate from his brethren.

**49:27**
Zolai: “Benjamin, a ne bakbak keivom hi a, zingsangin a sa matsa ne-in, nitakin a ngahsa teng hawm hi,” a ci hi.
English: Benjamin shall ravin as a wolf: In the morning he shall devour the prey, And at night he shall divide the spoil.

**49:28**
Zolai: Hihte khempeuh pen Israel minam sawm le nihte ahi hi. Hih thute pen amau tawh a kituak ciatin a pa in amaute thupha pia-in a gente ahi hi.
English: All these are the twelve tribes of Israel: and this is it that their father spake unto them, and blessed them; every one according to his blessing he blessed them.

**49:29**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Jakob in a tate thuhilhin amaute kiangah, “Kei, ka mipihte kiangah a kigawm ding ka hita hi. Kivui nading munin neih dingin Abraham in Hit mi Efron’ tung panin a lo tawh a leikhop, Kanaan gam, Mamre nisuahna lamah a om Makpelah lo-a leihawm, Hit mi Efron’ lo-a leihawm han sungah ka pate tawh hong vuikhawm un.
English: And he charged them, and said unto them, I am to be gathered unto my people: bury me with my fathers in the cave that is in the field of Ephron the Hittite,

**49:31**
Zolai: Tua lai munah amaute in Abraham le a zi Sarah vui uh hi. Tua lai munah amaute in Isaac le a zi Rebekah vui uh hi. Tua lai munah keimah in Leah ka vui hi.
English: There they buried Abraham and Sarah his wife; there they buried Isaac and Rebekah his wife; and there I buried Leah.

**49:32**
Zolai: Lo le tua sunga om leihawm Hit mite’ tung panin a kilei ahi hi,” a ci hi.
English: The purchase of the field and of the cave that is therein was from the children of Heth.

**49:33**
Zolai: Jakob in a tapate thuhilh a man khit ciangin, a lupna tungah laitat a, a nunung pen a hu sang-in ama mipihte kiang a zuan ta hi.
English: And when Jacob had made an end of commanding his sons, he gathered up his feet into the bed, and yielded up the ghost, and was gathered unto his people.

## Chapter 50

**50:1**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Josef a pa’ tungah pukin, ama tungah kap a, amah a nam hi.
English: And Joseph fell upon his father's face, and wept upon him, and kissed him.

**50:2**
Zolai: A pa a muat loh nadingin a bawl dingin Josef in a nasem zatui siamte thu pia hi. Tua ahih ciangin zatui siamte in zatui tawh Israel a bawl uh hi.
English: And Joseph commanded his servants the physicians to embalm his father: and the physicians embalmed Israel.

**50:3**
Zolai: Zatui tawh bawlna nasep hun tampi kisam a, ni sawmli sung sep ding kisam hi. Egypt mite ama hangin ni sawmsagih sung a kap uh hi.
English: And forty days were fulfilled for him; for so are fulfilled the days of those which are embalmed: and the Egyptians mourned for him threescore and ten days.

**50:4**
Zolai: Ama hangin kahna hun a bei ciangin Josef in Faro’ innkuante kiangah, “Tu-in note’ mai-ah maipha ka ngah leh Faro’ kiangah thu nong va gensak ding uh kong thum hi.
English: And when the days of his mourning were past, Joseph spake unto the house of Pharaoh, saying, If now I have found grace in your eyes, speak, I pray you, in the ears of Pharaoh, saying,

**50:5**
Zolai: Ka pa in kei hong kiciamsak a, ‘Kei a si ding ka hi ta hi. Kanaan leitangah kei a dingin ka khuatsa han sungah kei nong vui ding hi,’ hong ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin tu-in kei hong paitosak inla, ka pa hong vuisak in, ci-in kong thum hi. Tua ciangin kei kong ciahkik ding hi, ci hi, va cihsak un,” a ci hi.
English: My father made me swear, saying, Lo, I die: in my grave which I have digged for me in the land of Canaan, there shalt thou bury me. Now therefore let me go up, I pray thee, and bury my father, and I will come again.

**50:6**
Zolai: Faro in dawngin, “Paito inla, nang hong kiciamsak bangin na pa va vui in,” a ci hi.
English: And Pharaoh said, Go up, and bury thy father, according as he made thee swear.

**50:7**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin a pa a vui dingin Josef paito hi. Amah tawh Faro’ nasemte khempeuh, a innsung upate, Egypt gam upate khempeuh zong,
English: And Joseph went up to bury his father: and with him went up all the servants of Pharaoh, the elders of his house, and all the elders of the land of Egypt,

**50:8**
Zolai: Josef’ innkuante khempeuh, a sanggamte, a pa’ innkuante bangmahin paito uh hi. A tate uh, a tuuhonte uh le a ganhing honte bek uh Goshen gamah kinusia hi.
English: and all the house of Joseph, and his brethren, and his father's house: only their little ones, and their flocks, and their herds, they left in the land of Goshen.

**50:9**
Zolai: Tua lai munah amah tawh leengte le sakol tuangte zong paikhawm to uh hi. Tua lai-a paite tam mahmah hi.
English: And there went up with him both chariots and horsemen: and it was a very great company.

**50:10**
Zolai: Amaute Jordan gun galkhat, Atad’ buhcilna phual a tun uh ciangin, nakpitakin dahna tawh a thuum uh hi. Amah in a pa’ hangin ni sagih sung dahna hun a bawl hi.
English: And they came to the threshingfloor of Atad, which is beyond Jordan, and there they mourned with a great and very sore lamentation: and he made a mourning for his father seven days.

**50:11**
Zolai: Tua gam a teng Kanaan mite in, Atad’ buhcilna-ah tua banga kahna a muh ciangin amaute in, “Hih pen Egypt mite a dingin a nasia mahmah thuumna ahi hi,” a ci uh hi. Tua ahih ciangin tua mun pen Abelmizraim, kici hi. Tua mun pen Jordan gun galkhat ahi hi.
English: And when the inhabitants of the land, the Canaanites, saw the mourning in the floor of Atad, they said, This is a grievous mourning to the Egyptians: wherefore the name of it was called Abel-mizraim, which is beyond Jordan.

**50:12**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amah in amaute a thupiak bangin ama tapate in ama a dingin bawlsak uh hi.
English: And his sons did unto him according as he commanded them:

**50:13**
Zolai: Bang hang hiam cih leh ama tapate in Kanaan gamah amah pua-in, kivui nading mun a neih dingin Abraham in Hit mi Efron’ tung panin a lo tawh a leikhop, Mamre nisuahna lamah a om, Makpelah mun lo sunga leihawm sungah a vui uh hi.
English: for his sons carried him into the land of Canaan, and buried him in the cave of the field of Machpelah, which Abraham bought with the field for a possession of a buryingplace of Ephron the Hittite, before Mamre.

**50:14**
Zolai: Josef in a pa a vui khit ciangin, a sanggamte le a pa a vui dingin amah a zui khempeuhte tawh Egypt-ah a ciahkik hi.
English: And Joseph returned into Egypt, he, and his brethren, and all that went up with him to bury his father, after he had buried his father.

**50:15**
Zolai: Josef’ sanggamte in a pa uh a sih khit ciangin, “Josef in eite hong mudahin ama tunga siatna i bawl khempeuh hong thukkik kha ding hi,” ci uh hi.
English: And when Joseph's brethren saw that their father was dead, they said, Joseph will peradventure hate us, and will certainly requite us all the evil which we did unto him.

**50:16**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin amaute in Josef kiangah thu puak uh a, “I pa in a sih ma-in thu hong pia a,
English: And they sent a messenger unto Joseph, saying, Thy father did command before he died, saying,

**50:17**
Zolai: ‘Josef kiangah hih bangin ci un: Na sanggamte’ thupalsatna le a khialhna na maisak in, kong thum hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh nang’ tungah amaute in siatna hong bawl uh hi,’ ci hi. Tua ahih ciangin tu-in nang’ tungah kong thum uh hi. I pa’ Pasian’ nasemte’ thupalsatna hong maisak in,” a ci uh hi. Amaute in ama kiangah tua bangin thu a gen ciangun Josef a kap hi.
English: So shall ye say unto Joseph, Forgive, I pray thee now, the trespass of thy brethren, and their sin; for they did unto thee evil: and now, we pray thee, forgive the trespass of the servants of the God of thy father. And Joseph wept when they spake unto him.

**50:18**
Zolai: A sanggamte zong pai-in ama mai-ah puk uh a, “En in, kote, nangma nasemte ka hi uh hi,” a ci uh hi.
English: And his brethren also went and fell down before his face; and they said, Behold, we be thy servants.

**50:19**
Zolai: Ahih hangin Josef in amaute kiangah, “Lau kei un. Kei, Pasian’ za-ah om ka hi hiam?
English: And Joseph said unto them, Fear not: for am I in the place of God?

**50:20**
Zolai: Note in ahihleh, kei’ tungah a sia dingin na ngaihsun uh hi. Ahih hangin Pasian in tuhuna mah bangin mi tampite a nuntak theihna a pian nadingin a hoih dingin a ngaihsut ahi hi.
English: But as for you, ye thought evil against me; but God meant it unto good, to bring to pass, as it is this day, to save much people alive.

**50:21**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin lau kei un. Note le na tate uh a dingin an kong pia ding hi,” a ci hi. Amah in tua bangin kip gen pha kikin amaute a hehnem hi.
English: Now therefore fear ye not: I will nourish you, and your little ones. And he comforted them, and spake kindly unto them.

**50:22**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin Josef, amah le a pa’ innkuante tawh Egypt-ah teng uh a, Josef kum za le kum sawm nungta hi.
English: And Joseph dwelt in Egypt, he, and his father's house: and Joseph lived an hundred and ten years.

**50:23**
Zolai: Josef in khang thumna ahi Efraim’ tate mu hi. Manasseh’ tapa Makhir’ tate zong Josef’ innsung mahah suak uh hi.
English: And Joseph saw Ephraim's children of the third generation: the children also of Machir the son of Manasseh were brought up upon Joseph's knees.

**50:24**
Zolai: Josef in a sanggamte kiangah, “Kei a si ding ka hi ta hi. Ahih hangin Pasian in note hong kem ding a, hih leitang panin amah in Abraham, Isaac, le Jakob tunga a ciamsa leitangah note hong paikhiatpih to ding hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Joseph said unto his brethren, I die: and God will surely visit you, and bring you out of this land unto the land which he sware to Abraham, to Isaac, and to Jacob.

**50:25**
Zolai: Tua ciangin Josef in Israel tapate’ kiciamna bawlin, “Pasian in note hong kem ding a, note in hih lai panin ka guhte na pua to ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
English: And Joseph took an oath of the children of Israel, saying, God will surely visit you, and ye shall carry up my bones from hence.

**50:26**
Zolai: Tua ahih ciangin kum za le kum sawm a pha-in Josef a si hi. Amaute in a muat loh nadingin zatui tawh amah bawl uh a, Egypt-ah hankuang sung khatah amah kikoih hi.
English: So Joseph died, being an hundred and ten years old: and they embalmed him, and he was put in a coffin in Egypt.
